nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya naram ca eva narottamam dvaipāyana oṣṭha puṭa niḥsṛtam aprameyam puṇyam pavitram atha pāpa haram śubham ca pārāśaryāya śāntāya namaḥ nārāyaṇāya tvad kṛta abhiṣekam tanayam rājñaḥ pārīkṣitasya ha draṣṭum abhyāyayuḥ prītyā śaunaka ādyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ tān āgatān sa rājarṣiḥ pādya arghya ādibhiḥ arcitān sukha upaviṣṭān viśrāntān kṛta saṃpraśna sat kathān tad kathābhiḥ kṛta āhlādaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ śatānīkaḥ atha papraccha nārāyaṇa kathām parām yam āśritya jagannātham mama pūrva pitāmahāḥ vipakṣa apahṛtam rājyam avāpuḥ puruṣa uttamāḥ parīkṣit prāṇa saṃyogam devadevena lambhitaḥ śrutam su bahuśas mayā stutasya aśeṣa janmanaḥ tasya devasya kaḥ śaktaḥ pravaktum vā vibhūtayaḥ śrotum ārādhanam yena nistareyam bhava arṇavam ārādhitaḥ samastānām kleśānām hāni daḥ hariḥ śakyaḥ samārādhayitum tat naḥ śaṃsata sattamāḥ vidyānām api sā vidyā śrutānām api tat śrutam rahasyānām rahasyam tat yena viṣṇuḥ prasīdati mantrāṇām paramaḥ mantraḥ vratānām tat mahāvratam upoṣitam hi tat śreṣṭham yena tuṣyati keśavaḥ yat eva pulaka udbhāsi viṣṇoḥ nāma abhikīrtanāt sā hāniḥ tat mahat chidram sā ca andha jaḍa mūka tā yat muhūrtam kṣaṇam vā api vāsudevaḥ na cintyate nūnam tat kaṇṭhaśālūkam athavā pratijihvikā rogaḥ vā anyaḥ na sā jihvā yā na vakti hareḥ guṇān dharma artha kāma saṃprāptau puruṣāṇām viceṣṭitam janmani aviphalā sā ekā yā govinda āśrayā kriyā durga saṃsāra kāntāram apāram abhidhāvatām ekaḥ kṛṣṇa namaskāraḥ mukti tīrasya deśikaḥ evam ādi guṇaḥ bhogaḥ kṛṣṇasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ śrutaḥ me bahuśas siddhaiḥ gīyamānaḥ tathā aparaiḥ nārāyaṇam aśeṣasya jagataḥ hṛdi avasthitam śaṃkaram jagataḥ prāṇam smṛta mātra agha hāriṇam tat mama adya muni śreṣṭhāḥ prasādayitum icchataḥ sarve ca te muni śreṣṭhāḥ bhṛgu śreṣṭham ca śaunakam bhaktyā ca devadevasya pravaṇīkṛta mānasaḥ kṛtvā uttarīya paryaṅkam śithilam bhagavān atha pratyuvāca mahābhāgaḥ śaunakaḥ tam mahīpatim yat pṛcchasi mahīpāla kṛṣṇasya ārādhanam prati vrata upavāsa japya ādi tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu pradhāna puruṣa tvam ca tathā evā īśvara līlayā tatas sthitau pālayitā viṣṇu tvam jagataḥ kṣaye pravakṣyāmi yathā pūrvam mad pitrā kathitam mama tasya api kila tad pitrā tasmai ca āha kila uśanāḥ tena api bhṛgum ārādhya prāptam ārādhanam hareḥ sakāśāt brahmaṇaḥ prāptam bhṛguṇā api mahātmanā marīci miśraiḥ ca purā param etat mahā ṛṣibhiḥ prāptam sakāśāt devasya brahmaṇaḥ vyakta janmanaḥ yogam brahmā param prāha mahā ṛṣīṇām yadā prabhuḥ viṣayāḥ durjayāḥ nR̥ṇām indriya ākarṣaṇāḥ prabho vṛttayaḥ cetasaḥ ca api capalā ca ati durdharāḥ rāga ādayaḥ katham jetum śakyāḥ varṣa śataiḥ api alpa āyuṣaḥ ca puruṣāḥ brahman kṛta yuge api amī duḥkha ambu magnāḥ puruṣāḥ prāpya brahma mahā plavam evam uktaḥ tadā brahmā kriyā yogam mahātmanām teṣām ṛṣīṇām ācaṣṭa narāṇām hita kāmyayā ārādhayata viśveśam nārāyaṇam atandritāḥ bāhya ālambana sāpekṣāḥ tam ajam jagataḥ patim ijyā pūjā namaskāra śuśrūṣābhiḥ aharniśam vrata upavāsaiḥ vividhaiḥ brāhmaṇānām ca tarpaṇaiḥ taiḥ taiḥ ca abhimataiḥ kāmaiḥ ye ca cetasi tuṣṭi dāḥ tad niṣṭhāḥ tad gata dhiyaḥ tad karmāṇaḥ tad āśrayāḥ saṃnyasyadhvam sa vaḥ kartā samasta āvaraṇa kṣayam paraḥ parāṇām paramaḥ saḥ ekaḥ puruṣottamaḥ tam ārādhya jagannātham mokṣa kāraṇam avyaktam iti te brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā rahasyam ṛṣi sattamāḥ narāṇām upakārāya yoga śāstrāṇi cakrire kriyāyoga parāṇi iha mukti kāryāṇi anekaśas ārādhyate jagannāthaḥ yad anuṣṭhāna tatparaiḥ tāni te nṛpa śārdūla sarva pāpa harāṇi aham saṃsāra arṇava magnānām viṣaya ākrānta cetasām uttāram icchatām tasmāt bhṛśam yat na antaraiḥ api viṣṇu potam vinā na anyat kiṃcid asti parāyaṇam uttiṣṭhan cintaya harim vrajan cintaya keśavam janma mṛtyu jarā grāham saṃsāra ambhaḥ tariṣyasi anantam īḍyam puruṣam purāṇam jagat vidhātāram ajam janitryam samāśritāḥ ye harim īśitāram teṣām bhavaḥ na asti hi mukti bhājām śrūyatām kuru śārdūla saṃvādaḥ ayam anuttamaḥ ambarīṣasya rājarṣeḥ saha devena cakriṇā ambarīṣaḥ mahīpālaḥ pālayan eva medinīm tutoṣa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarva loka patiḥ prabhuḥ na aham ārādhayāmi tvām tava baddhaḥ ayam añjaliḥ vara arthinām tvam vara daḥ prayaccha abhimatān varān vara arthāya tvayā anyaiḥ ca kriyate nṛpate tapaḥ viṣṇoḥ ārādhana arthāya viddhi mām tvam kṛta udyamam pālayanti mama eva ājñām āditya ādyāḥ sadā surāḥ ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ nāsatyau marutām gaṇāḥ prajānām patayaḥ sādhyāḥ viśvedevāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ mattaḥ hi kaḥ anyaḥ vara daḥ pratigṛhṇīṣva vāñchitam tvayā api prāptam aiśvaryam yatas tam toṣayāmi aham sapta udare śayāḥ lokāḥ tam īśam toṣayāmi aham nimeṣaḥ brahmaṇaḥ rātriḥ unmeṣaḥ yasya vāsaraḥ tam īḍyam īśam ajaram praṇataḥ asmi janārdanam yaḥ hartā jagataḥ devaḥ kartā pālāyitā ca yaḥ trayasya asya ca yaḥ yoniḥ tam viṣṇum toṣayāmi aham hiraṇya kaśipuḥ pūrvam hiraṇya akṣaḥ ca te ripuḥ balinā apahṛtam śakra dattam yena purā tava trailokya rājyam tam baddhvā tam namāmi janārdanam tapaḥ tapsye jagannātham draṣṭum nārāyaṇam harim śrūyate kila govinde bhaktim udvahatām nṛṇām saṃsāra arṇau abhītānām tridaśāḥ paripanthinaḥ tāpasaḥ aham kva niḥsaṅgaḥ kva ca kopaḥ tava īdṛśaḥ sa tvam prahara vā mā vā mayi vajram puraṃdara na aham utsṛjya govindam anyam ārādhayāmi bhoḥ na ca api vajram vajrī vā tvam ca nā anye sura asurāḥ śaktāḥ nihantum īśāne hṛdaya sthe janārdane kim ca naḥ bahunā uktena na aham vakṣyāmi atas param cacāra maunam āsthāya tena atuṣyata keśavaḥ saṃdarśayām āsa tatas svam vapuḥ kaiṭabha ardanaḥ caturbhujam udāra aṅgam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam kirīṭa sraj dharam spaṣṭam nīlotpala dala chavim airāvataḥ ca garuḍaḥ tad kṣaṇāt samadṛśyata pratyuvāca ca bhūpālaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ jaya aspaṣṭa prakāśa aṇḍa bṛhat mūrte jaya akṣara jaya vijñāta siddhānta māyā mohaka keśava nṛsiṃha jaya devāri vakṣaḥsthala vidāraṇa devānām ari bhītānām ārti nāśana vāmana namaḥ astu avyapadeśyāya namaḥ sūkṣma svarūpiṇe viśeṣaiḥ aviśeṣyāya tasmai tubhyam namaḥ namaḥ puruṣa ākhyam tatas rūpam nirguṇam guṇa bhoktṛ ca prakṛteḥ paratas sūkṣmam tat namasyāmi te hare avyakta ādi viśeṣa antam ati sūkṣmatamam mahat prākṛtam tava tat rūpam tasmai deva namāmi aham prasīda viṣṇo govinda śaṅkha cakra gadā dhara dharādhara aravinda akṣa vāsudeva maheśvara ambarīṣam pṛthivī īśam jagat saṃnādayan girā varam vṛṇīṣva dharma jña yat te manasi vartate eṣaḥ eva varaḥ ślāghyaḥ yat dṛṣṭaḥ asi jagatpate vetti tām bhagavān eva hṛdisthaḥ sarva dehinām tvad prasādāt mama īśāna rājyam avyāhatam bhuvi kośa daṇḍau tathā atīva śarīra ārogyam uttamam striyaḥ anna pāna sāmarthyāḥ hāniḥ su alpā api nā asti me saṃtatiḥ nibhṛtā bhṛtyā sa anurāgāḥ ca me janāḥ jñātam mayā hi govinde na aprasanne vibhūtayaḥ punarāvṛtti duḥkhānām trāsāt udvigna mānasaḥ sukhāni tāni na eva ante yeṣām duḥkham na tat sukham yat ante duḥkham āgāmi kiṃpākasya eva bhakṣaṇam jñāna dānena yena imām vāgurāt nistaremahi upadiṣṭe tatas yoge praṇipatya acyutam nṛpaḥ punar prāha mahā bāhuḥ vinaya avanataḥ sthitaḥ viṣayāḥ durjayāḥ puṃbhiḥ indriya ākarṣiṇaḥ sadā indriyāṇām jayam teṣu kaḥ śaktānām kariṣyati aham mama iti ca ākhyāti durjayam cañcalam manaḥ rāga ādayaḥ katham jetum śakyāḥ janma antaraiḥ api rāga ādibhiḥ amartya tvam prāptum prakṣīṇa kalmaṣaḥ yadi evam mukti kāmaḥ tvam nara nātha śṛṇuṣva tat kriyā yogam samastānām kleśānām hāni kārakam mām eva eṣyasi yuktvā evam ātmānam mad parāyaṇaḥ mad bhāvanāḥ mad yajanāḥ mad bhaktāḥ mad parāyaṇāḥ mama pūjā parāḥ ca eva mayi yānti layam narāḥ sarva bhūteṣu mām paśya samavasthitam īśvaram kartāsi kena vaira tvam evam doṣān prahāsyasi jaṅgama ajaṅgame jñāte mayi ātmani tathā tava rāga lobha ādi nāśena bhavitrī kṛtakṛtya tā mayi anāsādavat bhūpa kuru mad rūpiṇīm tanum suvarṇa rajata ādyaiḥ tvam śaila mṛd dāru lekha jām tasyām cittam samāveśya tyājaya anyān vyapāśrayān pūjitā sā eva te bhaktyā dhyātā ca eva upakāriṇī gacchan tiṣṭhan svapan bhuñjan tām eva agre ca pṛṣṭhatas vāsobhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ bhakṣyaiḥ gīta vādyaiḥ manoharaiḥ yat ca yat ca nṛpa iṣṭam te kiṃcid bhojya ādi tena tām bhakti namraḥ nara śreṣṭha prīṇaya arcām kṛtām mama rāgeṇa ākṛṣyate cetaḥ gandharva abhimukham yadi mayi buddhim samāveśya gāyethāḥ mama tām kathām śrotavyā prīti yuktena avatāreṣu yā kathā evam mayi arpita manāḥ cetasaḥ ye vyapāśrayāḥ akṣīṇa rāga doṣaḥ api mad kriyā paramaḥ param rājyam kuru nara śreṣṭha nivedya pṛthivīm mama mad hitāya jagannātha kriyā yoga āśritam mama mad prasādāt avikalam sa ca vetsyati aśeṣatas vasiṣṭham paripapraccha viṣṇoḥ ārādhanam prati kriyā yoga āśritam sarvam vyākhyāsyati bhavān kila sa tvām pṛcchāmi aham sarvam kriyā yogena keśavam saṃtoṣayitum īśānam yathā śakṣyāmi tat vada deva prasādāt akhilā mama api smṛtiḥ āgatā jñānam etat aśeṣam te kathayāmi nibodha tat nārāyaṇe mahā prajñaḥ sarva loka parāyaṇe sa papraccha bhṛgu śreṣṭham śukram ātma purohitam bhagavat nṛsiṃha rūpasya viṣṇoḥ tātam jighāṃsataḥ dṛṣṭam dehe mayā sarvam trailokyam bhūrbhuva ādikam vasavaḥ aṣṭau tathā ādityāḥ dvādaśa ahar kṣapā mahī aśvinau marutaḥ sādhyāḥ viśvedevāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ varṣa acalāḥ tathā nadyaḥ sapta sapta kula acalāḥ samudrāḥ sapta ṛtavaḥ kāntārāṇi vanāni ca sa tiryak ūrdhva pātālam tasya dṛṣṭam tanau mayā saḥ aham tam ajaram devam duṣṭa daitya nivarhaṇam ārādhayitum icchāmi bhagavan tvad anujñayā tat mama upadiśa adya tvam mahat ārādhanam hareḥ na hi abhāgavataiḥ viṣṇuḥ jñātum stotum ca tattvataḥ draṣṭum vā śakyate martyaiḥ praveṣṭum kutas eva hi na akṣīṇe jāyate puṃsām govinda abhimukhī matiḥ pradveṣam yāti govinde dvijān vedān ca nindati yaḥ naraḥ tam vijānīyāt asura aṃśa samudbhavam pāṣaṇḍeṣu ratiḥ puṃsām hetuvāda anukūla tā jāyate viṣṇu māyā ambhaḥ patitānām durātmanām yadā pāpa kṣayaḥ puṃsām tadā veda dvijātiṣu viṣṇau ca yajñapuruṣe śraddhā bhavati te yathā yadā su alpa avaśeṣaḥ tu narāṇām pāpa saṃcayaḥ bhrāmyatām atra saṃsāre narāṇām karma durgame sa tvam bhāgavataḥ bhūtvā sarva pāpa haram harim ārādhaya param bhaktyā prītim eṣyati keśavaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇāḥ bhāgavatāḥ bhavanti puruṣāḥ guro karmaṇā manasā vācā prāṇinām yaḥ na hiṃsakaḥ yaḥ brāhmaṇān ca vedān ca nityam envā anumaṃsyati sarvān devān harim vetti sarva lokān ca keśavam tebhyaḥ ca na anyam ātmānam daitya bhāgavataḥ hi saḥ devam manuṣyam anyam vā paśu pakṣi pipīlikān taru pāṣāṇa kaṣṭha ādi bhūmi ambhaḥ gaganam diśaḥ ātmānam vā api deveśāt na atiriktam janārdanāt yaḥ bhajeta vijānīṣva tam vai bhāgavatam naram karmaṇā manasā vācā sa tu bhāgavataḥ naraḥ bhāvena niṣpādayati jñeyaḥ bhāgavataḥ tu saḥ na arayaḥ yasya na snigdhāḥ na ca udāsī na vṛttayaḥ paśyataḥ sarvam eva idam viṣṇum bhāgavataḥ hi saḥ su taptena iha tapasā yajñaiḥ vā bahu dakṣiṇaiḥ tām gatim na narāḥ yānti yām vai bhāgavatāḥ gatāḥ arvāk nirīkṣyate yajñī kimu ye yoga pāragāḥ yajña niṣpattaye vedāḥ yajñaḥ yajñapateḥ kṛte tad toṣaṇāya bhāvena tasmāt bhāgavataḥ bhava yena sarva ātmanā viṣṇau bhaktyā bhāvaḥ niveśitaḥ daitya īśvara kṛtārtha tvāt ślāghyaḥ bhāgavataḥ hi saḥ bhagavān bhakti bhāvena yena viṣṇuḥ upāsitaḥ yaḥ kārayati deva arcām hṛdaya ālambanam hareḥ sa naraḥ viṣṇu sālokyam upaiti dhūta kalmaṣaḥ yaḥ ca devālayam bhaktyā viṣṇoḥ kārayati svayam sa sapta puruṣān lokān viṣṇoḥ nayati mānavaḥ yāvanti abdāni deva arcā hareḥ tiṣṭhati mandire tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi viṣṇu loke sa modate deva arcā lakṣaṇa upetā tad gṛham satatam divi niṣkāmam ca manaḥ yasya sa yāti akṣara sātmya tām puṣpāṇi ati sugandhīni manojñāni ca yaḥ pumān prayacchati hṛṣīkeśe tad bhāva gata mānasaḥ dhūpān ca vividhān tān tān gandha āḍhyam ca anulepanam dīpa āvali upahārān ca yat ca abhīṣṭam atha ātmanaḥ naraḥ saḥ anudinam yajñam karoti ārādhanam hareḥ yajñeśaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ makhaiḥ api hi toṣyate bahu upakaraṇāḥ yajñāḥ nānā saṃbhāra vistarāḥ bhaktyā ca puruṣaiḥ pūjā kṛtā dūrvā aṅkuraiḥ api yāni puṣpāṇi hṛdyāni dhūpa gandha anulepanam dayitam bhūṣaṇam yat ca ye ca kauśeya vāsasī yāni ca abhyavahārāṇi bhakṣyāṇi ca phalāni ca ādi antam yajñapuruṣam yathāśaktyā prasādaya kṣīreṇa snāpayet īśam acyutam jagataḥ patim dadhi kṣīra hradān puṇyān tatas lokān madhu cyutaḥ prayāsyasi asura śreṣṭha nirvṛtim ca api śāśvatīm stotraiḥ gītaiḥ tathā vādyaiḥ brāhmaṇānām ca tarpaṇaiḥ manasaḥ ca eka tā yogāt ārādhaya janārdanam ārādhya tam videhānām puruṣāḥ saptasaptatiḥ haihayāḥ pañcapañcāśat amṛta tvam upāgatāḥ toṣayāt yaḥ hi tuṣṭaḥ asau viṣṇuḥ dvandva praśānti daḥ upavāsaiḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ katham tuṣyati bhārgava parihārān tathā ācakṣva ye tyājyāḥ ca upavāsinām yat yat kāryam yathā ca eva keśava ārādhane naraiḥ smṛtaḥ saṃpūjitaḥ dhūpa puṣpa ādyaiḥ dayitaiḥ hariḥ bhoginām upakārāya kim punar ca upavāsinām upāvṛttaḥ tu pāpebhyaḥ yaḥ tu vāsaḥ guṇaiḥ saha eka rātram dvi rātram vā tri rātram athavā aparam upavāsī harim yaḥ tu bhaktyā dhyāyati mānavaḥ yam ca kāmam abhidhyāyan keśava arpita mānasaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiḥ strībhiḥ tathā mune an ārādhya jagannātham sarva dhātāram acyutam sa katham pāpa paṅka aṅkī naraḥ yāsyati sat gatim tat ārādhaya sarva īśam jagaddhātāram acyutam puṣpaiḥ sugandhaiḥ hṛdyaiḥ ca dhūpaiḥ sa agaru candanaiḥ vāsobhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ bhakṣyaiḥ upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ tat ārādhaya govindam yat ca iṣṭam tava cetasi puṣpāṇi yadi te na syuḥ śastam pādapa pallavaiḥ sugandhi puṣpa dīpa ādyaiḥ yaḥ kuryāt keśava ālaye pūjitaḥ tuṣṭim atulām bhaktyā āyāti ekacetasām yaḥ sat āyatane viṣṇoḥ kurute mārjana kriyām sa pāṃsu bhūmeḥ dehāt ca sarva pāpam vyapohati yāvantyaḥ pāṃsu kaṇikāḥ mārjyante keśava ālaye gocarma mātram saṃmārjya hanti tat keśava ālaye yaḥ ca upalepanam kuryāt viṣṇoḥ āyatane naraḥ mṛdā dhātu vikāraiḥ vā varṇakaiḥ gomayena vā udaka abhyukṣaṇam viṣṇoḥ yaḥ karoti tathā gṛhe saḥ api gacchati yatra āste bhagavān yādasām patiḥ samāpnoti naraḥ dattvā dīpakam keśavālaye yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram pūrṇam tila pātra pradaḥ naraḥ vidhunvan hanti vātena dātuḥ ajñānataḥ kṛtam pāpam ketuḥ gṛhe viṣṇoḥ divārātram asaṃśayam gīta vādya ādibhiḥ devam yaḥ upāste janārdanam prāpnoti viṣṇvāyatane puṇya ākhyāna kathā karaḥ upoṣitaḥ pūjitaḥ vā dṛṣṭaḥ vā namitaḥ api vā veda vāda kriyā yajña snāna tīrtha phalam param aṣṭāṅga praṇipātena praṇipatya harim labhet pragamya hṛdā śirasā pāda padme mahī tale niṣkalmaṣaḥ bhavet sadyas na nāṭī pāda pāṃsunā ekasya kṛṣṇasya krājataḥ praṇāmaḥ daśa aśvamedha avabhṛthena tulyaḥ daśa aśvamedhaiḥ punar eti janma kṛṣṇa praṇāmī na punarbhavāya evam deveśvaraḥ bhaktyā yena viṣṇuḥ upāsitaḥ sa prāpnoti gatim ślāghyām yām yām icchati cetasā śakraḥ kratu śatena īśam ārādhya garuḍadhvajam tasya api yajñapuruṣaḥ viṣṇuḥ pūjyaḥ dvijottama vaikhānasānām ārādhyaḥ tapobhiḥ madhusūdanaḥ dhyeyaḥ parivrājakānām vāsudevaḥ mahātmanām evam sarva āśramāṇām hi vāsudevaḥ parāyaṇam sarveṣām ca eva varṇānām tam ārādhya āpnuyāt gatim śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ kāmyām upavāsān tathā aparān tat tam āśritya yān kāmān kurvīta īpsitam ātmanaḥ ekādaśyām śukla pakṣe phālgune māsi yaḥ naraḥ japet kṛṣṇa iti devasya nāma bhaktyā punar punar deva arcane ca aṣṭaśatam kṛtvā etat tu japet śuciḥ pāṣaṇḍa patitān ca eva tathā eva antyāvasāyinaḥ na ālapeta tathā kṛṣṇam arcayet śraddhayā anvitaḥ idam ca udāharet kṛṣṇe manaḥ saṃdhāya tad paraḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa kṛpāluḥ tvam agatīnām gatiḥ bhava saṃsāra antar nimagnānām prasīda madhusūdana evam prasādya upāvāsam kṛtvā niyata mānasaḥ pūrvāhne eva ca anyedyus gavyam saṃprāsya vai sakṛt snātaḥ arcayitvā kṛṣṇā iti punar nāma prakīrtayet vāri dhārā trayam ca eva vikṣipet deva pādayoḥ martya loke gatim śreṣṭhām dālbhya prāpnoti vai naraḥ utkrānti kāle kṛṣṇasya smaraṇam ca tathā āpnute āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe ca eva māse bhādrapade tathā upoṣya saṃpūjya tathā keśava iti ca kīrtayet go mūtra prāśanāt pūrvam svarga loka gatim vrajet ārādhitasya jagatām īśvarasya avyāya ātmanaḥ utkrānti kāle smaraṇam keśavasya tathā āpnuyāt kṣīrasya prāśanam yaḥ tu vidhim ca imam yathā uditam kārttika ādi yathānyāyam kuryāt māsa catuṣṭayam sa yāti viṣṇu sālokyam viṣṇum smarati ca kṣaye pratimāsam dvijātibhyaḥ dadyāt dānam yathā icchayā cāturmāsye ca saṃpūrṇe puṇyam śravaṇa kīrtanam kathām vā vāsudevasya tad gītīḥ vā api kārayet evam etām gatim śreṣṭhām deva nāma anukīrtanāt kathitam pāraṇam yat te kārṣṇam māsa catuṣṭayam ādhipatyam tathā bhogān tena prāpnoti mānuṣān dvitīyena tathā bhogān aindrān prāpnoti mānavaḥ viṣṇoḥ lokam tṛtīyena pāraṇena tathā āpnuyāt vidhānam dvijaśārdūla kṛṣṇa tuṣṭi pradam nṛṇām sugatidvādaśīm etām śraddadhānaḥ tu yaḥ naraḥ upoṣya ca tathā nārī prāpnoti trividhām gatim eṣā dhanyā pāpa harā tithiḥ nityam upāsitā ārādhanāya śiṣṭā eṣā devadevasya cakriṇaḥ pāṣaṇḍa patitān ca eva tathā eva antyāvasāyinaḥ nāstikān bhinnavṛttīn ca pāpinaḥ ca api an ālapan nārāyaṇe gata manāḥ puruṣaḥ niyata indriyaḥ rātrim ca lakṣmīm saṃcintya samyak arghyena pūjayet niṣpāditam bhavet ekam pāraṇam dālbhya bhaktitaḥ dvitīyam ca api vakṣyāmi pāraṇam dvijasattama āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe māsi prāpte bhādrapade tathā tathā eva āśvayuje abhyarcya śrīdharam ca śriyā saha dvitīyam etat ākhyātam tṛtīyam pāraṇam śṛṇu kārttika ādiṣu māseṣu tathā eva abhyarcya keśavam bhūtyā samanvitam dadyāt śaśāṅkāya arhanam niśi bhuñjīta ca tathā proktam tṛtīyam iti pāraṇam pratipūjāsu dadyāt ca brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca dakṣiṇām pratimāsam ca vakṣyāmi prāśanam kāya śodhanam caturaḥ prathamān māsān pañcagavyam udāhṛtam kuśa udakam tathā eva anyat uktam māsa catuṣṭayam sūrya aṃśu taptam tadvat ca jalam māsa catuṣṭayam gīta vādya ādikam pāṭhyam tathā kṛṣṇasya vā kathān ca devasya pāraṇe pāraṇe gate evam saṃpūjya vidhivat sa patnīkam janārdanam na āpnoti iṣta viyoga ādīn pumān yoṣit atha api vā sa śrīkam śrīdharam bhaktyā tṛtīye bhūti keśavau tāvanti janmāni asukham na āpnoti iṣṭa viyoga jam na arim prāpnoti na vyādhim narakam ca na paśyati pratimāsam tu nāmāni kṛṣṇasya etāni dvādaśa kṛta upavāsaḥ su snātaḥ pūjayitvā janārdanam tatas viprāya vai dadyāt uda kumbham sa dakṣiṇam yat vai māsa gatam nāma tad prītiḥ ca api saṃvadet saṃvatsara ante api athavā pratimāsam dvijān budhaḥ keśavam mārgaśīrṣe tu pauṣe nārāyaṇam tathā mādhavam māgha māse tu govindam phālgune tathā jyeṣṭhe trivikramam devam āṣāḍhe vāmanam tathā śrāvaṇe śrīdharam ca eva hṛṣīkeśa iti ca aparam nāma bhādrapade māsi gīyate puṇya kāṅkṣibhiḥ padmanābham ca āśvayuje dāmodaram atas param iha vai svastha tām prāpya maraṇe smaraṇam tatas tatas mānuṣyam āsādya nirātaṅkaḥ gata jvaraḥ upavāsa vratāni iha keśava ārādhanam prati mama ācakṣva mahābhāga param kautūhalam hi me kāmān yān yān naraḥ bhaktaḥ manasā icchati keśavāt vrata upavāsanāt prītaḥ tān tān viṣṇuḥ prayacchati mārgaśīrṣam tu yaḥ māsam eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet kurvan vai viṣṇu śuśrūṣām sa deśe jāyate śubhe pauṣa māsam tathā dālbhyaḥ eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet śuśrūṣaṇa paraḥ śaureḥ na rogī sa ca jāyate māgha māsam dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet viṣṇu śuśrūṣaṇa paraḥ sa kule jāyate satām kṣapayet eka bhaktena śuśrūṣuḥ yaḥ ca phālgunam saubhāgyam sva janānām sa sarveṣām eti sa unnatim suvarṇa maṇi muktā āḍhyam sa gārhasthyam avāpnuyāt naraḥ vā yadi vā nārī jñātīnām śreṣṭha tām vrajet kṛṣṇa arpita manāḥ jyeṣṭham eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet aiśvaryam atulam śreṣṭham pumān strī vā abhijāyate āṣāḍham eka bhaktena yaḥ nayet viṣṇu tanmanāḥ kṣapayet eka bhaktena śrāvaṇam viṣṇu tatparaḥ dhana dhānya hiraṇya āḍhye kule sa jñāti vardhanaḥ ekāhāraḥ bhādrapadam yaḥ ca kṛṣṇa parāyaṇaḥ nayan ca āśvayujam viṣṇum pūjayet eka bhojanaḥ dhanavān vāhana āḍhyaḥ ca bahu putraḥ ca jāyate kārttike ca ekadā bhuṅkte yaḥ ca viṣṇu paraḥ naraḥ śūraḥ ca kṛta vidyaḥ ca bahu putraḥ ca jāyate ahiṃsaḥ sarva bhūteṣu vāsudeva parāyaṇaḥ namaḥ astu vāsudevāya iti ahar ca aṣṭaśatam japet tad kṣayāt iha ca āgatya māhātmyam pratipadyate brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ strī śūdraḥ vā yathā uditān upavāsān imān kurvan phalāni etāni avāpnuyāt jayam śaraṇam abhyetya na janaiḥ śocyate janaḥ prāpnoti śāśvatam sthānam tatas pūjyataraḥ hi saḥ parāparam sukṛtavatām parām gatim svayaṃbhuvam prabhavan nidhānam avyayam śṛṇu dālbhya param kāmyam vratam saṃtati dam nṛṇām yam upoṣya na vicchedaḥ pitṛ piṇḍasya jāyate kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām caitra māse snātaḥ niyata mānasaḥ kṛṣṇam abhyarcya pūjām ca devakyāḥ kurute tu yaḥ nirāhāraḥ japan nāma kṛṣṇasya jagataḥ pateḥ upaviṣṭaḥ japa snāna kṣuta praskhalita ādiṣu pūjāyām ca api kṛṣṇasya sapta vārān prakīrtayet pāṣaṇḍinaḥ vikarma sthān na ālapet ca eva nāstikān prabhāte tu punar snātaḥ dattvā viprāya dakṣiṇām bhuñjīta kṛta pūjaḥ tu kṛṣṇasya eva jagatpateḥ vaiśākha jyeṣṭhayoḥ ca eva pāraṇam hi tri māsikam āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe ca eva māse bhādrapade tathā upoṣite dvitīyam vai pāraṇam pūrvavat tu tat tathā eva āśvayujam ca ādim kṛtvā māsa trayam budhaḥ upoṣya snāpayet devam haviṣā pāraṇe gate caturthe pāraṇe pūrṇe ghṛtena snāpayet harim evam kṛta upavāsasya puruṣasya tathā striyaḥ kṛṣṇa aṣṭamīm imām yaḥ tu naraḥ yoṣit atha api vā upoṣyati iha sa āhlādam nṛ loke prāpya nirvṛttim iti etat kathitam dālbhya mayā kṛṣṇa aṣṭaṃīvratam prāvṛṣ kāle tu niyamān śṛṇu kāmyān imān mama prāvṛṣ kāle yadā śete vāsudevaḥ payonidhau bhogi bhoge nijām māyām yoganidrām ca mānayan viśiṣṭāḥ na pravartante tadā yajña ādikāḥ kriyāḥ devānām sā bhavet rātriḥ dakṣiṇāyana saṃjñitā adhas śāyī brahmacārī keśava arpita mānasaḥ namaḥ namaḥ astu kṛṣṇāya keśavāya namaḥ namaḥ iti prātar tathā sāyam japet deva kriyā paraḥ śamayati ati duṣpāram duritam janma saṃcitam madhu māṃsam ca yaḥ māsān caturaḥ tān nirasyati arogī dhana dhānya āḍhyaḥ kula saṃtatimān naraḥ samasta mandirāṇām ca yaḥ supte madhusūdane śastam tu anantaram puṃsām tatas ca eva eka bhojanam taila abhaṅgam ca yaḥ māsān caturaḥ tān nirasyati saḥ api aṅga lāvaṇya guṇam ārogyam ca naraḥ labhet yaḥ tu etāni samastāni māsān etān naraḥ caret sa viṣṇu lokam āsādya viṣṇoḥ anucaraḥ bhavet brāhmaṇān bhojayet dadyāt tatas tebhyaḥ ca dakṣiṇām devadevasya suptasya dvādaśīm śṛṇu ca aparām māsi proṣṭhapade śukle dvādaśyām jalaśāyinam praṇamya anantam abhyarcya puṣpa dhūpa ādibhiḥ śuciḥ pāṣaṇḍa ādibhiḥ ālāpam akurvat niyata ātmavān viprāya dakṣiṇām dattvā naktam bhuṅkte tu yaḥ naraḥ tiṣṭhan vrajan svapan ca eva kṣuta praskhalita ādiṣu ananta nāma smaraṇam kurvan uccāraṇam tathā anena eva vidhānena māsān dvādaśa vai kramāt gīta vādyena hṛdyena prīṇayan vyuṣṭim aśnute anantam gīta vādyena yatas phalam udāhṛtam evam yaḥ puruṣaḥ kuryāt ananta ārādhanam śuciḥ evam dālbhya hṛṣīkeśaḥ naraiḥ bhaktyā yathāvidhi phalam dadāti asulabham salilena api pūjitaḥ rāga ādi apetam hṛdayam vāc duṣṭā na anṛta ādinā hiṃsā ādi rahitaḥ kāyaḥ keśava ārādhana trayam rāga ādi dūṣite citte na āspadī madhusūdanaḥ na yogyā keśava stutyai vāc duṣṭā ca anṛta ādinā tamasaḥ nāśanāya alam na indoḥ lekhā ghana āvṛtā hiṃsā ādi dūṣitaḥ kāyaḥ keśava ārādhane kutas sarva svam api kṛṣṇāya yaḥ dadyāt kuṭila āśayaḥ rāga ādi apetam hṛdayam kuru tvam keśava arpitam ārādhana vidhiḥ sarvaḥ bhūyas pṛcchāmi tat vada mātāmaham kāṇvam udāra vīryam mahā ṛṣim abhyarcya kula prasūtim yathāvat ācaṣṭa tatas mahātmā sa rāja varyāya yathā kuleṣu saṃpūjya viṣṇum vidhinā upavāsī sraj gandha dhūpa anna vara upahāraiḥ gṛhṇīta māsam prati māsa pūjām dāna ādi yuktam vratam abdam ekam ghṛtam tilān vrīhi yavam hiraṇyam yava annam ambhaḥ karaka anna pānam chattram payaḥ annam guḍa phāṇita āḍhyam sraj candanam vastram anukrameṇa aśnīta yāni ātma viśuddhi hetoḥ saṃprāśanāni iha nibodha tāni go mūtram ambhaḥ ghṛtam āma śākam dūrvāḥ dadhi vrīhi yavān tilān ca sūrya aṃśu taptam jalam ambu dārbham kṣīram ca māsa kramaśas upayuñjyāt kuruṣva viṣṇum bhagavantam īśam ārādhya kāmān akhilān upaiti yadā ca śukla dvādaśyām nakṣatram śravaṇam bhavet tadā sā tu mahā puṇyā dvādaśī vijayā smṛtā tasyām snātaḥ sarva tīrthaiḥ snātaḥ bhavati mānavaḥ saṃpūjya varṣa pūjāyāḥ sakalam phalam aśnute yat kṣemam api vai tasyām sahasram śrāvaṇe tu tat anyasyām eva tithyām śubhāyām śrāvaṇam yadā rohiṇyāḥ ca yadā kṛṣṇa pakṣe aṣṭamyām dvijottama jayantī nāma sā proktā sarva pāpa harā tithiḥ sapta janma kṛtam pāpam su alpam vā yadi vā bahu homa japya ādi dānānām phalam ca śata saṃmitam upavāsaḥ ca tatra uktaḥ mahāpātaka nāśanaḥ ekadaśyām śukla pakṣe yadā ṛkṣam vai punarvasuḥ nāmnā sā atijayā ākhyātā tithīnām uttamā tithiḥ yaḥ dadāti tila prastham tṛṣkālam vatsaram naraḥ upavāsam ca tasyām yaḥ karoti etat samam smṛtam pratyakṣatām prayāti alpam tadā ananta phalam smṛtam sagareṇa kakutsthena duṃdhumāreṇa gādhinā tasyām ārādhitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ dattavān nikhilām bhuvam kapilām vipra mukhyāya dadāti anudinam hi yaḥ snāpyamānam ca paśyati ye ghṛtena uttarāyaṇe te yānti viṣṇu sālokyam sarva pāpa vivarjitāḥ maitreyī brāhmaṇī pūrvam yājñavalkyam apṛcchata praṇipatya mahābhāgam yogeśvaram akalmaṣam pāpa praśamanāya alam yat puṇyasya upavṛṃhakam kāni dānāni śastāni snānāni ca yata vrata praśastāḥ tithayaḥ kāḥ ca prāśanāni ca śaṃsa me sarva dānāni śastāni yāni uddiśya janārdanam kriyante śradhayā samyak upavāsa vratāḥ sadā manorathānām saṃprāpti kārakam pāpa nāśanam śrūyatām mama dharma jñe vratānām uttamam vratam yat kṛtvā na jaḍaḥ na andhaḥ badhiraḥ na ca duḥkhitaḥ na ca eva iṣṭa viyoga ārtim kaścid prāpnoti mānavaḥ viṣṇu vratam idam khyātam bhāṣitam viṣṇunā svayam ṣaṣ māsa pāraṇa prāyam gṛhṇīyāt paramam vratam pūrvam siddhārthakaiḥ snānam tatas kṛṣṇa tilaiḥ smṛtam vacayā ca tṛtīye ahni sarva oṣadhyā tatas param nāmnā kṛṣṇa acyuta ākhyena tathā anantena pūjayet śaśi candra śaśāṅka indu saṃjñāni brahma vādini naktam bhuñjīta matimān yāvat tiṣṭhati candramāḥ evam sarveṣu māseṣu jyeṣṭha anteṣu yaśasvini kartavyam vai vrata śreṣṭham dvitīya ādi catur dinam viprāya dakṣiṇām dadyāt pañcamyām ca sva śaktitaḥ evam samāpayet māsaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ prathama pāraṇam ca devasya prīṇanam bhaktitaḥ śubhe yathāśaktyā tu kartavyam vitta śāṭhyam vivarjayet āṣāḍha ādi dvitīyam tu ṣaṣ māsena tapodhane pāraṇam vai samākhyātam vratasya asya śubha pradam tathā anyaiḥ pṛthivīpālaiḥ upavāsa vidhānataḥ caritam muni mukhyaiḥ ca ṛcīka cyavana ādibhiḥ surambhayā sukaikeyyā śāṇḍilyā dhūmrapiṅgayā sudeṣṇayā athavā riṇyā matimatyā kṛta āśayā sāvitryā paurṇamāsyā ca vairiṇyā ca subhadrayā brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām iti strībhiḥ anuṣṭhitam prathame pāda pūjā syāt dvitīye nābhi pūjanam tṛtīye vakṣasaḥ pūjā caturthe śirasaḥ hareḥ etat cīrtvā samastebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ śraddhayā anvitaḥ vratam etat mahābhāge tam tu pūrayate nṛṇām māghe snātasya yat puṇyam prayāge pāpa nāśanam sakalam tat avāpnoti śrutvā viṣṇu vratam tu idam sākṣāt bhagavatā proktam paramam pāpa nāśanam śukla pakṣe tu pauṣasya saṃprāpti dvādaśīm śṛṇu pāṣaṇḍa ādibhiḥ ālāpam akurvān viṣṇu tatparaḥ pauṣa ādi pāraṇam māsaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ jyeṣṭha antakam smṛtam prathame puṇḍarīkākṣam nāma devasya gīyate dvitīye mādhava ākhyam tu viśvarūpam tu phālgune ṣaṣṭhe jaya iti devasya guhyam nāma prakīrtyate pūrveṣu ṣaṭsu māseṣu snāna prāśanayoḥ tilāḥ āṣāḍha ādiṣu māseṣu pañcagavyam udāhṛtam snāne ca prāśane ca eva praśastam pāpa nāśanam pratimāsam ca devasya kṛtvā pūjām yathāvidhi viprāya dakṣiṇām dadyāt śraddadhānaḥ sva śaktitaḥ pāraṇa ante ca devasya prīṇanam bhakti pūrvakam ekādaśyām uṣitvā evam dvādaśyām athavā dine etām uṣitvā dharma jñe prīṇanam deva tatparaḥ tatas lokeṣu vikhyātā saṃprāptidvādaśī iti vai kṛta abhilaṣitā hi eṣā prārabdhā dharma tatparaiḥ pūrayati akhilān kāmān saṃśrutā ca dine dine tasmin eva dine puṇye govindadvādaśīm śṛṇu yasyām samyak anuṣṭhānāt prāpnoti abhimatam phalam pauṣa māse site pakṣe dvādaśyām samupoṣitaḥ saṃyak saṃpūjya govindam nāmnā devam adhokṣajam puṣpa dhūpa upahāra ādyaiḥ upavāsaiḥ samāhitaḥ viprāya dakṣiṇām dadyāt yathāśakti tapodhane pāṣaṇḍa ādi vikarma sthaiḥ ālāpam ca vivarjayet go mūtram gomayam vā api dadhi kṣīram atha api vā go dehataḥ samutpannam saṃprāśnīta ātma śuddhaye tena eva nāmnā saṃstūya dattvā viprāya dakṣiṇām evam eva akhilān māsān upoṣya prayataḥ śuciḥ dadyāt go āhnikam bhaktyā pratimāsam sva śaktitaḥ dattvā para gave bhūyas śṛṇu yat phalam aśnute suvarṇa śṛṅgāḥ pañca gāḥ ṣaṣṭham ca vṛṣabham naraḥ govindadvādaśīm etām upoṣya divi tārakāḥ vidyotamānāḥ dṛśyante lokaiḥ adya api śobhane upavāsa vratānām tu vaikalyam yat mahā mune dāna karma kṛtam tasya vipākaḥ vada yādṛśaḥ yajñānām upavāsānām vratānām ca yata vrate vaikalyāt phala vaikalyam yādṛśam tat śṛṇuṣva me upavāsa ādinā rājyam saṃprāpyam te tathā vasu bhraṣṭa aiśvaryāḥ nirdhanāḥ ca bhavanti puruṣāḥ punar kāṇāḥ kuṇṭhāḥ ca bhūyas te bhavanti andhāḥ ca mānavāḥ upavāsāt naraḥ patnīm nārī prāpya tathā patim ye dravye sati a dātāraḥ tathā anyena āhitāgnayaḥ kule ca sati duḥśīlāḥ dauṣkulāḥ śīlinaḥ ca ye vastra anulepanaiḥ hīnāḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ca ati rūpiṇaḥ virūpa rūpāḥ ca tathā prasādhana guṇa anvitāḥ guṇinaḥ api hi doṣeṇa saṃyuktāḥ saṃbhavanti te akhaṇḍa dvādaśīm etām aśeṣeṣu eva karmasu vaikalya praśamāya alam śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ mama mārgaśīrṣe site pakṣe dvādaśyām niyataḥ śuciḥ pañcagavya jala snātaḥ pañcagavya kṛta aśanaḥ yava vrīhi bhṛtam pātram dadyāt viprāya bhaktitaḥ sapta janmāni yat kiṃcid mayā khaṇḍa vratam kṛtam tathā akhilāni akhaṇḍāni vratāni mama santu vai evam eva anumāsam vai cāturmāsya vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ prīṇanam ca hareḥ kuryāt pārite pāraṇe tatas caitra ādiṣu ca māseṣu caturṣu anyam tu pāraṇam tatra api saktu pātrāṇi dadyāt śraddhā samanvitaḥ śrāvaṇa ādiṣu māseṣu kārttika anteṣu pāraṇam yatnāt tu ghṛta pātrāṇi dadyāt viprāya bhaktitaḥ evam samyak yathānyāyam akhaṇḍadvādaśīm naraḥ karoti avikalam sarvam akhaṇḍa dvādaśīvratam akhaṇḍadvādaśī samyak upoṣyā phala kāṃkṣibhiḥ evam purā yājñavalkyaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ patnyā mahā muniḥ ācaṣṭa puṇya phala dam upavāsa vidhim param tathā tvam api viprarṣe keśava ārādhane rataḥ punar ca etat mahābhāga śrūyatām gadataḥ mama proktam nareṇa devānām tithimāhātmyam uttamam vijayā atijayā ca eva jayantī pāpanāśanī tathā uttarāyaṇam śastam sarvadā keśava arcane sakṛt eva arcite kṛṣṇe tat etāsu api labhyate vijayā atijayā ca eva jayantī pāpanāśanī yatra saṃpūjitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sarva pāpam vyapohati ekādaśyām site pakṣe puṣya ṛkṣam yatra sattama tithau bhavati sā proktā viṣṇunā pāpa nāśanī tasyām saṃpūjya govindam jagatām īśvara īśvaram sapta janma kṛtāt pāpāt mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ yaḥ ca upavāsam kurute tasyām snātaḥ dvijottama dānam yat dīyate kiṃcid samuddiśya janārdanam ekā ṛc deva puratas japtā śraddhāvatā tathā japtam ekam muni śreṣṭha dadāti atra na saṃśayaḥ yatas pāpam aśeṣam vai nāśayati atra keśavaḥ puṣya ṛkṣa ekādaśī brahman tena uktā pāpa nāśanī tathā anyat api dharma jña śrūyatām gadataḥ mama pada dvayam jagaddhātuḥ devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ pāda pīṭham tatra nyastam pada dvayam vāsudevena vipra indra bhūtānām hita kāmyayā vāmam asya padam brahman uttarāyaṇa saṃjñitam deva ādyaiḥ sakalaiḥ vandyam dakṣiṇam dakṣiṇāyanam karoti ārādhanam tasya toṣam āyāti keśavaḥ katham ārādhanam tasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ghṛta kṣīra ādinā devam snāpayet dharaṇīdharam cāru vastra upahāraiḥ ca puṣpa dhūpa anulepanaiḥ samabhyarcya tatas samyak brāhmaṇānām ca tarpaṇaiḥ pada dvaya vratam samyak gṛhṇīyāt viṣṇu tatparaḥ snātaḥ nārāyaṇam vakṣye bhuñjan nārāyaṇam tathā bhuṅktvā nārāyaṇam ca aham gacchan nārāyaṇam tatas nārāyaṇasya anudinam kariṣye nāma kīrtanam yāvat adya dināt prāptam kramaśas dakṣiṇāyanam tāvat nārāyaṇam vakṣye sarvam eva uttarāyaṇam yāvat jīva vadham kiṃcid jñānataḥ ajñānataḥ api vā kariṣye aham tathā ca eva kīrtayiṣyāmi tam prabhum yadā tadā anṛtam kiṃcid atha vakṣyāmi durvacaḥ ajñānāt athavā jñānāt kīrtayiṣyāmi tam prabhum ṣaṣ māsam eṣa me jāpaḥ nārāyaṇa mayaḥ paraḥ tam smaran maraṇe yāti yām gatim sā astu me gatiḥ tat mayā vāsudevāya svayam ātmā niveditaḥ yam ante saṃsmaran yāti sa me viṣṇuḥ parā gatiḥ yadā prātar tadā sāyam madhyāhne vā mriye hi aham ṣaṣ māsa abhyantare nyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ vrata mayaḥ mayā nārāyaṇa yathā na anyam tvattaḥ yāmi mṛte gatim evam uccārya ṣaṣ māsa pāraṇam pravaram vratam tāvat niṣpādayet yāvat saṃprāptam dakṣiṇāyanam tatas ca prīṇanam kuryāt yathāśaktyā jagadguroḥ bhojayet brāhmaṇān samyak dadyāt tebhyaḥ ca dakṣiṇām evam vratam idam dālbhya yaḥ pārayati mānavaḥ nārī vā sarva pāpebhyaḥ ṣaṣ māsāt vipra mucyate ṣaṣ māsa abhyantare ca asya maraṇam yadi jāyate bhagavān ujjagau viṣṇuḥ purā gārgyāya pṛcchate phālguna amala pakṣasya ekādaśyām upoṣitaḥ snātvā samyak tam abhyarcya dadyāt viprāya dakṣiṇām praṇipatya jagannātham iti vāṇīm udīrayet pātāla saṃsthā vasudhā yam prasādya manorathān yam abhyarcya aditiḥ prāptā sakalān ca manorathān putrān ca eva īpsitān devaḥ pradadātu manorathān manorathān avāpa agryān sa dadātu manorathān evam abhyarcya pūjām ca niṣpādya haraye tatas phālgunam caitra vaiśākhau jyeṣṭha māsam ca pārthiva caturbhiḥ pāraṇam māsaiḥ ebhiḥ niṣpāditam bhavet dahet ca guggulam prāśya go śṛṅga kṣālanam jalam tatas ca śrūyatām anyat āṣāḍha ādau tu yā kriyā jātī puṣpāṇi dhūpaḥ ca śastaḥ sarjarasaḥ nṛpa prāśya darbha udakam ca atra śāli annam ca nivedanam svayam tat eva ca aśnīyāt śeṣam pūrvavat ācaret kārttika ādiṣu māseṣu go mūtram kāya śodhanam su gandham ca icchayā dhūpam pūjā bhṛṅgārakeṇa ca kāsāram ca atra naivedyam aśnīyāt tat ca vai svayam pratimāsam ca viprāya dātavyā dakṣiṇā tathā prīṇanam ca icchayā viṣṇoḥ pāraṇe pāraṇe gate yathāśakti yathāprīti vitta śāṭhyam vivarjayet sadbhāvena eva govindaḥ pūjitaḥ prīyate yatas pāraṇa ante yathāśaktyā snāpitaḥ pūjitaḥ hariḥ prīṇitaḥ ca īpsitān kāmān dadāti avyāhatān nṛpa eṣā dhanyā pāpa harā dvādaśī phalam icchatām yathā abhilaṣitān kāmān dadāti manuja īśvara pūrayati akhilān bhaktyā yatas ca eṣā manorathān manorathadvādaśī iyam tatas lokeṣu viśrutā upoṣya etām tribhuvanam prāptam indreṇa vai purā adityā ca īpsitāḥ putrāḥ dhanam ca uśanasā nṛpa rājarṣibhiḥ tathā vipraiḥ strībhiḥ śūdraiḥ ca bhūpate yam yam kāmam abhidhyāyet vratam etat upoṣitaḥ tam tam āpnoti asaṃdigdham viṣṇoḥ ārādhana udyataḥ roga abhibhūtaḥ ca ārogyam kanyā prāpnoti sat patim sarvān kāmān avāpnoti mṛtaḥ svarge ca modate na aputraḥ na adhanaḥ na iṣṭa viyogī na ca nirguṇaḥ yaḥ eva vrata saṃcīrṇaḥ viṣṇu loke mahīyate svarga loke sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām manuja adhipa bhogān abhimatān bhuktvā svarga loke abhikāṅkṣitān iha puṇyavatām nR̥ṇām dhaninām sādhu śīlinām gṛheṣu jāyate rājan sarva vyādhi vivarjitaḥ aśoka pūrṇimām ca anyām śṛṇu śva vadataḥ mama yām upoṣya naraḥ śokam na āpnoti strī tathā api vā phālguna amala pakṣasya pūrṇimāsyām nareśvara mṛd jalena naraḥ snātvā dattvā śirasi vai mṛdam mṛtprāśanam tathā kṛtvā kṛtvā ca sthaṇḍilam mṛdā puṣpaiḥ patraiḥ tathā abhyarcya bhūdharam na anya mānasaḥ dharaṇīm ca tathā devīm aśokā iti abhidhīyate yathā viśokām dharaṇīm kṛtavān tvam janārdanaḥ tathā mām sarva pāpebhyaḥ mocaya aśeṣa dhāriṇi yathā samasta bhūtānām dhāraṇam tvayi avasthitam tathā viśokam kuru mām sakala icchā vibhūtibhiḥ dhyāta mātre yathā viṣṇau svāsthyam yātāsi medini tathā manaḥ svastha tām me kuru tvam bhūta dhāriṇi anena eva prakāreṇa catvāraḥ phālguna ādayaḥ upoṣyāḥ nṛpate māsāḥ prathamam tat tu pāraṇam āṣāḍha ādiṣu māseṣu tadvat snānam mṛd ambunā tat eva prāśanam pūjā tathā eva indoḥ tathā arhaṇam caturṣu anyeṣu ca eva uktam tathā vai kārttika ādiṣu pāraṇam tritayam ca eva cāturmāsikam ucyate prathamam dharaṇī nāma stutyai māsa catuṣṭayam dvitīye medinī vācyā tṛtīye ca vasuṃdharā pāraṇe pāraṇe vastra pūjayā pūjayet nṛpa dharaṇīm devadevam ca ghṛta snānena keśavam vastra abhāve tu sūtreṇa pūjayet dharaṇīm tathā ghṛta abhāve tathā kṣīram śastam vā salilam hareḥ pātāla mūla gatayā cīrṇam etat mahā vratam dharaṇyā keśava prītyai tatas prāptā samunnatiḥ devena ca uktā dharaṇī varāha vapuṣā tadā vratena anena kalyāṇi praṇataḥ yaḥ kariṣyati vratam etat upāśritya pāraṇam ca yathāvidhi tathā eva kurute pūjām bhaktyā mama śubhaḥ janaḥ viśokaḥ sarva kalyāṇa bhājanaḥ matimān janaḥ sarvatra pūjyaḥ satatam sarveṣām aparājitaḥ tathā tvam api kalyāṇi bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ evam etat mahā puṇyam sarva pāpa upaśānti dam viśoka ākhyam vratam dhanyam tat kuruṣva mahīpate strīṇām dharmam dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ upavāsam bhavan mama kaumārake gṛhasthāyāḥ vidhavāyāḥ ca sattama dharmam prabrūhi aśeṣeṇa bhagavan prīti kārakam upakārāya ca strīṇām triṣu lokeṣu anuttamam praśnam etat purā devī śailarāja sutā patim kumārikābhiḥ deveśa gṛhasthābhiḥ ca keśavaḥ sādhu sādhvi tvayā pṛṣṭam etat nārāyaṇa āśritam upavāsa ādi yat tattvam śrūyatām asya yaḥ vidhiḥ yogyam patim samāsādya nārī dharmam avāpnute duḥśīle api hi kāma ārte nārī prāpnoti bhartari an ārādhya jagannātham sarva loka īśvaram harim katham āpnoti vai nārī patim śīla guṇa anvitam kartavyam lakṣaṇam tasya śrūyatām varavarṇini yat cīrtvā sarva nārīṇām śreṣṭham āpnoti asaṃśayam anujñām prāpya pitṛtaḥ mātṛtaḥ ca kumārikā triṣu uttareṣu su ṛkṣeṣu pati kāmā kumārikā ati bālye ca yat kiṃcid tayā pāpam anuṣṭhitam tat eva prāpnuyāt bhadre nārāyaṇa parāyaṇā ṣaṣ māsam prīṇanam kāryam bhaktyā śaktyā ca vai hareḥ pāraṇa ante mahābhage tathā brāhmaṇa tarpaṇam gārhasthye avasthitā nārī bhaktyā saṃpūjayet patim saḥ eva devatā tasyāḥ pūjyaḥ pūjyataraḥ ca saḥ toṣam āyāti sarva ātmā paramātmā janārdanaḥ na eva tasyāḥ pṛthak yajñaḥ na śrāddham na api upoṣitam bhartṛ śuśrūṣaṇena eva prāpnoti strī yathā īpsitam tena eva sā api anujñātā tasya śuśrūṣaṇāt anu ghṛta kṣīra abhiṣekaiḥ ca brāhmaṇānām ca tarpaṇaiḥ gīta vādyaiḥ tathā hṛdyaiḥ upavāsaiḥ ca bhāmini evam ārādhya govindam anujñātāḥ yathāvidhi patinā sakalān kāmān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ patinā tu an anujñātā kiṃcid puṇyam karoti yā viphalam tat aśeṣam vai tasyāḥ śailavara ātmaje na anujñātā tu yā nārī patinā arcati keśavam yā tu bhartṛ parā nārī nārāyaṇam atandritā bhaktyā saṃpūjayet devam toṣam āyāti keśavaḥ yā tu bhartrā parityaktā tathā yā mṛta bhartṛkā pāṣaṇḍa anugataḥ vā api yasyāḥ bhartā maheśvara prāyas dadāti na anujñām viṣṇoḥ ārādhane tadā katham ārādhanam kāryam viṣṇoḥ tat vada śaṃkara yā tu bhartrā parityaktā sā saṃpūjya nijam patim na nindā karaṇī tasya śreyaḥ abhidhyāyinī tathā ārādhayet jagannātham sarva dhātāram acyutam kṛta upavāsā puṣpa ādi nivedya sakalam tatas svayam yathā abhilaṣitam prārthayet tam varam tatas evam bhartṛ parityaktā yoṣit ārādhanam hareḥ kurvāṇā sakalān kāmān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ tasya puṇyasya saṃpūrṇam ardham prāpnoti sā śubhe yat tu sā kurute puṇyam vinā doṣeṇa yā ujjhitā kurvīta ārādhanam nārī upavāsa ādinā hareḥ etat tava uktam yat pṛṣṭam tvayā aham girinandini vidhavānām atas dharmam śrūyatām viṣṇu tuṣṭi dam snātā pratidinam dadyāt sva bhartṛ salila añjalim kuryāt yā anudinam bhaktyā devānām api pūjanam pūrta dharma āśritam ca anyat kuryāt nityam atandritā nityakarma ṛte ca asyāḥ na iṣṭam karma vidhīyate viṣṇoḥ ārādhanam ca eva kuryāt nityam upoṣitā upavāsān ca vividhān kuryāt śāstra uditān śubhe loka antara stham bhartāram ātmānam ca varānane tārayati ubhayam nārī yā ittham dharma parāyaṇā putra aiśvarya sthitā nārī upavāsa ādinā harim śubhān lokān tathā bhartuḥ ātmanaḥ ca yathā īpsitān sakalam pūrayati astam pāpam nayati ca akhilam ātmanaḥ ca eva bhartuḥ ca nārī paramikām gatim dadāti ārādhya govindam sa putrā vidhavā ca yā keśava ārādhanam kāryam loka dvaya phala pradam ye narāḥ mṛta patnikāḥ taiḥ api etat aśeṣatas viṣṇoḥ ārādhanam kāryam tīrtha sthaiḥ athavā gṛhe brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ strī śūdraḥ ca varānane an ārādhya hṛṣīkeśam na āpnoti paramām gatim aiśvaryam saṃtatim śreṣṭhām ārogyam dravya saṃpadam dadāti bhagavān viṣṇuḥ gatim agryām su toṣitaḥ evam śailasutā proktā svayam devena śaṃbhunā ārādhanīyaḥ na a tuṣṭe viṣṇau saṃprāpyate gatiḥ na durgatim raurava ādīn narakān ca na gacchati yam ārādhya īśvaram vandyam kaḥ tam viṣṇum na pūjayet tasmāt amuṣmikān kleśān narake yāḥ ca yātanāḥ bhagavan yātanāḥ ghorāḥ śrūyante narakeṣu yāḥ śṛṇu dālbhya ati ghorāṇām yātanānām mayā uditam aṅgāra pūrṇa madhyaḥ asau jvālā mālā pariṣkṛtaḥ satya hāni anṛtī yāti tatra pāpa ratiḥ naraḥ rauravāt dviguṇaḥ ca eva mahārauvara saṃjñitaḥ tapta tāmra puṭa aṅgāra jvalat pāvaka saṃvṛtaḥ na āścaryam dvijaśārdūla varṣa lakṣa yutāni ca kālasūtreṇa chidyante cakra ārūḍhāḥ ca mānavāḥ kāla aṅguli sthena sadā āpādatalamastakāt tatra api vañcakāḥ yānti ye ca eva utkoca jīvinaḥ deva veda dvijātīnām ye nindām kurvate sadā saṃśṛṇvanti ca ye mūḍhāḥ ye ca matsariṇaḥ adhamāḥ karambha vālukā kumbha saṃjñam ca narakam śṛṇu hṛtam yaiḥ ca jalam te api tasmin yānti nara adhamāḥ go nipāneṣu vighnāni mūḍhāḥ ye ca api kurvate andhe tamasi duṣpāre śīta ārti parikampitāḥ bhrāmyante mānavāḥ gātraiḥ samastaiḥ sphuṭita asthibhiḥ go vadhaḥ strī vadhaḥ pāpaiḥ kṛtam yaiḥ ca gavānṛtam utpāṭyate tathā jihvā saṃdaṃśaiḥ bhṛśa dāruṇaiḥ ākriśakānām duṣṭānām sadā eva abaddha bhāṣiṇām para dāra para dravya hiṃsakāḥ puruṣa adhamāḥ āyasīm ca śilām taptām aśeṣa aṅgaiḥ tathā narāḥ paradāra ratāḥ evam samāliṅganti pāpinaḥ sarva aṅgaiḥ vikṛtaiḥ raktam udgirantaḥ atipīḍitāḥ yantreṣu anyeṣu pīḍyante jantu pīḍā karāḥ narāḥ vṛkaiḥ saṃbhakṣyate pṛṣṭham narāṇām pāpa kāriṇām janasya pṛṣṭha māṃsam yaiḥ bhakṣitam pāpa kāribhiḥ sadbhāva pravaṇāḥ yaiḥ tu bhagnāḥ viśrambhinaḥ janāḥ ayomukhaiḥ khagaiḥ bhagnāḥ khaṇḍakhaṇḍam tathā aparaiḥ vrajanti pāpa karmāṇaḥ śva śṛgālaiḥ tathā aparaiḥ sūṣāyām api dhāsyante jvalat agni caya āvṛtāḥ pāṣāṇa peṣyam piṣyante tathā anye pāpa karmiṇaḥ devatā atithi bhṛtyāṇām a dattvā bhuñjate tu ye mṛṣā gatāḥ trapuṣā sīsakena ca prayānti puruṣāḥ tailaiḥ kvāthyante anye punar punar varṇa dharma parityāge na aikyam ye puruṣāḥ gatāḥ te api pāpa samācārāḥ varṇa saṃkara kāriṇaḥ svarūpam nārakasya agneḥ śṛṇuṣva kathayāmi te śastra dhārāḥ tathā eva etāḥ mṛṇāla prastaram naraḥ himakhaṇḍa caya āchannaḥ nivātam manyate naraḥ vimuktaḥ nārakāt śītāt prakāśam tamasaḥ tamaḥ protāḥ gudeṣu bhinna aṅgāḥ ārtāḥ rāva virāviṇaḥ śūleṣu loheṣu apare triśūleṣu tathā apare yājya upādhyāya dāmpatya suhṛd mitra suta ādiṣu kṛtaḥ bhedaḥ durācāraiḥ yaiḥ alīka ukti bhāṣibhiḥ āyasāḥ kaṇṭakāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ narake kūṭa śālmalau teṣu protāḥ durātmānaḥ para dāra bhujaḥ narāḥ kṛmi kīṭa jalaukā ādi tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭra āsya vikṣatāḥ bhrāmyante ca andhatāmisre vṛthāmāṃsa āśinaḥ hi ye etān ca anyān ca narakān śataśas atha sahasraśas karma antaram janaḥ bhuṅkte pariṇāmān ca cetasaḥ yādṛś karma manuṣyāṇām tādṛś viṣaya rūpavat pariṇāmam manaḥ yāti śubha aśubha mayam dvija atīva bhīṣaṇān ittham śastra agni bhaya dān naraḥ aho ati kaṣṭa pāpānām vipākaḥ naraka sthitaiḥ puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ pākaḥ puṇyaḥ eva dvijottama tathā eva pākaḥ pāpānām puruṣaiḥ naraka sthitaiḥ bhujyate tāvat akhilam yāvat pāpam kṣayam gatam yadā tu pāpasya jayaḥ kṣīyate sukṛtam tadā śubhasya karmaṇaḥ vṛddhau kṣayam āyāti aśobhanam jayāya dvādaśī śastā nR̥ṇām su kṛta karmaṇām yām upoṣya dvijaśreṣṭha na yāti narakam naraḥ phālguna amala pakṣasya ekādaśyām upoṣitaḥ dvādaśyām tu dvijaśreṣṭha pūjayet madhusūdanam ekādaśyām samuddiṣṭam viṣṇoḥ nāma anukīrtanam pūjāyām vāsudevasya kurvīta su samāhitaḥ namaḥ nārāyaṇāya iti vācyam ca svapatā niśi krodhaḥ prapañcaḥ īrṣyā ca dambhaḥ lobhaḥ ca varjitaḥ asāra tām ca loke asmin saṃsāre bhāvayet matim tathā eva kuryāt dvādaśyām nāmnām uccāraṇam dvija kāmam krodham ca lobham ca dambham īrṣyām ca varjayet māna droha ādi doṣān ca sarvān dhana mada udbhūtān bhāvayet viṣṇu bhaktān ca saṃsāra asāra tām tathā evam bhāvita cittena prāṇinām hitam icchatā yava pātrāṇi pūrvam tu dadyāt māsa catuṣṭayam āṣāḍha ādi dvitīyam tu pāraṇam yat mahāmate tatra api ghṛta pātrāṇi dadyāt śraddhā samanvitaḥ kārttika ādiṣu māseṣu māgha anteṣu tathā tilān viprāya dadyāt pātrashtān pratimāsam upoṣitaḥ nāma trayam aśeṣeṣu māsi māsi dina dvayam tathā eva uccārayet dadyāt dvādaśyām ca yava ādikam praṇamya ca hṛṣīkeśam kṛta pūjaḥ prasādayet nārāyaṇa tvām praṇataḥ asmi acintya jayaḥ astu me śāśvata puṇya rāśeḥ nārāyaṇā om bhūtim upaitu puṇyam prayātu ca aśeṣam agham vināśam viṣṇo puṇya udbhavaḥ me astu vāsudeva astu me śubham nārāyaṇa astu dharmaḥ me jahi pāpam aśeṣatas puṇyam vivṛddhim āyātu yātu pāpam tu saṃkṣayam ākāśa ādiṣu śabda ādau śrotra ādau mahat ādiṣu prayātu sukṛtasya astu mama anudivasam jayaḥ pāpasya hāniḥ puṇyam ca vṛddhim abhyeti anuttamām bhuñjīta kṛtakṛtyaḥ tu pāraṇe pāraṇe gate pāraṇa ante ca devasya prīṇanam śaktitaḥ dvija kurvīta akhila pāṣaṇḍaiḥ ālāpam ca vivarjayet dvādaśī narakam mṛtyo yām upoṣya na paśyati na agnayaḥ na ca śastrāṇi na ca loha mūkhāḥ khagāḥ nāma uccāraṇa mātreṇa viṣṇoḥ kṣīṇaḥ agha saṃcayaḥ na yāti narakam martyaḥ saṃkṣīṇa aśeṣa pātakaḥ tasmāt pāṣaṇḍi saṃsargam akurvan dvādaśīm imām upoṣya puṇya upacayī na yāti narakam naraḥ pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ a saṃsparśam a saṃbhāṣaṇam eva ca viṣṇoḥ ārādhana paraiḥ naraiḥ kāryam upoṣitaiḥ kim brūhi lakṣaṇam teṣām yādṛśān varjayet vratī kathaṃcid yadi saṃlāpa darśana sparśana ādikam upoṣitānām pāṣaṇḍaiḥ narāṇām vipra jāyate kim tatra vada kartavyam yena akhaṇḍam vratam bhavet śruti smṛti uditam dharmam varṇa āśrama vibhāga jam vikarma abhiratāḥ mūḍhāḥ yukti prāgalbhya durmadāḥ pāṣaṇḍinaḥ te duḥśīlāḥ naraka arhāḥ nara adhamāḥ tān tu pāṣaṇḍinaḥ pāpān vikarma sthān ca mānavān vaiḍālavratikān ca eva nityam eva tu na ālapet saṃbhāṣya etān śuciṣadam cintayet acyutam budhaḥ idam ca udāharet samyak kṛtvā tad pravaṇam manaḥ śārīram antaḥkaraṇa upaghātam vācaḥ ca viṣṇuḥ bhagavān aśeṣam śamam nayatu astu mama iha śarma pāpāt anante hṛdi saṃniviṣṭe antar śuddhim bahis śuddhim śuddhaḥ antar mama yaḥ acyutaḥ bāhya upaghātāt anaghaḥ boddhā ca bhagavān ajaḥ śuddhim nayatu ananta ātmā viṣṇuḥ cetasi saṃsthitaḥ etat saṃbhāṣya japtavyam pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ upoṣitaiḥ namaḥ śuciṣadā iti uktvā sūryam paśyeta vīkṣitaiḥ śrūyate ca purā martyāḥ sva icchayā svarga gāminaḥ yajña adhyayana dāneṣu vartamānaiḥ ca mānavaiḥ daiteyāḥ ca parābhāvam atuṣṭau asurāḥ yayuḥ tatas ca ṣaṇḍaḥ markaḥ ca daitya indrāṇām purohitau cakratuḥ karma devānām vināśāya ati bhīṣaṇam tatra utpannaḥ ati kṛṣṇa aṅgaḥ tamaḥ prāyaḥ ati dāruṇaḥ dambha ādhāraḥ śāṭhya sāraḥ nidrā prakṛtiḥ ulvaṇaḥ mahāmohaḥ iti khyātaḥ kṛtya rūpaḥ vibhīṣaṇaḥ veda deva dvijātīnām eka aṃśena sa nindanam vikarmaṇi apareṇa api saṃyojayati mānavān jñāna buddhyā tathā ajñānam gṛhṇāti ajñāna mohitaḥ evam sa tu mahā mohaḥ ṣaṇḍamarka upapāditaḥ tad mohitānām acirāt vivekaḥ yāti saṃkṣayam kṣīṇa jñānāḥ vikarmāṇi kurvanti aharahar dvija dharma buddhyā tatas pāpam kurvanti ajñāna durmadāḥ jñāna avalepaḥ tatra eva tatas teṣām prajāyate suhṛdbhiḥ vāryamāṇāḥ te paṇḍitaiḥ ca dayālubhiḥ prayacchanti uttaram ṃūḍhāḥ kūṭa yukti samanvitam pāṣaṇḍinaḥ durācārāḥ para anna guṇa vādinaḥ a saṃskṛta anna bhoktāraḥ vrātyāḥ saṃskāra varjitāḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ pāpa saṃkalpāḥ dāmbhikāḥ śaṭha buddhayaḥ varṇa saṃkara kartāraḥ māyā vyāja upajīvinaḥ niḥśaucāḥ vakra matayaḥ na anyat asti iti vādinaḥ evaṃvidhāḥ te sat mārgāt veda proktāt bahis sthitāḥ kriyā kalāpam nindantaḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma saṃjñitam ātmānam ca parān ca eva kurvanti naraka sthitān teṣām darśana saṃbhāṣa sparśanāni naraiḥ sadā parityājyāni dṛṣṭe ca proktaḥ saṃbhāṣaṇe ca yaḥ saṃsparśe ca budhaḥ snātvā śuciḥ śuciṣadam smaret bhavati atas sadā eva eṣām ālāpa sparśanam tyajet puṇya kāmaḥ mahābhāgaḥ kim punar yat upoṣitaḥ pāṣaṇḍinām aśeṣāṇām aprītiḥ veda karmaṇi te hi adhogāminaḥ proktāḥ āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ abhīṣṭāt anyatas vā api padāt yena na vicyutim prāpnoti puruṣaḥ brahman nārī vā apuṇya saṃkṣayāt satyam etat mahābhāga duḥkham prāptasya saṃkṣayaḥ tat etat śrūyatām dālbhya yathā na iṣṭāt paricyutiḥ sarga ādeḥ jāyate samyak upavāsavatām satām dvādaśa ṛkṣāṇi viprarṣe pratimāsam tu yāni vai tad nāmāni acyutam teṣu samyak saṃpūjayet budhaḥ āditas kṛttikām kṛtvā kārttike muni puṅgava naivedyam kṛsaram pūrvam annam māsa catuṣṭayam nivedayet kārttika ādi saṃyāvam ca tatas param āṣāḍha ādau ca devāya pāyasam vai nivedayet naivedyam svayam aśnīyāt naktam saṃpūjite acyute praṇamya prārthayet vidvān śuciḥ snātaḥ yathāvidhi aiśvarya vitta ādi sadā akṣayam me akṣayā ca me saṃtatiḥ acyutā astu tathā acyutam me kuru vāñchitam yat mayā padam pāpa hara aprameya yathāvat muni śārdūla cyutim na āpnoti mānavaḥ atrā api śrūyate siddhā kācid svarge mahā vratā nārī tapodhanā bhūtvā prakhyātā śāmbharāyaṇī samasta saṃdeha harā sadā svargaukasām hi sā pūrva indrā paratas pūrve ye babhūvuḥ sura īśvarāḥ teṣām caritam icchāmi śrotum āṅgirasām vara prāha dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭhaḥ parama ṛṣiḥ bṛhaspatiḥ na aham cirantanān vedmi devarāja sura īśvarān ātmanaḥ sama kālīnam mām avaihi sureśvara praṣṭavyaḥ atra mahābhāga kṛta ādi vasatiḥ divi bṛhaspatiḥ ciram dhyātvā punar āha śacīpatim tapasvinīm mahābhāgām smṛtvā asau śāmbharāyaṇīm na devāḥ na ca gandharvāḥ na ca anye cira saṃsthitāḥ cirantanānām cariteṣu abhijñā tridaśeśvara ekā eva cira kāla jñā dharma jñā śakra kevalam jānāti akhila deva indra caritam śāmbharāyaṇī yayau yatra mahābhāgā tāpasī śāmbharāyaṇī sā tau dṛṣṭvā samāyātau devarāja bṛhaspatī yat vām kāryam mahābhāgau sakalam tat iha ucyatām āvām abhyāgatau praṣṭum tvām atra ati vivekinīm yat ca kāryam mahābhāge tat pṛṣṭā kathaya iha nau tat ākhyāhi mahābhāge devendrasya kutūhalāt yadi śakyam mayā kartum tat kariṣye vimṛṣyatu tasmāt pūrvataraḥ yaḥ ca tasya api prathamāḥ ca ye teṣām pūrvatarāḥ ye ca vedmi tān akhilān aham teṣām ca caritam kṛtsnam jānāmi āṅgirasām vara manvantarāṇi anekāni sṛṣṭim ca tridivaukasām saptarṣīn su bahūn deva manūnām ca sutān nṛpa tat pṛccha tvam vadāmi eṣā pūrva indra caritam mune evam ukte tatas tābhyām pṛṣṭā sā śāmbharāyaṇī yathāvat ācaṣṭa tayoḥ pūrva indra caritam dvija tayoḥ jagāda caritam yathāvat śāmbharāyaṇī tatas kautūhala paraḥ devarāj tām tapasvinīm uvāca jānāsi katham tvam etat śāmbharāyaṇi sarve eva hi deva indrāḥ svarga sthāḥ ye manīṣiṇaḥ kim kṛtam vada dharma jñe tvayā yena iyam akṣayā caritam ca mayā teṣām śrutam dṛṣṭam tathā eva ca pratyuvāca mahābhāgā yathāvat śāmbharāyaṇī māsa ṛkṣeṣu acyutaḥ devaḥ pratimāsam sureśvara yathā ukta vratayā samyak sapta varṣāṇi pūjitaḥ tasya iyam karmaṇaḥ vyuṣṭiḥ acyuta ārādhanasya me svargam dravya maya aiśvaryam saṃtatim vā api yaḥ acyutām naraḥ vāñchati tena ittham toṣaṇīyaḥ acyutaḥ prabhuḥ svarga vāsa akṣaya tvam ca māsa ṛkṣa acyuta pūjanāt dharma artha kāma mokṣān tu vāñchatām vibudha adhipa viṣṇoḥ ārādhanāt na anyat paramam siddhi kāraṇam tasyāḥ tat vacanam śrutvā devarāja bṛhaspatī tām tathā iti ūcatuḥ sādhvīm ceratuḥ ca api tat vratam māsa ṛkṣa acyuta pūjāyām bhavethāḥ tad manāḥ sadā duṣṭa graha upaghātaiḥ ca sarvakālam upadrutāḥ ābhicāruka kṛtyābhiḥ sparṣa rogaiḥ ca dāruṇaiḥ sadā saṃpīḍyamānāḥ te tiṣṭhanti muni sattama te narāḥ muni śārdūla graha roga ādi bhāginaḥ viṣa graha jvarāṇām te manuṣyāḥ dālbhya bhājanāḥ ārogyam paramām ṛddhim manasā yat yat icchati kṛtyā sparśa bhayam vā api toṣite madhusūdane sarva duṣṭa śamaḥ tasya saumyāḥ tasya sadā grahāḥ devānām apradhṛṣyaḥ asau tuṣṭaḥ yasya janārdanaḥ yaḥ samaḥ sarva bhūteṣu yathā ātmani tathā apare upavāda ādinā tena toṣyate madhusūdanaḥ toṣite tatra jāyante narāḥ pūṛṇa manorathāḥ na teṣām śatravaḥ nā eva sparśa roga abhicārukāḥ graha roga ādikam vā api pāpa kāryam na jāyate avyāhatāni kṛṣṇasya cakra ādīni ātma yudhāni tam rakṣanti sakala āpadbhyaḥ yena viṣṇuḥ upāsitaḥ an ārādhita govindāḥ ye narāḥ duḥkha bhāginaḥ teṣām duḥkha abhibhūtānām kartavyam yat dayālubhiḥ paśyadbhiḥ sarva bhūta stham vāsudevam mahā mune sama dṛṣṭibhiḥ īśa īśam tat mama brūhi aśeṣatas kuśa mūla sthitaḥ brahmā kuśa madhye janārdanaḥ kuśa agre śaṃkaram vidyāt trayaḥ devāḥ vyavasthitāḥ gṛhītvā ca sa mūla agrān kuśān śuddhān upaspṛśet mārjayet sarva gātrāṇi kuśa agraiḥ dālbhya śānti kṛt śarīre yasya tiṣṭhanti kuśa stha jala bindavaḥ naśyanti tasya pāpāni garuḍena eva pannagāḥ viṣṇu bhaktāḥ viśeṣeṇa roga graha viṣa ārtānām kuryāt śāntim imām śubhām nārasiṃham samabhyarcya śucau deśe kuśa āsane vārāham nārasiṃham ca vāmanam viṣṇum eva ca dhyātvā samāhitaḥ bhūtvā dikṣu nāmāni vinyāset pūrve nārāyaṇaḥ pātu vārija akṣaḥ tu dakṣiṇe īśānyām avatāt viṣṇuḥ āgneyyām ca janārdanaḥ nairṛtyām padmanābhaḥ ca vāyavyām ca eva mādhavaḥ etābhyaḥ daśa digbhyaḥ tu sarvatas pātu keśavaḥ aṅguṣṭha agre tu govindam tarjanyān tu mahīdharam madhyamāyām hṛṣīkeśam anāmikyām tri vikramam kaṇiṣṭhāyām nyaset viṣṇum kara madhye tu mādhavam evam nyāsam purā kṛtvā paścāt aṅgeṣu vinyaset śikhāyām keśavam nyasya mūrdhni nārāyaṇam nyaset trivikramam kapāla stham vāmanam karṇa mūlayoḥ uttara uṣṭhe hṛṣīkeśam padmanābham tathā adhare jihvāyām vāsudevam ca tālvake garuḍadhvajam vāma bhuje mahābhāgam rāghavam hṛdi vinyaset kare tu dakṣiṇe vipra tatas saṃkarṣaṇam nyaset pṛṣṭhe kṣitidharam vidyāt acyutam skandhayoḥ api mādhavam bāhu kukṣau tu dakṣiṇe yoga śāyinam svayaṃbhuvam meḍhra madhye ūrubhyām tu gadā dharam gulpayoḥ narasiṃham ca pāda pṛṣṭhe amita ojasam śrīdharam ca aṅgulīṣu syāt padma akṣam sarva sandhiṣu romakūpe guḍākeśam kṛṣṇam rakta asthi majjāsu evam nyāsa vidhim kṛtvā sākṣāt nārāyaṇaḥ bhavet tanuḥ viṣṇu mayī tasya yāvat kiṃcid na bhāṣate evam nyāsam tatas kṛtvā yat kāryam śṛṇu tat dvija vanamālām tu vinyasya sarva deva abhipūjitām gadām vakṣaḥ sthale ca eva cakram ca eva tu pṛṣṭhatas śrīvatsa aṅgam śiraḥ nyasya pañcāṅga kavacam nyaset om apāmārjanakaḥ nyāsaḥ sarva vyādhi vināśanaḥ viṣṇuḥ ūrdhvam adhas rakṣet vaikuṇṭhaḥ vidiśaḥ diśaḥ pātu mām sarvatas rāmaḥ dhanvī cakrī ca keśavaḥ homa ārambheṣu sarveṣu trisaṃdhyāsu ca nityaśas āyuḥ ārogyam aiśvaryam jñānam vittam phalam bhavet atha dhyānam pravakṣyāmi sarva pāpa praṇāśanam vārāha rūpiṇam devam saṃsmarati aparājitam bṛhat tanum bṛhat gātram bṛhat daṃṣṭra su śobhanam samasta veda vedāṅgam yukta aṅgam bhūṣaṇaiḥ yutam uddhṛtya bhūmim pātālāt hastābhyām upagṛhṇatām āliṅgya bhūmim śirasi mūrdhni jighrantam āsthitam pīta ambara dharam devam śukla mālya anulepanam trayastriṃśa koṭi devaiḥ stūyamānam mudāniśam ittham dhyātvā mahātmānam japet nityam mahātmanaḥ suvarṇa maṇḍapa antastham padmam dhyāyet sa kesaram sa karṇika dalaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ pariśobhitam taḍit sama śaṭā śobhi kaṇṭha nāla upaśobhitam śrīvatsa aṅkita vakṣaḥstham tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭram trilocanam javākusuma saṃkāśam rakta hasta tala anvitam kaṭi sūtreṇa haimena nūpureṇa virājitam vanamālā ādi śobhā āḍhyam muktā hāra upaśobhitam aneka sūrya saṃkāśam mukuṭa āṭopa mastakam śaṅkha cakra gṛhītābhyām udbāhubhyām virājitam prātar sūrya sama prakhya kuṇḍalābhyām virājitam ati rakta oṣṭha vadanam vyātta āsyam ati bhīṣaṇam vāma aṅka stham śiva bhakta śānti dām su nitambinīm arhaṇīyām sujāta ūrum su nāsām śubha lakṣaṇām subhrūm sukeśīm suśroṇīm suśubhām su dvija ānanām su pratiṣṭhām su vadanām catur hastām vicintayet dukūle ca eva cāru aṅgīm hāriṇīm sarva kāma dām tapta kañcana saṃkāśām sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitām gṛhīta padma yugalam udbāhubhyām tathā anyayoḥ gṛhīta mātulaṅga ākhyam jāmbu nada karān tathā evam devīm nṛsiṃhasya vāma aṅka upari saṃsmaret su lalita dadhi khaṇḍam pāṇinā dakṣiṇena kalaśam amṛta pūrṇam savya haste dadhānam tat ati sakala duḥkham vāmanam bhāvayet yaḥ bhīma akṣa sphurat aṭṭahāsa vilasāt daṃṣṭra agra dīpta ānanaḥ dorbhiḥ cakra dharau gadā abja mukulau trāsān ca pāśa aṅkuśau manaḥ bhūtāni indriyāṇi guṇāḥ sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ trailokyasya īśvaram sarvam ahaṃkāre pratiṣṭhitāḥ om namaḥ parama arthāya puruṣāya mahātmane arūpa bahu rūpāya vyāpine paramātmane niṣkalmaṣāya śuddhāya sarva pāpa harāya ca varāha narasiṃhāya vāmanāya mahātmane trivikramāya rāmāya vaikuṇṭhāya narāya ca nārāyaṇāya devāya anantāya mahātmane garuḍadhvajāya kṛṣṇāya pīta ambara dharāya ca yogi īśvarāya siddhāya guhyāya paramātmane janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya upendra śrīdharāya ca bhakta priyāya vidhaye viṣvaksenāya śārṅgine cakra hastāya śūlāya tarjanya patrāya dhīmate ādityāya upendrāya bhūtānām jīvanāya ca viṣūvṛt śravase tasmai kṣīra ambu nichiśāyine adhokṣajāya bhadrāya śrīdharāya ādimūrtaye viśveśa dvāra mūrtiḥ ca mṛtyuḥ āyohitaḥ asti saḥ nānā rāgān ca dakṣān ca vikaṭāya mahā bhītī nārāyaṇāya viśvāya viśveśāya ambarāya ca dāmodarāya devāya anantāya mahātmane hayagrīva īśa sarva īśa hṛṣīkeśa hara aśubham hara amukasya duritam duṣkṛtam durupoṣitam para apadhyāna sahitam prayuktam ca abhicāruka om namaḥ vāsudevāya namaḥ kṣṛṇāya śārṅgiṇe namaḥ puṣkaranetrāya keśavāya ādicakriṇe mahā āhava ripu skandha ghṛṣṭa cakrāya cakriṇe daṃṣṭra uddhṛta kṣiti dhṛte trayī mūrtimate namaḥ mahāyajña varāhāya śeṣa bhoga ūru śāyine kāśyapāya ati hrasvāya ṛk yajuḥ sāma bhūṣita tubhyam vāmana rūpāya sṛjate gām namaḥ namaḥ varāha aśeṣa duṣṭāni sarva pāpa harāṇi vai bhañja bhañja ninādena duṣṭāni asya ārti nāśana ṛk yajuḥ sāma garbhābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ vāmana rūpa dhṛk ekāhikam dvyāhikam ca tathā tri divasam jvaram doṣa uttham saṃnipāta uttham tathā eva āgantukam jvaram śamam naya āśu govinda chittvā chittvā tu vedanām netra duḥkham śiraḥ duḥkham duḥkham ca udara saṃbhavam anucchvāsam atiśvāsam paritāpam sa vepathum guda ghrāṇa aṃhri rogān ca kuṣṭha rogam tathā kṣayam kāmalā ādīn tathā rogān pramehān ca ati dāruṇān bhagaṃdara atisārān ca mukha rogam sa valgulim aśmarī mūtrakṛcchrān ca rogān anyān ca dāruṇān kapha udbhavāḥ ca ye kecid ye ca anye sāṃnipātikāḥ āgantavaḥ ca ye rogāḥ lūtā visphoṭaka ādayaḥ te sarve praśamam yāntu vāsudeva apamārjitāḥ vilayam yāntu te sarve viṣṇoḥ uccāraṇena ca kṣayam gacchantu ca aśeṣāḥ te cakra abhihatāḥ hareḥ naśyantu sakalāḥ rogāḥ satyam satyam vadāmi aham sthāvaram jaṅgamam vā api kṛtrimam vā api yat viṣam śamam nayatu tat sarvam kīrtitaḥ asya janārdanaḥ grahān preta grahān ca eva tathā vai ḍākinī grahān vetālān ca piśācān ca gandharvān yakṣa rākṣasān śakunīpūtanā ādyān ca tathā vaināyaka grahān mukhamaṇḍinikām krūrām revatīm vṛddharevatīm vṛddhika ākhyān grahān ca ugrān tathā mātṛgrahān api bālasya viṣṇoḥ caritam hantu bālagrahān imān vṛddhānām ye grahāḥ kecid ye ca bālagrahāḥ kvacid narasiṃhasya te dṛṣṭyā dagdhāḥ ye ca api yauvane saṭā karāla vadanaḥ nara siṃhaḥ mahā ravaḥ grahān aśeṣān niḥśeṣān karotu jagataḥ hitam narasiṃha mahā siṃha jvālā mālā ujjvala ānana grahān aśeṣān sarva īśa khāda khāda agni locana ye rogāḥ ye mahā utpātāḥ yat viṣam ye mahā grahāḥ yāni ca krūra bhūtāni grahapīḍāḥ ca dāruṇāḥ śastra kṣateṣu ye doṣāḥ jvālā gardabhaka ādayaḥ yāni ca āryāṇi bhūtāni prāṇi pīḍā karāṇi vai tāni sarvāṇi sarva ātman parama ātman janārdana kiṃcid rūpam samāsthāya vāsudeva vināśaya kṣiptvā sudarśanam cakram jvālā mālā vibhīṣaṇam jvalat pāvaka saṃkāśa sūrya koṭi sama prabha trailokya rakṣa kartṛ tvam tvam duṣṭa dānava dāraṇa chindhi vātam ca dhūtam ca chindhi ghoram mahā viṣam ruja dāgham ca śūlam ca nimiṣa jvāla gardabham sarva duṣṭāni rakṣāṃsi kṣapaya ati vibhīṣaṇa hām hām hūm hūm phaṭkāreṇa ṭhadvayena hata dviṣaḥ sudarśanasya mantreṇa grahāḥ yānti diśaḥ diśaḥ sarva duṣṭāni rakṣāṃsi kṣayam yānti vibhīṣayā prācyām pratīcyām ca diśi dakṣiṇa uttaratas tathā rakṣām karotu sarva ātmā narasiṃhaḥ sva garjitaiḥ bhūmi antarikṣe ca tathā pṛṣṭhatas pārśvatas agratas rakṣām karotu bhagavān bahu rūpī janārdanaḥ yathā viṣṇuḥ jagat sarvam sa deva asura mānavam yathā viṣṇau smṛte samyak saṃkṣayam yāti pātakam paramātmā yathā viṣṇuḥ vedānteṣu abhidhīyate yathā yajñeṣu araḥ viṣṇuḥ vedeṣu api tu gīyate yathā yajña īśvaraḥ viṣṇuḥ yajña ante api gīyate śāntiḥ astu śivam ca astu praśāmyatu asukham ca yat vāsudeva śarīra utthaiḥ kuśaiḥ nirmārjitam mayā apāmārjati govindaḥ naraḥ nārāyaṇaḥ tathā tava astu sarva duḥkhānām praśamaḥ vacanāt hareḥ idam śāstram paṭhet yaḥ tu sapta ahan niyataḥ śuciḥ śāntim samasta rogāḥ te grahāḥ sarve viṣāni ca bhūtāni ca prayāntu īśe saṃsmṛte madhusūdane apamārjanakam śastam viṣṇu nāma abhimantritam ete kuśāḥ viṣṇu śarīra saṃbhavāḥ janārdanaḥ aham svayam eva ca āgataḥ hatam mayā duṣṭam aśeṣam asya svasthaḥ bhavati eṣa vacaḥ yathā hareḥ śāntiḥ astu śivam ca astu duṣṭam asya praśāmyatu yat asya duritam kiṃcid tat kṣiptam lavaṇārṇave svāsthyam asya sadā evā astu hṛṣīkeśasya kīrtanāt etat roga ādi pīḍāsu jantūnām hitam icchatā anena sarva duṣṭāni praśamam yānti asaṃśayam sarva aparādha śamanam apāmārjanakam param vināśāya ca rogāṇām avamṛtyu kṣayāya ca vyāghra apasmāra kuṣṭha ādi piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ paṭhatām śṛṇvatām nityam viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati surūpa tā manuṣyāṇām strīṇām ca dvijasattama surūpāṇām su gātrāṇām su veṣāṇām tathā mune nyūnam tathā adhikam vā api kiṃcid aṅgam prajāyate kāṇāḥ kubjāḥ ca jāyante truṭita śravaṇāḥ tathā narāṇām yoṣitām ca eva samasta aṅg surūpa tā lāvaṇya gati vākyāni sati rūpe mahāmate prayānti cāru tām rūpam tena uktaḥ paramaḥ guṇaḥ viḍambanā kurūpāṇām strī puṃsām abhijāyate rūpa kāraṇa bhūtāya yateta matimān tatas karmaṇā tat mama ācakṣva karma yat cāru rūpa dam samyak pṛṣṭam tvayā hi idam upavāsa āśritam dvija kathayāmi yathā proktam vasiṣṭhena mahātmanā vasiṣṭham ṛṣim āsīnam saptarṣi pravaram patim tasyāḥ sa paripṛcchantyāḥ jagāda muni sattamaḥ śrūyatām mama yat pṛṣṭaḥ tvayā aham brahma vādini surūpa tā nṛṇām yena yoṣitām ca upajāyate rūpa ādikāḥ guṇāḥ kena prāpyante anyena karmaṇā tasmāt ārādhanīyaḥ vai viṣṇuḥ eva yaśasvini yaḥ tu vāñchati dharma jñe rūpam sarva aṅga śobhanam nakṣatrapuruṣaḥ tena saṃpūjyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ nakṣatra aṅgam yathā āhāraḥ samupoṣyati yaḥ harim surūpaiḥ akhila aṅgaiḥ ca rūpavān abhijāyate yoṣitā ca param rūpam icchantyā jagataḥ patiḥ saḥ eva ārādhanīyaḥ atra nakṣatra aṅgaḥ janārdanaḥ nakṣatra rūpī bhagavān pūjyate puruṣottamaḥ caitra māsam samārabhya viṣṇoḥ pāda ādi pūjanam yathā kurvīta rūpa arthī tat niśāmaya tattvataḥ nakṣatram ekam ekam vai snātaḥ samyak upoṣitaḥ nakṣatrapuruṣasya aṅgam pūjayet sādhvī cakriṇaḥ mūle pādau tathā jaṅghe rohiṇīṣu arcayet śubhe jānunī ca āśvinī yoge āṣāḍhe ca ūru saṃjñite phālgunī dvitaye guhyam kṛttikāsu tathā kaṭim pārśve bhadrapadā yugme dve kukṣī revatīṣu ca anurādhe uraḥ pṛṣṭham śraviṣṭhāsu abhipūjayet punarvasau aṅgulīn ca āśleṣāsu tathā nakhān jyeṣṭhāyām pūjayet grīvam śravaṇe śravaṇe tathā puṣye mukham tathā svātau daśanān abhipūjayet hanvau śatabhiṣā yoge maghā yoge ca nāsikām mṛga uttamāṅge nayane pūjayet bhaktitaḥ śubhe citrā yoge lalāṭam ca bharaṇyām ca tathā śiraḥ saṃpūjanīyāḥ vidvadbhiḥ ca ādrāsu ca śiroruhāḥ nakṣatra yogeṣu eteṣu pūjitaḥ jagataḥ patiḥ nakṣatrapuruṣa ākhyaḥ ayam yathāvat puruṣottamaḥ pāpa apahāram kurute samyak śraddhāvatām satām aṅga upāṅgāni ca eva asya pāpa ādīni yaśasvini surūpāni abhijāyante sapta janmāntarāṇi vai sarvāṇi ca eva bhadrāṇi śarīra ārogyam uttamam saṃtatim manasaḥ prītim rūpam ca atīva śobhanam vāc mādhūryam tathā kāntim yat ca anyat abhivāñchitam dadāti nakṣatra pumān pūjitaḥ ca janārdanaḥ upoṣya samyak eteṣu krameṇa ṛkṣeṣu śobhane saṃpūjanīyaḥ bhagavān nakṣatra aṅgaḥ janārdanaḥ gandha puṣpa ādi saṃyuktam pūjayitvā yadāvidhi jānubhyām dharaṇīm gatvā idam ca udāharet tatas api sarvam etam protam sūtre maṇi gaṇāḥ iva eka puruṣa mahā puruṣa ṛkṣa puruṣa namaḥ astu te nakṣatra jñāya viprāya dadyāt dānam ca śaktitaḥ pārite ca punar dadyāt strī pūṃsām cāru hāsini strī vā sādhvī sadā viṣṇoḥ ārādhana parāyaṇā sarva kāmān avāpnoti samārādhya janārdanam nR̥ṇām strīṇām ca viprarṣe na anyat śokasya kāraṇam aputraḥ sarva duḥkhānām hetu bhūtaḥ mataḥ mama śastam praśāntam balinam parām nirvṛtim āgatāḥ śāstra jñam dharma tattva jñam dīna anātha janāśrayam deva anukūla tā yuktam yuktam samyak guṇena ca yena īdṛś lakṣaṇaḥ putraḥ prāpyate bhuvi mānavaiḥ atrā api śrūyatām vṛttam yat pūrvam abhavat mune kṛtavīryaḥ mahīpālaḥ haihayānām abhūt purā tasya śīladhanā nāma babhūva varavarṇinī patnī sahasra pravarā mahiṣī śīla maṇḍanā sā tu aputrā mahābhāgā maitreyīm paryapṛcchata guṇavat putra lābhāya kṛta āsana parigrahām tayā ca pṛṣṭā vai samyak maitreyī brahma vādinī kathayām āsa paramam nāmnā anantavratam vratam tasyāḥ sā putra lābhāya rāja putrāḥ tapasvinī yaḥ ayam icchet naraḥ kāmam nārī vā varavarṇini sa tam samārādhya vibhum samāpnoti janārdanam mārgaśīrṣe mṛgaśiraḥ bhīru yasmin dine bhavet tasmin saṃprāśya go mūtram snātaḥ niyata mānasaḥ anantaḥ sarva kāmānām anantam bhagavān phalam yathā abhilaṣita avāptim kurvan mā kṣayam etu ca iti uccārya abhipūjya enam yathāvat vidhinā naraḥ samāhita manāḥ bhūtvā praṇipāta puraḥsaram viprāya dakṣiṇām dadyāt anantaḥ prīyatām iti vāmām abhyarcayet kṛtvā go mūtraprāśanam budhaḥ anantaḥ sarva kāmānām iti ca uccārayet budhaḥ bhuñjīta ca tathā vipram vācayitvā yathāvidhi caturṣu eteṣu go mūtra prāśanam nṛpa nandini brāhmaṇāya tathā dadyāt tilān kanakam eva ca tathā eva prāśanam ca atra pañcagavyam udāhṛtam vipre vācanake dadyāt yāvat māsa catuṣṭayam vaiśākhe ca viśākhāsu bāhum saṃpūjya dakṣiṇam kaṭi pūjām ca jyeṣṭhāsu jyeṣṭhamūle śubha vrate āṣāḍhāsu tathā āṣāḍhe kuryāt pāda arcanam śubhe pada dvayam ca śravaṇe śrāvaṇe subhru pūjayet ghṛtam viprāya dātavyam prāśanīyam tathā dadhi kārttika anteṣu māseṣu prāśanam dānam eva ca tadvat āśvayuje pūjyam hṛdayam ca aśvinīṣu vai kuryāt samāhita manāḥ snāna prāśana śaucavān ananta śirasaḥ pūjām kārttike kṛttikāsu ca ghṛtena anantam uddiśya pūrva māsa catuṣṭayam kurvīta homam caitra ādau śālinā kula nandini kṣīreṇa śrāvaṇa ādau tu homam māsa catuṣṭayam śastam tu sarva māseṣu haviṣya annam ca bhojanam evam dvādaśabhiḥ māsaiḥ pāraṇam tritayam śubhe putra arthibhiḥ vitta kāmaiḥ bhṛtya dārān abhīpsubhiḥ anantavrata saṃjñam vai sarva pāpa praṇāśanam iti śīla dhanā śrutvā maitreyī vacanam śubham viṣṇuḥ tutoṣa tuṣṭe ca viṣṇau sā suṣuve sutam tasya vai jāta mātrasya pravavau anilaḥ śivaḥ deva dundubhayaḥ neduḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca prajaguḥ divi gandharvāḥ nanṛtuḥ ca apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ kṛtavīrya suta tvāt ca kārtavīryaḥ babhūva saḥ tena api bhagavān viṣṇuḥ dattātreya sva rūpavān ārādhitaḥ ati mahatā tapasā dālbhya bhūbhṛtā purā anusmaraṇam jñānam bhītānām ca ārti nāśanam tam āha devadeveśaḥ puṇḍarīka nibha īkṣaṇaḥ yaḥ ca prabhāte rātrau ca tvām naraḥ kīrtayiṣyati anaṣṭa dravya tā ca eva tava nāma abhikīrtanaiḥ sa ca api varam āsādya prasannāt garuḍadhvajāt pālayām āsa bhūpālaḥ saptadvīpām vasuṃdharām tena iṣṭam vividhaiḥ yajñaiḥ samāpta vara dakṣiṇaiḥ jitvā ari vargam akhilam dharmataḥ pālitāḥ prajāḥ ananta vrata māhātmyāt āsādya tanayam ca tam yat cīrtvā rāja patnī sā kārtavīryam asūyata yaḥ ca etat śṛṇuyāt janma kārtavīryasya mānavaḥ strī vā duḥkham apatya uttham sapta janmāni na aśnute rūpa saṃpad samākhyātā strī puṃsām jāyate śubhā samupoṣya jagannātham nakṣatrapuruṣam harim vāsaḥ ati śobhanam cāru vastra ādi ābharaṇa ujjvalam gṛham sarva guṇa upetam aśeṣa upaskara anvitam karmaṇā yena viprarṣe toṣitaḥ madhusūdanaḥ yat mām pṛcchasi dālbhya tvam gṛha upaskara bhūṣaṇam narāṇām jāyate yena tat sarvam kathayāmi te nandā bhadrā jayā riktā pūrṇā ca dvijasattama tithayaḥ vai samākhyātāḥ pratipad krama saṃjñayā pañcamī daśamī ca eva tathā pañcadaśī tithiḥ pūrṇāḥ etāḥ samākhyātāḥ tithayaḥ muni sattama mṛdā dhātu vikāraiḥ vā varṇakaiḥ gomayena vā pravāta āvāta guṇavat varṣāsu ati manoramam anuliptam śubha ākāram su gṛham labhate mune pūrṇam dhānya hiraṇya ādyaiḥ maṇi muktāphala ujjvalam pratyāsanna jala ābhogam gṛham āpnoti śobhanam yat sarveṣām uttamottamam yena anulipte tiṣṭhanti viṣṇu āyatana bhū tale brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśaḥ śūdrāḥ sādhvyaḥ tathā striyaḥ tasya pūṇya phalam dālbhya śrūyatām yat prajāyate apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇam muktā hāra gaṇa ujjvalam śreṣṭham sarva vimānānām svarge dhiṣṇyam avāpnute tasmin vimāne sa naraḥ strī vā tiṣṭhati sattama gandharva apsarasām saṃbhaiḥ pūjyamānaḥ sa tiṣṭhati liptam ca yāvataḥ hastān viṣṇoḥ āyatanam dvija pūjyamānaḥ sura gaṇaiḥ śīta uṣṇa ādi vivarjitaḥ manojña gātraḥ vipra indraḥ tiṣṭhati asta agha saṃhatiḥ cyutaḥ tasmāt iha āgamya viśiṣṭe jāyate kule na tatra tāvat dāridryam na upasargāḥ na vā kaliḥ na ca api mṛta niṣkrāntiḥ yāvat jīvati asau dvija viṣṇuḥ samasta bhūtāni sasarja etāni yāni vai teṣām madhye jagaddhātuḥ atīva iṣṭā vasuṃdharā prayāti paramam toṣam vaiṣṇavīyam mahī yatas dharaṇī pitaram viṣṇum idam vākyam udīrayet tvam mahī jagatām nātha sarva nātha namaḥ astu te śuśrūṣitaḥ prasīda īśa bhuvaḥ lepana karmaṇā iti uccārya kṣitau kṣiptvā prathamam dhāranī tale puṣpāṇi vā dvijaśreṣṭha yaḥ karoti anulepanam na āpnoti sā ca vaidhavyam gṛha bhaṅgam kadācana kṛtvā upalepanam bhūyas praṇipatya janārdanam snātaḥ viṣṇum samabhyarcya idam vākyam udīrayet kṛtam tena samastam me nāśam abhyetu pātakam evam saṃpūjya bhuñjīyāt aparāhne dvijottama tad kṣayāt svarge loke tu jātaḥ gṛha varam yathā sarva ābharaṇa saṃpūrṇam sarva upaskara dhānyavat go mahiṣī ādi saṃbhogam gṛham āpnoti mānavaḥ sapta dvīpavatīm kṛtsnām yathā indraḥ tridivam tathā alpa upalepanāt yasya māndhātā sakalām mahīm dīpam prayacchati naraḥ viṣṇoḥ āyatane hi yaḥ sa dakṣiṇasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti asaṃśayam kārttike tu viśeṣeṇa kaumude māsi dīpakam dālbhya anyat api vakṣyāmi purāvṛttam idam śṛṇu vidarbha rāj citrarathaḥ babhūva astra viśāradaḥ tasya putra śatam rājñaḥ jajñe pañcadaśa uttaram ekā eva kanyā dālbhyā āsīt lalitā nāma nāmataḥ sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpūrṇā bhrātR̥ṇām pituḥ eva ca tasya tasya ati cāru aṅgī babhūva iṣṭā dvijottama tām dadau kāśi rājāya sa pitā cāruvarmane upayeme ca tām subhrūm cāruvarmā mahīpatiḥ śatāni anyāni bhāryāṇām trīṇi āsan cāruvarmaṇaḥ tāsām madhye agra mahiṣī lalitā tasya ca abhavat viṣṇoḥ āyatane tasyāḥ sahasram dvijasattama dīpānām vai prajajvāla divārātram atandritam tasyāḥ dyuti parābhūtāḥ tasyāḥ lāvaṇya nirjitāḥ kautūhala parāḥ sarvāḥ yat pṛcchāmaḥ tat ucyatām na aham matsariṇī bhadrā na ca rāga ādi dūṣitā bhavatyaḥ mama sarvāsām bhavatīnām aham tathā apṛthak bhartṛ sāmanyāḥ deva loka abhikāmukāḥ pūrvam yūyam aham ca eva bhavatīnām sadharmiṇī na tathā puṣpa dhūpeṣu na tathā dvija pūjane prayatnam tava paśyāmaḥ viṣṇoḥ āyatane śubhe yathā ahani tathā rātrau yathā rātrau tathā ahani vyājahāra sapatnīḥ tāḥ na kiṃcid api bhāminī punar punar ca sā tābhiḥ bahuṣaḥ dālbhya coditā dākṣiṇya sārā lalitā kathāyām āsa bhāminī kautukam bhavatīnām ced atīva alpe api vastuni tat eṣā kathayāmi etat yat vṛttam mama śobhanāḥ tena ca āyatanam viṣṇoḥ kāritam devikā taṭe ahani ahani śuśrūṣām puṣpa dhūpa upalepanaiḥ āsīt nirvāṇa bhūyiṣṭhaḥ deva arcā puratas niśi devatāyatane ca āsam tatra aham api mūṣikā pradīpa varti haraṇe kṛta buddhiḥ varānanāḥ gṛhītā ca mayā vartiḥ vṛṣadaṃśaḥ nanāda ca naṣṭā ca aham tadā tasya mārjārasya bhaya āturā varti prāntena naśyantyā sa dīpaḥ preritaḥ mayā jajvāla pūrvavat dīptyā tasmin āyatane punar mṛtā aham ca tatas jātā vaidarbhī rāja kanyakā jātismarā kāntimatī bhavatīnām samā guṇaiḥ eṣa prabhāvaḥ dīpasya kārttike māsi śobhanāḥ dattasya viṣṇu āyatane yasya iyam vyuṣṭiḥ uttamā asaṃkalpitam api asya preraṇam yat kṛtam mayā lobha abhibhūtā hartum tam pradīpam aham āgatā tatas jāti smṛtiḥ janma mānuṣyam śobhanam vapuḥ vaśyaḥ patiḥ pṛthivīśaḥ kim punar dīpa dāyinām etasmāt kāraṇāt dīpān aham etān aharniśam bhavatīnām idam satyam mayā uktam keśava ālaye mūṣika tvāt aham yena karmaṇā siddhim āgatā viṣṇu āyatana dattasya jagāda lalitā yathā dadāti kārttike yaḥ tu viṣṇvāyatana dīpakam jātismara tvam prajñām ca prākāśyam sarva vastuṣu avyāhata indriya tvam ca saṃprāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ śeṣa kāle ca cakṣuṣmān medhāvī dīpa daḥ naraḥ jāyate narakam vā api tamaḥ saṃjñam na paśyati ekādaśīm dvādaśīm vā pratipakṣam ca yaḥ naraḥ dīpam dadāti kṛṣṇāya tasya api śṛṇu yat phalam suvarṇa maṇi muktā āḍhyam manojñam ati śobhanam dīpa mālā ākulam divyam vimānam saḥ adhirohati tasmāt āyatane viṣṇoḥ dadyāt dīpam dvijottama tān ca dattān na hiṃseta na ca taila viyojitān kurvīta dīpa hartā tu mūkaḥ andhaḥ jāyate yatas jāyate narakam ca api tapaḥ saṃjñam sa paśyati vikrośamānān kṣudh kṣāmān jagāda yama kiṃkaraḥ yadā pramādibhiḥ pūrvam ātmā atyantam upekṣitaḥ idānīm yātanā bhogaḥ kim vilāpaḥ kariṣyati dehaḥ dināni su alpāni viṣayāḥ ca ati durdharāḥ etat kaḥ na vijānāti yena yūyam pramādinaḥ tatra api ati vimūḍha tvāt kim bhogān abhidhāvati bhavadbhiḥ āgatam duḥkham vilāpa pariṇāmikam paritāpāya tat jātam duḥkham karma vipāka jam su alpam āyuḥ manuṣyāṇām tad ante paratantra tā yat abhūt para dāreṣu prītaye aṅga kuca ādikam yātanā duḥkha rūpāya narake ca tat āgatam hā mātar ityādi rutam tat idānīm vilapyate mṛtānām sva kṛtam karma paścāttāpāya kevalam aneka varṣa koṭiṣu duḥkha dam karma jāyate hā mātar tāta tāta iti bhavadbhiḥ kim vilapyate putra dāra gṛha kṣetra hitāya satata udyatāḥ na vetti sūrya candra ādīn kālam ātmānam eva ca sākṣi bhūtān aśeṣasya śubhasya iha aśubhasya ca janmāni anyāni jāyante putra dāra ādi dehinām krandate mātaram tātam pīḍyamānaḥ api yat svayam evam ākṛṣṭa cittānām viṣaya āsvāda tarṣulaiḥ nR̥ṇām na jāyate buddhiḥ parama artha avalokinī tathā ca viṣaya āsaktim karoti aviratam manaḥ kaḥ atibhāraḥ hareḥ nāmni jihvāyāḥ parikīrtane yena iyam teṣu hasteṣu svātantrye sati dīpakaḥ mahā phalaḥ viṣṇu gṛhe na dattaḥ naraka apahaḥ na vaḥ vilapite kiṃcid idānīm dṛśyate phalam avaśyaṃpātinaḥ prāṇāḥ bhoktā jīvaḥ hi aharniśam idānīm kim vilāpena sahadhvam yat upāgatam kṛte api pāpake karmaṇi ajñānāt agha nāśanam nārakāḥ tad vacaḥ śrutvā tām ūcuḥ ati duḥkhitāḥ kṣudh kṣāma kaṇṭhāḥ tṛṣayā parisphuṭita tālukāḥ dyūta udyotāya govinda gṛhāt dīpaḥ purā hṛtaḥ tena asmin narake ghore kṣudh tṛṣṇā paripīḍitāḥ bhavantaḥ patitāḥ tīvra śīta vāta vidāritāḥ puṇyam pāpam ca kathitam keśavāyatane dvija viśeṣeṇa jagaddhātuḥ keśavasya niveśane ye andhāḥ mūkāḥ niḥśrutāḥ nirvivekāḥ hīnāḥ taiḥ taiḥ sādhanaiḥ vipra varya taiḥ taiḥ dīpāḥ sādhu loka pradattāḥ devāgārāt anyatas vipraṇītāḥ āhlādam cakṣuṣaḥ prītim karoti manasaḥ tathā keṣāṃcid darśanam brahman manuṣyāṇām aharniśam udvejanīyāḥ bhūtānām animittam tathā apare manuṣyāṇām aśeṣam vai tat mama ācakṣva sattama deva brāhmaṇa vedeṣu yajñeṣu ca nara adhamaiḥ yaiḥ jugupsā kṛtā dālbhya manasā api atimānibhiḥ teṣām saṃdarśanāt sarvaḥ na sukham vindate dvija sparśāt udvijate lokaḥ kaṭu teṣām ca darśanam saṃbhāṣaṇam ca nindā vai kṛtā veda dvijātike tasmāt na nindām veda ādau na jugupsām ca paṇḍitaḥ yajña ādike ca eva kṛtā dālbhya tat darśanam nṛṇām āhlādaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ prītiḥ manasaḥ nirvṛtiḥ parā saṃbhāṣaṇe tathā āhlādaḥ sarva lokasya jāyate stutāḥ praśastāḥ saṃprītyā pūjitāḥ bahu mānataḥ śreyaḥ param prayacchanti devāḥ vedāḥ makhāḥ dvijāḥ ete eva samākhyātāḥ stava ādi grahaṇe nindāyāḥ śravaṇe doṣaḥ eteṣām evam eva hi tasmāt stavyāḥ praśaṃsyāḥ ca devāḥ vedāḥ dvijātayaḥ yajñāḥ ca manasā api eṣām na nindām ācaret budhaḥ śṛṇu dālbhya mahā puṇyām dvādaśīm pāpa nāśanīm yām upoṣya param puṇyam prāpnute śraddhayā anvitaḥ māgha māse tu saṃprāpte āṣāḍhārkṣam bhavet yadi mūlam vā kṛṣṇa pakṣasya dvādaśyām niyataḥ tadā gṛhṇīyāt puṇya phala dam vidhānam tasya me śṛṇu kṛṣṇa nāmnā ca saṃstūya ekādaśyām mahāmate upoṣitaḥ dvitīye ahni punar saṃpūjya keśavam saṃstūya nāmnā ca tatas kṛṣṇa ākhyena punar punar dadyāt tilān tu viprāya kṛṣṇaḥ me prīyatām iti snāna prāśanayoḥ śastāḥ tathā kṛṣṇa tilāḥ mune na andhaḥ na badhiraḥ ca iha na kuṣṭhī na jugupsitaḥ bhavati etām uṣitvā tu tila ākhyām dvādaśīm naraḥ viṣṇoḥ prīṇanam atra uktam samāpte varṣa pāraṇe pūjām ca kuryāt viprāya bhūyas dadyāt tathā tilān anena dālbhya vidhinā tila dānāt asaṃśayam mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ nirāyāsena mānavaḥ udbhṛta pulakaḥ sarvān nirāyāsena mānavaḥ dāna vidhiḥ tathā śraddhā sarva pātaka śāntaye na arthaḥ prabhūtaḥ na āyāsaḥ śārīraḥ muni sattama viśeṣaḥ kṣetra bhedena kathyatām yadi vidyate viśeṣaḥ kathitaḥ nāmnām viśeṣa phala dāyakaḥ tathā kṣetra viśeṣeṇa bhedam nāma kṛtam vada śṛṇu dālbhya yathā ākhyātam arjunāya mahātmane praṇipāta prasannena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā kṛte bhāra avataraṇe nivṛtte bhārate raṇe āgamya śibiram viṣṇuḥ ratha sthaḥ prāha phālgunam iṣudhī gāṇḍivam ca eva samādāya tvarā anvitaḥ avatīrya rathāt vīra dūre tiṣṭṛ dhanaṃjaya avarokṣyāmi aham paścāt avatīrṇe tatas tvayi evam uktaḥ tathā cakre vākyam pārthaḥ gadā dhṛtaḥ avārohat tatas paścāt svayam eva janārdanaḥ jajvāla sa rathaḥ sadyas bhasmībhūtaḥ ca tad kṣaṇāt vahninā ca yathā kāṣṭham sadyas bhasma lavīkṛtam tat adbhutam mahat dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ papraccha keśavam hṛṣṭa romā dvijaśreṣṭha bhaya vismaya gadgadaḥ āścaryam puruṣa vyāghra kim etat madhusūdana vinā agninā rathaḥ ayam me dagdhaḥ tṛṇa cayaḥ yathā bhīṣma droṇa kṛpa ādīnām karṇa ādīnām ca phālguna mad adhiṣṭhita tvāt kaunteya na śīrṇaḥ ayam tadā abhavat kam bhavantam aham vidyām atimānuṣa ceṣṭitam pūrvam eva yathā ākhyātam raṇa ārambhe tava arjuna kālaḥ asmi loka nāśāya pravṛttaḥ aham yathā adhunā tat mayā sādhitam kāryam tridaśānām tathā bhuvaḥ bhāra avataraṇa arthāya mama janma mahī tale tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ udbhūta pulakaḥ tatas namaḥ astu te cakradhara ugra rūpa namaḥ astu te śārṅgadhara aruṇa akṣa vācaḥ samuccārayataḥ skhalanti keśāḥ hṛṣīkeśa samucchvasanti kālaḥ bhavān kāla karāla karmā yena etat evam kṣayam akṣaya ātman kṣatram samudbhūta ruṣā samastam nītam bhuvaḥ bhāra virecanāya na me dṛś eṣā tava rūpam etat draṣṭum samarthā kṣubhitaḥ asmi ca antar smarāmi rūpam tava viśva rūpam yat darśitam pūrvam abhūt mama eva yasmin mayā viśvam aśeṣam āsīt dṛṣṭam sa yakṣa uraga deva daityam sā me smṛtiḥ darśana bhāṣana ādi prakurvataḥ nātha gatā praṇāśam kartā bhavān kāraṇam api aśeṣam kāryam ca niṣkāraṇa kartṛ rūpa brahmā bhavān viśvasṛj ādi kāle viśvasya rūpaḥ asi tathā visṛṣṭau viṣṇuḥ sthitau pālana baddha kakṣaḥ rudraḥ bhavān saṃharaṇe prajānām yathā hi mūle viṭapī mahā drumaḥ pratiṣṭhita skandha vara ugra śākhaḥ muñcāmi yāvat parama āyudhāni vairiṣu ananta āhava durmadeṣu dṛṣṭvā hi tāvat sahasā patantaḥ nūnam tava eva acyuta sa prabhāvaḥ hatāḥ hatāḥ te bhavataḥ dṛśā eva mayā punar keśava śastra pūgaiḥ kā ah karṇa bhīṣma pramukhān vijetum yuṣmad prasādena vinā samarthaḥ triśūla pāṇiḥ mama yaḥ purastāt niṣūdayan vairi balam jagāma jñātam mayā sāṃpratam etat īśa tava prasādasya hi sā vibhūtiḥ nāśāya na abhūt patitaḥ api kāye tvad saṃnidhānasya hi saḥ anubhāvaḥ bālye bhavān yāni cakāra deva karmāṇi asahyāni sura asurāṇām taiḥ eva jānīma na yat param tvām doṣaḥ sa nirdoṣaḥ manuṣya tāyāḥ tāla ucchrita agram guru bhāra sāram āyāma vistāra vat adya jātaḥ pāda agra vikṣepa vibhinna bhāṇḍam cikṣepa kaḥ anyaḥ śakaṭam yathā tvam anyena kena acyuta pūtanāyāḥ prāṇaiḥ samam pītam asṛj vimiśram viṣa anala uṣṇa ambu nipāta bhīmam āsphoṭya kaḥ vā bhuvi manuṣaḥ anyaḥ nanarta pāda abja nipīḍitasya phaṇam samāruhya ca kāliyasya pralamba cāṇūra mukhān nihatya kaṃsa asuram yasya bibheti śakraḥ tam aṣṭa varṣaḥ nijaghāna kaḥ anyaḥ nirāyodhaḥ na atha manuṣya janmā bāṇa artham abhyudyatam ugra śūlam nirjitya saṃkhye tripurārim ekaḥ kaḥ pārijātam sura sundarīṇām sadā upabhogyam vijita indra sainyaḥ hatvā hayagrīvam udāra vīryam niśumbha śumbhau narakam ca kaḥ anyaḥ maitrī na yeṣām vinayāya tān tān sarvān bhavān saṃharate avyaya ātman hitāya teṣām kapila ādi rūpiṇā tvayā anuśastāḥ bahavaḥ anujīvāḥ yeṣām na maitrī hṛdi te na neyā viśva upakārī vadhaḥ eva teṣām ittham bhavān duṣṭa vadhena nūnam viśva upakārāya vibho pravṛttaḥ etāni ca anyāni ca duṣkarāṇi dṛṣṭāni karmāṇi tathā api satyam manyāmahe tvām jagataḥ prasūtim kim kurma māyā tava mohanīyam prasīda kṛṣṇa acyuta vāsudeva janārdana ananta nṛsiṃha viṣṇo manuṣya sāmānya dhiyā yadi īśa dṛṣṭaḥ mayā tat kṣamasva ādideva prasīda īśa hṛṣīkeśa akṣauhiṇyāḥ daśa aṣṭa ca tvayā grastāḥ bhuvaḥ bhūtyai hetu bhūtāḥ hi madvidhāḥ evam stutaḥ tatas prāha prītimān tam janārdanaḥ pariṣvajya mahā bāhum samāśvāsya ca phālgunam prvāca bhagavān devaḥ prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā yaḥ tvām vetti sa mām vetti yaḥ tvām anu sa mām anu abhedena ātmanā vedmi tvām aham pāṇḍu nandana mama aṃśa tvam mahā bāho jagataḥ pālana icchayā bhuvaḥ bhāra avatāra artham pṛthak pārtha mayā kṛtam deva daitya uragāḥ yakṣāḥ gandharvāḥ kiṃnara apsarāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca piśācāḥ ca paśu pakṣi sarīsṛpāḥ vṛkṣa gulma ādayaḥ śailāḥ sarva bhūtāni ca arjuna mama eva aṃśāni bhūtāni viddhi sarvāṇi ariṃdama kṣetreṣu yeṣu yeṣu tvam cintanīyaḥ mayā acyuta cetasaḥ praṇidhāna artham tat mama ākhyātum arhasi sarva gaḥ sarva bhūtaḥ aham na hi kiṃcid mayā vinā puṣkare puṇḍarīkākṣam gayāyām ca gadādharam lohadaṇḍe tathā viṣṇum stuvan tarati duṣkṛtam kṣvāmācye kumāram nepāle loka bhāvanam rāghavam citrakūṭe tu prabhāse daitya sūdanam manda udapāne vaikuṇṭham māhantre ca acyutam vibhum vārāham kardamāle tu kāśmīre cakrapāṇinam janārdanam ca kubjāmre mathurāyām ca keśavam śālagrāme mahā yogim harim govardhana acale piṇḍārake caturbāhum śaṅkhoddhāre ca śaṅkhinam vāmanam ca kurukṣetre yamunāyām trivikramam viśveśvaram tathā śoṇe kapilam pūrva sāgare vanamālam ca kiṣkindhāyām devam raivatake dvija kāśī jale mahā yogam devam ca amita tejasam vaiśākha yūpe ajitam virajāyām viprakṣayam śvetadvīpa patim ca api gaṅgāsāgara saṃgame bhūdharam devikānadyām prayāge ca eva mādhavam naranārāyaṇa ākhyam ca tathā badarikāśrame dvārakāyām tathā kṛṣṇam stuvan tarati durgatim rāmam nāma mahendra adrau hṛṣīkeśam tathā arbude aśvatīrthe hayagrīvam viśvarūpam himācale nṛsiṃham kṛtasauce ca vipāśāyām dvija priyam naimiṣe yajñapuruṣam jambūmārge tathā acyutam anantam saindhavāraṇye daṇḍake śāṅga dhāriṇam utpalāvartake śaurim narmadāyām śriyaḥ patim dāmodaram raivatake nandāyām jalaśāyinam sahya adrau devadeveśam vaikuṇṭham māgadhe vane hṛdaye ca api kaunteya paramātmānam ātmanaḥ vaṭe vaṭe vaiśravaṇam catvare catvare śivam vāsudevam ca sarvatra saṃsmaran jyotiṣām patim arcayan praṇaman tu tvam saṃsmaran ca dhanaṃjaya eteṣu etāni nāmāni naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate sthāneṣu eteṣu mad nāmnām eteṣām prīṇanam naraḥ dvijānām prīṇanam kṛtvā svarga loke abhijāyate nāmāni etāni kaunteya sthānāni etāni ca ātmavān jayam vai pañcapañcāśat trisandhyam mad parāyaṇaḥ trīṇi janmāni yat pāpam avasthā tritaye kṛtam tat kṣālayati asaṃdigdham jāyate ca satām kule dviṣkālam vā japan eva divārātrau ca yat kṛtam dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam jayam kuru kula udvaha graha anukūla tām ca eva karoti āśu na saṃśayaḥ upoṣitaḥ mad paramaḥ sthāneṣu eteṣu mānavaḥ kṛta āyatana vāsaḥ ca prāpnoti abhimatam phalam utkrāntiḥ api aśeṣeṣu sthāneṣu eteṣu śasyate anya sthānāt śataguṇam eteṣu anaśana ādikam yaḥ tu mad paramaḥ kālam karoti eteṣu
