mānavaḥ yat na tāpāya vai puṃsām bhavati āmuṣmikam kṛtam upavāsa prabhāvam ca kṛṣṇa ārādhana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ śrūyatām dālbhya yat pṛṣṭāḥ kautukāt bhavatā vayam āmuṣmikam na tāpāya yat ca tāpāya jāyate upoṣita prabhāvam ca kṛṣṇa ārādhana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ kathayāmi yathāvṛttam pūrvam eva mahāmate bhāryā jāmātṛ duhitṛ putra pautra snuṣā anvitaḥ prabhūta bhṛtya vargaḥ ca bahu vyāpāra kārakaḥ cakāra anudinam saḥ atha nyāya anyāyaiḥ dhana arjanam na juhoti udite kāle na dadāti atitṛṣṇayā nitya naimittikānām ca hānim cakre sva karmaṇām tṛṣṇā abhibhūtaḥ viprarṣe sva varga bharaṇa ādhṛtaḥ kālena gacchatā saḥ atha mṛtaḥ vindhya aṭavī taṭe yātanā deha bhṛt pretaḥ grīṣma kāle abhavat mune tam dadarśa mahābhāgaḥ divya jñāna samanvitaḥ bhāskarasya aṃśubhiḥ dīptaiḥ dahyantam anivāraṇaiḥ pratapta vālukā madhye tṛṣā ca atyanta pīḍitam kṣudh kṣāma kaṇṭham śuṣka āsyam stabdha udvṛtta vilocanam niṣkrānta jihvam aṅgeṣu visphoṭaiḥ sarvatas citam niśvāsa āyāsa khedena virala āsyam anādaram śrāntam makṣikayā ākīrṇam durdagdham ca ati dāruṇam tam tādṛśam atho dṛṣṭvā gārdabheyaḥ mahā muniḥ pipītaḥ prāha viprarṣiḥ kāruṇya stimitam vacaḥ jānan api tathā prāptam tad anuṣṭhāna jam phalam adhas sūrya aṃśubhiḥ taptaiḥ bahubhiḥ yāna pāṃsubhiḥ upari arka karaiḥ ugraiḥ tṛṣā ca ārtaḥ tathā kṣudhā yātanā sthaḥ uvāca idam kṛcchrāt ucchvāsya mastakam aśāśvate śāśvata dhīḥ tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ na ātmanaḥ aham hita ārambhī tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ idam kariṣye kṛtvā idam kariṣyāmi aparam tu idam iti icchā śata saraḥ aham tena dahyāmi durmatiḥ śīta uṣṇa varṣa abhibhavam lobhāt mayā aśubham pitṛ deva manuṣyāṇām a dattvā apoṣitāḥ hi ye putra bhṛtya kalatreṣu mama tu ādṛta mānasaḥ kṛtvā karmāṇi asādhūni dahyāmi ekaḥ atra durmatiḥ na hi naḥ pūjitāḥ gehāt nirgatāḥ dvijasattamāḥ yat me na pūjitāḥ devāḥ kuṭumbam poṣītam param ekākī tena dahyāmi ye puṣṭāḥ te anyatas gatāḥ nityanaimittikam karma kṛte yeṣām na kṛtam dārāḥ putrāḥ ca bhṛtyāḥ ca pāpa vyāptyā mayā edhitāḥ putra dāra ādi bhṛtya arthe mayā anyāya artha saṃcayāḥ kṛtāḥ tena atra dahyāmi bhuñjate api anyatas gatāḥ na antar duḥkham na vā bhānuḥ pāpam eva dvidhā sthitam mama yena aham āhlādam āpnuyām muni sattama alpa kālikam uddhāram tava paśyāmi asaṃśayam prakṣīṇa prāyam etat te sukṛtam ca asti te param su karma jaya dām bhadra dvādaśīm tvam upoṣitaḥ alpaiḥ ahobhiḥ saṃkṣīṇam nava pātre yathā jalam gatam pāpam ayam tasyāḥ prabhāvaḥ atyanta durlabhaḥ śamam pāpasya kurute jayam su kṛta karmaṇaḥ sat karma jaya dā hi eṣā tatas vai dvādaśī smṛtā tat tathā na atra saṃdehaḥ mamatā pāpa hetukī pāpam atra kṛtam pretya bhadra tāpāya jāyate āhlādāya tathā puṇyam iha puṇya kṛtām nṛṇām vīrabhadram samāśvāsya yayau ittham mahā muniḥ evam dālbhya pare loke yat atra a su kṛtam kṛtam tat tāpāya sukhāya uktam yat atra eva śubham kṛtam tasmāt nareṇa puṇyāya patitavyam na pātake upavāsāḥ ca kartavyāḥ sadā eva ātma hita eṣiṇā saṃsāra asāra tām jñātvā viṣayān ca ati tarṣulān kartavyam yat mahābhāga puruṣeṇa tat ucyatām saṃsāra asāra tām jñātvā viṣayān ca ati tarṣulān gṛddhiḥ teṣu eva saṃtyājyā tad tyāgaḥ guṇavān nṛṇām yeṣām abda sahasrāṇām sahasraiḥ api naḥ naraḥ yāvataḥ vāñchate bhogān ahani ahani mānavaḥ teṣām sahasra bhāge api dālbhya prāptim na vindati tṛptaye ye na saṃprāptāḥ prāpyante ye na vāñchitāḥ buddhimān indriya artheṣu teṣu asaṅgī sadā bhavet yeṣām tṛptiḥ na bhogena tyāgaḥ ca eva upakārakaḥ kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādīni naraiḥ tasmāt mumukṣubhiḥ niṣkāmaiḥ dālbhya kāryāṇi phalāya ca phala īpsubhiḥ dasrābhyām saha saṃvādam ailasya ca mahātmanaḥ ailaḥ purūravāḥ pūrvam babhūva manuja īśvaraḥ cakame yam mahābhāgam urvaśī sura sundarī saṃtyajya tridaśa āvāsam rūpa audārya guṇa anvitam nāsatya dasrau rūpeṇa devānām adhikau tatas urvaśī lobhanam tasya rūpam draṣṭum samutsukau pratiṣṭhānam puram tasya budha putrasya dhīmataḥ draṣṭum tava aśvinau prāptau rūpa saṃpad guṇam tat ehi atra mahābhāga iha asmān saṃpraveśaya āścarya bhūtam lokeṣu urvaśī lobhanam vapuḥ āvām samāgatau tasmāt tvām draṣṭum manuja uttama ācacakṣe ca tat rājñe nāsatya vacanam dvija tat śrutvā vacanam rājā dvāstham āha muhūrtakam vilambyatām mahābhāgau tau brūhi vacanāt mama vyāyāma taila saṃsarga malinaḥ na vibhūṣitaḥ prasādhanam ca kṛtvā aham niṣkramāmi tvarā anvitaḥ samācaṣṭa tatas dālbhya tau ca bhūyas tam ūcatuḥ paśyāvaḥ tava bhūyas api tvām drakṣyāvaḥ prasādhitam iti uktaḥ nirgataḥ tūrṇam bhavanāt avanīpatiḥ sa praṇāmam tayoḥ kṛtvā kiṃcid nata śirāḥ nṛpaḥ sapta dvīpavatī pṛthvī putra dāra balam dhanam iti udāhṛtam ākarṇya nṛpateḥ aśvinau api aṅga upāṅga ādikam sarvam śanakais tau apaśyatām śiraḥ lalāṭa bāhum sa nayana ādi vilokanam kṛtvā ca tam mahīpālam ūcatuḥ tau idam surau praviśya snāhi bhūpāla yathārthaiḥ ca vibhūṣaṇaiḥ vibhūṣitam tu bhūyas tvām drakṣyāvaḥ avām nareśvara snātaḥ anuliptaḥ sraj dhārī su vastraḥ su vibhūṣitaḥ nāsatya dasrayoḥ pārśvam iyāya vasudhādhipaḥ bhūyas api tau yathā pūrvam aṅga upāṅga vilokanam tau saha asau samālakṣya sa tadā vasudhādhipaḥ hāsasya kāraṇam deva bhiṣajau tau apṛcchata pṛcchantam na tatas dālbhya nṛpatim hāsya kāraṇam yat ūcatuḥ mahābhāgau tat śṛṇuṣva vadāmi te śṛṇu bhūpāla sakalam hāsa kāraṇam āvayoḥ yuṣmad darśana saṃbhūtam kṣaṇa apacaya hetukam a snātasya abhavat bhūpa yādṛśī te surūpa tā sāṃpratam tādṛśī na iyam bhūṣitasya api bhūṣaṇaiḥ snātaḥ sragdāma dhārī tvam su anuliptaḥ su bhūṣitaḥ tathā api a snātaḥ eva prāc śobhanaḥ abhūt na sāṃpratam kiṃtu tad kāraṇam yena vyāyāma malina ambaraḥ śobhanaḥ aham abhūt pūrvam idānīm na vibhūṣitaḥ divyena cakṣuṣā bhūpa kālasya asya ca tasya ca vayaḥ pariṇatim sūkṣmām paśyāvaḥ apacaya pradām yathā hi nāḍikā pūrṇā galati aviratam nṛpa pariṇataḥ tadvat śarīra grahaṇāt anu janmataḥ anantaram bālyam paugaṇḍa tvam tatas param yauvanam madhyadehi tvam vārddhakam ca jarā nṛṇām sthūla dṛṣṭyā tu paśyanti na tu te sūkṣma darśinaḥ nimeṣa śata bhāgasya sahasra aṃśaḥ kṣaṇaḥ nṛpa tasya api ayuta bhāga aṃśaḥ bhavati apacayaḥ nṛṇām sūkṣma ati sūkṣma apacayī bhavati eṣa pumān nṛpa pariṇāmam kramāt yāti tṛptim vāri piban iva pratikṣaṇa aṃśayā vṛddhiḥ bāla tvam hīyate tayā kāntiḥ yā nṛpa bālasya pogaṇḍasya hi sā kutas kānti ādi saṃpadaḥ hāniḥ paramā nṛpa vārddhake tatra api anukṣaṇam hāniḥ hāniḥ mṛtyutaḥ nṛpa evam pratikṣaṇa aṃśāṃśaḥ nR̥ṇām apacaya pradaḥ asmad dṛṣṭaḥ bhavān yāvat praviṣṭaḥ nija mandiram tāvat hānim anuprāptaḥ kimu yāma ardha saṃsthitaḥ yādṛśaḥ adya bhavān tādṛś tvam na rūpī nareśvara paraśvas śastanam na eva evam samasta bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca pratikṣaṇa aṃśa apacayam prāpnuvanti mahī tale tasmāt na kautukam kāryam bhavatā tu nareśvara rājā purūravāḥ bhūyas śrutvā vākyam idam tayoḥ cintayitvā vacaḥ prāha saṃvega utkampi mānasaḥ ajñāna timira andhānām madvidhānām bhavadvidhāḥ pradīpa bhūtāḥ saṃdehaḥ vidyate na atra kaścana sadā apacaya doṣeṇa duṣṭa kāyaiḥ sura uttamau yat kāryam puruṣaiḥ tat ca kathyatām hita kāmyayā āsanam śayanam yānam paridhānam gṛha ādikam mūḍhaḥ adhruvam dhruva matiḥ kim ātmānam na budhyate bālyāt paugaṇḍa tām gatvā yaḥ punar yauvanam gataḥ bhuvaḥ śailam samārūḍhaḥ samārūḍhaḥ tatas drumam ārohaṇam sa kim anyat ṛkṣa bhītaḥ kariṣyati bālyāt paugaṇḍa tām yātaḥ yauvanāt vṛddha tām gataḥ tasmāt etat manuṣyeṇa vicārya ātma hita eṣiṇā śreyasi āmuṣmike yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ aharniśam nṛpa śreyaḥ param manuṣyāṇām kapilaḥ prāha pārthivaḥ śreyaḥ param manuṣyāṇām prāha pañcaśikhaḥ muniḥ śreyaḥ param manuṣyāṇām aṅgāriṣṭhaḥ abravīt nṛpaḥ śreyaḥ param manuṣyāṇām janakaḥ hi āha mokṣa vid hānim sarva vidhitsānām ātmanaḥ sukha hetukīm śreyaḥ param manuṣyāṇām devalaḥ api āha tattva vid etat eva param śreyaḥ vijñānam hita kāminām kāma anusārī puruṣaḥ kāmān anu vinaśyati aśreyasam param ca etat yat bhūpāla ati kāmi tā evam vijñāta tattva arthaḥ sanakaḥ yoginām varaḥ narendra prāha viprāṇām parama artha paraṃparam amuṣmin madhyamam śreyaḥ prāhuḥ sapta rṣayaḥ nṛpa tat āhuḥ aparam śreyaḥ ṛcīka cyavana ādayaḥ dve karmaṇī nara śreṣṭha brahmaṇā samudāhṛte karma svarūpataḥ bhraṣṭam an ākāṅkṣya phalam kṛtam sāmānyam ca aparam śreyaḥ sarva varṇa āśrameṣu yat tat śṛṇuṣva mahīpāla vadataḥ mama tattvataḥ satyam vaktavyam nityam maitreṇa bhāvyam kāryam ca tyājyam nityam āyāsa kāri loke amuṣmin yat hitam ca tathā asmin tasmin ātmā yojanīyaḥ anu dhīraiḥ tīrtha snānaiḥ sa upavāsaiḥ ajasram pātre dānaiḥ homa jāpaiḥ ca nityam śuddhiḥ neyaḥ devatā abhyarcanaiḥ ca śuddhaḥ api ātmā saṅga doṣāt aśuddhaḥ śuddham vastram saṅga doṣāt a śuddham bhūyas śuddhim śodhyamānam paryāti etat jñātvā na pramādaḥ manuṣyaiḥ śuddhe hi ātmani ātma vidbhiḥ vidheyaḥ samyak saṃpūjitau yātau nāka pṛṣṭham athā aśvinau niṣkāmaḥ anudinam yajñaiḥ iyāja puruṣottamam bhoga āsaṅgi manaḥ dālbhya yadā āsīt tasya bhūpateḥ tatyāja artheṣu mamatām ahaṃkāram tathā ātmani samatām sarva bhūteṣu saṃprāpa pṛthivīpatiḥ pūpa ādau tasya syāt iti kā kathā evam dālbhya manuṣyeṇa sama tām anutiṣṭhatā tasmāt niḥsaṅga cittena śakyaḥ cintayitum hariḥ prīti dveṣa ādayaḥ tyaktvā mahā ṛṣe yasya cetasā kārya ārambheṣu sarveṣu duḥsvapneṣu ca sattama yena ārambhāḥ ca sidhhyanti duḥsvapnam ca upaśāmyati amaṅgalānām sarveṣām pratighātaḥ ca jāyate janārdanam bhūtapatim jagadgurum smaran manuṣyaḥ satatam mahā mune duṣṭāni aśeṣāṇi apahanti sādhayati aśeṣa kāryāṇi tathā yadi icchati śṛṇuṣva ca anyat vadataḥ mama akhilam vadāmi yat te dvija varya maṅgalam sarva artha siddhim pradadāti yaḥ sadā nihanti aśeṣāṇi ca pātakāni vyoma ambu vāyu agni mahī svarūpaiḥ vistāravān yaḥ aṇutaraḥ aṇu bhāgāt sa sthūla sūkṣmaḥ satata īśvara īśvaraḥ yasmāt parastāt puruṣāt anantāt an ādi madhyāt akhilam na kiṃcid hiraṇyagarbha acyuta rudra rūpī sṛjati aśeṣam paripāti hanti guṇa āśrayī yaḥ bhagavān sa sarvadā paraḥ surāṇām paramaḥ asurāṇām paraḥ munīnām paramaḥ yatīnām dhyātaḥ yatīnām apakalmaṣaiḥ yaḥ dadāti muktim parameśvara īśvaraḥ manobhiḥ ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ sa sarvadā yena uddhṛtā iyam dharaṇī rasātalāt aśeṣa sattva sthiti kāraṇāt idam bibharti viśvam jagataḥ sa mūlavān pādeṣu vedāḥ jaṭhare carācaram romasu aśeṣāḥ munayaḥ mukhe makhāḥ samasta yajña aṅga mayam vapuḥ vibhoḥ yasya aṅgam īśa īśvara saṃstutasya yajñeśvaraḥ yajñapumān sa sarvadā pātāla mūla īśvara bhogi saṃhatau vinyasya pādau pṛthivīm ca bibhrataḥ ekārṇavāt yasya mahīyasaḥ mahīm ādāya vegena samutpatiṣyataḥ hataḥ hiraṇyākṣa mahā asuraḥ purā purāṇa puṃsā parameṇa yena varāha rūpaḥ sa patiḥ prajāpateḥ daṃṣṭrā karālam sura bhīti nāśanam kṛtvā vapuḥ divya nṛsiṃha rūpiṇam daitya indra vakṣaḥsthala dāra dāruṇaiḥ karoruhaiḥ śatru rujā anukāribhiḥ danta anta dīpti dyuti nirmalāṇi cakāra sarvāṇi diśam mukhāni yad nāma saṃkīrtanataḥ mahā bhayāt vimokṣam āpnoti na saṃśayam naraḥ saṭā kalāpa bhramaṇa anila hatāḥ sphuṭanti yasya ambudharāḥ samantataḥ sa divya siṃhaḥ sphurita ākula īkṣaṇaḥ yat īkṣaṇa jyotiṣi raśmi maṇḍalam pralīnam eva na rarāja bhāsvataḥ kutas śaśāṅkasya sa siṃha rūpa dhṛk dravanti daityāḥ praṇamanti devatāḥ naśyanti rakṣāṃsi apayānti ca arayaḥ aśeṣa deva īśa nara īśvara īśvaraiḥ sadā stutam yat caritam mahā adbhutam ṛk kāritam yaḥ yajuṣā ati śāntimat sāma dhvani dhvasta samasta pātakam yad pāda vinyāsa pavitra tām mahī yayau viyat ṛk yajuṣām udīraṇāt sa vāmanaḥ divya śarīradhṛk sadā yasmin prayāte sura bhūbhṛtaḥ adhvaram nanāma khedāt avaniḥ sa sāgarā samasta deva iṣṭi mayam mahā dyutiḥ dadhāra yaḥ rūpam atīndriyam prabhuḥ saṅghaiḥ surāṇām divi bhū tale sthitaiḥ tathā manuṣyaiḥ gagane sa sarvadā krāntvā dharitrīm gaganam tathā divam marutpateḥ yaḥ pradadau triviṣṭapam surān ca yajñasya bhujaḥ sa sarvadā rasātalāt yena purā samāhṛtāḥ samasta vedāḥ vara vāji rūpiṇā niḥkṣatriyām yaḥ ca cakāra medinīm anekaśas bāhu vanam tathā achinat jaghāna ca anyān rajanīcarān asau cikṣepa bālaḥ śakaṭam babhañja yaḥ yamala arjunau kaṃsam arim jaghāna mamarda cāṇūra mukham sa sarvadā prātar sahasrāṃśu marīci nirmalam kareṇa bibhrat bhagavān sudarśanam kaumodakīm ca api gadām anuttamām hima indu kunda sphaṭika abhra komalam mukha anila āpūritam īśvara īśvaraḥ sarveṣu kāleṣu samasta deśeṣu aśeṣa kāryeṣu tathā īśvara īśvaraḥ sarvaiḥ sva rūpaiḥ bhagavān anādimān sidhyanti kāryāṇi tathā asya sarvāṇi arthān avāpnoti tathā yatheṣṭam prārambhaḥ drutam upayāti siddhim īśaḥ pāpāni kṣapayati ca asya vāsudevaḥ vaidehaḥ parama padam prasādya viṣṇum saṃprāptaḥ sakala phala pradaḥ hi viṣṇuḥ sarva ārambheṣu dālbhya etat duḥsvapneṣu ca paṇḍitaḥ śamam prayānti duṣṭāni graha pīḍāḥ ca dāruṇāḥ karoti akhila rūpaiḥ ca rakṣām akṣata śakti dhṛk kurvīta kim pumān sthānam kaḥ pumān brahmaṇaḥ balam sva karmaṇā dhanam labdhvā nitya naimittikāḥ kriyāḥ kurvīta śuddhim āsthāya sva icchayā ca tathā paraḥ tyaktvā rāga ādikān doṣān samaḥ sarvatra vai bhavet sarvatra maitrīm kurvīta dadyāt iṣṭāni ca arthinām kuryāt dīneṣu karuṇām duḥśīlān parivarjayet muditām dharma śīleṣu bhāvanām muni sattama niḥśeṣa artha mala apetām ekatra vā jagannāthe bhāvanām puruṣottame śuddhām kurvīta paṇḍitaḥ śarīra bāhya tām śaśvat hiṃsām kurvīta na kvacid nindā avamānam anyeṣām yat ca anyat upaghātakam śarīra vāc manaḥ śuddhim kurvīta ca sat ātmanaḥ bhūtānām upakāraḥ ca tapobhiḥ ca ātma karṣaṇam eṣa dharmaḥ samāsena dālbhya ākhyātaḥ mayā tava adharmaḥ ca ayam eva uktaḥ viparītaḥ manīṣibhiḥ ete yatra guṇāḥ pūrvam kathitāḥ jñāna saṃyutāḥ brahmaṇaḥ sa āśrayaḥ śuddhaḥ upacārāt tat eva saḥ nāmnām bahu tvam lokānām upakāra karam śṛṇu sādhakam puruṣa vyāghra saumya krūreṣu vastuṣu vāsudeva acyuta ananta satya ājya puruṣottamaiḥ dhana kṛt dharma kṛt dharmī dharma ātmā viśva kṛt śuciḥ śuciṣad viṣṇuḥ abja akṣaḥ puṣkara akṣaḥ hi adhokṣayaḥ śuciśravāḥ śipiviṣṭaḥ yajñeśaḥ yajñabhāvanaḥ nāmnām iti evam ādīnām samuccāraṇataḥ naraḥ dharmam mahāntam āpnoti pāpa bandha kṣayam tathā tathā artha prāptaye brahman deva nāmāni me śṛṇu yeṣām samuccāraṇataḥ vittam āpnoti bhaktimān śriyaḥ patiḥ śrī paramaḥ śrīmān śrīvatsalāñcchanaḥ ānandaḥ mādhavaḥ ca eva kāma saṃsiddhaye nṛpa rāmaḥ paraśurāmaḥ ca nṛsiṃhaḥ viṣṇuḥ eva ca vikramaḥ ca evam ādīni japyāni ari jigīṣubhiḥ keśavam puṇḍarīkākṣam puṣkarākṣam tathā japet netra bādhāsu sarvāsu hṛṣīkeśam bhayeṣu ca acyutam ca amṛtam ca eva japet auṣadha karmaṇi cakriṇam gadinam ca eva śārṅginam khaḍginam tathā kṣema arthe prasavan rājan dikṣu prācya ādiṣu smaret ajitam ca adhikam ca eva sarvam sarvaśvaram tathā saṃsmaret puruṣaḥ bhaktyā vyavahāreṣu sarvadā nārāyaṇam sarvakālam kṣuta praskhalita ādiṣu graha nakṣatra pīḍāsu devabādhā aṭavīṣu ca asyu vairi nirodheṣu vyāghra siṃha ādi saṃkaṭe tarati akhila durgāṇi tāpa ārtaḥ jalaśāyinam jvara duṣṭa śiraḥ roga viṣa vīryam praśāmyati snāne deva arcane home praṇipāte pradakṣiṇe kurvīta tad manāḥ bhūtvā ananta acyuta kīrtanam nārāyaṇam śārṅgadharam śrīdharam puruṣottamam vāmanam khaḍginam ca eva duḥsvapneṣu ca saṃsmaret smaret vāyu agnī gṛha dāhāya pravṛddhau upalakṣya ca manuṣyaḥ muni śārdūla sadā aśvaśirasam smaret śrīśam sarva ābhyudayike karmaṇi saṃprakīrtayet ariṣṭa anteṣu aśeṣeṣu viśokam ca sadā japet marut pratāpa agni jala bandhana ādiṣu mṛtyuṣu sarva artha siddhim āpnoti nāmnām eka artha tā yatas sarvāṇi etāni nāmāni parasya brahmaṇaḥ anagha yam yam kāmam abhidhyāyet tam tam āpnoti asaṃśayam sarvān kāmān avāpnoti samārādhya jagadgurum tad mayaḥ vāñchitān kāmān yat avāpnoti mānavaḥ vāc manaḥ kāyikam dveṣam yat ca kurvan prayāti adhas sva rūpa śaktiḥ sā tasya mati bheda kṛtam na tat sa śāktaḥ nirguṇaḥ śuddhaḥ brahma bhūtaḥ jagadguruḥ eka svarūpam adhyātmam puṇya apuṇya vibhedibhiḥ bhrānti jñāna anvitaiḥ miśram sita asita viceṣṭitaiḥ tāpa ārtāḥ tāpa śamanam ati prīti ati śītalam kapha doṣa anvitaiḥ na ati prīti yuktaiḥ niraṃśubhiḥ madhyastha buddhyā ca eva anye na ati śīta ati tāpibhiḥ mṛṣṭam etat iti iti anyaiḥ matsyāḍhyam iti ca aparaiḥ na ativega ativegam ca hṛṣṭa udvignaiḥ tathā aparaiḥ kim etena iti ca eva anyaiḥ para dāra abhilāṣibhiḥ dālbhya saṃdṛśyate ca anyaiḥ jantubhiḥ bhāya kātaraiḥ tat eva pūyam paśyanti preta ādyāḥ hṛti pāpinaḥ na ete gaṅgā ambhasaḥ bhedāḥ prīti aprīti pradāyinaḥ prāṇinām cetasaḥ bhedāt dālbhya ete karma yonayaḥ viśeṣa kāraṇa abhāvāt viśeṣa abhāvaḥ eva hi yogibhiḥ dṛśyate śuddham rāga ādi upaśama amalaiḥ rāgibhiḥ viṣaya ākāram tat eva brahma dṛśyate ātma putra suhṛd bhartṛ bhūta indriya antaḥkaraṇa pradhāna puruṣa ātmakam aparam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam param dālbhya niśāmaya aheyam akṣaram śuddham asaṃbhūti nirañjanam viṣṇu ākhyam paramam brahma yat vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ patnī nR̥ṇām muni śreṣṭha yoṣitaḥ ca tathā naraḥ upoṣītena yena agryā patnyā ca rahitaḥ naraḥ a śūnyaśayanā nāma dvitīyām śṛṇu tām mama śete jagatpatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śriyā sārdham yadā dvija a śūnya śayanā nāma tadā grāhyā hi sā tithiḥ kṛṣṇa pakṣa dvitīyāyām śrāvaṇe dvijasattama śrīvatsa dhāriṇam śrīśam bhaktyā abhyarcya śriyā saha śrīvatsa dhārin śrīkānta śrī dhāma śrīpate acyuta gārhasthyam mā praṇāśam me yātu dharma artha kāma dam agnayaḥ mā praṇaśyantu mā praṇaśyantu devatāḥ lakṣmyāḥ na śūnyam vara da yathā te śayanam sadā śayyā mama api a śūnyā astu tathā eva madhusūdana evam prasādya pūjām ca kṛtvā lakṣmyāḥ tathā hareḥ phalāni dadyāt śayyāyām abhīṣṭāni jagatpateḥ naktam praṇamya āyatane haviḥ bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ brāhmaṇāya dvitīye ahni śaktyā dadyāt ca dakṣiṇām a śūnya śayanaḥ ca asau dharma karma artha sādhakaḥ bhavati avyāhata aiśvaryaḥ puruṣaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ kathitam bhavatā sarvam yat pṛṣṭaḥ asi mayā dvija saṃsāra hetum muktim ca saṃsārāt muni sattama saṃsārasya asya tad muktiḥ saṃkṣepāt śrūyatām mama kurvataḥ kṣīyate pūrvam manyu bandhaḥ ca na iṣyate apūrva saṃbhava abhavāt kṣayam yāti ādikarmaṇi dālbhya saṃsāra vicchedaḥ kāraṇa abhāva saṃbhavaḥ bhavati asaṃśayam ca anyat śrūyatām atra kāraṇam saṃsārāt mucyate dālbhya samāsāt vadataḥ mama gṛhīta karmaṇā yena puṃsām jātiḥ dvijottama tat prāyaścitta bhūtam vai śṛṇu karma kṣaya āvaham brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām śūdra antyānām ca sattama jāti pradasya kṣaya dam tat eva ādyasya karmaṇaḥ jñāna kāraṇa bhāvam ca tat eva pratipadyate pumān ca adhigata jñānaḥ bhedam nā āpnoti sattama brahmaṇā viṣṇu saṃjñena parameṇa avyaya ātmanā etat te kathitam dālbhya saṃsārasya samāsatas kāraṇam bhava muktiḥ ca jāyate yoginaḥ yathā ārādhayām āsa harim lebhe kāmān ca vāñchitān ārādhya tam jagannātham na kaścid avasīdati iti śukra vacaḥ śrutvā prahlādaḥ madhusūdanam ārādhya prāptavān kṛtsnam trailoka aiśvaryam ūrjitam an ārādhya acyutam devam kaḥ kāmān prāpnute naraḥ śrutvā babhūva satatam keśava arpita mānasaḥ bhogān vā vilupān devāt tasmāt ārādhaya acyutam dadāti vāñchitān kāmān sa kāmaiḥ arcitaḥ hariḥ muktim dadāti govindaḥ niṣkāmaiḥ abhipūjitaḥ bhagavān avatīrṇaḥ abhūt martya lokam janārdanaḥ bhāra avataraṇa arthāya bhuvaḥ bhūtapatiḥ hariḥ cakāra prītim atulām sāmānya puruṣaḥ yathā sārathyam kṛtavān ca eva teṣām sarva īśvaraḥ hariḥ upakārī mahābhāgaḥ sa teṣām sarva vastuṣu keśavaḥ pāṇḍu putrāṇām sutānām janakaḥ yathā dhanyāḥ te kṛta puṇyāḥ ca mama pāṇḍu sutāḥ matāḥ rājya hetoḥ arīn jaghnuḥ akasmāt pāṇḍu nandanāḥ jātam nirdhūta pāpe asmin kule viṣṇu parigrahe evam deva varaḥ teṣām prasāda su mukhaḥ hariḥ pṛcchatām kaccit ācaṣṭe kiṃcid guhyam mahātmanām guhyam janārdanam yān tu dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣeṣu yat guhyam madhusūdanaḥ śara talpa gatāt bhīṣmāt dharmān śrutvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pṛṣṭavān yat jagannātham tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu pañcamena aśvamedhena yadā snātaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tadā nārāyaṇam devam praśnam etam apṛcchata bhagavan vaiṣṇavāḥ dharmāḥ kiṃphalāḥ kiṃparāyaṇāḥ kim kṛtyam adhikṛtya ete bhavatā utpāditāḥ purā śrotavyāḥ ced mayā dharmāḥ tatas tān kathaya akhilān pavitrāḥ ca eva ye dharmāḥ sarva pāpa praṇāśanāḥ yān śrutvā brahma hā go ghnaḥ pitṛ ghnaḥ gurutalpa gaḥ surāpaḥ vā kṛtaghnaḥ ca mucyate sarva kilbiṣaiḥ vasiṣṭha ādyaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ munibhiḥ bhāvitātmabhiḥ tatas aham tava deveśa pāda mūlam upāgataḥ śrutāḥ me mānavāḥ dharmāḥ vāsiṣṭhāḥ ca mahāmate parāśara kṛtāḥ ca eva tathā ātreyasya dhīmataḥ jāpāleḥ ca mahā bāho muneḥ dvaipāyanasya ca umā maheśvarāḥ ca eva jāti dharmāḥ ca pāvanāḥ guṇeḥ ca guṇabāhoḥ ca kāśyapeyāḥ tathā eva ca bahvāyanakṛtāḥ ca eva śākuneyāḥ tathā eva ca agastyagītāḥ maudgalyāḥ śāṇḍilyāḥ saurabhāḥ tathā bhṛgoḥ aṅgirasaḥ ca eva kaśyapa uddālakāḥ tathā saumantūgrāyaṇa agrāḥ ca pailasya ca mahātmanaḥ vaiśampāyana gītāḥ ca piśaṅgama kṛtāḥ ca ye aindrāḥ ca vāruṇāḥ ca eva kauberāḥ vātsyapauṇakāḥ āpastambāḥ śrutāḥ dharmāḥ tathā gopālakasya ca bhṛgu aṅgiraḥ kṛtāḥ ca eva sauryāḥ hārītakāḥ tathā yājñavalkya kṛtāḥ ca eva tathā saptarṣayaḥ ca ye etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca vividhāḥ śrutāḥ me dharma saṃhitāḥ bhagavan śrotum icchāmi tava vaktrāt viniḥsṛtān bahu mānāt ca prītyā ca dharmaputram yudhiṣṭhiram iṣṭaḥ tvam hi mahā bāho sadā mama yudhiṣṭhira parama artham tava brūyām kim punar dharma saṃhitām evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena ṛṣayaḥ amita tejasaḥ samājagmuḥ sabhā madhye śrotu kāmāḥ hareḥ giram deva gandharva ṛṣayaḥ guhyakāḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ vālakhilyāḥ mahātmānaḥ munayaḥ saṃmita vratāḥ vaiṣṇavān akhilān dharmān yaḥ paṭhet pāpa nāśanān bhaveyuḥ akṣayāḥ tasya lokāḥ sat puṇya bhāginaḥ kṛṣṇa dṛṣṭi hatam ca asya kilbiṣam saṃpraṇaśyati vaiṣṇavasya ca yajñasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ kautūhala samāviṣṭaḥ papraccha idam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kīdṛśam kiṃpramāṇam vā katham vā antam janārdana taranti puruṣāḥ kṛṣṇa kena upāyena saṃśame pratyuvāca mahātmānam dharmaputram yudhiṣṭhiram sādhu sādhuḥ ayam praśnaḥ śrūyatām bho yudhiṣṭhira ṣaṣ aśīti sahasrāṇi yojanānām narādhipa tāmra pātram iva ātaptam śūla vyāmiśra kaṇṭakam dvādaśa āditya saṃkāśam bhairavam duratikramam na tatra vṛkṣāḥ na chāyā pānīyam ketanāni ca yatra viśramate śrāntaḥ puruṣaḥ adhvānakaḥ nṛpa yāmyaiḥ dūtaiḥ nīyamānaḥ yamasya ājñākaraiḥ balāt avaśyam ca mahā rāja sa gantavyaḥ mahā pathaḥ naraiḥ strībhiḥ tathā tiryaiḥ pṛthivyām jīva saṃjñakaiḥ ekaviṃśat ca narakāḥ yamasya viṣaye smṛtāḥ ye tu duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ te patanti pṛthak pṛthak kṣuradhārāḥ mahā raudraḥ sūkaraḥ tālaḥ eva ca kīṭādaḥ kṛmibhakṣaḥ ca śālmaliḥ ca mahādrumaḥ tathā pūyavahaḥ pāpāḥ rudhirāndhaḥ mahattamaḥ agnijvālaḥ mahānādaḥ saṃdāmśaḥ śuna bhojanaḥ tathā vaitaraṇī ca uṣṇā asipattravanam tathā viṣṇoḥ tat vacanam śrutvā papāta bhuvi pāṇḍavaḥ sa saṃjñaḥ ca muhūrtena bhūyas keśavam abravīt bhītaḥ ca asmi mahā bāho śrutvā mārgasya vistaram kena upāyena tam mārgam taranti puruṣāḥ sukham brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradānāni nānā rūpāṇi pārthiva upānaha pradāḥ yānti sukham chāyāsu chattra dāḥ na teṣām aśubham kiṃcid śūla ādi na ca kaṇṭakāḥ aśvataryaḥ pradātāram upatiṣṭhanti tam naram vitṛṣṇāḥ ca ambu dātāraḥ tarpitāḥ ca anna dāḥ tathā auprāvṛtāḥ vastra dāḥ ca nagnāḥ vai yānti a vastra dāḥ hiraṇya dāḥ sukham yānti puruṣāḥ sva abhyalaṃkṛtāḥ go pradāḥ yānti ca sukham vimuktāḥ sarva kilbiṣaiḥ bhūmi dāḥ sukham sarva kāmaiḥ su tarpitāḥ yānti ca eva aparikliṣṭāḥ narāḥ śayyā āsana pradāḥ tatas sukhataram yānti vimāneṣu gṛha pradāḥ ārāma ropī chāyāsu śītalāsu sukham vrajet a datta dānāḥ gacchanti padbhyām yānena yāna dāḥ dīpa pradāḥ sukham yānti dīpayantaḥ ca tad patham vimānaiḥ haṃsa yuktaiḥ tu yānti māsopavāsinaḥ tatas barhiṇa yuktena ṣaṣ rātram upavāsinaḥ anantaram ca yaḥ aśnīyāt tasya lokāḥ yathā mama panīyam para lokeṣu pāvanam paramam smṛtam pānīyasya pradānena tṛptiḥ bhavati śāśvatī pānīyasya guṇāḥ divyāḥ preta loke sukha āvahāḥ tatra puṇyodakā nāma nadī teṣām pravartate ye ca duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ pūyam teṣām pravartate eṣā nadī mahā rāja sarva kāmadughā śubhā adhvani khinna gātraḥ tu dvijaḥ yaḥ kṣudh tṛṣṇā anvitaḥ pṛcchan sadā anna dātāram abhyeti gṛham āśayā tam pūjaya prayatnena saḥ atithiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ pitaraḥ devatāḥ ca eva ṛṣayaḥ ca tapodhanāḥ pūjitāḥ pūjite tasmin nirāśe tu nirāśakāḥ tasmin dvije pūjite pūjitāḥ te gate nirāśe pratiyānti nāśam āgamiṣyati yat pātram tat pātram tārayiṣyati kapilāyām tu dattāyām yat phalam jyeṣṭhapuṣkare tat phalam pāṇḍava śreṣṭha viprāṇām pāda śaucane dvija pāda udaka klinnā yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī deva mālya apanayanam dvija ucchiṣṭa apamārjanam śrānta saṃvāhanam ca eva dīnasya paripālanam ekaikam pāṇḍava śreṣṭha go pradānāt viśiṣyate pāda śaucam tathā abhyaṅgam dīpam annam pratiśrayam svāgatena agnayaḥ prītāḥ āsanena śatakratuḥ pitaraḥ pāda śaucena annādyena prajāpatiḥ yeṣām taḍāgāni bahu udakāni prapāḥ ca kūpāḥ ca pratiśrayāḥ ca sa vṛṣam go śatam tena dattam bhavati śāśvatam śochayet kapilām dattvā etat vai na atra saṃśayaḥ prāsādāḥ yatra sauvarṇāḥ vasordhārā ca syandate prayacchate yaḥ kapilām sa vatsām kāṃsya upadohām kanaka agra śṛṅgīm yān yān hi kāmān abhivāñchate asau tān tān avāpnoti amalān ca lokān tāvat gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvat garbham na muñcati tasmin kāle pradātavyā vidhinā yā mayā uditā antarikṣa gataḥ vatsaḥ yāvat yonyām pradṛśyate tāvat gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvat garbham na muñcati yāvanti tasya romāṇi tāvat varṣāṇi mānavaḥ haṃsa yuktena yānena yuktena apsarasām gaṇaiḥ tiladhenum pravakṣyāmi yaḥ ca asyāḥ vidhiḥ uttamaḥ suvarṇa nābhim yaḥ kṛtvā sukhūram kṛṣṇa mārgaṇām kutapa prastara sthām tu tilām kṛtvā prayatnataḥ tilaiḥ prastha ādi tām dadyāt sarva ratnaiḥ alaṃkṛtām catur antā bhavet dattā pṛthivī na atra saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇājine tilām kṛtvā kṛṣṇām vā yadi vā itarām yāvat jīva kṛtam pāpam tena dānena pūyate rājateṣu tu pātreṣu koṇeṣu madhu sarpiṣī dhanam prāpnoti puṇyena maunena ājñām prayacchati ahiṃsayā param rūpam dīkṣayā kula janma ca phala mūla aśanāt rājyam svargaḥ parṇa aśanaḥ bhavet payaḥ bhakṣa divam yānti snānena draviṇa adhikāḥ śākam sādhayataḥ rājyam nāka pṛṣṭham anāśanāt sthaṇḍile ca śayānasya gṛhāṇi śayanāni ca cīra valkala dhāriṇām vastrāṇi ābharaṇāni ca śayana āsana yānāni ye gatāḥ hi tapaḥ vanam rasānām pratisaṃhārāt saubhāgyam abhijāyate āmiṣa pratiṣedhāt tu bhavati āyuṣmatī prajā kīrtiḥ bhavati dānena ārogyam ca api ahiṃsayā dvija śuśrūṣayā rājyam divya rūpam avāpnute dvija śuśrūṣayā rājyam dvija tvam ca api puṣkalam dīpa āloka pradānena cakṣuṣmān jāyate naraḥ gandha mālya pradānena tuṣṭiḥ bhavati puṣkalā keśa śmaśrūn dhārayataḥ hi agrā bhavati saṃtatiḥ vāc śaucam manasaḥ śaucam yat ca śaucam jala āśrayam tribhiḥ śaucaiḥ upetaḥ yaḥ sa svargī na atra saṃśayaḥ tāmra āyasānām bhaṇḍānām dātā ratna adhipaḥ bhavet labhate tu param sthānam balavān puṣyate sadā dhānyam krameṇa arjita vitta saṃcayam vipre suśīle te prayacchate yaḥ vasuṃdharā tasya bhavet su tuṣṭā dhārāḥ vasūnām pratimuñcati iha sa śrī samṛddham bahu ratna pūrṇam labhati adhiṣṭhāna varam samṛddham indhanāni ca yaḥ dadyāt dvijebhyaḥ śiśira āgame kāya agni dīptim saubhāgyam aiśvaryam ca adhigacchati chattra pradānena gṛham variṣṭham ratham tathā upānaha saṃpradānāt svargīyam api āha hiraṇya dānam tathā variṣṭham kanaka pradānam svādhyāya cāritra guṇa anvitāya tasya api lokāḥ pravarāḥ bhavanti hiraṇya dānam ca tathā viśiṣṭam sa śakraḥ lokam labhate durāpam su citra vastra ābharaṇa upadhānam dadyāt naraḥ yaḥ śayanam dvijāya rūpa anvitām dakṣavatīm manojñām bhāryām ayatna upacitām labhet saḥ lavaṇasya tu dātāraḥ tilānām sarpiṣaḥ tathā svarge apsarobhiḥ saha bhukta bhogaḥ tatas cyutaḥ śīlavatīm sa bhāryām rūpa anvitām dakṣavatīm su raktām sukhena dharmeṇa tathā api kāle kīdṛgvidhāsu avasthāsu dattam dānam janārdana avasthām kṛṣṇa kathaya param kautūhalam hi me vṛthājanmāni catvāri vṛthādānāni ṣoḍaśa aputrāṇām vṛthā janma ye ca dharma bahiṣkṛtāḥ para pākam ca ye aśnanti para dāra ratāḥ ca ye pari asthānam vṛthā dānam sa doṣam parikīrtitam ārūḍha patite ca eva anyāya upārjitam ca yat vyartham ca abrāhmaṇe dānam patite taskare tathā guroḥ ca aprīti janake kṛtaghne grāmayājake paricārake ca yat dattam vṛthādānāni ṣoḍaśa sa īrṣyā manyu manāḥ ca eva dambha artham ca artha kāraṇāt yaḥ śuddhiḥ prayataḥ bhūtvā prasanna mānasa indriyaḥ deśe deśe ca pātre ca yaḥ dadāti dvijātiṣu trailokya kṛṣṇa bhūtānām sarva loka ātmakaḥ hi asi nRﾱṇām yadu vara śreṣṭha tuṣyase kena karmaṇā brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjitaiḥ nityam pūjitaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ vipra aparā gatiḥ mahyam yaḥ tān pūjayate nṛpa tam aham tena rūpeṇa prapaśyāmi yudhiṣṭhira kāṇāḥ kubjāḥ ca khañjāḥ ca daridrāḥ vyādhitāḥ ca ye na avamanyet dvijān prājñaḥ mama rūpam hitam tathā bahavaḥ api na jānante narāḥ jñāna bahiṣkṛtāḥ yathā aham dvija rūpeṇa carāmi pṛthivī tale ye kecid sāgara antāyām pṛthivyām kīrtitāḥ dvijāḥ a preṣaṇe preṣayantaḥ dāsa tvam kārayanti hi mṛtān tān kara pattrena yama dūtāḥ mahā balāḥ nikṛntanti yathā kāṣṭham sūtra mārgeṇa śilpinaḥ ye ca eva aślakṣṇayā vācā tarjayanti nara adhamāḥ mṛtān tān yama lokeṣu nihatya dharaṇī tale agni varṇaiḥ ca saṃdaṃśaiḥ jihvām uddharate yamaḥ pāpāḥ ca nārake vahnau dhāsyante yama kiṃkaraiḥ ye tu viprān nirīkṣanti pāpāḥ pāpena cakṣuṣā abrahmaṇyāḥ śruteḥ bāhyāḥ nityam brahma dviṣaḥ narāḥ teṣām ghorāḥ mahā kāyāḥ vajra tuṇḍāḥ bhayānakāḥ uddharanti muhūrtena cakṣuḥ kākāḥ yama ājñayā yaḥ tāḍayati viprān tu kṣatam kuryāt sa śoṇitam asthi bhaṅgam ca yaḥ kuryāt prāṇaiḥ vā api viyojayet kīlaiḥ vinihataḥ pāpaḥ mīrāyām pacyate bhṛśam su bahūni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām kleśa bhāj bhavet ravāt muñcati durbuddhiḥ na tasmai niṣkṛtiḥ smṛtā tasmāt viprāḥ nara śreṣṭha namaskāryāḥ ca nityaśas anna pāna pradānaiḥ tu pūjā arhāḥ satatam dvijāḥ āmantrayitvā yaḥ viprān gandhaiḥ mālyaiḥ ca mānavaḥ sa mām prasādayet ca eva sa ca mām paritoṣayet tapaḥ dama anviteṣu eva nityam pūjām prayojayet ye brāhmaṇāḥ saḥ aham asaṃśayam nṛpa teṣu arciteṣu arcitaḥ aham yathāvat yaḥ pūjayet bhojayitvā dvijāgryān saṃpūjayitvā paritoṣayet ca tena eva mām eva sadā pūjayanti na saṃśayaḥ virūpāḥ ca surūpāḥ ca vijanān niṣkalān api kṛpayā bhāvita ātmānaḥ ye arcayanti dvijottamān anasūyā hita ātmānaḥ viprān ārādhate kvacid asaṃśayam sadā bhaktyā mām eva arcayate hi saḥ yaḥ candanaiḥ sa agaru gandha mālyaiḥ abhyarcayet dāru mayīm mama arcām vipra prasādāt madhaḥ eva ca aham vipra prasādāt asurān jayāmi sāyam prātar ca yaḥ saṃdhyām upāste a skanna mānasaḥ japan hi pāvanīm devīm gāyatrīm vedamātaram sa tayā pāvitaḥ devyā brāhmaṇaḥ pūta kilbiṣaḥ na sīdet pratigṛhṇānaḥ pṛthivīm tu sa sāgarām ye ca anye dāruṇāḥ kecid grahāḥ sūrya ādayaḥ divi te ca asya saumyāḥ jāyante śivāḥ śivatamāḥ āh sadā yatra tatra gatam ca enam dāruṇāḥ piśita aśanāḥ ghora rūpāḥ mahā kāyāḥ na karṣanti dvijottamam yāvantaḥ ca pṛthivyām hi cīrṇa veda vratāḥ dvijāḥ a cīrṇa vrata vedāḥ vā vikarma patham āśritāḥ teṣām tu pāvana artham hi nityam eva yudhiṣṭhira nā asti kiṃcid nara vyāghra duṣkṛtam brāhmaṇasya tu pūrṇāhutim vā prāpnoti juhute ca trayaḥ aghnayaḥ dahanti duṣkṛtam tasya agnayaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ purāṇam mānavāḥ dharmāḥ sa aṅgaḥ vedaḥ cikitsitam ājñā siddhāni catvāri na hantavyāni hetubhiḥ hatvā hi etāni saṃmūḍhaḥ kalpam tamasi pacyate na brāhmaṇam parīkṣeta śrāddha kāle hi upasthite su mahān parivādaḥ hi brāhmaṇānām parīkṣaṇe kāṇāḥ kuṇṭhāḥ ca ṣaṇḍāḥ ca daridrāḥ vyādhitāḥ tathā sarve śrāddhe niyoktavyāḥ miśritāḥ vedapāragaiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ hi mahat bhūtam janmanā saha jāyate lokāḥ loka īśvarāḥ ca api sarve brāhmaṇa pūjakāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kupitāḥ hanyuḥ bhasma kuryuḥ ca tejasā lokān anyān sṛjeyuḥ ca lokapālān tathā aparān brāhmaṇāḥ hi mahātmānaḥ virajāḥ svarga saṃkramāḥ brāhmaṇānām parīvādāt asurāḥ salileśayāḥ apeyaḥ sāgaraḥ yaiḥ tu kṛtaḥ kopāt mahātmabhiḥ yeṣām kopa agniḥ adya api daṇḍake na upaśāmyati ete svargasya netāraḥ bhūmi devāḥ sanātanāḥ ebhiḥ ca adhikṛtaḥ panthāḥ deva yānaḥ saḥ ucyate te pūjyāḥ te namaskāryāḥ teṣu sarvam pratiṣṭhitam pramāṇam sarva lokānām niyatāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ tān apāśritya tiṣṭhante trayaḥ lokāḥ sanātanāḥ gūḍha svādhyāya tapasaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśita vratāḥ vidyā snātāḥ vrata snātāḥ an apāśritya jīvinaḥ āśīviṣāḥ iva kruddhāḥ upacaryāḥ hi brāhmaṇāḥ tapasā dīpyamānāḥ te daheyuḥ sāgarān api brāhmaṇeṣu ca tuṣṭeṣu tuṣyante sarva devatāḥ brāhmaṇānām namaskāraiḥ sūryaḥ divi virājate brāhmaṇānām parīvādāt pateyuḥ api devatāḥ dhuri ye na avasīdanti praṇīte yajña vahnayaḥ te gatiḥ sarva bhūtānām adhyātma gati cintakāḥ ādi madhya avasānānām jñānānām chinna sāmśayāḥ para apara viśeṣa jñāḥ netāraḥ paramām gatim avadhyāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tasmāt pāpeṣu api ratāḥ sadā yaḥ ca sarvam idam hanyāt brāhmaṇam vā api tad samam saḥ agniḥ saḥ arkaḥ mahā tejāḥ viṣam bhavati kopitaḥ bhūtānām agra bhuj vipraḥ varṇa śreṣṭhaḥ pitā guruḥ praṇītaḥ ca apraṇītaḥ ca yathā agniḥ daivatam mahat evam vidvān a vidvān vā brāhmaṇaḥ daivatam mahat śmaśāneṣu api tejasvī pāvakaḥ nā eva duṣyati sarvathā brāhmaṇāḥ pūjyāḥ sarvathā daivatam mahat śakraḥ api hi dvijendrāṇām bibheti vibudha adhipaḥ dānam devāḥ praśaṃsanti iti dharma vidaḥ viduḥ nānā dāna vidhim tasmāt śṛṇuṣva su samāhitaḥ hiraṇya dānam go dānam pṛthivī dānam eva ca yat yat iṣṭatamam loke yat ca asti dayitam gṛhe suvarṇa dānam go dānam pṛthivī dānam eva ca yat dadāsi viśiṣṭebhyaḥ yat ca aśnāsi dine dine tat te vittam aham manye śeṣam kasya api rakṣasi tulya nāmāni śastāni trīṇi tulya phalāni ca nityam deyāni rāja indra gāvaḥ pṛthvī sarasvatī deyāni yācamānebhyaḥ pānam annam tathā eva ca evam dānam samuddiṣṭam vyuṣṭimat tārakam param eṣa te vihitaḥ yajñaḥ śraddhā pūtaḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ sa ca yajñeṣu dadatām anasūyayā dāna vidbhiḥ kṛtaḥ panthāḥ yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ evam dattvā brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dātā phalam upāśnute brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva vidyante satyavantaḥ bahu śrutāḥ dattam vā dāpitam vā api vā utsāhyam api vā kṛtam utthāya utthāya dātavyam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ yudhiṣṭhira āgamiṣyati yat pātram tat pātram tārayiṣyati asaṃkīrṇam ca yat pātram tat pātram tārayiṣyati adhyāyam tapasaḥ vakṣye tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu tapasā prāpyate svargam tapasā prāpyate yaśaḥ āyuḥ prakarṣam bhogān ca tapasā vindate naraḥ jñānam vijñānam āstikyam saubhāgyam rūpam uttamam yat kāryam kiṃcid āsthāya puruṣaḥ tapyate tapaḥ surāpaḥ pāradārī ca bhrūṇa hā gurutalpa gaḥ api sarva īśvaraḥ sthāṇuḥ viṣṇuḥ ca eva sanātanaḥ brahmā hutāśanaḥ śakraḥ tapasyanti sanātanāḥ ṣaḍaśīti sahasrāṇi munīnām ūrdhvaretasām tapasā prāpyate rājyam śakraḥ sarva sura īśvaraḥ tapasā eva prakāśete nakṣatrāṇi grahāḥ tathā viśvāmitraḥ ca tapasā brāhmaṇa tvam upāgataḥ ṛcam ekām api paṭhan sa yāti paramām gatim tapaḥ yaśaḥ ca puṇyam ca pitṛ deva ṛṣi pūjanam satyam yajñaḥ tathā vedāḥ mantrāḥ devī sarasvatī satyena ca apaḥ kṣipati parjanyaḥ pṛthivī tale pāraṇam sarva vedānām sarva tīrtha avagahanaḥ satyam ca vadataḥ loke tat samam syāt na saṃśayaḥ munayaḥ satya prapathāḥ parām siddhim itas gatāḥ satyena devāḥ prīyante pitaraḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tathā munayaḥ satya niratāḥ tasmāt satyam viśiṣyate apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇaiḥ vimānaiḥ upayānti te etat pramāṇam yaḥ kuryāt sarva yajña phalam labhet snātavyam manasā yuktaiḥ snānam tat paramam smṛtam ātma arthe ca para arthe vā putra arthe vā api pārthiva ye anṛtam na abhibhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ yaḥ satya vādī puruṣaḥ na anṛtam paribhāṣate saṃprāpya virajān lokān uṣitvā śāśvatīḥ samāḥ śucīnām śrīmatām gehe jāyate su mahāmatiḥ āditya candrau anala anilau ca dyauḥ bhūmiḥ āpaḥ hṛdayam yamaḥ ca satyam vadan tejasā dīpyamānaḥ na hīyate dharma yaśaḥ artha kāmaiḥ eṣa vāṇī kṛtaḥ dharmaḥ vaidikaḥ dharma niścaye sarveṣām eva varṇānām pravakṣyāmi yudhiṣṭhira avāpnoti yathā kāmān upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ upavāsāḥ manuṣyāṇām mayi eva arpita cetasām pañcamīm ca eva ṣaṣṭhīm ca paurṇamāsīm ca pāṇḍava upoṣya rūpavān dhanyaḥ subhagaḥ ca eva jāyate aṣṭamīm ca eva kaunteya śukla pakṣe caturdaśīm upoṣya vyādhi rahitaḥ vīryavān ca eva jāyate mārgaśīrṣam tu yaḥ māsam nityam eka aśanaḥ bhavet kṛṣi bhāgī bhavet rājan bahu putraḥ ca jāyate subhagaḥ darśanīyaḥ ca jñāna bhāgī ca jāyate strīṣu vallabha tām yāti vaśyāḥ ca asya bhavanti tāḥ strīṣu vallabha tām yāti vaśyāḥ ca asya bhavanti tāḥ naraḥ vā yadi vā nārī jñātīnām śreṣṭha tām vrajet jyeṣṭha māsam apānīyam eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet aiśvaryam puruṣa vyāghra strī bhāgī ca upajāyate āṣāḍham bharata śreṣṭhaḥ eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet śūraḥ ca bahu dhānyaḥ ca bahu putraḥ ca jāyate śrāvaṇam tu nara vyāghra bhaktena ekena yaḥ kṣapet māsam bhādrapadam rājan eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet dhana āḍhyaḥ vīryavān ca eva aiśvaryam pratipadyate yaḥ kṣapet eka bhaktena māsam āśvayujam naraḥ dhanavān vāhana āḍhyaḥ ca bahu putraḥ ca jāyate kārttikam tu naraḥ māsam nityam eka aśanaḥ bhavet śūraḥ ca bahu bhāryaḥ ca kīrtimān ca eva jāyate ete māsāḥ nara śreṣṭhaḥ eka bhaktena kīrtitāḥ tithīnām niyamān ca eva tān śṛṇuṣva narādhipa pakṣe pakṣe caturtham tu bhaktam yaḥ kṣapayet naraḥ kṛṣi bhāgī yaśaḥ bhāgī tejasvī ca api jāyate pakṣe pakṣe tri rātram tu yaḥ kṣapet nara puṅgava gaṇe ghoṣe pure grāme māhātmyam pratipadyate gaṇa ādhipatyam labhate niḥsapatnam akaṇṭakam yaḥ tu sāyam tathā kalyam bhuṅkte na eva antarā pibet ṣaḍbhiḥ eva tu varṣaiḥ tu sidhyate na atra saṃśayaḥ agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ gavāmayasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ pūrṇam varṣa sahasram tu svarga loke mahīyate ārtaḥ vā vyādhitaḥ vā api gacchet anaśanam tu yaḥ ārūḍha strī śata ākīrṇe viharan sukham edhate gacchet anaśanam yaḥ tu tasya api śṛṇu yat phalam śatam varṣa sahasrāṇām svarga loke mahīyate yāvanti romakūpāni tasya gātreṣu bhārata na asti vedāt param śāstram na asti mātṛ samaḥ guruḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ param nā asti divi ca iha ca pāvanam divyam varṣa sahasram tu viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā sarve hi ete divam prāptāḥ kṣamāvantaḥ bahu śrutāḥ brāhmaṇa tvam su duṣprāpam nisargāt brāhmaṇaḥ bhavet kṣatriyaḥ vā athavā vaiśyaḥ nisargāt eva jāyate duṣkṛtena tu duṣṭa ātmā sthānāt bhraśyati mānavaḥ śreṣṭham sthānam samāsādya tasmāt rakṣeta paṇḍitaḥ brāhmaṇyāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣatra yonyām prasūyate śūdra karmāṇi kurvāṇaḥ śūdra tvam upapadyate sa tatra durgatim prāpya sthānāt bhraṣṭaḥ yudhiṣṭhira tasmāt prāpya śubham sthānam pramādāt na tu nāśayet śūdra annena avaśeṣeṇa yaḥ mriyet jaṭhare dvijaḥ āhitāgniḥ tathā yajvā sa śūdra gati bhāj bhavet kṣatra annena avaśeṣeṇa kṣatra tvam upapadyate vaiśya annena avaśeṣeṇa vaiśya tvam upapadyate tām yonim labhate vipraḥ bhuktvā annam yasya vai mṛtaḥ brāhmaṇa tvam śubham prāpya durlabham yaḥ avamanyate karmaṇā yena medhāvī śūdraḥ vaiśyaḥ abhijāyate śūdra karma yathā uddiṣṭam śūdraḥ bhūtvā samācaret yathāvat paricaryām tu triṣu varṇeṣu nityadā kurute avimanāḥ yaḥ tu sa śūdraḥ vaiśya tām vrajet kṣatriya tvam yathā vaiśyaḥ tat vakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas caukṣaḥ pāpa jana dveṣṭā śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriya kule jāyate na atra saṃśayaḥ kṣatriyaḥ brahma yonyām tu jāyate śṛṇu tat yathā adhīte svargam anvicchan tretāgni śaraṇaḥ sadā ṛtu kāle tu svām bhāryām abhigacchan vidhānataḥ śūdrāṇām yācakānām ca nityam siddhim iti bruvan go brāhmaṇasya ca arthāya raṇe ca abhimukhaḥ hataḥ tretāgni mantra pūta ātmā kṣatriyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhavet vidhi jñaḥ kṣatriya kule yājakaḥ sa tu jāyate brāhmaṇa tvam su duṣprāpam kṛcchreṇa āsādyate naraiḥ suvarṇam paramam dānam suvarṇam dakṣiṇā parā daśa pūrva aparān vaṃśān ātmānam ca viśāmyate api pāpa śatam kṛtvā dattvā vipreṣu tārayet agniḥ hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇam ca hutāśanaḥ tasmāt suvarṇam dadatā dattāḥ sarvāḥ ca devatāḥ sarva veda pramāṇa jñāḥ veda śruti nidarśanāt suvarṇa daḥ svarga loke kāmān iṣṭān upāśnute viraja ambara saṃvītaḥ pariyāti yatas tatas vimānena arka varṇena bhāsvareṇa virājatā apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇe bhāsvatā svena tejasā tasmāt sva śaktyā dātavyam kāñcanam mānavaiḥ bhuvi lokān tu sṛjatā pūrvam gāvaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā prīti artham sarva bhūtānām tasmāt tāḥ mātaraḥ smṛtāḥ tasmāt tāḥ varṇayiṣyāmi dānam ca āsām yathāvidhi yādṛśī vidhinā yena dātavyā yādṛśāya ca dvijāya poṣaṇa artham tu homadhenu kṛte na vai prathamā gaurakapilā dvitīyā gaurapiṅgalā tṛtīyā rakta kapilā caturthī nīla piṅgalā tu saptamī citra piṅga akṣī aṣṭamī babhru rohiṇī navamī śveta piṅga akṣī daśamī śveta piṅgalā tādṛśāḥ ye api anaḍvāhaḥ kapilāḥ te prakīrtitāḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vāhayet tān tu na anyaḥ varṇaḥ kadācana dhenum dattvā suvratām sa upadhānām kalyāṇa vatsām ca payasvinīm ca yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti dhenvāḥ duhyeta kāmān nṛpa varṣāṇi tāvat prayacchate yaḥ kapilām sa vatsām kāṃsya upadohām kanaka agra śṛṅgīm taiḥ taiḥ guṇaiḥ kāmdughā hi bhūtvā naram pradātāram upaiti sā gauḥ parām vṛddhim śriyam prāpya svarga loke mahīyate daśa ca ubhayatas pretya mātāmaha pitāmahaiḥ gacchet su kṛtinām lokān gāvaḥ dattvā yathāvidhi tasya api ca akṣayāḥ lokāḥ bhavanti iha paratra ca yaḥ dyūtena dhanam jitvā krītvā gāvaḥ prayacchati pratigṛhya tu yaḥ dadyāt gāvaḥ śuddhena cetasā yaḥ ca ātma vikrayam kṛtvā gāvaḥ dadyāt yathāvidhi saṃgrāme yaḥ tanum tyaktvā gāvaḥ krītvā prayacchati deha vikraya mūlyaḥ tāḥ śāśvatāḥ kāma dohanāḥ rūpa anvitāḥ śīla vayaḥ upapannāḥ sarvāḥ praśastāḥ hi su gandhavatyaḥ yathā hi gaṅgā saritām variṣṭhā tathā arjunīnām kapilā variṣṭhā antar jātāḥ su kraya jñāna labdhāḥ prāṇān tyaktvā sa udakāḥ sa udvahāḥ ca kṛcchra utsṛṣṭāḥ poṣaṇāya abhyupetāḥ dvāraiḥ etaiḥ go viśeṣāḥ variṣṭhāḥ tisraḥ rātryaḥ ca api upoṣya iha dātā tṛptāḥ gāḥ vai tarpitebhyaḥ prayacchet loke jyeṣṭhāḥ loka vṛttānta vṛttāḥ vedaiḥ gītāḥ soma nisyanda bhūtāḥ saumyāḥ puṇyāḥ kāma dāḥ prāṇa dāḥ ca gāvaḥ dattvā sarvadā santi santaḥ na ca eva āsām dāna mātram praśastam pātram kālaḥ go viśeṣaḥ vidhiḥ ca dṛṣṭvā gāvaḥ pāvaka āditya bhūtāḥ svādhyāya āḍhye pātra varye viśiṣṭe vaitāna stham satya vākyam kṛtajñam goṣu kṣāntam go śaraṇyam su vṛttam śastam pātram go pradānasya bhūmeḥ tathā suvarṇasya ca sarvakālam bhikṣā dānam ca adhikam saṃpraśastam pāthaḥ dānam ca anna dānam tathā ca bhikṣate bahu bhṛtyāya śrotriyāya āhitāgnaye dātavyā gauḥ prayatnena ekā api atiphalā hi sā tām ced vikrīṇate rājan vacasā kaluṣīkṛtām jīrṇām ca eva upabhuktām ca jarat kūpam iva aphalām tamaḥ praviśate dātā dvijam kleśena yojayan duṣṭāḥ kṛśāḥ ca eva pālayatīḥ ca na etādṛśāḥ dāna yogyāḥ bhavanti anaḍvāham su vratam yaḥ dadāti halasya voḍhāram ananta vīryam prayacchate yaḥ puruṣaḥ dvijāya svādhyāya cāritra guṇa anvitāya balena yuktam vṛṣabham tu nīlam ṣaḍāṅgavam prīti karam surūpam yuvānam balinam śyāmam śatena saha yūthapam gavendram brāhmaṇa indrāya bhūri śṛṅgam alaṃkṛtam vṛṣabham ye prayacchanti śrotriyāya āhitāgnaye aiśvarye te abhijāyante jāyamānāḥ punar punar sa dakṣiṇām kāñcana rūpya śṛṅgīm kāṃsya upadohām kanaka uttarīyām dhenum tilānām kanaka uttarīyām lokāḥ vasūnām acalāḥ bhavanti tila alābhe tu yaḥ dadyāt ghṛtadhenum yata vrataḥ ghṛta alābhe tu yaḥ dadyāt jaladhenum yata vrataḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva gāvaḥ ca kulam ekam dvidhā kṛtam yāvanti tāsām romāṇi tāvat svarge mahīyate śṛṇu tvam me gavām lokāḥ yādṛśāḥ yatra vā sthitāḥ manojñāḥ ramaṇīyāḥ ca sarva kāmadughāḥ sadā puṇyāḥ pāpa harāḥ ca eva gavām lokāḥ na saṃśayaḥ pramodante mahāsthāne narāḥ vigata kalmaṣāḥ evam yaiḥ datta satkārāḥ surabhyaḥ ca arcitāḥ sadā kāmarūpāḥ mahātmānaḥ pūtāḥ vigata kilbiṣāḥ gandharvaiḥ upagīyante go śaraṇyāḥ na saṃśayaḥ brahmaṇyāḥ sādhu vṛttāḥ ca dayāvantaḥ anukampinaḥ ghṛṇinaḥ śubha karmāṇaḥ modante te amaraiḥ saha gobhiḥ pāpa kṛtam karma dṛḍham eva mayā uhyate mātaraḥ sarva bhūtānām prajā saṃrakṣaṇe smṛtāḥ brahmaṇā loka sāreṇa gāvaḥ pāpa bhaya apahāḥ kṛśāya tu viśeṣeṇa vṛtti glānāya sīdate bhū dānena samam dānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati iti dharma vidaḥ prāhuḥ tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi svarge vasati bhūmi daḥ atidānam tu sarveṣām bhūmi dānam iha ucyate acalā hi akṣayā bhūmiḥ sarvān kāmān prayacchati bhūmi daḥ svargam āruhya śāśvatīḥ edhati samāḥ yathā bhūmiḥ sadā devī dātāram kurute patim evam sa dakṣiṇā dattā kurute gauḥ janādhipam api pāpa kṛtam prāpya pratigṛhṇīta bhūmi dam mahīm dadan pavitrī syāt puṇyā hi jagatī yatas tat asyāḥ satatam prītyai kīrtanīyam prayacchatā yat kiṃcid kurute pāpam puruṣaḥ vṛtti karṣitaḥ suvarṇam rajatam tāmram maṇi muktā vasūni ca sarvān etān mahā prājña dadāti vasudhām dadan tapaḥ yajñāḥ śrutam śīlam alobhaḥ satya vādi tā bhartuḥ niḥśreyase yuktāḥ tyaktātmānaḥ raṇe hatāḥ phala kṛṣṭām mahīm dattvā sa udakām sa phala anvitām sa udakam vā api śaraṇam prāpnoti mama saṃpadam vasudhām yaḥ dadāti dvijātaye ikṣubhiḥ saṃtatām bhūmim yava godhūma śādbalām na bhūyas bhūmi dānāt hi dānam anyat viśiṣyate puṇyām sarva rasām bhūmim yaḥ dadāti nara ṛṣabha na tasya lokāḥ kṣīyante bhūmi dasya mahātmanaḥ yathā janitrī puṣṇāti kṣīreṇa sva sutam nṛpa evam sarva guṇā bhūmiḥ dātāram anupuṣyati agniṣṭoma ādibhiḥ yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā vipula dakṣiṇaiḥ na tat phalam avāpnoti yat dattvā vasudhām nṛpa mṛtyoḥ hi kiṃkarāḥ daṇḍāḥ hi agni tāpāḥ su dāruṇāḥ ghorāḥ ca vāruṇāḥ pāśāḥ na upasarpanti bhūmi dam saṃtarpayanti dātāram bhūmeḥ prabhavatām vara kṛśāya kṛśa bhṛtyāya vṛtti kṣīṇāya sīdate bhūmim vṛtti kārīm dattvā sattrī bhavati mānavaḥ siṃhāsanam tathā chattram vara aśvāḥ vara vāraṇāḥ bhūmi dānasya puṣpāṇi phalam svargam tathā eva ca ādityāḥ iva dīpyante tejasā divi mānavāḥ ye prayacchanti vasudhām brāhmaṇāya āhitāgnaye yathā bījāni rohanti prakīrṇāni mahī tale tathā kāma adhirohanti bhūmi dāna guṇa arjitāḥ āsphoṭayanti pitaraḥ pravalganti pitāmahāḥ bhūmi daḥ naḥ kule jātaḥ sa naḥ saṃtārayiṣyati śūlapāṇiḥ ca bhagavān abhinandanti bhūmi dam sa dātā sa ca vikrāntaḥ yaḥ dadāti vasuṃdharām dātāram anugṛhṇāti yathā dattena rocate pūrva dattām haran bhūmim narakāya upapadyate vindhya aṭavīṣu atoyāsu śuṣka koṭara vāsinaḥ kṛṣṇa sarpāḥ hi jāyante ye haranti vasuṃdharām patanti aśrūṇi rudatām dīnānām avasīdatām brāhmaṇānām hṛtam kṣetram hanyāt tri puruṣam kulam pūrva dattām dvijātibhyaḥ yatnāt rakṣa yudhiṣṭhira mahīm mahībhṛtām śreṣṭha dānāt śreyaḥ anupālanam yatra eṣaḥ paṭhyate śrāddhe bhūmi dānasya saṃstavaḥ na tatra rakṣasām bhāgaḥ na asurāṇām kathaṃcana akṣayam tu bhavet śrāddham pitR̥ṇām na atra saṃśayaḥ tasmāt viśrāvayet enam śrāddheṣu brāhmaṇān sadā evam etat yathoddiṣṭam pitRṇām dattam akṣayam bhūmi dānam mahā rāja sarva pāpa apaham śubham agniṣṭoma ādibhiḥ yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā vipula dakṣiṇaiḥ iti yajña vidaḥ prāhuḥ yajña karma viśāradāḥ tasmāt tat te pravakṣyāmi yat phalam śastra jīvinām yaḥ śūraḥ vadhyate yuddhe vimṛdan para vāhinīm tasya dharma artha kāmāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca eva āpta dakṣiṇāḥ viṣṇukrāntam sa yajate evam yudhyan raṇa ajire yaḥ tu śastram an utsṛjya vīryavān vāhinī mukhe rājānam rāja putram vā senāpatim atha api vā hanyāt kṣatreṇa yaḥ śūraḥ tasya lokaḥ akṣayaḥ dhruvaḥ gavā arthe brāhmaṇa arthe vā svāmi arthe tu kṛtam ca yaiḥ ūrdhvam tiryak ca yaḥ ca arvāk prāṇān saṃtyajate yudhi yasya cihnīkṛtam gātram śara śakti ṛṣṭi tomaraiḥ vara apsaraḥ sahasrāṇi śūram āyodhane hatam bhūyas gatim pravakṣyāmi raṇe ye abhimukhāḥ hatāḥ śakyam tu iha samṛddhaiḥ tu yaṣṭum kratu śataiḥ naraiḥ yām yajña saṃghaiḥ tapasā ca viprāḥ svarga eṣiṇaḥ tatra cayaiḥ prayānti kṣaṇena tām eva gatim prayānti mahā āhave svām tanum saṃtyajantaḥ sarvān ca vedān saha ṣaḍbhiḥ aṅgaiḥ sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca vane ca vāsam etān guṇān ekaḥ eva atiśete saṃgrāma dhāmni ātma tanum tyajet yaḥ imām giram citra padām śubha akṣarām su bhāṣitām vṛta bhidām divaukasām eṣa puṇyatamaḥ svargyaḥ su yajñaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ sarveṣām eva varṇānām kṣatriyasya viśeṣataḥ bhūyas ca eva pravakṣyāmi bhīṣma vākyam anuttamam yādṛśāya prahartavyam yādṛśam parivarjayet ātatāyinam āyāntam api veda antagam raṇe jighāṃsantam jighāṃsīyān na tena brahma hā bhavet hata aśvaḥ ca na hantavyaḥ pānīyam yaḥ ca yācate bhagna dhanvā acchina guṇaḥ prāṇa īpsuḥ kṛpaṇam bruvan parṇa śākhā tṛṇa grāhī tava asmi iti ca yaḥ vadet brāhmaṇaḥ asmi iti yaḥ ca āha bālaḥ vṛddhaḥ napuṃsakaḥ tasmāt etān pariharet yathā uddiṣṭān raṇa ajire a māṃsa bhakṣaṇe rājan yaḥ dharmaḥ kuru puṅgava tat me śṛṇu yathātathyam yaḥ ca asya vidhiḥ uttamaḥ māsi māsi aśvamedhena yaḥ yajeta śatam samāḥ na ca khādati yaḥ māṃsam samam etat yudhiṣṭhira yaḥ māṃsa rasam āsvādya sarva māṃsāni varjayet catur vratam idam śreṣṭham prāṇinām mṛtyu bhīruṇām tadā bhavati loke asmin prāṇinām jīvita eṣiṇām viśvāsyaḥ ca upagamyaḥ ca na hi hiṃsā rudiḥ yadā duṣṭarān tarate māṃsasya parivarjanāt prāṇāḥ yathā ātmanaḥ abhīṣṭāḥ bhūtānām api te tathā ahiṃsā paramaḥ dharmaḥ satyam eva ca pāṇḍava ahiṃsā ca eva satyam ca dharmaḥ hi paramaḥ smṛtaḥ na hi māṃsam tṛṇāt kāṣṭhāt upalāt vā api jāyate jīvāt utpadyate māṃsam tasmāt garhanti tat budhāḥ lobhāt vā buddhi mohāt vā yaḥ māṃsāni atti mānavaḥ bhakṣayitvā tu yaḥ māṃsam paścāt api nivartate idam anyat pravakṣyāmi purāṇam ṛṣi nirmitam yaḥ dadyāt kāñcanam merum kṛtsnām vā api vasuṃdharām a bhakṣaṇam ca māṃsasya na tu tulyam yudhiṣṭhira śrūyate ca purākalpe hi ṛṣīṇām vrīhayaḥ paśuḥ yajante yena vai yajñān ṛṣayaḥ puṇya karmiṇaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saṃśayam pṛṣṭaḥ vasuḥ rājā tatas purā abhakṣyam bhakṣyam iti vai māṃsam āha narādhipa ākāśāt medinīm prāptaḥ tatas sa pṛthivīpatiḥ kaumudam tu viśeṣeṇa śukla pakṣe narādhipa caturaḥ vārṣikān māsān yaḥ māṃsam parivarjayet catvāri bhadrāṇi āpnoti kīrtiḥ āyuḥ yaśaḥ balam atītya sarva duḥkhāni sukham jīvet nirāmayaḥ yaḥ hi varṣa śatam pūrṇam tapaḥ tapyet su dāruṇam api ekam varjayet māsam māṃsam etat samam matam yaḥ varjayati māṃsāni māsam pakṣam atha api vā sarvakālam tu māṃsāni varjitāni mahā ṛṣibhiḥ manvā kṣupeṇa śvetena tathā evā ikṣvākunā api ca bhṛguṇā nala rāmābhyām dilīpa raghu pauravaiḥ āyuṣā ca eva gārgyeṇa janakaiḥ cakravartibhiḥ dhundhumāra ambarīṣābhyām nahuṣeṇa ca dhīmatā gādhinā purukutsena kuruṇā puruṇā tathā mucukundena māndhātrā sagareṇa mahātmanā śibinā ca aśvapatinā vīrasena ādibhiḥ tathā saṃjayena atha bhīṣmeṇa puṣkareṇa atha pāṇḍunā suvarṇaṣṭhīvinā ca eva duṣvanta nṛga rohitaiḥ etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ sarvaiḥ māṃsam na bhakṣitam śarad kaumudikam māsam tatas svargam gatāḥ nṛpāḥ brahma loke ca pūjyante jvalamānāḥ śriyā āvṛtāḥ upāsyamānāḥ gāndharvaiḥ strī sahasra samanvitāḥ tat evam uttamam dharmam ahiṃsā lakṣaṇam śubhan ye rakṣanti mahātmānaḥ nāka pṛṣṭhe vasanti te madhu māṃsam ca ye nityam varjayanti iha mānavāḥ pravṛttau ca nivṛttau ca pramāṇam ṛṣi sattamaiḥ go brāhmaṇa hita arthāya cāturvarṇya hitāya ca aśiṣṭa nigraha arthāya śiṣṭānām rakṣaṇāya ca yudhiṣṭhirasya rājarṣeḥ evam nārāyaṇaḥ abravīt pañca rūpāṇi rājānaḥ dhārayanti amita ojasaḥ tān na hiṃset na ca ākrośet na ākṣipet na apriyam vadet devāḥ mānuṣa rūpeṇa caranti pṛthivīm imām indrāt prabhu tvam jvalanāt pratāpam krauryam yamāt vaiśravaṇāt prabhāvam sattva sthitim rāma janārdana ābhām ādāya rājñaḥ kriyate śarīram mahatī devatā hi eṣā nara rūpeṇa tiṣṭhati svayam indraḥ naraḥ bhūtvā pṛthivīm anuśāsati na hi pālayitum śaktaḥ manuṣyaḥ pṛthivīm imām yat prajā pālanaiḥ puṇyam prāpnuvanti iha pārthivāḥ ṣaṣṭham labhati bhāgam tu prajāḥ dharmeṇa pālayan grāma ādhipatyam nagara ādhipatyam deśa ādhipatyam pṛthivīpati tvam na prāpnuvanti iha manuṣya mātrāḥ ye devatānām na bhavanti bhāgāḥ evaṃvṛttāḥ tu rājānaḥ deva bhāgāḥ na mānuṣāḥ na abhītaḥ yajate kāṃścan na abhītaḥ daṇḍam icchati ye eva devāḥ hantāraḥ tān lokaḥ arcayate bhṛśam hantā śakraḥ ca rudraḥ ca hantā vaiśravaṇaḥ yamaḥ varuṇaḥ vāyuḥ ādityaḥ parjanyaḥ agniḥ bṛhaspatiḥ etān devān namasyanti pratāpa praṇatāḥ janāḥ na brahmāṇam na dhātāram na pūṣāṇam kathaṃcana na hi paśyāmi jīvantam rājan kaṃcid ahiṃsayā na hatvā lipyate rājā prajāḥ dharmeṇa pālayan yadi daṇḍaḥ na vidyeta durvinītāḥ narāḥ hanyuḥ paśūn manuṣyān ca yājñiyāni haviṃṣi ca tasmāt prāṇi hite daṇḍe hiṃsā doṣaḥ na bādhate na eva ustrāḥ na balīvardāḥ na aśva aśvatara gardabhāḥ yuktāḥ vaheyuḥ yānāni daṇḍaḥ ced na udyataḥ bhavet satyam kila etat yat uvāca śakraḥ daṇḍaḥ prajāḥ rakṣati sādhu vṛttaḥ yasya agnayaḥ pratimāsasya bhītāḥ saṃtarjitāḥ daṇḍa bhayāt jvalanti yatra śyāmaḥ lohita akṣaḥ daṇḍaḥ carati pāpa hā daṇḍanītau sunītāyām sarve sidhyanti upakramāḥ daṇḍaḥ ced na pravarteta vinaśyeyuḥ imāḥ prajāḥ kāka ādyāḥ ca purodāśam śvā ca eva avalihet haviḥ cāturvarṇya vimokṣāya durvinīta bhayāya ca daṇḍasya hi bhayāt bhītāḥ narāḥ tiṣṭhanti śāsane ti api bhogāya kalpante daṇḍena uparipīḍitāḥ guruḥ ātmavatām śāstā śāstā rājā durātmanām iha pracchanna pāpānām śāstā vaivasvataḥ yamaḥ pāpānām atha mūḍhānām para dravya apahāriṇām paradāra ratāḥ ye ca ye ca pātaka saṃjñitāḥ teṣām tu śāsana arthāya mayā etat samudāhṛtam brāhmaṇyam duṣkaram jñātvā tasya daṇḍam nipātayet karma anurūpaḥ daṇḍaḥ syāt go hiraṇya ādikaḥ bhavet avadhyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ rājan strī vṛddhaḥ bālaḥ eva ca yaḥ caret aśubham karma pāpam rāja vigarhitam śirasaḥ muṇḍanam kṛtvā gomayena anulepayet khara yānena nagaram ḍiṇḍimena tu bhrāmayet rāja nirdiṣṭa daṇḍasya prāyaścittam na vidyate eṣa te kathitaḥ daṇḍaḥ brāhmaṇasya yudhiṣṭhira kṣatriyasya tu yaḥ daṇḍaḥ tam vakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas tasya daṇḍam pravakṣyāmi tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu sarva sva haraṇam kṛtvā para rāṣṭrāya preśayet rājyam kāṅkṣeta yaḥ mūḍhaḥ rāja patnīm atha api vā śaraiḥ tu rājā vidhyeta śakti cakra gadā ādibhiḥ kṣatriyasya tu duṣṭasya daṇḍaḥ eṣa vidhīyate vaiśyasya api ca yaḥ daṇḍaḥ tam pravakṣyāmi bhārata pātakeṣu eva krūreṣu yaḥ tu vaiśyaḥ pravartate śūlāyām bhedanam tasya vṛkṣa śākhā avalambanam etat vaiśyasya nirdiṣṭam śūdrasya api anupūrvaśas śūle śūdrasya yaḥ duṣṭaḥ tasya ekasya vadhaḥ smṛtaḥ kuñjareṇa abhimardeta mīnīyām atha pācayet etat śūdrasya nirdiṣṭam na anyaḥ daṇḍaḥ vidhīyate na ekasya arthe kulam hanyāt na rāṣṭram na ca grāmakam ekam su śiṣṭitam kṛtvā śeṣam kośam praveśayet dhana lobhāt na moktavyaḥ rāgāt vā śāsanam vinā yudhiṣṭhirasya rājarṣeḥ evam nārāyaṇaḥ abravīt samāsena yathānyāyam daṇḍanītim anuttamām uttama adhama kāryeṣu sameṣu viṣameṣu ca rāja dharmān tu paśyeta viṣṇunā samudāhṛtān etān dharmān jagannāthaḥ pāṇḍu putrāya pṛcchate yādṛś sattvam manuṣyāṇām tādṛś ārādhya keśavam mukti kāmāḥ narāḥ muktim svargam deva tvam īpsavaḥ gandharva yakṣa siddhānām vṛṇvanti anye salokatām varṣeṣu abhīpsavaḥ viṣṇum pātāleṣu tathā apare bhogān abhīpsavaḥ viṣṇum toṣayaṇti narādhipa dharma upadeśāt acalām vahan bhaktim janārdane sa śarīraḥ gataḥ svargam dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tathā eva janakaḥ kṛṣṇe viniveśya sva mānasam avāpa paramām siddhim vasuḥ prāyāt tripiṣṭapam avāpuḥ atulān kāmān te te saṃtoṣya keśavam an ārādhya jagannātham sarva pāpa haram harim sat gatiḥ kena saṃprāptā bhogāḥ ca api manoramāḥ viṣṇoḥ kārya manuṣyasya darśanāt utthitaḥ punar samam vināśam āyāti devaḥ kaḥ abhyadhikaḥ tatas rāṣṭrasya śaraṇam rājā pitarau bālakasya ca dharmaḥ samasta martyānām sarvasya śaraṇam hariḥ śrutam mayā yathā pūrvam āryakaḥ me yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sa śarīraḥ gataḥ svargam jitam ātmīya karmabhiḥ yat tu etat bhagavān āha sa yathā pāṇdu pūrvajaḥ uvāca śvapacaḥ dvāḥstham praśraya avanata sthitaḥ śuddha sphaṭika sopānam maṇi kāñcana toraṇam aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi brāhmaṇānām dine dine yudhiṣṭhiram ṛte bhūpam bhuñjate kasya veśmani duḥkha ārtaḥ kāryavān rājan caṇḍālaḥ dvāri tiṣṭhati kena api hetu mātreṇa bhavantam duṣṭam āgataḥ kim rūpam kīdṛśam śīlam kaḥ asya arthaḥ kim prayojanam brūhi dvāḥstha yathāvat me naraḥ tiṣṭhati kīdṛśaḥ kāka kokila kṛṣṇa aṅgaḥ bhagna nāsā aruṇa īkṣaṇaḥ yava madhyaḥ kṛśa grīvaḥ vakra pādaḥ mahā hanuḥ brūhi gaccha durācāram caṇḍālam pāpa karmiṇam caṇḍāla patitau dṛṣṭvā naraḥ paśyeta bhāskaram pratyuvāca pratīhāram īṣat manyu pariplutaḥ kim deva kāryeṇa narādhipasya kṛtvā hi manyum viṣaya sthitānām tat deva kāryam sa ca yajña homaḥ yat aśru pātāḥ na patanti rāṣṭre iti uktaḥ sa tvaram gatvā dharmarājam tathā tatham kathayām āsa tat sarvam cāṇḍālena yat īritam su śobhanam idam vākyam na bhavet antya jātiṣu cintayitvā tatas rājā nirjagāma yudhiṣṭhiraḥ iti etat vacanam śrutvā nirjagāma yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pratyuvāca ca caṇḍālam īṣan kopa samanvitaḥ āvādha kāraṇam sarvam yathāvat kathayasva me tat aham te pratijñāya caṇḍa karmaka rakṣaṇam apāsya deva kārya artham praviśyāmi antaram punar na bhuñjate brāhmaṇāḥ me sarvāḥ ca udvijate janaḥ prāṇi hiṃsā ca naḥ vṛttiḥ deva puṣṇāti me anṛtam aneka janma sāhasrīm prāpya saṃsāra paddhatim mānuṣye kutsitām jātim āpannaḥ muṣitaḥ asmi bhoḥ tām saṃprāpya vṛthājanmā muṣṭaḥ asmi kuru sattama duḥkhe duḥkha adhikān paśyet sukhe paśyet sukha adhikān ātmānam śoka harṣābhyām śatrubhyām iva na arpayet saḥ aham icchāmi vijñātum ati duṣkṛta karma kṛt vaktum arhasi dharma jña kaḥ pāpiṣṭhataraḥ mayā adhvānam upari śrāntam brāhmaṇam gṛham āgatam an arcayitvā yaḥ bhuṅkte sa pāpiṣṭhataraḥ tvayā go dhanasya tṛṣā ārtasya jala artham paridhāvataḥ vivāhayitvā yaḥ kanyām kula jām śīla maṇḍanām vinā tyajati doṣeṇa sa pāpiṣṭhataraḥ tvayā āśākāraḥ tu a dātā yaḥ dātuḥ ca pratiṣedhakaḥ dattam ca yaḥ kīrtayati sa pāpiṣṭhataraḥ tvayā brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vā api vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ api vā naraḥ kṛtārthaḥ aham gamiṣyāmi yaśaḥ dharmam avāpnuhi tuṣṭaḥ asmi aham svayā yonyā mattaḥ proktāḥ tvayā adhamāḥ devatānām ṛṣīṇām ca pitR̥ṇām ca kṛtam mayā sāṃpratam deśa kālaḥ ayam tvam eva atra bhava atithiḥ caṇḍālaḥ aham mahā rāja patitaḥ loka varjitaḥ caṇḍālaḥ bhava pāpaḥ vā śatruḥ vā pitṛ ghātakaḥ deśa kāla abhyupetam tvām bharaṇīyam hi vedmi aham daśa sūnā samam cakram daśa cakra samaḥ dhvajaḥ daśa dhvaja samāḥ veśyāḥ daśa veśyā samaḥ nṛpaḥ daśa sūnā sahasrāṇi kurute yaḥ hi saunikaḥ nānā gotra ādi caraṇāḥ bhuñjate brāhmaṇāḥ mama na te vadanti vāgduṣṭam yathā etat kīrtitam tvayā lobha ātmānaḥ na jānīyuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ rāja kilbiṣam rāja kilbiṣa dagdhānām brāhmaṇānām yudhiṣṭhira chinnānām iva bījānām punarjanma na vidyate narendra bhavane bhuṅktvā viṣṭhāyām jāyate kṛmiḥ nindase sarva rājānaḥ na ca ātmānam praśaṃsasi athavā nindya rūpeṇa pitā naḥ tvam iha āgataḥ dhairyavān ātmanaḥ anindyaḥ na āśvāsa artham ca pṛcchasi anindyaḥ nindya rūpeṇa mahātmā tvam hi me mataḥ bhavān upendraḥ śakraḥ vā śarvaḥ vā tvam pinākadhṛk jñātaḥ asmi pṛthivīpāla tuṣṭaḥ ca tava darśanāt nandantu bhūmi bhāgāḥ te yeṣu tvam pṛthivīpatiḥ kim me rājyena bhoḥ tāta viṣayaiḥ jīvitena vā yaḥ aham sūnā sahasraiḥ tu daśabhiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ mā viṣādam nara śreṣṭha samupaihi yudhiṣṭhira yajñeśvaram yajñamūrtim tvam ca viṣṇum samāśritaḥ yeṣām na viṣaye viprāḥ yajñaiḥ yajñapatim harim yeṣām pāṣaṇḍa saṃkīrṇam na rāṣṭram brāhmaṇa utkaṭam te tu sūnā sahasrāṇām daśānām bhāginaḥ nṛpāḥ yeṣām na yajñapuruṣaḥ kāraṇam puruṣottamaḥ te tu pāpa samācārāḥ sūnā pāpa ogha bhāginaḥ iṣṭiḥ vaiśvānarī pāpam upahaṃsyati te akhilam avaśyam viṣaye kaścid brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśrita vrataḥ iṣṭim vaiśvānarīm kḷptām nirvapet abda paryaye tasya ṣaṣ bhāga mātreṇa tvam pāpam nirdahiṣyasi samyak śraddhā samācārāt aham ārādhitaḥ tvayā paraḥ parāṇām ādyaḥ asau jñeyaḥ dhyeyaḥ janārdanaḥ lobha ādi vyāpta hṛdayaḥ yat pāpam kurute naraḥ śamāya alam jalam vahneḥ tamasaḥ bhāskara ādayaḥ kṣāntiḥ kaleḥ agha oghasya nāma saṃkīrtanam hareḥ yā kācid manasaḥ vṛttiḥ sā bhavatu acyuta āśrayā yā yā jāyeta me buddhiḥ yāvat jīvāmi aham pitar sā sā chinattu saṃdehān kṛṣṇā āptau paripanthinaḥ yathā govindam ārādhya sa śarīraḥ surālayam evam etat aśeṣam te mad prasādāt bhaviṣyati nā asti govinda bhaktānām vāñchitam bhuvi durlabham ārādhya pāṇḍavaḥ yātaḥ sa śarīraḥ surālayam bhūyas ca śṛṇu rāja indra janakena mahātmanā yat gītam vahatā bhaktim jñānam āsādya keśave sarvatra sama dṛṣṭim tam janakam mithilā īśvaram dvija rūpam samāsthāya devadevaḥ janārdanaḥ pṛthivīm pṛthivī pālaḥ pālayitvā pitā tava śabda ādayaḥ ye viśayāḥ te vairāgya phalāḥ nṛpa nītyā vihīnaḥ tu bhavān katham rājyam kariṣyati sarvaiḥ nītim samāsthāya yathā te prapitāmahaiḥ kṛtam rājyam tathā bhūpa kuru mā ati jaḍaḥ bhava tava prajñā matā hi eṣā mama mohaḥ mahīpate mama api śrūyatām vākyam bhavataḥ yadi rocate yadā sarva gataḥ viṣṇuḥ paramātmā prajāpatiḥ tadā mitra ādi madhyastha saṃjñā keṣu nipātyatām pitā mātā tathā bhrātā yadā na anyat janārdanāt pitṛ mātṛ mayīm saṃjñām tadā kutra karomi aham aneka rūpa rūpaḥ ayam viṣṇuḥ eva akhilam jagat viṣṇuḥ pitā me jagataḥ pratiṣṭhā viṣṇuḥ mātā viṣṇuḥ eva agrajaḥ me viṣṇuḥ gatiḥ viṣṇu mayaḥ tathā asmi viṣṇau sthitaḥ asmi akṣa gataḥ ca viṣṇuḥ yaḥ me mamatva upagataḥ sa viṣṇuḥ yaḥ ca ari bhūtaḥ mama saḥ api viṣṇuḥ divam viyat bhūḥ kakubhaḥ ca viṣṇuḥ bhūtāni viṣṇuḥ bhuvanāni viṣṇuḥ paśyāmi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat śṛṇomi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat spṛśāmi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat jighrāmi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat rasāmi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat manye ca viṣṇum na param tatas anyat budhyāmi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat sarvam hi viṣṇuḥ na param tatas anyat jighrāmi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat namāmi viṣṇum na param tatas anyat viṣṇuḥ samastam na param tatas asti viṣṇuḥ samastam na param ca devaḥ viṣṇuḥ laghīyān na param tatas asti viṣṇuḥ garīyān na param tatas anyat viṣṇuḥ sthārīyān na param tatas asti yathā na viṣṇu vyatiriktam anyat śṛṇomi paśyāmi tathā spṛśāmi tvam ca aham anye ca śarīra bhedaiḥ vibhinnam īśasya hareḥ svarūpam mūrta amūrti viśeṣam tu paśyataḥ tad mayam dvija krodha harṣa ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ sthāsyanti hṛdaye katham tathā api mā ruṣam kārṣīḥ acikitsyāḥ hi mohitāḥ bahu rūpaḥ tatas rūpam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam darśayām āsa su prītaḥ janakāya janārdanaḥ tatas tad darśanāt bhūpam śirasā praṇatam prabhuḥ ādyaḥ prajāpati patiḥ pratyuvāca acyutaḥ hariḥ evam bhaviṣyati iti uktvā gataḥ antardhānam īśvaraḥ iti kṛṣṇe nara vyāghra kurvan bhaktim naraḥ sadā mama avatārān akhilān śrotum icchā pravartate yathā yathā hi kṛṣṇasya kathā iyam kathyate tvayā manaḥ prītiḥ anāyāsāt apuṇya caya saṃkṣayaḥ sa kuruṣva amala mate prasāda pravaṇam manaḥ avatārān sureśasya viṣṇoḥ icchāmi veditum nārāyaṇam purākalpe pṛṣṭavān kamalodbhavaḥ oṃkāra pravaṇāḥ vedāḥ jagmuḥ te ca rasātalam kṛṣṇanābhi hrada udbhūta kamala udara śāyini bhogi śayyā āśayaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ dvitīyām tanum ātmanaḥ kṛtvā mīna mayīm sadyas praviveśa rasātalam madhu kaiṭabhābhyām ca punar bhogi śayyā gataḥ hariḥ hṛtān hayaśirāḥ bhūtvā vedān āhṛtavān rasāt āhṛteṣu atha vedeṣu devadevam pitāmahaḥ tuṣṭāva praṇataḥ bhaktyā tasya ca āvis babhau hariḥ uvāca prakaṭībhūtam praṇipatya abja saṃbhavaḥ namaḥ sūkṣma ati sūkṣmāya namaḥ tubhyam trimūrtaye saḥ aham icchāmi tam jñātum ātmānam prabhava avyayam tat mām bhaktaḥ iti jñātvā kathaya ātmānam acyuta kathayāmi tava ātmānam an ākhyā godaram param na vācām viṣaye yaḥ asau a viśeṣaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ an ākhyāta svarūpam mām bhavān jñāsyati yogataḥ mad jijñāsā parā brahman tena jātā matiḥ tava evam uktaḥ tatas brahmā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā viṣṇoḥ svarūpam jijñāsuḥ yuyoja ātmānam ātmanā sa dadarśa ati sūkṣmam ca sūkṣma jyotiṣi ajam vibhum niyuta ardha ardha mātreṇa vyāpta aśeṣa carācaram ātmānam indra rudra arka candra aśvi vasu mārutān kha ādīni atha ca śabda ādīn dadṛśe ca sa tanmayān ye vyaktāḥ ye tathā avyaktāḥ bhāvāḥ ye ca api pauruṣāḥ tān ca tatra ati sūkṣmaḥ api dṛṣṭavān akhilān vibhuḥ jñātam sva rūpam ajñāta sva rūpa bhagavan tava bhagavan jñātam ajñātam ananta aja namaḥ astu te paramam ca avatāreṣu yat rūpam tat vadasva me keṣu keṣu mayā jñeyaḥ sthāneṣu tvam adhokṣaja saṃbhūtayaḥ mama ācakṣva yāḥ bhaviṣyanti te bhuvi saṃbhūtayaḥ yāḥ tu bhavān kariṣyati vadasva tāḥ tvam kartā sarva bhūtānām saṃhartā ca īśvara īśvaraḥ tava api kartā nā anyaḥ asti sva icchayā krīḍate bhavān yat mām tvam pṛcchasi brahman avatāra āśritam param deveṣu nR̥ṣu tiryakṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca mama avatārāḥ kārya artham jagataḥ ca upakāriṇaḥ abhyutthānam adharmasya tadā ātma aṅgam sṛjāmi aham paritrāṇāya sādhūnām vināśāya ca duṣkṛtām pūrva utpanneṣu bhūteṣu nṛdeva ādiṣu ca api aham praviśya ca tathā pūrvam tanum dharma bhṛtām vara deva tve devikā ceṣṭā tiryaktve mama tāmasī icchayā mānuṣa tve ca vicarāmi nṛ ceṣṭayā pratikṣaṇam ca bhūteṣu sṛjāmi jagataḥ sthitim caritam mānuṣa ādīnām tat vai jānīhi mad kṛtam yat ca pṛcchasi mām brahman kāḥ kāḥ saṃbhūtayaḥ tava tāḥ śṛṇuṣva samāsena yāḥ bhaviṣyanti sāṃpratam matsyena bhūtvā pātālāt tava vedāḥ samuddhṛtāḥ madhu kaiṭabhābhyām ca hṛtā dattā aśva śirasā mayā tvam api atra mahābhāga mad aṃśaḥ kamala udarāt mad na abhisaṃbhavāt jātaḥ prajā sṛṣṭi karaḥ paraḥ ekārṇavam ca yat idam brahman paśyasi aśeṣatas asmin vasumatīm devīm magnām pātālam āgatām veda pādaḥ yūpa daṃṣṭraḥ kratu dantaḥ citī mukhaḥ agni jihvaḥ darbha romā brahma śīrṣaḥ mahā tapāḥ ājya nāsaḥ śruvastuṇḍaḥ sāma ghoṣa svaraḥ mahān prāc vaṃśa kāyaḥ dyutimān nānā dīkṣābhiḥ ācitaḥ dakṣiṇā hṛdayaḥ yogī mahā sattra mayaḥ mahān bhūtvā yajñavarāhaḥ aham iti brahman rasātalāt pṛthivīm uddhariṣyāmi sthāpayaiṣyāmi ca sthitau parvatānām nadīnām ca dvīpa ādīnām ca yā sthitiḥ tām ca tadvat kariṣyāmi śaila ādīnām anukramāt hiraṇyākṣam ca durvṛttam kaśyapasya ātmasaṃbhavam tena eva ghātayiṣyāmi rūpeṇa aham prajāpate utpādya pṛthivīm samyak sthāpayitvā yathā purā sṛṣṭim tatas kariṣyāmi tvām āviśya prajāpatim jānāsi kāpilam rūpam prathamam pauruṣam mama sarva vidyā praṇetāram tvayā vedeṣu darśitam tatas utsṛjya rūpāṇi amara ādi vibhedataḥ vyāpayiṣyāmi lokān tu bhū loka ādīm aśeṣatas sṛṣṭam jagat idam deva mānuṣya ādi viśeṣaṇam nṛsiṃha rūpam kṛtvā aham ghātayiṣyāmi tam ripum kṣīra abdau kūrma rūpaḥ aham devānām kamala udbhava mandaram dhārayiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhena amṛta manthane hariṣyati ca devānām yajña bhāgān yadā baliḥ tadā aham vāmanaḥ bhūtvā gatvā tasya mahā adhvaram vañcayitvā asura patim kariṣyāmi tripiṣṭapam balim ca api kariṣyāmi pātāla tala vāsinam dattātreyaḥ bhaviṣyāmi nihaṃsyāmi tathā asurān sattvānām upakārāya pradhāna puruṣa antaram darśayiṣyāmi lokeṣu kāpilam rūpam āsthitaḥ kārtavīrya ādibhiḥ ca anyaiḥ caturdaśabhiḥ anvitāḥ bhaviṣyanti mad aṃśena tretāyām cakravartinaḥ tatas ca bhārgavaḥ rāmaḥ gṛhīta paraśuḥ dvijaḥ bhūtvā kṣatriya hīnām ca kariṣyāmi vasuṃdharām punar ca rāghavaḥ rāmaḥ bhūtvā daśaratha ātmajaḥ baddhvā mahā udadhim kartā rākṣasānām kula kṣayam uttīrya ca param pāram laṅkām āsādya durjayām nihatya rāvaṇam vīram vara dānena darpitam māyāvinām mahā vīryam rakṣasām vana śāyinām lakṣmaṇa anucaraḥ rāmaḥ kariṣyāmi kula kṣayam aṣṭāviṃśatime prāpte dvāpare kaṃsam ucchritam keśinam dhenukam ca eva śakunim pūtanām tathā ariṣṭam ca haniṣyāmi murum narakam eva ca niśumbham tathā anyān ca asura īśvarān haniṣyāmi su durvṛttān lokānām hita kāmyayā govardhanam giri varam dhārayiṣyāmi bāhunā bhāra ākrāntām imām urvīm dhanaṃjaya sahāyavān ghātayitvā akhilān bhūpān laghvīm kartāsmi sattama dvārakām plāvayiṣyāmi utsrakṣyāmi manuṣya tām dvitīyaḥ yaḥ mama aṃśaḥ tu rāmaḥ anantaḥ sa lāṅgalī narāṇām atha nārīṇām dayām bhūteṣu darśayan rakta ambarāḥ hi āñjita akṣāḥ praśānta manasaḥ tatas eḍūka cihnā pṛthivī na devagṛha bhūṣitā śūdrāḥ śūdreṣu dāsyanti mayi buddha tvam āgate naraka arhāṇi karmāṇi kariṣyanti prajāpate svādhyāyeṣu avasīdantaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ śauca varjitāḥ na śroṣyanti pituḥ putrāḥ śvaśrū śvaśurayoḥ snuṣāḥ na bhāryā bhartuḥ īśasya na bhṛtyāḥ vinaya sthitāḥ varṇa saṃkara tām prāpte loke asmin dasyu tām gate brāhmaṇa ādiṣu varṇeṣu bhaviṣyati adhara uttaram mānuṣān bhakṣayiṣyanti mlecchāḥ pārthiva rūpiṇaḥ daśa pañca ca vai śākhāḥ pramāṇena bhaviṣyati tatas aham saṃbhaviṣyāmi brāhmaṇaḥ hari piṅgalaḥ kalkī viṣṇuyaśaḥputraḥ yājñavalkya purohitaḥ mlecchān utsādayiṣyāmi gṛhīta astraḥ kuśa āyudhaḥ sthāpayiṣyāmi maryādāḥ cāturvarṇye yathā uditāḥ tathā āśrameṣu sarveṣu brahmacāri vrata ādikāḥ sthāpayitvā tatas sarvāḥ prajāḥ saddharma vartmani kalki rūpam parityajya divam eṣyāmi aham punar tatas kṛta yugam bhūyaḥ pūrva vat saṃpravartsyate varṇa āśramāḥ ca dharmeṣu dveṣu sthāsyanti sattama mama avatārāḥ śataśas ye bhavanti jagat hitāḥ saṃkarṣaṇa ātmajaḥ ca eva kalpa ante ca rasātalāt samutpatsyet tadā rudraḥ kālāgniḥ iti yaḥ śrutaḥ tatas kṣayam kariṣyāmi jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam tvad rūpī ca tatas bhūtvā jagat srakṣyāmi aham punar aṃśāvataraṇam sarvam mattaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu yat dṛśyam yat ca vai spṛśyam yat ghreyam rasyate ca yat yat śravyam yat ca mantavyam bodhavyam ca aham aṃśa gaḥ labhante abhimatān kāmān narāḥ tān tān yathā īpsitān rahasyam idam ākhyātam tava api kathitam mayā viṣṇuḥ sarva gataḥ anantaḥ sarvam tatra pratiṣṭhitam etat pavitram paṭhitam tathā duḥsvapna nāśanam jātismara tvam prajñām ca dadāti paṭhatām nṛṇām śrutāḥ saṃbhūtayaḥ sarvāḥ gadataḥ tava suvrata tat aham śrotum icchāmi nR̥ṇām duḥsvapna nāśanam svapnāḥ hi su mahābhāga dṛśyante ye śubha aśubhāḥ idam eva mahā rāja pṛṣṭavān te pitāmahaḥ bhīṣmam dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭham dharma putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ devavratam mahā prājñam sarva śāstra viśāradam tat aham śrotum icchāmi brūhi me vadatām vara śṛṇu rājan mahā bāho vartayiṣyāmi te akhilam atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam gaja indra mokṣaṇam puṇyam kṛṣṇasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ sarva ratna mayaḥ śrīmān trikūṭaḥ nāma parvataḥ utthitaḥ sāgaram bhittvā deva ṛṣi gaṇa sevitaḥ apsarobhiḥ samākīrṇaḥ śrīmān prasravaṇa ākulaḥ mṛgaiḥ dvīpaiḥ dvijaiḥ ca eva vṛtaḥ sauvarṇa rājataiḥ puṃnāgaiḥ karṇikāraiḥ ca puṣpitaiḥ upaśobhitaḥ śālaiḥ tālaiḥ tamālaiḥ ca kuṭajaiḥ ca arjunaiḥ tathā evam bahuvidhaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ sarvatas samalaṃkṛtaḥ nānā dhātu ujjvalaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ prasravadbhiḥ samantataḥ mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ siṃhaiḥ mātaṃgaiḥ ca sadāmadaiḥ jīvaṃjīvaka saṃghuṣṭam cakora śikhi nāditam tasya ekam kāñcanam śṛṅgam sevate yat divā ādaraḥ nānā puṣpa samākīrṇam nānā gandha samākulam dvitīyam rājatam śṛṅgam sevate yat niśākaraḥ pāṇḍura ambuda saṃkāśam tuṣāra caya saṃnibham tṛtīyam brahmasadanam prakṛṣṭam śṛṅgam uttamam na tat kṛtaghnāḥ paśyanti na nṛśaṃsāḥ na nāstikāḥ na atapta tapasaḥ śailam tam vai paśyanti mānavāḥ tasya sānumataḥ pṛṣṭhe saraḥ kāñcana paṅkajam kāraṇḍava samākīrṇam rājahaṃsa upaśobhitam utpalaiḥ śatapattraiḥ ca kāñcanaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam pattraiḥ maṇi dala prakhyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kāñcana saṃnibhaiḥ gulmaiḥ kīcaka veṇūnām samantāt parivāritam tasmin sarasi duṣṭa ātmā virūpaḥ antar jalāśayaḥ āsīt grāhaḥ gaja indrāṇām durādharṣaḥ mahā balaḥ ājagāma asita abhra ābhaḥ kareṇu parivāritaḥ mada srāvī mahā raudraḥ pāda cārī iva parvataḥ sa gajaḥ añjana saṃkāśaḥ madāt calita mānasaḥ tṛṣitaḥ sa jalam prāpya kusumākara śītalam gṛhītaḥ tena raudreṇa grāheṇa avyakta mūrtinā paśyantīnām kareṇūnām krośantīnām ca dāruṇam kriyate paṅkaja vane grāheṇa ati balīyasā gajaḥ ca ākarṣate tīram grāhaḥ ca ākarṣate jalam vāruṇaiḥ saṃyataḥ pāśaiḥ niḥprayatna gatiḥ kṛtaḥ veṣṭyamānaḥ su ghoraiḥ tu pāśaiḥ nāgaḥ dṛḍhaiḥ tathā vyathitaḥ saṃnirutsāhaḥ gṛhītaḥ ghora karmaṇā sa tu nāga varaḥ śrīmān nārāyaṇa parāyaṇaḥ tam eva paramam devam gataḥ sarva ātmanā tadā ekāgram cintayām āsa viśuddhena antarātmanā ādyam devam mahātmānam pūjayām āsa keśavam nava megha pratīkāśam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam diś bāhum sarva mūrdhānam bhū pādam gagana udaram āditya candra nayanam samagram loka sākṣiṇam pragṛhya puṣkara agreṇa kāñcanam kamala uttamam anāśritāya devāya niḥspṛhāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ ādyāya bījāya śivāya ca praśāntāya ārṣeyāya pravartine niścalāya yaśasvine anantarāya ca ekāya sanātanāya pūrvāya avyaktāya namaḥ namaḥ purāṇāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ guhyāya gūḍhāya guṇāya a guṇa vartine atarkyāya aprameyāya viśveśvarāya devāya śivāya haraye namaḥ nārāyaṇāya viśvāya devānām paramātmane namaḥ namaḥ kāraṇa vāmanāya nārāyaṇāya amita vikramāya śrī śārṅga cakra asi gadā dharāya namaḥ astu tasmai puruṣottamāya pītāmbarāya madhu kaiṭabha nāśanāya bhakti priyāya vara dīpta sudarśanāya viśvāya cāru mukuṭāya namaḥ akṣarāya nānā vicitra mukuṭa aṅgada bhūṣaṇāya sarveśvarāya vara dāya namaḥ varāya viśvātmane parama kāraṇa kāraṇāya phulla aravinda vimala āyata locanāya lokāyanāya tridaśāyanāya brahmāyanāya ātmabhavāyanāya dharma ayanāya eka jalāyanāya mahāvarāhāya sadā nataḥ asmi acintyam avyaktam ananta rūpam nārāyaṇam kāraṇam ādidevam yuga anta śeṣam puruṣam purāṇam tam vāsudevam śaraṇam prapadye kṣetrajñam ātma prabhavam vareṇyam tam vāsudevam śaraṇam prapadye vadanti yam vai puruṣam sanātanam tam vāsudevam śaraṇam prapadye tam īśvaram tṛptam anopamaiḥ guṇaiḥ parāyaṇam viṣṇum upaimi śāśvatam kāryam kriyā kāraṇam aprameyam hiraṇyanābham varapadmanābham mahābalam veda nidhim surottamam vrajāmi viṣṇum śaraṇam janārdanam pīta ambaram kāñcana bhakti citram mālā dharam keśavam abhyupaimi bhavodbhavam veda vidām variṣṭham yoga ātmānam sāṃkhya vidām variṣṭham śrīvatsa aṅkam mahādevam veda guhyam anuttamam prabhavam sarva lokānām nirguṇam parameśvaram prapadye mukta saṃgānām yatīnām paramām gatim bhagavantam surādhyakṣam akṣaram puṣkara īkṣaṇam śaraṇyam śaraṇam bhaktyā prapadye brāhmaṇapriyam bhūtātmānam mahātmānam prapadye madhusūdanam ādidevam ajam śambhum vyakta avyaktam janārdanam kṣetrajñam puruṣam yajñam triguṇa atītam avyayam nārāyaṇam aṇīyāṃsam prapadye parameśvaram vareṇyam anagham devam ṛṣayaḥ vedapāragāḥ namaḥ te puṇḍarīkākṣa bhaktānām abhaya prada subrahmaṇya namaḥ te astu trāhi mām śaraṇa āgatam prītimān abhavat rājan śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ sāṃnidhyam kalpayām āsa tasmin sarasi mādhavaḥ grāha grastam gajam tam ca saṃgṛhya salilāśayāt ujjahāra aprameya ātmā tarasā eva ari sūdanaḥ sthala stham dārayām āsa grāham cakreṇa mādhavaḥ mokṣayām āsa ca gajam pāśebhyaḥ śaraṇa āgatam gaja tvam agamat kṛṣṇāt mokṣam prāpya divam gataḥ śāpāt vimuktaḥ sadyas ca gajaḥ gandharva tām gataḥ grāhaḥ api yakṣa tām yātaḥ yaḥ kṛṣṇena nipātitaḥ tasya api śāpa mokṣaḥ asau jaigīṣavya kṛtaḥ abhavat prītimān trāti govindaḥ sadyas saṃsāra sāgarāt gandharva rāj tathā yakṣaḥ parām nirvṛtim āgatau dṛṣṭvā muktau gaja grahau bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ yaḥ grāham nāga rājam ca mām ca eva praṇidhānavān smariṣyati saraḥ ca idam yuvayoḥ mokṣaṇam tathā gulmam kīcaka veṇūnām tam ca śaila varam tathā aśvattham bhāskaram gaṅgām naimiṣa araṇyam eva ca saṃsmariṣyanti ye martyāḥ samyak śroṣyanti vā api ye sarva pāpaiḥ pramokṣyante kalyāṇānām ca bhāginaḥ bhaviṣyanti tathā puṇyām gatim yāsyanti mānavāḥ duḥsvapnam ca nṛṇām teṣām susvapnam ca bhaviṣyati kaurmam mātsyam ca vārāham vāmanam tārkṣyam eva ca nārasiṃham tathā rūpam sṛṣṭi saṃhāra kārakam etāni prātar utthāya saṃsmariṣyanti ye narāḥ aspṛśat gaja gandharvam grāha yakṣam ca tam tadā tena spṛṣṭau ubhau sadyas divya mālya ambara anvitau tatas devapatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ mokṣayitvā gaja uttamam ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamānaḥ hi guhyaiḥ veda pada akṣaraiḥ gataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ durvijñeya gatiḥ prabhuḥ gaja indra mokṣaṇam dṛṣṭvā sarve ca indra purogamāḥ brahmāṇam agratas kṛtvā sarve prāñjalayaḥ abhavan vavandire mahātmānam prabhum nārāyaṇam harim vismaya utphulla nayanāḥ prajāpati puraḥsarāḥ yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt nityam prātar utthāya mānavaḥ prāpnuyāt paramām siddhim duḥsvapnaḥ tasya naśyati śraddhayā hi kuruśreṣṭha smṛtena kathitena ca gaja indra mokṣaṇena iha dīrgham āyuḥ avāpnuyāt mayā te kathitam divyam pavitram pāpa nāśanam kīrtayasva mahā bāho mahā duḥsvapna nāśanam kīrtyamānam ca viprebhyaḥ śṛṇu bhaktyā yathā uditam gaja indra mokṣaṇam śrutvā kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīṣmāt bhagīrathī putrāt pūjayām āsa keśavam ye ca api pāṇḍu putrasya samīpa sthāḥ dvijottamāḥ te api bhīṣmasya pārśva stham vāsudevam praṇemire varam vareṇyam vara padmanābham nārāyaṇam brahma nidhim sureśam tam deva guhyam puruṣam purāṇam vavandire brahma vidām variṣṭham etat puṇyam mahā rāja narāṇām pāpa karmaṇām bhaktimān puṇḍarīkākṣe gajaḥ duḥkhāt vimocitaḥ mahāmate mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada śrīvatsa aṅkam jagadbījam anantam loka bhāvanam purā nārāyaṇam devam nāradaḥ paryapṛcchata kim vā japyam japet nityam kalyam utthāya mānavaḥ śrutvā tasya tu devarṣeḥ vākyam vākya viśāradaḥ provāca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ nāradam jagataḥ gatiḥ maraṇe yām anusmṛtya prāpnoti paramām gatim oṃkāram āditas kṛtvā mām anusmṛtya manmanāḥ avyaktam śāśvatam devam anantam puruṣottamam purāṇam paramam viṣṇum adbhutam loka bhāvanam prapadye puṇḍarīkākṣam īśam bhakta anukampinam sraṣṭāram sarva bhūtānām ananta bala pauruṣam padmanābham hṛṣīkeśam papadye satyam avyayam sahasraśirasam devam vaikuṇṭham tārkṣyavāhanam nārāyaṇam naram haṃsam yoga ātmānam sanātanam śaraṇyam sarva lokānām prapadye dhruvam īśvaram carācara guruḥ devaḥ sa naḥ viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu yasmāt jātaḥ purā brahmā padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ prasīdatu sa naḥ viṣṇuḥ pitā mātā pitāmahaḥ yaḥ purā pralaye prāpte naṣṭe loke carācare ekaḥ tiṣṭhati yoga ātmā sa naḥ viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu hūyate ca punar dvābhyām sa naḥ viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu parjanyaḥ pṛthivī sasyam kālaḥ dharmaḥ kriyā phalam guṇa ākaraḥ sa naḥ babhruḥ vāsudevaḥ prasīdatu ajeya khaṇḍaparaśo viśvamūrte vṛṣākape trigarte pañca kāla jña namaḥ te jñānasāgara avyaktāt aṇḍam utpannam avyakta ādyaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ yasmāt parataram na asti tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ niścayam na adhigacchanti tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ jita indriyāḥ mahātmānaḥ jñāna dhyāna parāyaṇāḥ yam prāpya na nivartante tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ eka aṃśena jagat sarvam yaḥ avaṣṭabhya vibhuḥ sthitaḥ agrāhyaḥ nirguṇaḥ śāstā tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ kṣetrajñam iti yam prāhuḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu āsthitaḥ prakṛtim bhuṅkte sa mahātmā prasīdatu kṣetrajñaḥ pañcadhā bhuṅkte prakṛtim bahubhiḥ guṇaiḥ manaḥ guṇān ca yaḥ bhuṅkte sa mahātmā prasīdatu sāṃkhyāḥ yogāḥ ca ye ca anye siddhāḥ ca eva mahā ṛṣayaḥ ye tu tvām na abhijānanti saṃsāre saṃsaranti te aśarīram śarīra stham samam sarveṣu dehiṣu avyaktam buddhi ahaṃkārau mahābhūta indriyāṇi ca tvayi tāni na teṣu tvam teṣu tvam tāni na tvayi sraṣṭā bhoktā asi kūṭasthaḥ guṇānām prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ bhaktānām yat hitam deva tat dhyāya tridaśeśvara ahaṃkāreṇa buddhyā vā tathā sattva ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ viṣayaiḥ indriyaiḥ vā api mā me bhūyāt samāgamaḥ pṛthivīm yātu me ghrāṇam yātu me rasanā jalam cakṣuḥ hutāśanam yātu sparśaḥ me yātu mārutam śabdaḥ hi ākāśam abhyetu manaḥ vaikārikam tathā pūrva deha kṛtāḥ ye me vyādhayaḥ te viśantu mām ārdayantu ca duḥkhāni pravimuñcāmi yat ṛṇam upatiṣṭhantu me rogāḥ ye mayā pūrva saṃcitāḥ anṛṇaḥ gantum icchāmi tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam tasya aham na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati imām anusmṛtim nityam vaiṣṇavīm pāpa nāśanīm api pāpa samācāraḥ saḥ api yāti parām gatim paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyām dvādaśyām ca viśeṣataḥ śrāvayet śraddadhānaḥ tu ye ca anye mām upāśritāḥ tasya syuḥ akṣayāḥ lokāḥ śvapākasya api nārada dhyāyanti ca yathānyāyam te yānti paramām gatim aśvamedha sahasrāṇām yaḥ sahasram samācaret iṣṭam dattam tapaḥ adhītam vratāni niyamāḥ ca ye sarvam etat vināśa antam jñānasya antaḥ na vidyate dāna ādīni antavanti iha mad bhaktaḥ na antam aśnute yaḥ dadyāt bhagavat jñānam kuryāt vā dharma deśanām kṛtsnām vā pṛthivīm dadyāt na tu tulyam kathaṃcana kāntāra vana durgeṣu kṛcchreṣu āpatsu saṃbhrame dasyubhiḥ saṃniruddhaḥ ca nāmabhiḥ mām prakīrtayet varāhaḥ rakṣatu jale viṣameṣu ca vāmanaḥ aṭavyām nārasiṃhaḥ tu sarvatas pātu keśavaḥ rāmaḥ rāmaḥ ca rāmaḥ ca trāyantām dasyu doṣataḥ janma antara sahasrāṇi tapaḥ jñāna samādhibhiḥ narāṇām kṣīṇa pāpānām kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate gatvā gatvā nivartane candra sūrya ādayaḥ grahāḥ adya api na nivartante dvādaśa akṣara cintakāḥ tasmāt mām eva deva ṛṣe dhyāyasva atandritaḥ sadā cakāra keśave bhaktim tasmāt tvam kuru bhūpate yaḥ paṭhet parayā bhaktyā sa gacchet viṣṇu sāmya tām etat puṇyam pāpa haram dhanyam duḥsvapna nāśanam pāpam praṇaśyate yena puṇyam yena vivardhate yat japan sugatim yāti śṛṇvan ca mama tat vada kaścid āsīt dvija drogdhā piśunaḥ kṣatriya adhamaḥ para pīḍā ruciḥ duṣṭaḥ svabhāvāt eva nirghṛṇaḥ paribhūtāḥ sadā tena pitṛ deva dvijātayaḥ para dāreṣu ca eva asya babhūva abhiratam manaḥ sa tu āyuṣi parikṣīṇe jajñe ghoraḥ niśācaraḥ tena vai karma doṣeṇa svena pāpa kṛtām varaḥ krūraiḥ eva tatas vṛttim rākṣasa tve viśeṣataḥ cakāra karmabhiḥ pāpaḥ sarva prāṇi vihiṃsakaḥ yat yat paśyati sattvam sa tat tat ādāya rākṣasaḥ evam tasya ati duṣṭasya kurvataḥ prāṇinām vadham jagāma su mahān kālaḥ pariṇāmam tathā vayaḥ ūrdhvabāhum mahābhāgam kṛta rakṣam samantataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sa tu durbuddhiḥ brāhmaṇam rākṣasa adhamaḥ samabhyadhāvat vegena samādātum cikhādiṣuḥ tena rakṣā ca yā dikṣu brāhmaṇena abhavat kṛtā tayā nirastam tat rakṣaḥ nipapāta avidūrataḥ bhagavan kīdṛśīm rakṣām sa cakāra dvijottamaḥ tapaḥ cacāra vipraḥ asau praviṣṭaḥ viṣṇu pañjaram viṣṇu pañjaram icchāmi śrotum dharma bhṛtām vara tripuram jaghnuṣaḥ pūrvam brahmaṇā viṣṇu pañjaraḥ śaṃkarasya kuru śreṣṭha rakṣaṇāya nirūpitaḥ vāgīśena tu śakrasya balam hantum prayāsyataḥ viṣṇuḥ prācyām sthitaḥ cakrī viṣṇuḥ dakṣiṇatas gadī pratīcyām śārṅgadhṛk viṣṇuḥ viṣṇuḥ khaḍgī mama uttare hṛṣīkeśaḥ vikoṇeṣu tad chidreṣu janārdanaḥ asya aṃśumālā duḥprekṣā hantu preta niśācarān gadā ca iyam sahasrārciḥ udvamat pāvaka ulvaṇā rakṣaḥ bhūta piśācānām ḍākiṇīnām ca nāśanī śārṅga visphūrjitam ca eva vāsudevasya mad ripūn tiryak manuṣya kūṣmāṇḍa preta ādīn hantu aśeṣatas khaḍga dhārā jvalat jyotsnā nirdhūtāḥ ye samāhatāḥ ye kūṣmāṇḍāḥ tathā yakṣāḥ ye daityāḥ ye niśācarāḥ pretāḥ vināyakāḥ krūrāḥ manuṣyāḥ jambhakāḥ khagāḥ siṃha ādayaḥ ye paśavaḥ dandasūkāḥ ca pannagāḥ sarve bhavantu te saumyāḥ kṛṣṇa śaṅkha rava āhatāḥ citta vṛtti harāḥ ye me ye janāḥ smṛti hārakāḥ bala ojasām ca hartāraḥ chāyā vibhraṃśakāḥ ca ye ye ca upabhoga hartāraḥ ye ca lakṣaṇa nāśakāḥ kūṣmāṇḍāḥ te praṇaśyantu viṣṇu cakra raya āhatāḥ pṛṣṭhe purastāt mama dakṣiṇa uttare vikoṇa gaḥ ca astu janārdanaḥ hariḥ tat īḍyam īśānam anantam īśvaram janārdanam praṇipatitaḥ na sīdati ṛtena tena acyuta nāma kīrtanāt praṇāśam etu trividham mama aśubham iti asau ātma rakṣā artham nyastavān viṣṇu pañjaram tena asādhyaḥ sa duṣṭānām babhūva nṛpa rakṣasām etayā ārakṣayā rakṣaḥ nirdhūtam bhuvi pātitam dṛṣṭvā ca kṛpayā āviṣṭaḥ samāśvāsya niśācaram papraccha āgamane hetum tam ca ācaṣṭa yathātatham prasīda vipra varya tvam nirviṇṇasya ati pāpinaḥ pāpa praśamanāya alam upadeśam prayaccha me bahūni pāpāni mayā kṛtāni bahavaḥ hatāḥ kṛtāḥ striyaḥ ca me bahvyaḥ vidhavāḥ hata putrikāḥ anāgasām ca sattvānām anekānām kṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ pāpasya asya kṣayam kartum kuru me dharma deśanām sahasā eva samāyātā jijñāsā dharma vartmani tvām attum āgataḥ kṣiptaḥ rakṣayā kṛtayā tvayā kā sā rakṣā na tām vedmi vedmi na asyāḥ parāyaṇam kiṃtu asyāḥ saṃgam āsādya nirvedam prāpitam param sa kṛpām kuru dharma jña mayi anukrośam āvaha pratyuvāca mahābhāga vimṛśya su ciram tadā yat tvam āttha upadeśa artham nirviṇṇaḥ svena karmaṇā yuktam etat na pāpānām nivṛtteḥ upakārakam kariṣye yātudhānānām na tu aham dharma deśanām tān tvam pṛccha dvijān saumya ye vai pravacane ratāḥ evam uktvā yayau vipraḥ cintām āpa ca rākṣasaḥ katham pāpa apanodaḥ syāt iti asau vyākula indriyaḥ na tadā khādate sattvān kṣudhā saṃpīḍitaḥ api san ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe tadā kāle jantum ekam abhakṣayat sa kadācid kṣudhā āviṣṭaḥ paryaṭan
