vipine vane dadarśa atha phala āhāram agratas kauśikam dvijam tam jagrāha ca bhakṣa artham ṣaṣṭhe kāle bubhukṣitaḥ guroḥ arthe phala āhāram āgatam brahmacāriṇam gṛhītaḥ rakṣasā tena sa tadā muni dārakaḥ nirāśaḥ jīvite prāha sāma pūrvam niśācaram ṣaṣṭhe kāle mama āhāraḥ kṣudhitasya tvam āgataḥ niḥśūkasya ati pāpasya nirghṛṇasya dvija druhaḥ yadi avaśyam tvayā adhyāham bhakṣaṇīyaḥ niśācara mama atra niṣṭhām prāptasya tat pāpāya niveditam sa tvam muhūrta mātram mām atra eva pratipālaya ṣaṣṭhe kāle na me brahman kaścid grahaṇam āgataḥ ekaḥ eva atra mokṣasya tava hetuḥ śṛṇuṣva tam mayā nisargataḥ brahman jāti doṣāt viśeṣataḥ ā bālyāt mama pāpeṣu na puṇyeṣu ratam manaḥ tad pāpa saṃcayāt mokṣam prāpnuyām yena tat vada yāni pāpāni karmāṇi bāla tvāt caritāni me duṣṭām yonim imām prāpya tad muktim kathaya dvija tat kṣudhā ārtāt sama ārtaḥ tvam niyatam mokṣam āpsyasi na ca etat pāpa śīlaḥ aham adya tvām kṣudh pipāsitaḥ ṣaṣṭhe kāle nṛśaṃsa ātmā bhakṣayiṣyāmi nirghṛṇaḥ vimṛśya su ciram vipraḥ śaraṇam jātavedasam jagāma jñāna dānāya saṃśayam paramam gataḥ yadi śuśrūṣitaḥ vahniḥ guroḥ śuśrūṣaṇāt anu vratāni vā su cīrṇāni saptārciḥ pātu mām tatas yathā aham avagacchāmi tathā mām pātu pāvakaḥ yathā gurum na manasā karmaṇā vacasā api vā avajānāmi aham tena pātu satyena pāvakaḥ saptārciṣā samādiṣṭā prādurāsīt sarasvatī sā ca uvāca dvija sutam rākṣasa grahaṇa ākulam mā bhaiḥ dvija sutā aham tvām mokṣayāmi ati saṃkaṭāt adṛśyā rakṣasā tena proktvā ittham tam sarasvatī adarśanam itā saḥ api dvijaḥ prāha niśācaram śrūyatām tava yat śreyaḥ tathā anyeṣām ca pāpinām prātar utthāya satatam madhyāhne ahnaḥ kṣaye api vā ayam śastaḥ sadā jāpaḥ sarva pāpa upaśānti daḥ harim kṛṣṇam hṛṣīkeśam vāsudevam janārdanam viśveśvaram ajam viṣṇum aprameya parākramam praṇataḥ asmi prajāpālam sa me pāpam vyapohatu viṣṇum acyutam īśānam anantam aparājitam praṇataḥ asmi mahātmānam sa me pāpam vyapohatu carācara gurum nātham govindam śeṣa śāyinam praṇataḥ asmi gadā pāṇim sa me pāpam vyapohatu śaṅkhinam cakriṇam śāntam śārṅgiṇam sraj dharam param praṇataḥ asmi patim lakṣmyāḥ sa me pāpam vyapohatu dāmodaram udāra akṣam puṇḍarīkākṣam avyayam nārāyaṇam naram śaurim mādhavam madhusūdanam praṇataḥ asmi dharādhāram sa me pāpam vyapohatu keśavam keśihantāram kaṃsa ariṣṭa niṣūdanam praṇataḥ asmi śriyaḥ kāntam sa me pāpam vyapohatu yam īśam sarva bhūtānām dhyāyanti yatayaḥ akṣaram vāsudevam anirdeśyam tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ dhyāyanti vāsudeva ākhyam tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ sarvagam sarva bhūtam ca sarvasya a dhātam īśvaram vāsudevam param brahma tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ karma kṣaye akṣayam devam tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ na yoginaḥ prāpnuvanti tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ brahmā bhūtvā jagat sarvam sa deva asura mānuṣam yaḥ sṛjati acyutaḥ devaḥ tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ sūtam prabho purā jajñe tam asmi śaraṇam gataḥ sraṣṭṛ tve saṃsthitam sṛṣṭau praṇataḥ asmi sanātanam yaḥ pāti sṛṣṭam ca vibhuḥ sthitau asurasūdanaḥ tam ādipuruṣam viṣṇum praṇataḥ asmi sanātanam dhṛtā mahī hatā daityāḥ paritrātāḥ tathā amarāḥ yena tam viṣṇum ādya īśam praṇataḥ asmi sanātanam yajñaiḥ yajanti yam viprāḥ yajñeśam yajña bhāvanam tam yajñapuruṣam viṣṇum praṇataḥ asmi sanātanam varṇa āśramān sthitau ādyaḥ yaḥ sthāpayati vartmani tam ādipuruṣam viṣṇum praṇataḥ asmi sanātanam tam ādipuruṣam viṣṇum praṇataḥ asmi janārdanam pātāla vīthī bhūḥ ādīn tathā lokān bibharti yaḥ tam antapuruṣam viṣṇum praṇataḥ asmi janārdanam saṃbhakṣayitvā sakalam yathā sṛṣṭam idam jagat sura asurāḥ pitṛ gaṇāḥ yakṣa gandharva rākṣasāḥ yasya aṃśa bhūtāḥ devasya sarvagam tam namāmi aham samasta devāḥ sakalāḥ mānuṣāṇām ca jātayaḥ yasya aṃśa bhūtāḥ devasya sarvagam tam namāmi aham vṛkṣa gulma ādayaḥ yasya tathā paśu mṛga ādayaḥ eka aṃśa bhūtāḥ devasya sarvagam tam namāmi aham yathā sarveṣu bhūteṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca viṣṇuḥ eva tathā pāpam mama aśeṣam praṇaśyatu yat ca jñāna paricchedyam pāpam naśyatu me tathā pravṛttam ca nivṛttam ca karma viṣṇu mayam yathā yat niśāyām tathā prātar yat ca madhya aparāhṇayoḥ saṃdhyayoḥ ca kṛtam pāpam karmaṇā manasā girā tiṣṭhatā vrajatā yat ca śayyā āsana gatena ca kṛtam yat aśubham karma kāyena manasā girā ajñānataḥ jñānataḥ vā vāsudevasya kīrtanāt tat sarvam vilayam yātu toya stham lavaṇam yathā paripīḍā udbhavam nindām kurvataḥ yat mahātmanām yat ca bhojye tathā peye yat ca kaṇḍūyana ādiṣu viṣṇave vāsudevāya haraye keśavāya ca janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya namaḥ bhūyas namaḥ namaḥ idam sārasvatam stotram aśeṣa agha vināśanam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva sarva pāpa vināśanam idam yaḥ prātar utthāya praṇipatya janārdanam yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram pūrṇam sāyam prātar samāhitaḥ japati etat naraḥ puṇyam kṛtvā manasi keśavam śārīram mānasam vāc jam jñānataḥ ajñānataḥ api vā kṛtam tena tu yat pāpam sapta janmāntarāṇi vai mahāpātakam alpam vā tathā yat ca upapātakam viprāya su viśiṣṭāya tila pātrāṇi ṣoḍaśa avipluta matiḥ ca ante saṃprāpya smaraṇam hareḥ yathā enam paṭhati nityam stavam sārasvatam pumān api pāpa samāyuktaḥ mokṣam prāpnoti asau api rākṣasa grasta sarva aṅgam tathā mām eṣa muñcatu etat bhadra mukha ākhyātam tava pātaka nāśanam viṣṇoḥ sārasvatam stotram yat jagāda sarasvatī hutāśanena prahitā mama jihvā agra saṃsthitā jagāda imam stavam viṣṇoḥ sarva pāpa praśānti dam tatas pāpa apanodam tu stute prāpsyasi keśave aharniśam hṛṣīkeśam stavena anena rākṣasa stauhi bhaktim parām kṛtvā tatas pāpāt vimokṣyase stutaḥ hi sarva pāpāni nāśayiṣyati asaṃśayam bhaktyā rākṣasa śārdūla sarva pāpa haraḥ hariḥ tatas praṇamya tam vipram prasādya ca niśācaraḥ śālagrāmam mahā rāja tadā eva tapase yayau deva kriyā ratiḥ bhūtvā tapaḥ tepe sa rākṣasaḥ tathā tvam api rājarṣe sarva pāpa praśānti dam ārādhaya hṛṣīkeśam japan sārasvatam stavam brahman asāre saṃsāre roga ādi vyāpta mānasaḥ śabda ādi lubdhaḥ puruṣaḥ kim kurvan na avasīdati śoka moha vinirmuktam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati a prāṇa citikam brahma vedānteṣu prakāśitam ādyam puruṣam īśānam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati aśanā ādyaiḥ a saṃspṛṣṭam sevitam yogibhiḥ sadā sarva doṣa vinirmuktam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati niṣkalam śāśvatam devam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati abhayam satya saṃkalpam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati amṛtam sādhanam sādhyam yam paśyanti manīṣiṇaḥ jñeya ākhyam paramātmānam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati atulam sukha dharmāṇam vyoma deham sanātanam dharma adharma vinirmuktam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati vyāsa ādyaiḥ munibhiḥ sarvaiḥ dhyāna yoga parāyaṇaiḥ arcitam bhāva kusumaiḥ viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati viṣṇu aṣṭakam idam puṇyam yoginām prīti vardhanam yaḥ paṭhet parayā prītyā sa gacchet viṣṇu sātmya tām etat puṇyam pāpa haram dhanyam duḥsvapna nāśanam paṭhatām śṛṇvatām ca eva viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam uttamam kurvan bhaktim hṛṣīkeśe mānavaḥ bhṛgu nandana nirvāṇam samavāpnoti yādṛśam tat vadasva me tasya api karma abhiratāḥ duḥkha bhājaḥ katham narāḥ kaiḥ ca dānaiḥ jagat svāmī svāmī nārāyaṇaḥ nṛṇām upakārāya bhaktānām jāyate sa mahā mune tvad yuktaḥ ayam anupraśnaḥ mahā rāja śṛṇuṣva tam yathā pṛṣṭam idam samyak kathyamānam yathākhilam pṛthivīm ratna saṃpūrṇām yaḥ kṛṣṇāya prayacchati śrūyate ca purā ākhyātaḥ rājā uparicaraḥ vasuḥ iyāja su bahūn yajñān śraddhā pūtena cetasā sa vipra śāpāt rājarṣiḥ kasmiṃścid kāraṇa antare ākāśa cārī sahasā praviveśa rasātalam devānām eṣa yajña aṃśaiḥ yajvī pakṣa vivardhanaḥ cedi rāj iti daityānām matiḥ āsīt rasātale iti saṃmantrya te daityāḥ cedi rāja jighāṃsavaḥ tad samīpam anuprāptāḥ gṛhīta vividha āyudhāḥ sa ca api vasuḥ āsīnaḥ keśava arpita mānasaḥ jajāpa mantram oṃkāram praṇavam dvādaśa akṣaram dadarśa ca sa viśveśam dhyāna avasthita mānasaḥ prāk īśam akṣaram dhyānam jñānam jñeyam jagadgurum saṃcintya vāsudeva ākhyam anirdeśyam parāyaṇam brahma viṣṇu śivānām ca svarūpaiḥ saṃsthitam tridhā sthāvara anteṣu bhūteṣu sarveṣu eva samāsthitam dikṣu ambara dharā bhūbhṛt toya vāyu anala ādiṣu dṛśya adṛśyeṣu ca eva īśam cintayām āsa pārthivaḥ sarvam ca tanmayam dṛṣṭvā virarāma samādhitaḥ indriyāṇi indriya artheṣu pūrvavat sa narādhipaḥ tān sa dṛṣṭvā gṛhīta arghyaḥ ekaikasya eva pārthivaḥ pādya pūrveṇa vidhinā pūjayām āsa bhaktimān prasādam kuru bhadram vaḥ bhagavān jagataḥ patiḥ vāsudevaḥ bhavān prāptaḥ mama anugraha kāmyayā pūjayām āsa pādya ādi nivedya vacasā tathā te api tam cedi rājānam papracchuḥ asurāḥ tadā kva vāsudevaḥ atra vayam prāptāḥ dākṣāyaṇī sutāḥ praṇāma namraḥ rāja indra sarva darśī mahāmatiḥ brahma ādiṣu tṛṇa anteṣu saḥ eva ekaḥ jagadguruḥ aham bhavantaḥ deva ādyāḥ manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ ca ye tena eva māyā vitatā vaiṣṇavī bhinna darśanī tayā sva aṅgeṣu devaḥ asau pradarśayati sarvaśas tatas purohitam sarve kāvyam nīti viśāradam asmad pakṣa kṣayāya eṣa devānām pakṣa vardhanaḥ sva gocaram ariḥ prāptaḥ śatru pakṣa upakārakaḥ tasmāt pragṛhya divyāni sarva astrāṇi amara ardanāḥ kṛtam na śakitaḥ hantum niryatnaḥ api hi pārthivaḥ tapasaḥ vā muni śreṣṭha vistarāt tat vadasva naḥ sā asya rakṣā parā manye kaḥ hinasti acyuta āśrayam kīrtitaḥ saṃsmṛtaḥ dhyātaḥ pūjitaḥ saṃstutaḥ tathā aihika āmuṣmikīm rakṣām karoti bhagavān hariḥ śarīra ārogyam arthān ca bhogān ca eva ānuṣaṅgikān yat idam cedi rājānam hantum icchatha dānavāḥ tat asya keśavāt cittam upāyena apanīyatām tatas te tad vacaḥ śrutvā dānavāḥ kuru puṅgava dadṛśuḥ te mahātmānam praṇatam cedi puṅgavam kṛta pūjam jagaddhātuḥ vāsudevasya pārthivam saṃstutau udyatam śāntam sarvatra sama darśinam kṛṣṇa arpita manovṛttim jānubhyām avaniṃgatam tatas saṃśṛṇvatām teṣām tuṣṭāva madhusūdanam tad nāma smaraṇa udbhūta pulakaḥ cedi puṅgavaḥ jagāda yam sa rājarṣiḥ stavam kṛṣṇasya śaunaka śṛṇvatām dānava indrāṇām tat me pāpa haram vada śṛṇu yat devadevasya viṣṇoḥ adbhuta karmaṇaḥ stotram jagāda rājā asau rasātala talam gataḥ a vṛddhi kṣayam īśānam acyutam paratas param kalpanā kṛta nāmānam anirdeśyam ajam vibhum mūla hetum ahetum tvām vāsudevam namāmi aham parama artha paraiḥ īśaḥ cintyate yaḥ prajākaraiḥ tam vāsudevam īśa īśam namāmi adya guṇam param jñeyam jñātāram ajaram bhoktāram prakṛteḥ prabhum puruṣa svarūpiṇam devam nataḥ asmi puruṣam param pradhāna ādi viśeṣa anta svarūpam ajam avyayam sthūla sūkṣma mayam sarvam vyāpinam tam namāmi aham sraṣṭā pālayitā ca ante yaḥ ca saṃhāra kārakaḥ trayī mayam tam triguṇam nataḥ asmi puruṣottamam vyakta rūpī ca tam devam nataḥ aham viṣṇum avyayam tava agniḥ āsam vasudhā aṅghri yugmam nabhaḥ śiraḥ candra ravī ca netre namaḥ hṛṣīkeśa tava aprameya namaḥ ca tubhyam parama artha sāra viṣṇo namaḥ te astu parāpara īśa kṛṣṇa acyuta ananta jagannivāsa saṃhṛtya viśvam jalaśāyine namaḥ namaḥ ca te kaiṭabhasūdanāya rudrāya ca ante kṣaya hetave te nataḥ asmi saṃhāra karāya viṣṇo jitam jita akṣa amala citta dṛśya carācara ādhāra dharādhara īḍya yajña āśrayaḥ yajña pumān aśeṣa deveśa martya asura yajña bhoktaḥ tvam īḍyamānaḥ abhimatam dadāsi dharādhara īśa acyuta vāsudeva kṛṣṇa acyuta hṛṣīkeśa sarva bhūta īśa keśava mahātman trāhi mām bhaktam vāsudeva prasīda me iti stotra avasāne tam cedi rājam tatas asurāḥ jahasuḥ sa tala ākṣepam procuḥ ca dvija rūpiṇaḥ prājñaḥ kila prajāpālaḥ cedi rāj saṃśrutaḥ bhuvi tas asya jñānam akhilam viparīta artham īdṛśam kva vāsudevaḥ kva bhavān imām antyām daśām gataḥ yaḥ bhavān vipra śāpena rasātala tala āśrayaḥ bhaviṣyati smṛtaḥ devaḥ trātā kila tava acyutaḥ yaḥ anyatras trāṇa kāmaḥ vā yajña bhāgam abhīpsate yadā tvam bhagavat bhaktaḥ vipra śāpāt nipātitaḥ śāpam dadatsu vipreṣu paritrāṇa paraḥ bhavet na vayam puṇḍarīkākṣam na anantam na acyutam harim saṃśritāḥ na ca sīdāmaḥ sva pauruṣam upāśritāḥ tat āśrayasva svam vīryam parityajya vimūḍha tām iti udīritam ākarṇya sa teṣām cedi puṅgavaḥ ajñāna paṭala channān hṛdayena śuśoca tān yena sarva īśvare viṣṇau eteṣām āvṛtā matiḥ prakāśam ca sa tān āha dānavān prīti pūrvakam pāpataḥ tad paritrāṇam cikīrṣuḥ vasudhādhipaḥ saṃsāra abdhau manuṣyāṇām ekaḥ potaḥ janārdanaḥ sukha duḥkha mayaḥ nR̥ṇām vipākaḥ karmaṇām ca yaḥ parīkṣām ca jagannāthaḥ karoti adṛḍha cetasām narāṇām artha vidhvaṃsa nikāśeṣu janārdanaḥ alpa yatnena ca āyānti vimuktim keśava āśrayāt yadā janārdane bhaktim vahan sīdati mānavaḥ nirviṇṇa cetāḥ śaithilyam manasaḥ kurute tadā devānām mahatī śaṅkā bhakti yuktā janārdane satyam śatena vighnānām sahasreṇa tathā tapaḥ svam ca api karma puruṣaḥ śubha aśubham upāgatam maryādām ca kṛtām tena yaḥ bhinatti sa mānavaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ devadevena mukhāt sṛṣṭāḥ mahātmanā devānām api saṃpūjya bhūmidevāḥ dvijottamāḥ anuvṛttiḥ sadā kāryā teṣām varṇaiḥ anuvrataiḥ te pūjyāḥ te namaskāryāḥ toṣaṇīyāḥ ca yatnataḥ teṣu tuṣṭeṣu aśeṣāṇām devānām prītiḥ uttamā teṣām mayā yat ajñānāt jñānāt vā kṛtam apriyam tena api tuṣṭaḥ eva aham viṣṇoḥ aṃśāḥ dvijottamāḥ kriyāvān mama potaḥ ayam bhū talāt yaḥ rasātale rasātala tala uttāram na hi vāñchāmi aham dvijāḥ saṃsāra gartāt uttāram vṛṇomi ārādhanāt dhareḥ yathā aham na abhivāñchāmi bhogān ārādhya keśavam yathā na mātā na pitā na ātmā na suhṛdaḥ sutāḥ kṛṣṇa ālāpāt priyatarāḥ tathā mām pātu keśavaḥ yathā viṣṇu mayam sarvam etat paśyāmi aham jagat tathā mama manaḥ doṣān aśeṣān sa vyapohatu jātā viṣṇu vilomeṣu bhavatsu api dayā mama yathā na aham bhavat dveṣāt na saṃharṣāt bravīmi aham evam uccārite teṣām daityānām tad kṣaṇāt tathā sva rūpa dhāriṇaḥ ca enam praṇamya asura puṅgavāḥ pratyūcuḥ pārthivam viṣṇu bhaktam sat brahmacāriṇam saṃsāre tvad samaiḥ saṅgaḥ puṇya bhājām pravartate vayam sva jāti doṣeṇa deva pakṣa virodhinaḥ vaiphalyam ati puṇyeṣu viṣṇu śuśrūṣaṇā nṛṇām diṣṭyā krodha abhibhūtānām asmākam tvad nivarhaṇe matiḥ jātā yatas prāptā tvad saṅgāt durlabhā matiḥ kuruṣva ca prasādam tvam praṇatānām nareśvara śatrau api kṛpā śīlam yat naḥ duṣṭam abhūt manaḥ diśām vaimalyam vimalam cakṣuṣaḥ ca upapāditam bhavatā duṣṭa tām etām āsurīm apamārjatā duṣṭāḥ sma varṣa pūgāni yat yātāni vṛthā eva naḥ viṣaya ākṣipta cittānām kṛṣṇe bhaktim a kurvatām karma bhūmau manuṣyāṇām tat eva viphalam dinam yat acyuta kathā ālāpa dhyāna arcā rahitam gatam iti uktvā te asurāḥ bhūyas prasādya ca tathā vasum viṣṇau bhakti parāḥ yātāḥ tīvra saṃyoginaḥ alayan sa ca api cedi rāj tasmāt devadevena cakriṇā pātālāt uddhṛtaḥ paścāt saṃsāra gahanāt api iti etat sarvam ākhyātam yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi dṛḍhā janārdane bhaktiḥ yadā evā avyabhicāriṇī iti etat asuraiḥ sārdham saṃvādam yaḥ purā vasoḥ praṇipatya aham etam tvām yat pṛcchāmi tat ucyatām yaiḥ upāyaiḥ pradānaiḥ vā narāṇām amara arcitaḥ prītimān puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ bhavati ācakṣva tat mama vidharmeṣu na vartante prītimān teṣu keśavaḥ brahmacāri gṛhastha ādyāḥ na cyavanti āśramāt ca ye svadharmataḥ hariḥ teṣām prītimān eva sarvadā tyakta grāmya ādi saṃgāḥ ca teṣu prītiḥ parā hareḥ dātāraḥ na apahartāraḥ para svānām amāyinaḥ ye narāḥ teṣu govindaḥ putreṣu iva sadā hitaḥ yeṣām narāṇām na matiḥ jihvā vāsatyam ujjhati te priyāḥ vāsudevasya ye ca dvija parāyaṇāḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā ye na hiṃsā anuvartinaḥ te narāḥ vāsudevasya priyāḥ pāṇḍu kula udvaha brahma ādyam sthāvara antam ca bhūta grāmam janārdanāt ye ca paśyanti abhedena te viṣṇoḥ satatam priyāḥ deva veda dvijātīnām nindāyām ye na mānavāḥ prīti bhājaḥ bhavanti iṣṭāḥ te sadā śārṅgadhanvinaḥ priyāṇām atha sarveṣām devadevasya sa priyaḥ tasmāt priya tvam kṛṣṇasya vāñchatā nija dharma jaiḥ guṇaiḥ ātmā sadā yojyaḥ na dūre guṇinaḥ hariḥ yeṣām na gṛddhiḥ pārakye dāre dravye ca cetasaḥ hiṃsāyām ca manuṣyāṇām te kṛṣṇena avalokitāḥ vedāḥ pramāṇam smṛtayaḥ yeṣām sat mārga sevinām para upakāra saktānām te kṛṣṇena avalokitāḥ kali kalmaṣa doṣeṇa yeṣām nā upahatā matiḥ pāṣaṇḍa anugatāḥ na eva te kṛṣṇena avalokitāḥ na vivitsā samudbhūtaḥ te kṛṣṇena avalokitāḥ svapantaḥ saṃsthitāḥ yāntaḥ tiṣṭhantaḥ ca janārdanam ye cintayanti aviratam te kṛṣṇena avalokitāḥ yathā ātmani tathā apatye yeṣām a drohiṇī matiḥ samasta sattva jāteṣu te kṛṣṇena avalokitāḥ ye kurvanti narāḥ viddhi te kṛṣṇena avalokitāḥ devān pitR̥n tathā āpannān atithīn jāmayaḥ adhvagān tam vijānīhi bhartavyam devadevasya śārṅginaḥ kurvan ālakṣya tām eti keśavena avalokitaḥ na ātma saṃstavam anyeṣām na nindām ca artha lipsayā karoti puruṣa vyāghra yasya nārāyaṇaḥ hṛdi sarva bhūta dayām satyam akrodham dharma śīla tām narāṇām jāyate rājan govinde hṛdaya sthite kṣamām karoti kruddheṣu dayām mūḍheṣu mānavaḥ tadā kuru vara śreṣṭha naraḥ kṛṣṇena vīkṣitaḥ putra dāra gṛha kṣetra dravya ādeḥ mamatām naraḥ na āyāsyati jagannāthe hṛṣīkeśe parāṅmukhe kalau kṛta yugam teṣām kleśāḥ teṣām sukha adhikāḥ yeṣām śarīra grahaṇe hari śuśrūṣaṇe matiḥ yadā na icchati pāpāni yadā puṇyāni vāñchati jñeyaḥ tadā manuṣyeṇa hṛdaye asya hariḥ sthitaḥ parama arthe matiḥ puṃsām asāre tu bhava arṇave śraddadhānaḥ dayā śīlaḥ sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ parārthe mānavaḥ kṛṣṇe prasanne nṛpa jāyate vahataḥ api sadā kṛṣṇe bhaktim avyabhicāriṇīm pāṇiṣu asamadṛś buddheḥ sulabhaḥ nā eva keśavaḥ kāma lobha āśritam yeṣām cittam krodha ādi dūṣitam teṣām janma sahasre api na matiḥ keśava āśrayā heyām kṛṣṇa āśrayām vṛttim manyante hetu saṃśritāḥ aviyā upahata jñānāḥ ye ajñāne jñāna māninaḥ veda vāda virodhena kūṭayuktim apāśritāḥ mānuṣam tam manuṣya tve manyamānāḥ ku buddhayaḥ karmāṇi ye asya nindanti na teṣām niṣkṛtiḥ nṛṇām tiryaktvam ca apare viṣṇum māyayā tasya mohitāḥ deva tvam api kṛṣṇasya yasya nindā mahātmanaḥ stutim tasya katham śaktāḥ kartum īśasya mānavāḥ vyāpi tvam śāśvata tvam ca janma bhāva vivarjitam sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ procyate yadi paṇḍitaḥ nindā api tasya na nṛbhiḥ kartum īśasya śakyate yadā kāṇāḥ ca kūṇṭhāḥ ca mūḍhaḥ durbuddhiḥ āturaḥ sraṣṭā pālayitā hartā jagataḥ asya jagat ca saḥ yaṣṭā yājayitā yājyaḥ saḥ eva bhagavān hariḥ dātā dānam tathā adātā kartā kāryam tathā kriyāḥ hantā ghātayitā hiṃsyaḥ hāryam hartā ca yaḥ svayam sarva kāraṇa bhūtasya tasya īśasya mahātmanaḥ kaḥ karoti stutim viṣṇoḥ nindām vā pṛthivīpate śakyate sarva bhūta tvāt cokṣa acokṣa svarūpiṇā stuteḥ pādāt yatas na anyat utkṛṣṭam upalabhyate tasya api uccāraṇena īśaḥ na stotum śakyate hariḥ yatas atas sarva bhūtasya kā nindā tasya kā stutiḥ yena sarva ātmanā tatra hṛdayam saṃniveśitam kuru viṣṇum ca hṛdaye sarva vyāpinam īśvaram viṣṇoḥ evam priya tvam tvam āśu yāsyasi pārthiva tam īśvara īśvaram viṣṇum hṛdaye saṃniveśaya tam īśvara īśvaram viṣṇum hṛdaye kuru pārthiva eṣa śāstra artha sadbhāvaḥ kim uktaiḥ bahu vistaraiḥ tam tam cintaya govindam manasaḥ sthairya kāraṇāt yathā agni saṃgāt kanakam apadoṣam prajāyate saṃśliṣṭam vāsudevena manuṣyāṇām tathā manaḥ bhūyas ca śṛṇu rāja indra yat jagāda janārdanaḥ nāga paryaṅka śayane pṛṣṭaḥ kṣīrābdhikanyayā purā śayānam govindam prāvṛṣ kāle mahā udadhau śeṣa bhogi mahā bhoge vīci ambu kaṇa śītale śrīvatsa vkṣasam lakṣmīḥ kara saṃvāhana ādṛtā an anya āsakta dṛṣṭim ca kim api ekāgra mānasam papraccha puṇḍarīkākṣam puṇḍarīka karāḥ harim sṛṣṭam jagat idam sarvam bahuśas ca upasaṃhṛtam devān manuṣyān gandharvān yakṣa vidyādhara asurān sṛṣṭvā sṛṣṭān nirghṛṇa tvāt upasaṃharate bhavān kaścid eteṣu bhūteṣu deva ādiṣu tava acyuta tathā api guṇa gṛhyaḥ aham pratyeka hṛdaya sthitaḥ puṇya apuṇya kṛtau teṣu prīti dveṣau śubhe mama dveṣa anubhāvena apuṇyam phala dam teṣu bhāmini śrūyatām ca mahābhāge nareṣu śubha cāriṣu satatam yeṣu me prītiḥ tathā aprītiḥ varānane pralaya utpatti tattva jñāḥ ātma jñāna parāḥ ca ye ete sva karmaṇā bhadre mama prīti patham gatāḥ vāc manaḥ kāyikīm hiṃsām ye na kurvanti kutracid svakīya dravya saṃtuṣṭāḥ nivṛttāḥ caurya karmaṇaḥ satya śīla dayā yuktāḥ narāḥ mama sadā priyāḥ mātṛ svasṛ sutā tulyān para dārān ca ye narāḥ manyante te ca me lakṣmi dṛḍham priyatamāḥ sadā na kāmāt na ca saṃrambhāt na dveṣāt ye ca bhāmini viśvāsyāḥ sarva bhūtānām ahiṃsrāḥ ca dayālavaḥ tyakta anṛta kathāḥ devi manuṣyāḥ dayitāḥ mama dharma labdhān tu ye bhogān bhuñjate na ati kīkaṭāḥ yeṣām matiḥ manuṣyāṇām te atīva dayitāḥ mama dharma labdheṣu dāreṣu ṛtu kāla abhigāminaḥ para randhreṣu jātyandhāḥ paradāreṣu apuṃsakāḥ para apavāde ye mūkāḥ dayitāḥ te narāḥ mama para apavādam nindām ca para marma avaghaṭṭanam satyām ślakṣṇām nirābādhām madhurām prīti dāyinīm ye vācam īrayanti sma te manuṣyāḥ mama priyāḥ sākṣāt devam iva āyāntam yā patim nityam arcati pāda śauca ādibhiḥ nārī tasyāḥ na aham su durlabhaḥ pūrṇa candram iva udyatam bhartāram yā gṛha āgatam hṛṣṭā paśyati tām viddhi dayitām yoṣitam mama śruti smṛti uditam dharmam manasā api na ye narāḥ brahma rūpa dharasya āsyāt mama vedāḥ viniḥsṛtāḥ manu ādi rūpiṇaḥ ca eva samastāḥ smṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ mama eva ājñā tām ullaṅghya yajet śubhe sarva svena api mām devi na āpnoti ājñā vighāta kṛt etat devi mayā ākhyātam yat pṛṣṭaḥ aham iha tvayā priyāṇām mama sarveṣām śṛṇu yaḥ atitaram priyaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ ca varavarṇini vāc manaḥ karmabhiḥ śāntaḥ dayitaḥ satatam mama evam śrīḥ devadevena prāk uktā harimedhasā tava api hi nara śreṣṭha yathāvat kathitam mayā yaḥ śṛṇoti sa pāpebhyaḥ samastebhyaḥ pramucyate samyak ārādhanāya alam kriyā yogam bravīhi me yat phalam keśavasya arcām pratiṣṭhāpya labhet naraḥ yat ca devakulam viṣṇoḥ kārayitvā phalam labhet yat dīpa dhūpa puṣpāṇām gandhānām ca nivedane dhvaja ādi dāne yat puṇyam yat puṇyam gīta vādite tathā pavitra paṭhane jaya śabda ādi udīraṇe saṃmārjana ādau yat puṇyam namaskāre pradakṣiṇe śīrṇa sphuṭita saṃskāra karaṇe ca api yat phalam teṣām phalam ca yat kṛtsnam tat mama ācakṣva vistarāt saṃkṣepāt pūrvam eva etat bhavataḥ kathitam mayā vistareṇa mahā rāja śrūyatām bruvataḥ mama aditiḥ nāma devānām mātā parama duścaram tapaḥ cacāra varṣāṇām sahasram pṛthivīpate ārādhanāya kṛṣṇasya vāgyatā vāyu bhojanā daityaiḥ nirākṛtān dṛṣṭvā tanayān kuru nandana vṛthāputrā aham asmi iti nirvedāt praṇatāḥ harim tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ parama artha avabodhinī deva daitya nṛpa śvāpa vyoma vāyu ādi rūpiṇam śaraṇyam śaraṇam viṣṇum praṇatāḥ bhakta vatsalam namaḥ smṛta ārti nāśāya namaḥ puṣkara māline namaḥ parama kalyāṇa kalyāṇāya ādivedhase namaḥ paṅkaja netrāya namaḥ paṅkaja nābhaye namaḥ paṅkaja saṃbhūti saṃbhavāya ātmayonaye śriyaḥ kāntāya dāntāya dānta dṛśyāya cakriṇe namaḥ śaṅkha asi hastāya namaḥ kanaka retase tathā ātma jñāna vijñāna yoga citta ātma yogine nirguṇāya viśeṣāya haraye brahma rūpiṇe jagat pratiṣṭhitam yatra jagatā yaḥ na dṛśyate namaḥ sthūla ati sūkṣmāya tasmai devāya śaṅkhine ādyaḥ prajāpati patiḥ yaḥ pitR̥ṇām paraḥ patiḥ patiḥ surāṇām yaḥ tasmai namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase yaḥ cintyamānaḥ manasā sadyas pāpam vyapohati yam praviśya akhila ādhāram īśānam ajam avyayam tam yajñapuruṣam viṣṇum namāmi prabhum īśvaram yaḥ tasmai veda vedyāya viṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ yatas viśvam samudbhūtam yasmin ca layam eṣyati māyām na alam samuttartum tam upendram namāmi aham yam ārādhya viśuddhena manasā karmaṇā girā viṣāda toṣa roṣa ādyaiḥ yaḥ ajasram sukha duḥkha jaiḥ viśvam viśvapatim viṣṇum tam namāmi prajāpatim rātri jam sūrya rūpī ca tam upendram namāmi aham kapila ādi svarūpa sthaḥ yaḥ ca ajñāna mayam tamaḥ yasya akṣiṇī candra sūryau sarva loka śubha aśubham na anṛtam tam ajam viṣṇum namāmi prabhava avyayam satyena tena sakalāḥ pūryantām me manorathāḥ adṛśyaḥ sarva bhūtānām tasyāḥ saṃdarśane sthitaḥ tān rājyam na duḥkhāya mama putrasya keśava sapatnāt āyati bhraṃśaḥ bādhām naḥ kurute hṛdi sva aṃśena ca eva te garbhe saṃbhaviṣyāmi kaśyapāt tān aham nihaniṣyāmi nirvṛtā bhava nandini na aham tvām udareṇa īśa voḍhum śakṣyāmi keśava yasmin pratiṣṭhitam viśvam yaḥ viśvam svayam īśvara tat aham na udareṇa tvām voḍhum śakṣyāmi durdharam pratiṣṭhitam na mām śaktāḥ voḍhum sa indrāḥ divaukasaḥ kintu aham sakalān lokān sa deva asura mānuṣān jaṅgama ajaṅgamam sarvam tvām ca devi sa kāśyapām dākṣāyaṇi prasādam te karomi anyaiḥ su durlabham tejasaḥ tasya hānim ca kariṣye mā vyathām kṛtāḥ evam uktvā tatas sadyas gataḥ antardhānam īśvaraḥ garbha sthite tatas kṛṣṇe cacāla sakalā kṣitiḥ cakampire mahā śailāḥ jagmuḥ kṣobham atha abdhayaḥ tatas tatas kṣitiḥ khedāt nanāma vasudhādhipa babhūva tejasaḥ hāniḥ yathā uktam parameṣṭhinā nistejasaḥ asurān dṛṣṭvā samastān asura īśvaraḥ duriṣṭam kim nu daityānām kim kṛtyā vairi nirmitā nāśāya eṣām samudbhūtāḥ yena nistejasaḥ asurāḥ iti āsura varaḥ tena pṛṣṭaḥ pautreṇa pārthiva ciram dhyātvā jagāda idam asura indram tadā balim sadyas samudrāḥ kṣubhitāḥ daityāḥ nistejasaḥ kṛtāḥ sūrya ādayaḥ yathā pūrvam tathā gacchanti na grahāḥ devānām ca parā lakṣmīḥ kāraṇaiḥ anumīyate mahat etat mahā bāho kāraṇam dānava īśvara iti uktvā dānava patim prahrādaḥ saḥ asura uttamaḥ sa dhyāna patha gam kṛtvā prahrādaḥ svam manaḥ asuraḥ sa dadarśa udare adityāḥ prahrādaḥ vāmana ākṛtim sādhyān viśve tathā ādityān gandharva uraga rākṣasān jambham kujambham narakam bāṇam anyān tathā asurān ātmānam urvī gaganam vāyum ambhaḥ hutāśanam samudra adri druma sarit sarāṃsi paśavaḥ mṛgān vayaḥ manuṣyān akhilān tathā eva ca sarīsṛpān samasta loka sraṣṭāram brahmāṇam bhavam eva ca graha nakṣatra tārāḥ ca dakṣa ādyān ca prajāpatīn saṃpaśyan vismaya āviṣṭaḥ prakṛti sthaḥ kṣaṇāt punar prahrādaḥ prāha daitya indram balim vairocanim tadā vatsa jñātam mayā sarvam yad artham bhavatām iyam tejasaḥ hāniḥ utpannā tat śṛṇu tvam aśeṣatas para aparāṇām paramaḥ paraḥ paravatām api prabhuḥ pramāṇam mānānām saptaloka guroḥ guruḥ sthitim kartum jagannāthaḥ saḥ adityāḥ garbha tām gataḥ prabhuḥ prabhūṇām paramaḥ parāṇām an ādi madhyaḥ bhagavān anantaḥ trailokyam aṃśena
