manaḥ nivāsaḥ sa vāsudevaḥ kalayā avatīrṇaḥ yam akṣaram veda vidaḥ viditvā viśanti tam jñāna vidhūta pāpāḥ vijñāyate sarva pitāmaha ādyaiḥ tam vāsudevam praṇamāmi acintyam rūpasya cakṣuḥ grahaṇe tvac eṣā sparśa grahītrī rasanā rasasya śrotram ca śabda grahaṇe narāṇām ghrāṇam ca gandha grahaṇe niyuktam na ghrāṇa cakṣuḥ śravaṇa ādibhiḥ yaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ veditum avyaya ātmā śakyaḥ tam īḍyam manasā eva devam grāhyam nataḥ aham harim īśitāram yena eka daṃṣṭra agra samuddhṛtā iyam dharā acalā dhārayati iha sarvam grastvā sa śete sakalam jagat yaḥ tam īḍyam īśam praṇataḥ asmi viṣṇum aṃśa avatīrṇena ca yena garbhe hṛtāni tejāṃsi mahā asurāṇām namāmi tam devam anantam īśam aśeṣa saṃsāra taroḥ kuṭhāram devaḥ jagadyoniḥ ayam mahātmā sa ṣoḍaśa aṃśena mahā asura indra sura indra mātuḥ jaṭharam praviṣṭaḥ hṛtāni vaḥ tena bale vapūṃṣi santi me śataśas daityāḥ vāsudeva bala adhikāḥ vipracittiḥ śibiḥ śaṅkuḥ ayaḥśaṅkuḥ tathā eva ca ayaḥśirāḥ aśvaśirāḥ bhaṅgakāraḥ mahā hanuḥ pratāpī praghasaḥ śaṃbhuḥ kurkurākṣaḥ ca durjayaḥ mahā balāḥ mahā vīryāḥ bhū bhāra dharaṇa kṣamāḥ yeṣām ekaikaśas kṛṣṇaḥ na vīrya ardhena saṃmitaḥ dhik dhik iti āha sa balim vaikuṇṭha ākṣepa vādinam vināśam upayāsyanti manye daiteya dānavāḥ yeṣām tvam īdṛśaḥ rājā durbuddhiḥ avivekavān devadevam mahābhāgam vāsudevam ajam vibhum tvām ṛte pāpa saṃkalpam kaḥ anyaḥ evam vadiṣyati ye ete bhavatā proktāḥ samastāḥ daitya dānavāḥ sa brahmakāḥ tathā devāḥ sthāvara antāḥ ca bhūtayaḥ tvam ca aham ca jagat ca idam sa adri druma nadīnadam samudra dvīpa lokāḥ ca yat ca iṅgam yat ca na iṅgati eka aṃśa aṃśa kalā janma kaḥ tam evam pravakṣyati ṛte vināśa abhimukham tvām ekam avivekinam durbuddhim ajita ātmānam vṛddhānām śāsana atigam yasya tvam īdṛśaḥ putraḥ devadeva avamanyakaḥ tiṣṭhatu aneka saṃsāra saṃhṛta agha vināśanī kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ aham tāvat avekṣyaḥ bhavataḥ na kim na me priyataraḥ kṛṣṇāt api dehaḥ ayam ātmanaḥ iti jānāti ayam lokaḥ bhavān ca ditija adhamaḥ mama api sarva jagatām guruḥ nārāyaṇaḥ guruḥ nindām karoṣi tasmin tvam kṛṣṇe guru guroḥ gurau yasmāt tasmāt iha aiśvaryāt acirāt bhraṃśam eṣyasi mā devaḥ mā jagannāthaḥ bale mā asau janārdanaḥ na apekṣitāḥ vayam yasmāt tasmāt śāpam dadāmi te yathā me śirasaḥ chedāt idam gurutaram bale yathā na kṛṣṇāt aparam paritrāṇam bhava arṇave prasādayām āsa gurum praṇipatya puṇar punar rājya bhraṃśam vasu bhraṃśam saṃprāpsyāmi iti na tu aham viṣaṇṇaḥ asmi yathā tāta tava eva avinaye kṛte saṃsāre durlabhāḥ tāta guravaḥ ye bhavadvidhāḥ tvad kopa hetu duṣṭaḥ aham paritapye na śāpataḥ yadi mohena me jñānam na ākṣiptam syāt mahā asura tat katham sarvagam jñānan harim kaṃcid śāpāmi aham bhāvyam etena nūnam te tasmāt tvam mā viṣīdathāḥ bhavethāḥ bhaktimān īśaḥ sa te trātā bhaviṣyati śāpam prāpya ca mām vīra saṃsmarethāḥ smṛtaḥ tvayā tathā tathā yatiṣyāmi śreyasā yokṣyate yathā ajāyata sa govindaḥ bhagavān vāmana ākṛtiḥ avatīrṇe jagannāthe tasmin sarvam aśīśamat yat āsuram abhūt duḥkham devānām aditeḥ tathā vavuḥ vātāḥ sukha sparśāḥ nīrajaskam abhūt nabhaḥ dharme ca sarva bhūtānām tadā matiḥ ajāyata na udvegaḥ ca api abhūt dehe manujānām janeśvara tathā hi sarva bhūtānām bhūmi ambara divaukasām tam jāta mātram bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ jātakarma ādikāḥ kṛtvā kriyāḥ tuṣṭāva pārthiva paramārtha artha sarvajña jñāna jñeya ātma niḥsṛta jaya aśeṣa jagat sākṣin jaya kartar jagadguroḥ jaya akhila jaya aśeṣa jaya akhila hṛdi sthita mumukṣubhiḥ anirdeśya svayaṃdṛṣṭa jaya īśvara yogibhiḥ mukti phala da dama ādi guṇa bhūṣaṇaiḥ jaya sthūla ati sūkṣma tvam jaya atīndriya sa indriya jaya sva māyā yoga stha śeṣa bhoga śaya akṣara jaya eka daṃṣṭra prānta anta nṛ kesarin jaya arāti vakṣaḥsthala vidāraṇa sāṃpratam jaya viśvātman māyā vāmana keśava tvayi eṣā jagatām īśa saṃsthitā dharma paddhatiḥ na tvām aham na ca īśānaḥ na indra ādyāḥ tridaśāḥ hare jñātum īśāḥ na munayaḥ sanaka ādyāḥ na yoginaḥ kaḥ tvām vetsyati sarva īśam tvad prasādam vinā naraḥ tat īśvara īśvara īśāna vibho vardhasva bhāvana prabhāvāya asya viśvasya viśvātman pṛthu locana evam stutaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ sa tadā vāmana ākṛtiḥ bhūyas ca aham stutaḥ adityā tasyāḥ ca api pratiśrutam yathā śakrāya dāsyāmi trailokyam hata kaṇṭakam saḥ aham tathā kariṣyāmi yathā indraḥ jagataḥ patiḥ tatas kṛṣṇājinam brahmā hṛṣīkeśāya dattavān āṣāḍham adadat daṇḍam marīciḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ kamaṇḍalum vasiṣṭhaḥ ca kauśyam vedam atha aṅgirāḥ akṣa sūtram ca pulahaḥ pulastyaḥ sita vāsasī upatasthuḥ ca tam vedāḥ praṇava svara bhūṣaṇāḥ śāstrāṇi aśeṣāṇi tathā sāṃkhya yoga uktayaḥ ca yāḥ sa vāmanaḥ jaṭī daṇḍī chattrī dhṛta kamaṇḍaluḥ dadāti bhūmiḥ vivaram tatra tatra atipīḍitā sa abdhi dvīpavatīm sarvām ca ālayām āsa medinīm tatas saṃśayam āpannāḥ sarve daiteya dānavāḥ sa parvata vanām urvīm dṛṣṭvā saṃkṣubhitām baliḥ papraccha uśanasam śukram praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ ācārya kṣobham āyāti sa abdhi bhūbhṛt dharā mahī kasmāt ca na asurān bhāgān pratigṛhṇanti vahnayaḥ iti pṛṣṭaḥ atha balinā kāvyaḥ veda vidām varaḥ uvāca daitya adhipatim ciram dhyātvā mahāmatiḥ avatīrṇaḥ jagadyoniḥ kaśyapasya gṛhe hariḥ vāmanena iha rūpeṇa paramātmā sanātanaḥ sa nūnam yajñam āyāti tava dānava puṅgava tad padanyāsa vikṣobhāt iyam pracalitā mahī kampante girayaḥ ca amī kṣubhitāḥ makara ālayāḥ na enam bhūtapatim bhūmiḥ samarthā voḍhum īśvaram anena eva dhṛtā bhūmiḥ āpaḥ agniḥ pavanaḥ nabhaḥ dhārayati akhilān deva manuṣya ādīn mahā asura iyam asya jagaddhātuḥ māyā kṛṣṇasya gahvarī dhārya dhāraka bhāvena yayā saṃpiṇḍitam jagat tad saṃnidhānāt asurāḥ na bhāga arhāḥ suradviṣaḥ bhuñjate ca asurān bhāgān amī te na tava agnayaḥ śukrasya vacanam śrutvā hṛṣṭa romā bravīt baliḥ yam yoginaḥ sadā udyuktāḥ paramātmānam avyayam tam adhvara īśvaram viṣṇum mattaḥ kaḥ anyaḥ upaiṣyati sarva īśvara īśvare viṣṇau mama adhvaram upāgate yat mayā ca ārya kartavyam tat mama ādeṣṭum arhasi yajña bhāga bhujaḥ devāḥ veda prāmāṇyataḥ asura tvayā tu dānavāḥ daityāḥ yajña bhāga bhujaḥ kṛtāḥ nisṛṣṭeḥ ca ayam ante ca svayam atti prajāḥ prabhuḥ tvayā anubandhī bhavitā nūnam viṣṇuḥ sthitau sthitaḥ pratijñā nā eva voḍhavyā vācyam sāma tathā aphalam na alam dātum dhanam deva iti evam vācyam tu yācataḥ kṛṣṇasya deva bhūti artham pravṛttasya mahā asura brahman katham aham brūyām anyena api hi yācitaḥ na asti iti kimu devena saṃsāra agha ogha hāriṇā yad artham upahāra āḍhyāḥ dama śauca guṇa anvitaiḥ yajñāḥ kriyante deveśaḥ sa mām dehi iti vakṣyati tat sādhu su kṛtam karma tapaḥ su caritam ca naḥ yat mayā dattam īśa īśaḥ svayam ādāsyate hariḥ na asti iti aham guro vakṣye tam api āgatam īśvaram yajñe asmin yadi yajñeśaḥ yācate mām janārdanaḥ na asti iti yat mayā na uktam anyeṣām api yācatām ślāghyaḥ eva hi dhīrāṇām dānāt āpad samāgamaḥ na ābādha kāri yat dānam tat aṅga malavat katham mad rājye na asukhī kaścid na daridraḥ na ca āturaḥ hṛṣṭa tuṣṭaḥ sugandhī ca tṛptaḥ sarva sukha anvitaḥ janaḥ sarvaḥ mahābhāga kim uta aham sadā sukhī etat viśiṣṭa pātra uttham dāna bīja phalam mama viditam bhṛguśārdūla mayā etat tvad prasādataḥ janārdane mahā pātre kim na prāptam tatas mayā mattaḥ dānam avāpya īśaḥ yadi puṣṇāti devatāḥ upabhoga anvaya guṇam dānam ślāghyataram tatas mad prasāda paraḥ nūnam yajñena ārādhitaḥ hariḥ tena abhyeti na saṃdehaḥ darśanāt upakāra kṛt mām nihantum atas api syāt vadhaḥ ślāghyataraḥ acyutāt sa mām yācitum abhyeti na anugraham ṛte hariḥ yaḥ sṛjati ātmabhūḥ sarvam cetasā eva apahanti ca sa mām hantum hṛṣīkeśaḥ katham yatnam kariṣyati tam dṛṣṭvā yajña vāṭa antar praviṣṭam asurāḥ prabhum jagmuḥ prabhāvataḥ kṣobham tejasā tasya niṣprabhāḥ tatas saṃkṣobham āpannaḥ na kaścid kiṃcid uktavān pratyekaḥ devadeveśam pūjayām āsa cetasā athā asura patim prahvam dṛṣṭvā muni varān ca tān devadeva patiḥ sākṣāt viṣṇuḥ vāmana rūpadhṛk tuṣṭāva yajñam vahnin ca yajamānam atha ṛtvijaḥ tatas prasannam akhilam vāmanam prati tad kṣaṇāt yajña vāṭa sthitam vīram sādhu sādhu iti udīrayan sa ca argham ādāya baliḥ prodbhūta pulakaḥ tadā pūjayām āsa govindam prāha ca idam vacaḥ asuraḥ suvarṇa ratna saṃghātam gaja aśvam amitam tathā striyaḥ vastrāṇi alaṃkārān gāvaḥ grāmān ca puṣkalān sarva svam sakalām urvīm bhavataḥ vā yat īpsitam tat dadāmi vṛṇuṣva tvam mama arthī satatam priyaḥ prāha sa smita gambhīram bhagavān vāmana ākṛtiḥ mama agni śaraṇa arthāya dehi rājan pada trayam śatam śata sahasram vā padānām mārgatām bhavān etāvatā daitya pate kṛtakṛtyaḥ asmi mārgatām anyeṣām arthinām vittam icchayā dāsyate bhavān pāṇau tu patite toye vāmanaḥ bhūtabhāvanaḥ sarva deva mayam rūpam darśayām āsa tad kṣaṇāt candra sūryau ca nayane dyauḥ śiraḥ caraṇau kṣitiḥ pāda aṅgulyaḥ piśācāḥ ca hasta aṅgulyaḥ ca guhyakāḥ viśvedevāḥ ca jānu sthāḥ jaṅghe sādhyāḥ sura uttamāḥ yakṣāḥ nakheṣu saṃbhūtāḥ rekhāsu apsarasaḥ sthitāḥ dṛṣṭiḥ dhiṣṇāni aśeṣāṇi keśāḥ sūrya aṃśavaḥ prabho tārakāḥ romakūpāṇi romāṇi ca mahā ṛṣayaḥ bāhavaḥ vidiśaḥ tasya diśaḥ śrotram mahātmanaḥ aśvinau śravaṇau tasya nāsā vāyuḥ mahā balaḥ prasādaḥ candramāḥ devaḥ manaḥ dharmaḥ samāśritaḥ satyam asya abhavat vāṇī jihvā devī sarasvatī grīvā aditiḥ devamātā vidyāḥ tad valayaḥ tathā svarga dvāram abhūt maitram tvaṣṭā pūṣā ca vai bhruvau mukham vaiśvānaraḥ ca asya vṛṣaṇau tu prajāpatiḥ hṛdayam ca param brahma puṃstvam vai kaśyapaḥ muniḥ pṛṣṭhe asya vasavaḥ devāḥ marutaḥ sarva saṃdhiṣu sarva sūktāni daśanāḥ jyotīṃṣi vimala prabhāḥ vakṣaḥ sthale tathā rudraḥ dhairye ca asya mahā arṇavaḥ udare ca asya gandharvāḥ marutaḥ ca mahā balāḥ lakṣmīḥ medhā dhṛtiḥ kāntiḥ sarva vidyāḥ ca vai kaṭiḥ sarva jyotīṃṣi yāni iha tapaḥ ca paramam mahat stanau kukṣau ca vedāḥ ca jānū ca asya mahā makhāḥ iṣṭayaḥ paśubandhāḥ ca dvijānām ceṣṭitāni ca tasya deva mayam rūpam dṛṣṭvā viṣṇoḥ mahā balāḥ kṛtvā rūpam mahā kāyam sa jahāra āśu medinīm param vikramamāṇasya jānu mūle prabhākarau viṣṇoḥ āstām mahīpāla deva pālana karmaṇi jitvā lokatrayam kṛtsnam hatvā ca asura puṅgavān sutalam nāma pātālam adhastāt vasudhā talāt baleḥ dattam bhagavatā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā atha daitya īśvaram prāha viṣṇuḥ sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ yat tvayā salilam dattam gṛhītam pāṇinā mayā sāṃpratam devarājāya trailokyam akhilam mayā dattam catur yugānām vai sādhikā hi ekasaptatiḥ tena aham parayā bhaktyā pūrvam ārādhitaḥ bale sutalam nāma pātālam tam āsādya manoramam vasa asura mama ādeśam yathāvat paripālayan sugandhi dhūpa saṃbādhe vara ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ upabhuñjan mahā bhogān vividhān dānava īśvara mama ājñayā kālam imam tiṣṭha strī śata saṃvṛtaḥ yadā ca deva viprāṇām viruddhāni ācariṣyasi bandhiṣyanti tathā pāśāḥ vāruṇāḥ tvām asaṃśayam etat viditvā bhavatā mayā ājñaptam aśeṣatas iti evam uktaḥ devena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā baliḥ prāha mahā rāja praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ tatra āsataḥ me pātāle bhagavan bhavat ājñayā āpyāyitaḥ yena deva smareyam tvām aham sadā dānāni a vidhi dattāni śrāddhāni a śrotriyāṇi ca hutāni aśraddhayā yāni tāni dāsyanti te phalam a dakṣiṇāḥ tathā yajñāḥ kriyāḥ ca avidhinā kṛtāḥ baleḥ varam idam dattvā śakrāya trividam tathā vyāpinā tena rūpeṇa jagāma adarśanam hariḥ siṣeva ca parān kāmān baliḥ pātālam āśritaḥ bali prahrāda saṃvādam mantritam bali śukrayoḥ bali viṣṇvoḥ ca kathitam yaḥ smariṣyati mānavaḥ na ādhayaḥ vyādhayaḥ vā asya na ca moha ākulam manaḥ bhaviṣyati kuruśreṣṭha puṃsaḥ tasya kadācana cyuta rājyaḥ nijam rājyam iṣṭa prāptim viyogavān avāpnoti mahābhāga naraḥ śrutvā kathām imām kāma upabhoga saṃprāptyā mudam prāpa parām vibhuḥ alaṃbuṣā miśrakeśī puṇḍarīkā atha vāmanā ghṛtācī menakā rambhā nanṛtuḥ tasya saṃnidhau tuṣṭuvuḥ ca mahābhāga balim siddhāḥ sa cāraṇāḥ tasmin saṃgīta gītā tu vīṇā veṇu rava ākule śarkāra sava mādhvikām puṣpa āsava phala āsavam divyāḥ prasannāḥ ca surāḥ tad arhāṇi madhūni ca parāvadaṃśān madhurān lavaṇān tiktakān kaṭūn kaṣāyān ca mahā rāja sumṛṣṭāni aparāṇi ca prāsādāḥ kāñcanāḥ sarve suvarṇa maṇi maṇḍitāḥ sphāṭika amala sopānāḥ muktā hāra śata ujjvalāḥ teṣu sarveṣu daiteyāḥ baleḥ saṃbandhi bāndhavāḥ nṛtya vādya ādi muditāḥ bubhujuḥ viṣayān priyān upagīyamānaḥ bubhuje yatheṣṭam viṣayān priyān sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpūrṇā śrīḥ iva abjam vinā aparā na devī nā api gandharvī nā apsarāḥ na ca mānuṣī tasyāḥ rūpeṇa sadṛśī babhūva manuja īśvara sā tu pīna āyata śroṇī mṛdu aṅgī madhura svarā mṛdu alpa pāṇi pāda abjā su madhyā gaja gāminī sukeśī sumukhī śyāmā sarvaiḥ yoṣit guṇaiḥ yutā tanayā merusāvarṇeḥ dauhitrī mṛgamokinaḥ vapuṣā rūpa saṃpadā pautanāḥ mṛga locanāḥ tīkṣṇāṃśuḥ madhyamām vīthīm yayau vaiṣuvatīm raviḥ yadā yadā ca viṣuvam bhāskaraḥ pratipadyate tadā tadā hareḥ cakram pātāle parivartate sravanti yoṣitām garbhāḥ tasya dhārā aṃśu tāpitāḥ sahasā daitya patnīnām yāsu puṃsām samudbhavaḥ tat dṛṣṭvā sahasā āyāntam āditya śata tejasam jvālā mālā su duḥprekṣyam viṣṇu cakram sudarśanam hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvam pātālam ari sūdana babhūvuḥ praṇatāḥ ca anye siddha gandharva cāraṇāḥ vaiklavyam ca āgatāḥ sarvāḥ striyaḥ para puraṃjaya tat dṛṣṭvā vyākulībhūtam pātālam asurāḥ tatas ye tasthuḥ pauruṣa parāḥ te hatāḥ śataneminā bhrāmyatā tena cakreṇa sapta loka vicāriṇā śrutvā cakram mahā cakraḥ niścakrāma gṛhāt baliḥ vimalam khaḍgam ādāya śata candram ca bhānumat vidhyāvalī nāma śubhā dadhāra dayitam patim uvāca ca pariṣvajya krodha tāmra īkṣaṇam balim kalyāṇī guṇa doṣa jñā praṇayāt mṛdu bhāṣiṇī vimṛśya tad jñaḥ sāma ādīn prayuñjīta balābalam cakram ittham vicārya tvam krodham yāhi praśāmya vā etat kila jagaddhātuḥ cakram viṣṇoḥ sudarśanam puṅgarbhān nikhilān etat dānavānām mahā asura vināśayati anantarām sarva duṣṭa nibarhaṇam puruṣāṇām na sarvatra saṃsthitā jagataḥ pateḥ tasya etat cakram āyāntam puruṣaḥ kaḥ na pūjayet sadṛśe puruṣe krodham naraḥ kurvīta daityapa śaraṇyam śaraṇam viṣṇum yam praṇamya na sīdati bhraṣṭaḥ ca yad adhikṣepāt tam tvam śaraṇam āvraja śreyase sarva dharma jña śaraṇam vraja keśavam sa vyājahāra bhagavān tava anugraha kāmyayā saṃsmaryatām mahābhāga sarva dharma bhṛtām varaḥ viṣṇu bhaktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sa te śreyaḥ abhidhāsyati yayau tadā argham ādāya viṣṇoḥ cakrasya pūjakaḥ sasmāra ca baliḥ sarvam prahrāda vacanam nṛpa tuṣṭāva vāsudevasya cakram avyakta mūrtinaḥ jvālā mālā karāla antam udyat indu sama prabham madhyāhna arka sama ābhāsam tejasaḥ piṇḍa saṃsthitam tam dṛṣṭvā tejasā rāśim upasaṃgamya ca vibhum uvāca daitya śārdūlaḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ namāmi cakriṇaḥ cakram kara saṅgi sudarśanam kālāgnim iva yat cakram sahasram iva sūryāṇām saṃghātam vidyutām iva tat viṣṇoḥ praṇamāmi aham yasya arakeṣu śakra ādyāḥ lokapālāḥ vyavasthitāḥ tad antar vasavaḥ rudrāḥ tathā eva marutām gaṇāḥ dhārāyām dvādaśa ādityāḥ samastāḥ ca hutāśanāḥ dhārā jāle abdhayaḥ sarve nābhi madhye prajāpatiḥ samasta nemiṣu akhilāḥ yasya vidyāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ yat bhramat sura saṅghānām tejasaḥ paribṛṃhaṇam daitya ojasām ca nāśāya tat namāmi sudarśanam prasāda su mukhe kṛṣṇe tasya cakram sudarśanam prasīda saṃyuge ariṇām sudarśana su darśanam vidyut jvālā mahā kakṣam daha antar mama yat tamaḥ visphoṭaya akhilām māyām kuruṣva vimalām matim evam saṃsthūyamānam tat vahni piṇḍa upamam mahat dadarśa sa mahā bāhuḥ prabhā maṇḍala durdṛśam agni jvālā gatam tāmram tapta cakram iva aparam trailokyam akhilam daityaḥ dṛṣṭavān bhūrbhuva ādikam meru ādīn akhilān śailān gaṅgā ādyāḥ saritaḥ tathā kṣīrābdhi pramukhān ca abdhīn dvīpān jambu ādi saṃjñitān vaimānikān sa gandharvān sūrya ādīn ca tathā grahān nakṣatra tāraka ākāśam śakra ādīn ca divaukasaḥ rudra ādityān ca marutām sādhyānām ca mahīpate saṃnidhānam nirīkṣya asau daityānām vismitaḥ abhavat tatas praṇamya ārti haram surāṇām apāra sāram parama āyudham hareḥ yat naḥ aśubham cetasi vāyu vega yat naḥ aśubham vāci hutāśana uttha yat ca aśubham kāya kṛtam hareḥ tat vara āyudham tvam praśamam naya āśu prasīda satkāra kṛtam mama agham prayātu te nāśam ananta vīrya satām ca sat mārgavatām manāṃsi sthirībhavantu acyuta pāda yugme puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ baleḥ mūrdhni nipapāta antarikṣataḥ tatas tat adbhutam dṛṣṭvā cakrasya āgamanam hareḥ tam smariṣyāmi daitya indram sa naḥ śreyaḥ abhidhāsyati saṃsmṛtaḥ ca sa pātālam ājagāma mahāmatiḥ cakra udyata karaḥ sākṣāt bhagavān iva keśavaḥ tāta aṃhri darśanāt adya pāvitaḥ asmi apakalmaṣaḥ iti saṃstūya dattvā ca varāsanam udāra dhīḥ paryupāsata rāja indraḥ daityānām sva pitāmaham tam upāsīnam anaghaḥ prahrādaḥ daitya puṅgavaḥ pratyuvāca mahātmānam balim vairocanim nṛpa tātena aham purā jñaptaḥ bhraṣṭa rājyena te bale saṃsmartavyaḥ asmi asaṃdigdham śreyaḥ vakṣyāmi aham tadā saḥ aham rājya paribhraṣṭaḥ viṣaya āsakti hṛṣitaḥ indriyaiḥ avaśaḥ tāta yat kāryam tat praśādhi mām tam devadevam anagham prayāhi śaraṇam harim śabda ādiṣu anuraktāni tava akṣāṇi asura adhipa gītakaiḥ gīyatām viṣṇuḥ manohāribhiḥ ātmanaḥ anya ālambanataḥ cittam ākṛṣya ādhatsva keśave gandhān udārān bhakṣān ca srajaḥ vāsāṃsi ca asura ātmānam acyutam viddhi śatrum ca ripum ātmanaḥ śabda ādayaḥ ye viṣayāḥ viṣayī yaḥ ca puruṣaḥ tat aśeṣam vijānīhi svarūpam paramātmanaḥ paramātmā ca bhagavān viṣvaksenaḥ janārdanaḥ bhagavān bhūta kṛt bhavyaḥ bhūtānām prabhavaḥ hi yaḥ prāpsyase parama āhlāda kāriṇīm paramām gatim tatra cittam samāveṣṭum na śaknoti bhavān yadi tatra api a sāmarthyavataḥ kriyā yogaḥ mahātmanā brahmaṇā yaḥ samākhyātaḥ tad manāḥ satatam bhava kṣīṇa karmā mahā bāho śubha aśubha vivarjitaḥ niḥsaṃśayam avāpnoti dhundhumāraḥ yathā nṛpaḥ rājyam ārādhya govindam kārtavīryaḥ tathā āptavān dharmam kṛṣṇa prasādena mudgalaḥ jājaliḥ kuṇiḥ prāpuḥ anye tathā kāmān narendrāḥ nahuṣa ādayaḥ dharmadhvajaḥ tathā muktim keśava ārādhanāt gataḥ tathā anye munayaḥ daitya rājānaḥ ca sahasraśas prāpuḥ muktim mahābhāgāḥ kṛtvā bhaktim janārdane śīta hānim tathā anyeṣām svedam sveda abhilāṣiṇām karoti kṣudhitānām ca bhojya pākam tathā utkaṭam tathā eva kāmān bhūteśaḥ sa dadāti yathā īpsitān tat etat akhilam jñātvā yat tava iṣṭam śṛṇuṣva tat etat prahrāda vacanam niśāmya ditija īśvaraḥ pratyuvāca mahābhāgam praṇipatya pitāmaham saṃprāptasya amṛtasya iva tava vākyasya nā asti me tṛptiḥ etat aham tāta śrotum icchāmi vistarāt akṣīṇa karmā puruṣaḥ maraṇe samupasthite kīdṛśam lokam āyāti yaḥ saṃsmarati keśavam yathā ca vāsudevasya smaraṇam tāta mānavaiḥ mumūrṣubhiḥ prakartavyam tat mama ācakṣva vistarāt kim japyam kīdṛśam rūpam smartavyam ca hareḥ tadā sādhu vatsa tvayā praśnaḥ su guhyaḥ ayam udāhṛtaḥ tapasām tāta sarveṣām tapaḥ na anaśanāt param kathyate ca mahā bāho saṃvādaḥ ayam purātanaḥ bhagīrathasya rājarṣeḥ brahmaṇaḥ ca prajāpateḥ atītya amara lokam ca gavām lokam ca mānada ṛṣi lokam ca yaḥ agacchat bhagīrathaḥ iti śrutaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sa vacaḥ prāha brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ katham bhagīratha agāḥ tvam imam deśam durāsadam āyānti atapta tapasaḥ katham vai tvam iha āgataḥ niḥśaṅkam annam adadam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śatam sahasrāṇi sadā eva dāyam brāhmaṇam vratam nityam āsthāya vidvan na tu eva aham tasya phalāt iha agām daśa ekarātrān daśa pañcarātrān ekādaśa ekādaśakān tathā eva jyotiṣṭomānām ca śatam yat iṣṭam phalena tena api na ca āgataḥ aham yat ca avasam jāhnavī tīra nityaḥ śatam samāḥ tapyamānaḥ tapaḥ aham daśa dhenu sahasrāṇi maṇi ratna vibhūṣitāḥ daśa arbudāni ca aśvānām ayutāni ca viṃśatiḥ puṣkareṣu dvijātibhyaḥ prādām gāḥ ca sahasraśas suvarṇa candra uttama dhāriṇīnām kanyā uttamānām adadam sragviṇīnām ṣaṣṭim sahasrāṇi vibhūṣitānām jāmbūnadaiḥ ābharaṇaiḥ na tena daśa arbudāni adadam gosave yāḥ tu ekaikaśas daśa gāḥ lokanātha samāna vatsāḥ payasā samanvitāḥ na tena gṛṣṭīnām kṣīra dātrīṇām rohiṇīnām śatāni ca dogdhrīṇām vai gavām ca eva prayutāni daśa eva tu prādām daśaguṇam brahman na ca tena aham āgataḥ koṭīḥ ca kāñcanasya aṣṭau prādām brahman daśa tu aham vājinām śyāma karṇānām haritānām pitāmaha prādām hema srajām brahman koṭīḥ daśa ca sapta ca īṣā dantān mahā kāyān kāñcana sraj vibhūṣitān patnīvataḥ sahasrāṇi prāyaccham daśa sapta ca alaṃkṛtānām deveśa divyaiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇaiḥ rathānām kāñcana aṅgānām sahasrāṇi adadam daśa sapta ca anyāni yuktānām vājibhiḥ samalaṃkṛtaiḥ dakṣiṇa avayavāḥ kecid devaiḥ ye saṃprakīrtitāḥ vājapeyeṣu daśasu prādām tena api na āgataḥ śakra tulya prabhāvānām vikrameṇa ca sahasram niṣka kaṇṭhānām pradadan dakṣiṇām aham vijitya nṛpatīn sarvān makhaiḥ iṣṭvā pitāmaha aṣṭābhyaḥ rājasūyebhyaḥ na ca tena aham āgataḥ srotaḥ ca yāvat gaṅgāyām chinnam āsīt jagatpate dakṣiṇābhiḥ pravṛttābhiḥ mama nāgam ca tad kṛte vājinām ca sahasre dve suvarṇa maṇi bhūṣite vāraṇānām śatam ca aham ekaikasya tridhā adadam varam grāma śatam ca aham ekaikasya tridhā adadam tapasvī niyata āhāraḥ śamam āsthāya vāgyataḥ dīrgha kālam himavati gaṅgāyāḥ ca durutsahām mūrdhnā dhārām mahādevaḥ śirasā yām adhārayat śamyā ākṣepaiḥ ayajam devadeva tathā kratūnām ayutaiḥ ca api yattaḥ trayodaśa dvādaśa ahaiḥ ca deva sa puṇḍarīkaiḥ na ca teṣām phalena aṣṭau sahasrāṇi kakudminām aham śukla ṛṣabhāṇām adam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ patnīḥ ca eṣām adadam niṣka kaṇṭhīḥ teṣām phalena iha na ca āgataḥ asmi dhana dhānya sahasrān ca grāmān śata sahasraśas śatam śatānām gṛṣṭīnām adadam ca api atandritaḥ iṣṭvā anekaiḥ mahā yajñaiḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dhanena ca ekādaśa ahaiḥ ayajam sudakṣiṇaiḥ dvis dvādaśa ahaiḥ aśvamedhaiḥ ca deva arkāyaṇaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ ca brahman teṣām phalena iha na ca āgataḥ asmi bṛhadbhiḥ dvādaśa ahaiḥ ca aśvamedhaiḥ pitāmaha niṣkrāmakam ca api adadam yojanānām dvis vistīrṇam kāñcana pādapānām vanam cūtānām ratna vibhūṣitānām na ca eva teṣām āgataḥ aham phalena turāyaṇam tu vratam apradhṛṣyam akrodhanaḥ akaravam triṃśataḥ abdān śatam gavām aṣṭa śatāni ca aham dine dine prādadam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ payasvinīnām atha rohiṇīnām tathā eva ca api anaḍuhām lokanātha prādām nityam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sureśa na iha āgataḥ tena phalena ca aham triṃśatam vidhivat vahnīn ayajam yat ca nityaśas aṣṭābhiḥ sarvamedhaiḥ ca nṛmedhaiḥ dviguṇaiḥ tathā daśabhiḥ ca stobhaiḥ aṣṭādaśa uttaraiḥ na ca eva teṣām deveśa phalena aham iha agamam saravyām bāhudāyām ca gayāyām atha naimiṣe gavām śatānām ayutam adadam na ca tena vai bhagīratham mahīpālam puṇya loka nivāsinam tat etat uktam tapasām samastānām mahāmate guṇaiḥ anaśanam brahmā pradhānataram abravīt sa yāti viṣṇu sālokyam yāvat indrāḥ caturdaśa atīta anāgatāni iha kulāni puruṣa ṛṣabha ślokāḥ ca atra mahā bāho śrūyante yān bhagīrathaḥ jagāda brahmaṇaḥ lokam upetaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ brahma brahma mayam viṣṇoḥ yaḥ padam paramātmanaḥ saṃsmaran tyajati prāṇān sa viṣṇum praviśati ajam yaḥ kṣīṇa karmā bhogena tapasā vā api saṃsmaran akṣīṇa karmā maraṇe saṃsmaran devam acyutam yathā tvam eva devānām loke bhogān upāśnute kṣutite api kule kaścid jāyeyam karmaṇaḥ kṣaye tat cintaya adhunā aśeṣa puṇya pāpa vivarjitaḥ iti etān āha rājarṣiḥ ślokān ādyaḥ bhagīrathaḥ viṣṇu saṃsmaraṇāt prāpya lokān anaśane mṛtaḥ evam atyanta śastānām karmaṇām asura īśvara na anyat utkṛṣṭam uddiṣṭam tad jñaiḥ anaśanāt param tasya aham lakṣaṇam vakṣye yat ca japyam mumūrṣubhiḥ yādṛgrūpaḥ ca bhagavān cintanīyaḥ janārdanaḥ āsannam ātmanaḥ kālam jñātvā prājñaḥ mahā asura nirdhūta mala doṣaḥ ca snātaḥ niyata mānasaḥ samabhyarcya hṛṣīkeśam puṣpa dhūpa ādibhiḥ tatas praṇipātaiḥ stavaiḥ puṇyaiḥ dhyāna yogaiḥ ca pūjayet mitrān amitrān madhyasthān parān svān ca punar punar abhyarthana upacāreṇa kṣāmayet kukṛtam svakam śubha aśubhānām daitya indra vākyam ca idam udāharet parityajāmi aham bhogān tyajāmi suhṛdaḥ akhilān bhojana ādi mayā utsṛṣṭam utsṛṣṭam anulepanam sraj bhūṣaṇa ādikam geyam dānam ādānam eva ca homa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ ye yāḥ ca nitya kriyāḥ mama naimittikāḥ tathā kāmyāḥ varṇa dharmāḥ tathā ujjhitāḥ guṇa dharma ādayaḥ dharmāḥ yāḥ ca kāścid mama kriyāḥ kariṣye prāṇinām pīḍām prāṇinaḥ santu nirbhayāḥ kṣiteḥ antara gāḥ ye ca ye ca pāṣāṇa saṃpuṭe ye dhānya ādiṣu vastreṣu śayaneṣu āsaneṣu ca na me asti bāndhavaḥ kaścid viṣṇum muktvā jagadgurum mitra pakṣe ca me viṣṇuḥ adhas ca ūrdhvam tathā agratas pārśvatas mūrdhni pṛṣṭhe ca hṛdaye vāci cakṣuṣi śrotra ādiṣu ca sarveṣu mama viṣṇuḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ dakṣiṇa agreṣu darbheṣu śayīta prācchirāḥ tatas viṣṇum jiṣṇum hṛṣīkeśam keśavam madhusūdanam nārāyaṇam naram kṛṣṇam vāsudevam janārdanam vārāham yajñapuruṣam puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam vāmanam śrīdharam śrīśam nṛsiṃham aparājitam sarva īśvara īśvaram śuddham anantam rāmam īśvaram cakriṇam gadinam śārṅgim śaṅkhinam garuḍadhvajam ayam viṣṇuḥ ayam śauriḥ ayam kṛṣṇaḥ puras mama nīlotpala dala śyāmaḥ padma pattra upama īkṣaṇaḥ eṣa paśyatu mām īśaḥ paśyāmi aham adhokṣajam āsīnaḥ sukha duḥkheṣu samaḥ mitra ahiteṣu ca praśānta netra bhrū vaktram śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam śrīvatsa vakṣasam ca eva catur bāhum kirīṭinam pīta ambara dharam viṣṇum cāru keyūra dhāriṇam cintayet ca tadā rūpam manaḥ kṛtvā eka niścayam yādṛśe vā manaḥ sthairyam rūpe badhnāti cakriṇaḥ ā prāṇa uparamāt vīraḥ tad cittaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ yathā agniḥ tṛṇa jālāni dahati anila saṃgataḥ tathā anaśana saṃkalpaḥ puṃsām pāpam asaṃśayam viṣṇoḥ saṃsmaraṇe prāpya lokam anaśane mṛtaḥ evam atyanta śastānām karmaṇām asura īśvara na asti vidyā samam cakṣuḥ tapaḥ na anaśanāt param na asti jñāna samam dānam na saṃtoṣa samam sukham na ca eva īrṣyā samam duḥkham tapaḥ na anaśanāt param na asti aroga samam dhanyam na asti gaṅgā samā sarit na asti viṣṇu samam dhyeyam tapaḥ na anaśanāt param utkrānti kāle bhūtānām muhyante citta vṛttayaḥ jarā vyādhi vidhīnānām kimu vyādhi ādi doṣataḥ atyanta vayasā vṛddhyā vyādhinā ca atipīḍitaḥ na atra bhūmiḥ na ca kuśāḥ saṃstaraḥ ca na kāraṇam cittasya ālambanībhūtaḥ viṣṇuḥ eva atra kāraṇam bhuñjan a bhuñjan gacchan ca svapan tiṣṭhan atha api vā kim japaiḥ kim bhuvā kṛtyam kim kuśaiḥ daitya sattama iti etat kathitam sarvam pṛṣṭaḥ aham yat tvayā bale utkrānti kāle smaraṇam kim bhūyas kathayāmi te kriyā yogaḥ tvayā pūrvam mama uktaḥ yaḥ pitāmaha deva arcām devatāgāre tad maya tvena pūjayam tapasā brahmacaryeṇa puṇya svādhyāya saṃstavaiḥ kriyāyogaḥ sa vidvadbhiḥ yoginām samudāhṛtaḥ deva arcām kārayitvā vā yat puṇyam puruṣaḥ aśnute kāni mālyāni śastāni kāni na arhanti keśave ke dhūpāḥ kṛṣṇa dayitāḥ ke varjyāḥ ca jagatpateḥ upahāre phalam kīm syāt kim phalam gīta vādite ghṛta kṣīra ādinā yat ca snāpite keśave phalam vāsudeva gṛhe sarvam tat aśeṣam vadasva me śuśrūṣaṇa vidhau puṇyam tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu brahmaṇā kila devānām ṛṣīṇām ca mahātmanām śuśrūṣaṇa phalam viṣṇoḥ proktam daitya pate purā tebhyaḥ sakāśāt manunā prāptam svārociṣeṇa tu svārociṣaḥ sva putrāya dattavān ṛtacakṣuṣe ṛta cakṣuḥ ca bhargave śukraḥ tasmāt avāpa ca mama ākhyātam ca śukreṇa yathāvat su mahātmanā śuśrūṣave mahābhāga daitya ācāryeṇa dhīmatā tat etat śrūyatām tāta kriyā yoga āśritam phalam jñāna yogaḥ tu saṃyogaḥ cittasya eva ātmanā tu yaḥ yaḥ tu bāhya artha sāpekṣaḥ sa kriyā yogaḥ ucyate devālaya ādi karaṇe tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu yaḥ tu devālayam viṣṇoḥ dārvam śaila mayam tathā kārayet mṛd mayam vā api śṛṇu tasya bale phalam kulānām śatam āgāmi samatītam tathā śatam sapta janma kṛtam pāpam su alpam vā yadi vā bahu viṣṇoḥ ālayavinyāsa prārambhāt eva naśyati pratiṣṭhām samavāpnoti sa naraḥ sapta laukikīm praśasta deśa bhū bhāge yaḥ śastam bhavanam hareḥ kārayati akṣayān lokān sa naraḥ pratipadyate iṣṭakā caya vinyāsaḥ yāvanti ṛkṣāṇi tiṣṭhati pratimām lakṣaṇavatīm yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi sa modate pratiṣṭhāpya hareḥ arcām su praśaste niveśane puruṣaḥ kṛtakṛtya tvāt na enam śvomaraṇam tapet ye bhaviṣyanti ye atītāḥ ā kalpāt puruṣāḥ kule tān tārayati saṃsthāpya devasya pratimām hareḥ anuśastāḥ kila purā yamena yama kiṃkarāḥ pāśa udyata āyudhāḥ daitya prajā saṃyamane ratāḥ viharadhvam yathānyāyam niyogaḥ me anupālyatām na ājñā bhaṅgam kariṣyanti bhavatām jantavaḥ kvacid kevalam ye jagat dhātum anantam samupāśritāḥ bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyāḥ teṣām na asti atra saṃsthitiḥ ye tu bhāgavatāḥ loke tad cittāḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ pūjayanti sadā viṣṇum te vaḥ tyājyāḥ su dūratas saṃkīrtayati govindam te vaḥ tyājyāḥ su dūratas ye dhūpa puṣpa vāsobhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ca api vallabhaiḥ arcayanti na te grāhyāḥ narāḥ kṛṣṇa āśraya uddhatāḥ upalepana kartāraḥ saṃmārjana parāḥ ca ye kṛṣṇa ālaye parityājyam teṣām tri puruṣam kulam yena ca āyatanam viṣṇoḥ kāritam tad kula udbhavam puṃsām śatam na avalokyam bhavadbhiḥ duṣṭa cakṣuṣā yena arcā bhagavat bhaktyā vāsudevasya kāritā nara ayutam tat kula jam bhavatām śāsana atigam bhavatām bhramatām atra viṣṇu saṃśraya mudrayā vinā ājñā bhaṅga kṛt nā eva bhaviṣyati naraḥ kvacid vatsa vaivasvatasya etāḥ śrutvā gāthāḥ marīcinā purukutsāya kathitāḥ pārthiva indrāya dhīmate etām mahā phalām yaḥ arcām kārayate naraḥ tava ākhyātam mahā bāho gṛhakārayituḥ ca yat yajñāḥ narāṇām pāpa ogha kṣālakāḥ sarva kāma dāḥ sthāpitām pratimām viṣṇoḥ samyak saṃpūjya mānavaḥ yam yam prārthayate kāmam tam tam āpnoti asaṃśayam yaḥ snāpayati devasya ghṛtena pratimām hareḥ prasthe prasthe dvijāgryāṇām sa dadāti gavām śatam gavām śatasya viprāṇām yat dattasya bhavet phalam bhūridyumnena saṃprāptā sapta dvīpā vasuṃdharā ghṛta āḍhakena govinda pratimā snāpanāt kila pratimāsam sita aṣṭamyām ghṛtena jagataḥ patim dvādaśyām pañcadaśyām ca gavyena haviṣā hareḥ snāpanam daitya śārdūla mahāpātaka nāśanam jñānataḥ ajñānataḥ vā api yat pāpam kurute naraḥ tat kṣālayati saṃdhyāyām ghṛtena snāpayan harim sarva yajña mayaḥ viṣṇuḥ havyānām paramam ghṛtam tayoḥ aśeṣa pāpānām kṣālakaḥ saṃgamaḥ asura yeṣu kṣīra vahāḥ nadyaḥ hradāḥ pāyasa kardamāḥ tān lokān puruṣāḥ yānti kṣīra snāna karāḥ hareḥ āhlādam nirvṛtim svāsthyam ārogyam cāru rūpa tām sapta janmāni avāpnoti kṣīra snāna karaḥ hareḥ dadhi ādīnām vikārāṇām kṣīrataḥ saṃbhavaḥ yathā tathā eva aśeṣa kāmānām kṣīra snāpanataḥ hareḥ yathā ca vimalam jñānam yathā nirvṛti kārakam graha anukūla tām puṣṭim priya tvam ca akhile jane karoti bhagavān viṣṇuḥ kṣīra snāpana toṣitaḥ sarvaḥ asya snigdha tām eti dṛṣṭa mātraḥ prasīdati ghṛta kṣīreṇa deveśe snāpite madhusūdane atra api udāharanti imam saṃvādam keśava āśritam śāṇḍilyā saha kaikeyyāḥ sumanāyāḥ surālaye svarge ati śobhanām dṛṣṭvā kaikeyīm patinā saha brāhmaṇī śāṇḍilī nāma paryapṛcchata vismitā śataśas santi kaikeyi devāḥ svarga nivāsinaḥ deva patnyaḥ tathā eva etāḥ siddhāḥ siddha aṅganāḥ tathā na teṣām īdṛśaḥ gandhaḥ na kāntiḥ na surūpa tā na vāsasām ca śobheyam yathā te patinā saha na eva ābharaṇa jātāni teṣām bhrājanti vai tathā śakra ādyānām apīsānām kṣaya atiśaya varjitaḥ tapaḥ prabhāvaḥ dānam vā karma vā homa saṃjñitam yajñaiḥ yajñeśvaraḥ viṣṇuḥ āvābhyām yat tu toṣitaḥ surūpa tām manaḥprīti paśyatām cāru veṣa tām yat pṛcchasi mahābhāge tat api eṣā vadāmi te tīrtha udakaiḥ tathā snānaiḥ snāpitaḥ ayam janārdanaḥ tena kāntiḥ atītya etān devān tribhuvana īśvarān manaḥ prasādaḥ saumya tvam śārīrā yā ca nirvṛtiḥ yāni abhīṣṭāni vāsāṃsi yat ca abhīṣṭam vibhūṣaṇam ratnāni yāni abhīṣṭāni yat priyam ca anulepanam ye dhūpāḥ yāni mālyāni dayitāni abhavan tadā dattāni tad samutthaḥ ayam gandha bhūṣā ātmakaḥ guṇaḥ āhārāḥ dayitāḥ ye ca pavitrāḥ ca niveditāḥ te loka kartre kṣṛṇāya tṛptiḥ tad guṇa saṃbhavā kṛtam etat atas na abhūt āvayoḥ bhava saṃkṣayaḥ ye tu akāmām narāḥ samyak etat kurvanti śobhane teṣām dadāti viśveśaḥ bhagavān muktim acyutaḥ prāpnoti abhimatān kāmān daityā āha sumanāḥ yathā nRﾱṇām bhavanti rogāya dattāni puruṣottame yāni ātmanaḥ sadā iṣṭāni tāni śastāni upākuru na śallakī jam na akṣaulam na śukta āsava saṃbhṛtam dadyāt kṛṣṇāya dharma jñaḥ dhūpān ārādhana udyataḥ mālatī mallikā ca eva yūthikā atha atimuktakā pāṭalā karavīraḥ ca javā pārantiḥ eva ca campakaḥ rotakaḥ kundaḥ bāṇaḥ varvara mālikāḥ aśoka tilakāḥ rodhrāḥ tathā ca eva āṭarūṣakaḥ amī puṣpa prakārāḥ tu śastāḥ keśava pūjane bilva patram śamī patram patram bhṛṅgārakasya ca tulasī kālatulasī patram bhṛṅgarajasya ca ketakī patra puṣpam ca sadyas tuṣṭi karam hareḥ sita utpalam ca kṛṣṇasya dayitāni sadā asura na arkam na unmattakam kāṃcid tathā eva girikarṇikām na kaṇṭakārikā puṣpam acyutāya nivedayet kauṭajam śālmalīpuṣpam śairīṣam ca janārdane yeṣām na pratiṣedhaḥ asti gandha varṇa anvitāni ca tāni puṣpāṇi deyāni viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave sugandhaiḥ ca surāmāṃsī karpūra agaru candanaiḥ dukūla paṭu kauśeya vārkṣa karpāsika ādibhiḥ vāsobhiḥ pūjayet viṣṇum daiteya indra ātmanaḥ priyaiḥ bhakṣyāṇi yāni abhīṣṭāni bhojyāni abhimatāni ca ātmānam keśavam matvā yat yat tasya eva rocate cakravartī mahā vīryaḥ māndhātā yuvanāśva jaḥ śaśāsa sa mahā bāhuḥ saptadvīpām vasuṃdharām agāyanta ca yāḥ gāthāḥ ye purāṇa vidaḥ janāḥ māndhātari mahā bāho yauvanāśve samāśritāḥ sarvam tat yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetram ucyate sa yauvana gataḥ saṃrāj sapta dvīpavatīm mahīm śaśāsa dharmeṇa purā cakravartī mahā balaḥ na anyāya kṛt na ca aśaktaḥ na daridraḥ na kīkaṭaḥ tasya abhūt puruṣaḥ rājye samyak dharma anuśāsinaḥ tasya bhaktiḥ atīva abhūt nisargāt eva bhūpateḥ vāsudeve jagat dhāmni sarva kāraṇa kāraṇe sa cintayām āsa nṛpaḥ samṛddhyā vismitaḥ tayā evam su bahuśas rājā daitya indra su mahā balaḥ cintayan api tad mūlam na ca āsīt niścaya anvitaḥ yadā na niścayam rājā sa yayau yuvanāśva jaḥ praṇipatya mahā bāhuḥ gṛhīta āsana satkriyān yadi sa anugrahā buddhiḥ bhavatām mayi sattamāḥ sametya akhila vijñānam samyak dhauta antarātmabhiḥ yat yathā tat mayā pṛṣṭāḥ bhavantaḥ mad prasādhitāḥ gadiṣyāmaḥ yathānyāyam yat te sāṃśayikam hṛdi vayam hi nara śārdūla bhavatā paritoṣitāḥ samyak prajāḥ pālayatā sapta dvīpe mahī tale su tuṣṭaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ aśnīyāt chindyāt vā dharma saṃśayam vivakṣum atha bhūpālam bhāryā tasya eva dhīmataḥ praṇāma pūrvam āha idam vinayāt praṇaya anvitam na strīṇām avanīpāla vaktum īdṛś iha īśyate tathā api bhūpate vakṣye saṃpad īdṛś su durlabhā bhūyas api saṃśayam praṣṭum alam īśa bhavān ṛṣīn na tu aham puruṣa vyāghra sadā antaḥpura cāriṇī tat madīyam ṛṣīn praṣṭum saṃśayam pārthiva arhasi brūhi subhru matam yat te praṣṭavyāḥ yat mayā dvijāḥ bhūyas aham ātma saṃdeham prakṣyāmi etān dvijottamān śrūyante pṛthivīpāla nṛpa ye ca purātanāḥ teṣām na saṃpad bhūpāla yathā tava kila abhavat tat īdṛś saṃpadām dhāma tvam aśeṣa kṣiti īśvaraḥ atīva karmaṇā yena tad vijñāne kutūhalam nirasta atiśaya tvena nūnam na alpena karmaṇā munīn pṛcchatu yā ca aham yat mayā ca purā kṛtam sa tathā uktaḥ tayā rājā patnyā vismita mānasaḥ munīnām puratas bhāryām praśaṃsan vākyam abravīt satyam muni vacaḥ puṃsām ardham vai gṛhiṇī yathā mama api etat abhipretam imān praṣṭum mahā munīn saḥ aham etat mahābhāge prakṣyāmi etān mahā munīn na eṣām aviditam kiṃcid triṣu lokeṣu vidyate evam uktvā priyām bhāryām praṇipatya ca tān ṛṣīn bhagavantaḥ mama aśeṣam prasāda āhṛta cetasaḥ kathayantu yathāvṛttam yat mayā su kṛtam kṛtam kaḥ aham āsam purā viprāḥ kim ca karma mayā kṛtam kim vā anayā su cāru aṅgyā mama patnyā kṛtam dvijāḥ aśeṣāḥ bhūbhṛtaḥ vaśyāḥ kośasya antaḥ na vidyate balam ca eva apratihatam śarīra ārogyam uttamam nija anuṣṭhānam akhilam yasya aśeṣam idam phalam iti praṣṭāḥ narendreṇa samastāḥ te tapodhanāḥ vasiṣṭham codayām āsuḥ kathyatām iti bhūbhṛtaḥ yogam āsthāya su ciram yathāvat yata mānasaḥ jñātavān nṛpateḥ tasya pūrva deha viceṣṭitam māndhātāram mahā buddhim sa patnīkam idam vacaḥ śṛṇu bhūpāla sakalam yasya idam karmaṇaḥ phalam tava rājya ādikam subhrūḥ yā iyam ca āsīt mahīpate tvam āsīḥ śūdra jātīyaḥ para hiṃsā parāyaṇaḥ vāc krūraḥ daṇḍa pāruṣyaḥ niḥsnehaḥ sarva jantuṣu tathā iyam bhavataḥ bhāryā pūrvam api āyata īkṣaṇā dveṣyā babhūva tad cittā tava śuśrūṣaṇe ratā pativratā mahābhāgā bhartsyamānā api aniṣṭhurā kṣayam jagāma yaḥ arthaḥ abhūt saṃcitaḥ prapitāmahaiḥ tasmin kṣīṇe kṛṣi paraḥ tvam āsīḥ pṛthivīpate sā api karma vipākena kṛṣiḥ viphala tām gatā tatas niḥsvam parikṣīṇam pareṣām bhṛtya tām gatam tatyāja sādhvī vā iyam tvām tyajyamānā api pārthiva anayā ca samam sādhvyā viṣṇoḥ āvasathe tvayā kṛtam śuśrūṣaṇam vīra parivrāj brahmacāriṇām tad vṛtti lipsuḥ śuśrūṣām jana rañjana hetukaḥ kṛtavān yoginām vīra kṛṣṇasya jagataḥ pateḥ vāsudeva ajire nityam kṛtam saṃmārjanam tvayā tathā eva abhyukṣaṇam vīra nityam ca eva anulepanam patnyā anayā ca dharma jña yaṣmad citta anuvṛttayā viṣṇoḥ kāryam mayā kāryam yogi śuśrūṣaṇam tathā bhṛtya avasāyinaḥ samyak yathā ukta adhika kāriṇaḥ smarataḥ puṇḍarīkākṣam kāryeṇa ati dṛḍha ātmanaḥ niḥśeṣam upaśāntam tat pāpam yogi niṣevaṇāt saṃmārjanam ca bahuśas sapatnikena te kṛtam tatra āgataḥ ca sauvīraḥ purujit nāma bhūpatiḥ mahā sainya parīvāraḥ prabhūta gaja vāhanaḥ sarva saṃpad upetam tam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam vṛtam bhāryā sahasreṇa dṛṣṭvā sraj candana ujjvalam spṛhā kṛtā tvayā tatra cāru maulini pārthive tatra eva āvasathe dīpaḥ praśāntaḥ sneha saṃkṣayāt anayā ca uttarīya anta cīra vartī upavṛṃhitaḥ tava api akhila bhūpāla manaḥ kṣobha karam tatas evam narendra śūdra tvāt viṣṇu karma parāyaṇaḥ kim punar yaḥ naraḥ bhaktyā viṣṇu śuśrūṣaṇa ādṛtaḥ karoti satatam pūjām niṣkāmaḥ na anya mānasaḥ pūjaya acyutam īśa īśam tam ārādhya na sīdati ārādhaya acyutam tadvat veśma saṃmārjana ādibhiḥ tat tat dāttvā jagaddhātre vaikuṇṭhāya na sīdati sugandha agaru karpūra candana ākṣoda kuṃkumaiḥ anna upahāraiḥ vividhaiḥ ghṛta kṣīra abhiṣecanaiḥ gīta vādita nṛtya ādyaiḥ toṣayasva acyutam nṛpa puṇya rātriṣu govindam nṛtya gīta rava ujjvalaiḥ evam saṃtoṣyate bhaktyā bhagavān bhava bhaṅga kṛt yeṣām na vittam taiḥ bhaktyā mārjana ādi upalepanaiḥ deva karma asamarthāṇām prāṇinām smṛti saṃstavaiḥ toṣitaḥ abhimatān kāmān prayacchati janārdanaḥ sadbhāvena eva govindaḥ toṣam āyāti saṃsmṛtaḥ kṛtvā alpam īdṛśam prāptam rājyam atyanta durlabham tasmāt tvam anayā devyā saha atyanta vinītayā keśava ārādhane yatnam kuru dharma bhṛtām vara etat muneḥ vasiṣṭhasya niśāmya vacanam nṛpaḥ bhāryā sahāyaḥ sa tadā saṃprahṛṣṭa tanūruhaḥ kṛta kāryam iva ātmānam manyamānaḥ asura uttama uvāca praṇataḥ bhūtvā māndhātā vāruṇim vacaḥ yathā amara tvam saṃprāpya yathā vā brahma śāśvatam param nirvāṇam āpnoti tathā aham vacasā tava kṛtakṛtyaḥ sukhī ca asmi nirvṛtim paramām gataḥ aham eṣā ca tanvaṅgī vibhūti bhraṃsa bhīrukau āḍhyau āpāditau brahman iha adya vacasā tava saṃpadām kathitam bījam āvayoḥ bhavatā mune tad uptau udyatau āvām vijānīhi dvijottama ārādhyate jagannāthaḥ bhāva śūnyaiḥ janārdanaḥ niḥsvaiḥ ārādhyate devaḥ viṣṇuḥ sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ sarvam etat mayā jñātam yat tvam āttha mahā mune kāni vratāni yaiḥ devaḥ naraiḥ strībhiḥ ca keśavaḥ toṣam ārādhitaḥ abhyeti kaiḥ ca dānaiḥ mahā mune tāni aśeṣāṇi me brūhi kṛṣṇa ārādhana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ śṛṇu bhūpāla yaiḥ viṣṇuḥ naraiḥ ārādhyate vrataiḥ nārībhiḥ ca ati ghore asmin patitābhiḥ bhava arṇave ekam aśnāti yaḥ bhaktam dvitīyam brāhmaṇa ātmakam karoti keśava prītyai kārttikam māsam ātmavān pūrve vayasi yat tena jñānataḥ ajñānataḥ api vā pāpam ācaritam tasmāt mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ anena eva vidhānena mārgaśīrṣe api mādhavam bhagavat prīṇana arthāya phalam tasya śṛṇuṣva me madhye vayasi yat pāpam yoṣitā puruṣeṇa vā kṛtam tasmāt ca tena uktaḥ vimokṣaḥ paramātmanā puṇḍarīkākṣam abhyarcya pauṣa māse mahīpate tad prīṇanāya yat pāpam vārddhike tena vai kṛtam sa tasmāt mucyate rājan pumān yoṣit atha api vā tadvat tṛtīye api kṛtam mahāpātaka nāśanam tribhiḥ saṃvatsaraiḥ eva pradadāti phalam nṛṇām trīṇi nāmāni devasya mocayanti tri vārṣikaiḥ sarva pāpa praśamanam keśava ārādhanam param śṛṇuṣva ca mahīpāla vratam viṣṇu pada trayam sarva pāpa praśamanam yat jagāda purā hariḥ prācetasāya dakṣāya dakṣaḥ ca āha vivasvate asitena samākhyātam alpa āyāsam mahā phalam tat idam śrūyatām samyak vratam viṣṇu pada trayam dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ pūrvam viṣṇum ārādhya pṛṣṭavān bahuśas tu vipannāyām sṛṣṭau ari nisūdana bhagavan mama ādiṣṭam svayaṃbhuvā brahmaṇā devadeveśa tava ādeśena keśava vipannā ca jagannātha mama sṛṣṭiḥ kṛtā kṛtā pūrva karma vipākena vyākulaḥ ca asmi cetasā yathā ca deva mucyeya asmāt saṃsāra saṃkaṭāt viṣaya āsaṅga viṣamāt tat mama ājñāpaya acyuta ācaṣṭa duḥkha kṣaya dam vratam viṣṇu pada trayam saṃsāra ucchedakam dhīraiḥ ācīrṇam sthira buddhibhiḥ kathayāmi samācaṣṭa yathā pūrvam mama asitaḥ āṣāḍhe māsi pūrvāsu tathā āṣāḍhāsu pārthiva yavān ca dadyāt viprāya bhū gatiḥ prīyatām iti naktam bhuñjīta rāja indra haviṣya annam susaṃskṛtam tathā uttarāsu āṣāḍhāsu śrāvaṇe māsi mānavaḥ viprāya ca yavān dadyāt prīṇayitvā ca bhū gatim naktam bhūñjīta rāja indra naraḥ yoṣit atha api vā viprāya ca yavān dattvā prīṇayitvā bhuvogatim bhuñjīta gorasa prāyam naraḥ yoṣit atha api vā pada dvayasya pūjām ca prīṇanam ca bhuvogateḥ strī vā rāja indra pūrvāsu tathā bhadrapadāsu vai phālgune phalgunī pūrvā bhavatī ha yadā nṛpa hiraṇyam dakṣiṇām dattvā svargatiḥ prīyatām iti eṣaḥ eva uttarā yoge caitre māse vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ etat jagāda govindaḥ purā dakṣāya pṛcchate sarva pāpa haram puṇyam vratam viṣṇu pada trayam samāgamam proṣitaiḥ ca tathā prāpnoti bāndhavaiḥ dravyam aiśvaryam ārogyam saubhāgyam cāru rūpa tām yān yān kāmān naraḥ strī vā hṛdayena abhivāñchanti tān tān ca āpnoti niṣkāmaḥ viṣṇu lokam ca gacchati pūrvam kṛtvā api pāpāni naraḥ strī vā narādhipa viṣṇoḥ ārādhana arthāya yāni dānāni sattama deyāni tāni aśeṣāṇi mama ācakṣva dvijottama yena ca eva vidhānena dānam puṃsaḥ sukha āvaham prīṇanāya ca kṛṣṇasya tat mama ākhyāhi vistarāt kṛta upavāsaḥ saṃprāśya pañcagavyam nareśvara ghṛta kṣīra abhiṣekam ca kṛtvā viṣṇoḥ samāhitaḥ udak mukhīm arcayitvā tathā gṛṣṭim payasvinīm sa putrām vastra saṃvītām sita yajña upavītinīm svarṇa śṛṅgīm śubha ākārām hiraṇya upari saṃsthitām hiraṇyam vācayitvā agre brāhmaṇāya upapādayet imām tvam pratigṛhṇīṣva govindaḥ prīyatām iti govinda prīṇanāt rājan viṣṇu lokam ca gacchati sapta avarān tathā pūrvān sapta ātmānam ca mānavaḥ sarveṣām eva pāpānām kṛtānām a vijānatā prāyaścittam idam śastam anutāpa upavṛṃhitam ikṣvākunā eṣā rāja indra pūrvam dattā mahātmanā tatas sa lokān amalān prāptavān avanīpatiḥ lokāḥ kāmadughāḥ prāptāḥ dattvā īdṛś vidhinā nṛpa tiladhenum pravakṣyāmi keśava prīṇanāya yā yām dattvā brahma hā go ghnaḥ pitṛ ghnaḥ gurutalpa gaḥ āgāradāhī garadaḥ sarva pāpa rataḥ api vā su anulipte mahī pṛṣṭe vastra ajina samāvṛte dhenum tila mayīm kṛtvā sarva ratnaiḥ samanvitām suvarṇa śṛṅgīm raupya khurām gandha ghrāṇavatīm śubhām mṛṣṭa anna jihvām kurvīta guḍa āsyām sūtra kambalām ikṣu pādām tāmra pṛṣṭhām kuryāt muktāphala īkṣaṇām praśasta patra śravaṇām phala dantavatīm śubhām sraj dāma pucchām kurvīta navanīta stana anvitām īdṛś saṃsthāna saṃpannām kṛtvā śrāddha samanvitaḥ kāṃsya upadohanām dadyāt keśavaḥ prīyatām iti prapitāmaham tathā pūrvam puruṣāṇām catuṣṭayam ātmānam tanayam pautram tad adhas tu catuṣṭayam yaḥ ca gṛhṇāti vidhivat tasya api evaṃvidhān kulān caturdaśa tathā ca eva dadataḥ ca anumodakāḥ dīyamānām prapaśyanti tiladhenum ca ye narāḥ te api aśeṣa agha nirmuktāḥ prayānti paramām gatim praśāntāya su śīlāya tathā amatsariṇe budhaḥ cāndrāyaṇāt abhyadhikam śastam tat tila bhakṣaṇam tila abhāve tathā dadyāt ghṛtadhenum yata vrataḥ yena bhūpa vidhānena tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu vāsudevam jagannātham puruṣeśam ajam vidhum sarva pāpa nihantāram ghṛta kṣīra abhiṣecanāt saṃpūjya pūrvavat puṣpa gandha dhūpa ādibhiḥ naraḥ ahar rātra uṣitaḥ bhūtvā tad paraḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ parameśam atho nāmnā abhiṣṭūya ghṛta arciṣā gavyasya sarpiṣaḥ kumbham puṣpa mālya ādi bhūṣitam ikṣu yaṣṭi mayān pādān khurān raupya mayān tathā sauvarṇe ca akṣiṇī kuryāt śṛṅge ca agaru kāṣṭha je kuryāt turuṣka karpūrau ghrāṇam phala mayān stanān maṇi ratna suvarṇānām samyak kalpanayā kṛtām tadvat śarkarayā jihvām guḍa kṣīra mayam mukham kṣauma sūtreṇa lāṅgūlam romāṇi sita sarṣapaiḥ tāmra pātra mayam pṛṣṭham kuryāt śraddhā samanvitaḥ īdṛś svarūpām saṃkalpya ghṛtadhenum narādhipa tam ca vipram mahābhāga manasā eva ghṛta etām mama upakārāya ghṛhṇīṣva tvam dvijottama prīyatām mama deveśaḥ ghṛtāṛciḥ puruṣottamaḥ maṇi muktā suvarṇānām samyak kalpanayā kṛtām dattvā eka rātram sthitvā ca ghṛta āhāraḥ narādhipa mucyate sarva pāpebhyaḥ tathā dāna phalam śṛṇu ghṛta kṣīra vahāḥ nadyaḥ yatra pāyasa kardamāḥ teṣu lokeṣu loka īśa sa puṇyeṣu upajāyate tān teṣu nṛpa lokeṣu sa nayati asta kalmaṣaḥ sa kāmānām iyam vyuṣṭiḥ kathitā nṛpa sattama viṣṇu lokam narāḥ yānti niṣkāmāḥ ghṛtadhenu dāḥ ghṛtam agniḥ ghṛtam somaḥ tad mayāḥ sarva devatāḥ jaladhenum pravakṣyāmi prīyate dattayā yayā devadevaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarva īśaḥ sarva bhāvanaḥ kuṣṭham māṃsīm uśīram ca vālaka āmalakaiḥ yutam caturbhiḥ saṃvṛtam bhūpa tila pātraiḥ caturdiśam puṣpa dhūpa upahāraiḥ tu yathāvibhavam ādṛtaḥ evam saṃpūjya govindam jaladhenum sa vatsakām sita vastra dharaḥ śāntaḥ vīta rāgaḥ vimatsaraḥ dadyāt viprāya rāja indra prīti artham jalaśāyinaḥ jala śāyī jagadyoniḥ prīyatām mama keśavaḥ iti ca uccārya bhūnātha viprāya pratipādyatām apakva anna āśinā stheyam ahorātram atas param sarva āhlādān avāpnoti ye divyāḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ śarīra ārogyam ābādhā praśamaḥ sārvakāmikaḥ nṛṇām bhavati dattāyām jaladhenvām na saṃśayaḥ atrā api śrūyate bhūpa pudgalena mahātmanā dadarśa yātanāḥ ghorāḥ pāpa karma kṛtām kila dīpta agni tīkṣṇa śastra utthāḥ kvātha taila gatāḥ tathā uṣṇa kṣāra nadī pātāḥ bhairavāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha vraṇāḥ kṣāra nipāta ugrāḥ kumbhīpāka mahā bhayāḥ tāḥ dṛṣṭvā yātanāḥ vipraḥ cakāra paramām kṛpām āhlādam te tadā jagmuḥ pāpāḥ tad anukampitāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā nārakāḥ kecid kecid tad avalokinaḥ dharmarājam sa papraccha teṣām praśama kāraṇam tasmai ca ācaṣṭa rāja indra tadā vaivasvataḥ yamaḥ āhlāda hetum viprāya pṛcchate pṛthivīpate tava anubhāvāt eteṣām nārakāṇām dvijottam saṃpravṛttaḥ ayam āhlādaḥ kāraṇam yat śṛṇuṣva tat tvayā abhyarcya jagannātham sarveśam jalaśāyinam tasya dānasya te vyuṣṭiḥ iyam āhlāda dāyinī saṃprāptaḥ asi mahā prajña sarva śāstra viśārada ye tvām paśyanti śṛṇvanti ye ca dhyāyanti pāpinaḥ śṛṇoṣi yān tvam vipra indra yān ca dhyāyasi paśyasi nirvṛtiḥ paramā teṣām sarva āhlāda pradāyinī āhlāda hetu jananam nā asti vipra indra tādṛśam jaladhenuḥ yathā nR̥ṇām janmāni ekonasaptatiḥ eka janma kṛtam vāñchā tri janma uttham samāhṛtā sapta janma kṛtam pāpam hanti datta ambu gauḥ nṛṇām yeṣām samāśrayaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ na niyamyāḥ hi te mayā kṛṣṇaḥ saṃpūjitaḥ yaiḥ tu ye kṛṣṇa artham upoṣitāḥ yaiḥ ca nityam smṛtaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ na te mad viṣaya upagāḥ namaḥ kṛṣṇa acyuta ananta vāsudeva iti udīritam yaiḥ saṃsmṛtaḥ dvijaśreṣṭha na te mad viṣaya upagāḥ kṛṣṇa iti udīritam yaiḥ ca na te mad viṣaya upagāḥ sarva ābādhāsu ye kṛṣṇam smaranti uccārayanti ca tad bhāva bhāvitāḥ vipra na te mad viṣaya upagāḥ ūcuḥ te nārakāḥ sarve vahni śastra astra bhīravaḥ namaḥ kṛṣṇāya haraye viṣṇave jiṣṇave namaḥ hṛṣīkeśāya devāya jagaddhātre acyutāya ca namaḥ paṅkaja netrāya namaḥ paṅkaja nābhaye janārdanāya śrīśāya śrīpate pīta vāsase namaḥ karāla vaktrāya nṛsiṃhāya ati nādine śārṅgiṇe sita khaḍgāya śaṅkha cakra gadā dhṛte varāha rūpāya tathā namaḥ yajña aṅga dhāriṇe vyāpta aśeṣa diś antāya śāntāya paramātmane śastrāṇi kuṇṭhatām jagmuḥ analaḥ ca api aśīśamat saṃśuṣkāḥ kṣārasaritaḥ patitaḥ kūṭaśālmaliḥ prakāśa tāmasī tattvam narakaḥ ca āgataḥ tu saḥ nirutsāhāḥ jaḍa dhiyaḥ babhūvuḥ yama kiṃkarāḥ āsan gandha ambu vāhinyaḥ pūya śoṇita nimnagāḥ veṇu vīṇā svana yutān gīta śabdān ca śuśruvuḥ tam tādṛśam atha ālakṣya nṛpa vaivasvataḥ yamaḥ jājvalyamānān tejobhiḥ amala ambara vāsasaḥ namaḥ namaḥ astu kṛṣṇāya govindāya avyaya ātmane vāsudevāya devāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave kṣīṇa pāpa cayān tān tu pādya arghya ādibhiḥ arcayan pūjayitvā ca tān āha sa kṛṣṇāya kṛtāñjaliḥ samāhita manāḥ bhūtvā dharmarājaḥ nareśvara viṣṇoḥ devātidevasya jagaddhātuḥ prajāpateḥ praṇāmam ye api kurvanti teṣām api namaḥ namaḥ ye viṣṇoḥ praṇatāḥ tebhyaḥ namaḥ sadyas punar punar praṇāmam ye api kurvanti teṣām api namaḥ namaḥ evam te saṃstutāḥ tena dharmarājena nārakāḥ vimānāni samārūḍhāḥ nṛtta gāndharvavanti vai saṃsmṛtya yama vākyāni viṣṇoḥ māhātmyam eva ca jaladhenvāḥ ca māhātmyam saṃsmṛtya etat agāyata jīvaḥ vāñchati kīṭa tvam yūkā matkuṇa yonitaḥ tasmāt ca śalabha ādīnām yonim tasmāt ca pakṣiṇām tatas ca paśu tām prāpya nara tvam abhivāñchati vimukti hetukī dhanyā nara yoniḥ kṛtātmanām jīvāḥ mānuṣya tām anye janmanām ayutaiḥ api viṣṇu māyā parītāḥ te prāpya api na taranti ye patanti bhūyas saṃsāre viṣṇu māyā vimohitāḥ dustarā api tu sādhyā asau māyā kṛṣṇasya mohanī chindanti vaiṣṇavīm māyām keśava arpita mānasāḥ avirodhena viṣayām bhuñjan viṣṇu vyapāśrayaḥ kṛtvā manaḥ tarati etām viṣṇoḥ māyām su dustarām īdṛś bahu phalām bhaktim sarva dhātari keśave mudhā eva uktam mudhā āyātam mudhā tat vidhi ceṣṭitam ārādhitaḥ hi yaḥ puṃsām aihika āmuṣmikam phalam saṃvatsarāḥ tathā māsāḥ viphalāḥ divasāḥ ca te narāṇām viṣaya andhānām yeṣu na ārādhitaḥ hariḥ tuṣyate hṛdayena eva kaḥ tam īśam na pūjayet jaladhenvāḥ ca māhātmyam niśāmya api īdṛśam narāḥ tām na yacchanti ye teṣām vivekaḥ kutra tiṣṭhati saṃprāpya tat na yaiḥ viṣṇuḥ toṣitaḥ nā ambu dhenukā dattā ca samyak te muṣṭā janmani su bahūni bhoḥ ūrdhvabāhuḥ viraumi eṣa dṛṣṭa loka dvayaḥ asmi bhoḥ duḥsahaḥ nārakaḥ vahniḥ aviṣahyāḥ ca yātanāḥ jñānam mama etat ālambya kṛṣṇe bhavata su sthirāḥ vimṛṣya satyam iti etat manaḥ kṛṣṇe niveśyatām prātar kṛṣṇa iti deva iti govinda iti ca jalpatām madhyāhne ca aparāhne ca yaḥ avasādaḥ saḥ ucyatām mudhā eva jihvā kṛṣṇā iti keśava iti ca vakṣyati etāḥ pudgala gāthāḥ te yama vākyam tava uditam jaladhenvāḥ ca māhātmyam viṣṇu saṃpūjanasya ca vratam anyat mahābhāga sarva kāma pradam śṛṇu bhaviṣyati śamīkasya śiṣyaḥ parama saṃmataḥ sa ca rājā jagaddhātuḥ devadevasya śārṅginaḥ prakṣyati ārādhana arthāya devadevasya cakriṇaḥ ārādhayitum icchāmi sarva icchā pūrakam harim saṃkuruṣva mahābhāga prasādam mama suvrata kṛṣṇa ārādhana kāmasya manasaḥ deśikaḥ bhava ārādhanena yena īśaḥ jagatām īśvara īśvaraḥ viṣṇuḥ ārādhyate puṃbhiḥ saṃsāra abdhi parikṣataiḥ kṛtvā sadā eva ārtimatām śaraṇyam śaraṇam guruḥ evam sa tena bhūpāla bhūpālena ṛṣi puṅgavaḥ keśava ārādhana arthāya samyak pṛṣṭaḥ pravakṣyati namaskṛtya jagaddhātre devadevāya śārṅgine parameśa sureśāya hṛṣīkeśāya vedhase sarva kalyāṇa bhūtāya śaṅkha cakra gadā dhṛte vara asi carma avitate krūra śānta ātma mūrtaye yad yad bhūta upakārāya tad tad rūpa vikāriṇe paramāṇu anta paryanta sahasrāṃśa aṇu mūrtaye jaṭhara anta ayuta aśānta sthita brahmāṇḍa dhāriṇe śveta ādi dīrgha hrasva ādi kaṭhina ādi vikalpanā tam ajam śāśvatam nityam pariṇāma vivarjitam praṇamya jagatām īśam anantam paratas param param parāṇām sraṣṭāram purāṇam puruṣam prabhum varam vareṇyam vara dam sthūla sūkṣma svarūpiṇam aśeṣa jagatām mūlam an ādi nidhana sthitim jñāna jñeyasya munibhiḥ jñāna vidbhiḥ mahātmabhiḥ śrūyatām sa muni śreṣṭhaḥ yat vakṣyati parīkṣite bhāryā sā vasudevasya satya dharma parāyaṇā na ca atuṣyata govindaḥ tatas tām āha bhārgavaḥ aputrā aham dvijaśreṣṭha patyuḥ me nā asti saṃtatiḥ tapaḥ tāvat kariṣyāmi parameṇa samādhinā yāvat ārādhitaḥ viṣṇuḥ dāsyati abhimatam mama tat idam vratam āsthāya toṣaya āśu janārdanam pañcagavya jala snātaḥ pañcagavya kṛta aśanaḥ ghṛtena vācayet vipram gṛhṇīyāt ca tatas vratam adya prabhṛti aham māsam virataḥ prāṇinām vadhāt asatya vacanāt stainyāt madhu māṃsa ādi bhakṣaṇāt para apavāda paiśūnyam para pīḍā karam tathā kṛtvā evam puratas viṣṇoḥ nivṛttim pāpataḥ śubhe naivedyam svayam aśnīyāt maunī nityam udak mukhaḥ mārgaśīrṣe tathā māsi jāti puṣpaiḥ janārdanam dattvā tathā eva gṛhṇīyāt niyamam ca asya rocate sarveṣu eva tu māseṣu pañcagavya ādikam samam puṣpa dhūpa upahāreṣu viśeṣaḥ dakṣiṇāsu ca snāna prāśanayoḥ sāmyam tathā vai naktabhojane arcayet pratimāsam ca yaiḥ puṣpaiḥ tāni me śṛṇu ye ca dhūpāḥ pradātavyāḥ naivedya annam ca yat yadā śvetaiḥ tatas mālikayā tathā mallikayā tatas kārttike mārgaśīrṣe ca dhūpaḥ pauṣe ca candanam māgha phālguna caitreṣu dadyāt viṣṇoḥ tathā agarum vaiśākha ādiṣu māseṣu triṣu devaki bhaktitaḥ karpūram devadevāya guggulam śrāvaṇa ādiṣu kārttika ādiṣu māseṣu paramānnam śubhe triṣu kāsāram māgha pūrveṣu yava annam ca tatas triṣu ghṛtam tilān jala ghaṭān hiraṇyam athavā ajinam pratimāsam tathā dadyāt brāhmaṇāya śubha vrate yathā uktam niyamānām ca grahaṇam pratimāsikam kurvan jagatpatiḥ viṣṇuḥ prīyatām iti mānavaḥ vratena ārādhitaḥ viṣṇuḥ anena jagataḥ patiḥ dadāti abhimatān kāmān alpa kālena bhāmini dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam saubhāgya ārogya dam tathā vratena anena śuddhānām abdena ekena keśavaḥ sukha dṛśyaḥ na saṃdehaḥ dīpena eva agratas sthitaḥ kāya vāc manasaḥ śuddhim karoti etat mahā vratam śuddhānām ca amalaḥ devaḥ dṛśyaḥ eva janārdanaḥ tasmin ekāgra cittānām prāṇinām varavarṇini śuddhi vratam idam tasmāt mahāpātaka nāśanam ārādhanāya kṛṣṇasya kuru devaki pāvanam tasmin cīrṇe hṛṣīkeśaḥ tubhyam dāsyati darśanam dṛṣṭe ca abhimatam yat te tat aśeṣam bhaviṣyati devakī bhārgavasya etat śrutvā vākyam narādhipa śuddhi kāmā cacāra atha sarva kāma pradam vratam vratena ārādhitaḥ tena tadā devyā janārdanaḥ dadau darśanam īśa īśaḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ dṛṣṭe tasmin aśeṣa īśe jagaddhātari keśave kṛtvā praṇāmam āha idam bhakti namrā atha devakī jagatām īśvara īśa īśa jñāna jñeya bhava avyaya pradhāna puṃsoḥ ajayoḥ yaḥ kāraṇam akāraṇam tvam pradhānam pumān ca eva kāraṇa akāraṇa ātmakaḥ prasīda deva devānām ari śātana vāmana aditiḥ tvam mahābhāge bhuvam prāptā surāraṇi tvām aham jagat dhātāram udāra uru parākramam dhārayiṣyāmi garbheṇa katham acyuta śaṃsa me kurvatā vidhṛtāḥ sapta lokāḥ tvam ca ātma māyayā tathā sāṃpratam api etān lokān sa sthāṇu jaṅgamān dhārayiṣyāmi atha ātmānam tvām ca devaki līlayā iti evam uktvā tām devīm devakīm bhagavān prabhuḥ avāpa ca tatas garbham ajāyata ca viśveśaḥ svena aṅgena janārdanaḥ devakī vasudevataḥ pratimāsam ca te pūjām aṣṭamyām yaḥ kariṣyati mama ca eva akhilān kāmān saṃprāpnoti apakalmaṣaḥ nīlotpala dala śyāmam tāmra āyata vilocanam catur bāhum udāra aṅgam śrīvatsa aṅkita vakṣasam tam jātam devakī devam nidhānam sarva tejasām praṇipatya abhituṣṭāva saṃprastuta payodharā abālaḥ bāla rūpeṇa yena īśa tvam iha āsthitaḥ namaḥ te puṇḍarīkākṣa namaḥ te astu janārdana namaḥ te śārṅga cakrā asi gadā parigha pāṇaye upendrāya aprameyāya hṛṣīkeśāya vai namaḥ namaḥ astu te aṇu rūpāya bṛhat rūpāya vai namaḥ aśeṣa bhūta rūpāya tathārūpāya te namaḥ anirdeśya viśeṣāya tubhyam sarva ātmane namaḥ sarveśvarāya sarvāya sarvabhūtāya te namaḥ aśeṣa bhūta rūpāya tathābhūtāya te namaḥ namaḥ astu te aśva rūpāya tathārūpāya te namaḥ anirdeśya viśeṣāya tubhyam sarva ātmane namaḥ viṣṇo namaḥ astu te kṛṣṇa namaḥ te puruṣottama śrīśa śrīvatsa yogi īśa śrī kānta īśa namaḥ astu te māyā vāmana rūpāya tubhyam deva namaḥ namaḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāma bhūtāya veda āharaṇa karmaṇe praṇava udgīta vacase mahā aśva śirase namaḥ niḥkṣatriya urvīkaraṇa vikarāla parākrama paulastya kula nāśāya sādhu mārga vicāriṇe sāṃpratam mad prasannāya saṃbhūtāya mama udare sva māyā bāla rūpāya namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vai hare yāvanti tava rūpāṇi yāvatyaḥ ca vibhūtayaḥ namāmi kṛṣṇa sarvebhyaḥ tebhyaḥ tābhyaḥ ca sarvadā sva rūpa ceṣṭitam yat te yat deva tve viceṣṭitam parameśa pareśa īśa tiryagīśa nareśvara evam stutaḥ tayā devyā devakyā madhusūdanaḥ bāla rūpī jagāda evam vasudevasya śṛṇvataḥ tat kṛtam sakalam bhūyas yat vṛṇoṣi dadāmi tat avatāre tathā eva asmin varṣāṇām adhikam śatam sthāsyāmi nara tām prāptaḥ duṣṭa daitya nibarhaṇaḥ vṛṇomi tat aham nityam tava keśava darśanam na alam viyogam saṃsoḍhum tava aham madhusūdana dākṣāyaṇī tvam aditiḥ saṃbhūtā vasudhā tale ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe tadā pakṣe dine asmin eva bhāmini tvam mām drakṣyasi asaṃdigdham prasādaḥ te kṛtaḥ mayā anena eva mahābhāge bāla rūpeṇa saṃvṛtaḥ tasmin kāle ca lokāḥ tvām pūjayiṣyanti devaki saṃpūjitaḥ aham lokānām tasmin kāle su toṣitaḥ aputrāṇām varān putrān adhanānām tathā dhanam śubhān dārān a dārāṇām sa rogāṇām aroga tām sugatim gati kāmānām vidyām vidyā arthinām api pradāsyasi mahābhāge mad prasāda upavṛṃhitā prasāditāḥ hi martyānām yat tvam dāsyasi śobhane tvām abhyarcya upacāreṇa snāpayitvā ghṛtena mām sarva kāmān avāpsyanti kāle ṣaṣ pakṣa saṃjñite tvad aṅka stham ca mām bālam saṃsmariṣyanti bhaktitaḥ evam pūrvam hṛṣīkeśaḥ devakyāḥ pradadau varam tasmāt kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī puṃsām aśeṣa agha ogha hāriṇī tasyām hi pūjitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ devakī ca samādhinā tat eṣa puṣṭi kāmānām nR̥ṇām puṇya arthinām api upavāsaḥ mahīpāla śastaḥ keśava toṣa daḥ śrāvaṇe śukla pakṣe tu dvādaśyām prīyate nṛpa pauṣa śukle tu tadvat ca dvādaśyām ghṛtadhenukām ghṛtārciḥ prīṇanāya alam pradadyāt phala dāyinīm tathā eva māgha dvādaśyām pradattā tila gauḥ nṛpa keśavam prīṇayati āśu sarva kāmān prayacchati jyaiṣṭhe māsi site pakṣe dvādaśyām jaladhenukā dattā yathāvat vidhinā prīṇayati ambu śāyinam lavaṇam mārgaśīrṣe tu kṛṣṇam abhyarcya yaḥ naraḥ pauṣa māse tu yaḥ dadyāt ghṛtam viprāya pārthiva māgha māse tu saṃpūjya mādhavam brāhmaṇāya yaḥ prayacchati tilān lokān saṃprāpnoti abhivāñchitān phālgune puṇḍarīkākṣam yaḥ samabhyarcya yacchati jyaiṣṭhe abhyarcya hṛṣīkeśam udakumbha pradaḥ hi yaḥ sa parām nirvṛtim yāti sapta janmāntarāṇi vai āṣāḍha māse ca harim yaḥ samabhyarcya yacchati śrāvaṇe navanītam tu sa svargam sukṛtī vrajet chattram ca yaḥ bhādrapade vāsudeva abhipūjakaḥ kāmyāni etāni aśeṣāṇi yaḥ saṃpūjya jagatpatim dānāni yacchati naraḥ sa saṃpūrṇa manorathaḥ sarva śreṣṭhaḥ samastānām bandhūnām āśrayaḥ bhavet evam sarvāṇi dānāni prīṇanāya acyutasya yaḥ prayacchati sa sarveṣām phalānām bhuvi bhājanam yadi icchasi punar prāptum bhūtim abhraṃśanīm nṛpa tat ārādhaya govindam na anyathā syuḥ vibhūtayaḥ evam vasiṣṭhena tadā māndhātā nṛpa bodhitaḥ saha patnyā mahīpālaḥ paritoṣam param yayau saha patnyā nara śreṣṭhaḥ samutthāya varāsanāt an āsajya manaḥ kṛṣṇe viṣaya āsakta cetasaḥ tāḥ niśāḥ te ca divasāḥ te rtavaḥ te ca vatsarāḥ narāṇām saphalāḥ yeṣu cintitaḥ bhagavān hariḥ cintyamānaḥ samastānām pāpānām hāṇidaḥ hi saḥ kaṣṭam muṣṭaḥ asmi śiṣṭeṣu vidyamāneṣu mantriṣu parāṅmukhānām govinde yat prāptam paramam vayaḥ evam vinindya saḥ atmānām māndhātā pṛthivīpatiḥ cakāra ārādhane yatnam devadevasya prāpa siddhim parām pūrvam dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ yathā samārādhaya govindam tam ārādhya na sīdati puṣpa upahāraiḥ dhūpaiḥ ca tathā ca eva anulepanaiḥ vāsobhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ samyak brāhmaṇānām ca tarpaṇaiḥ bhagavan cañcalam cittam manuṣyāṇām aharniśam viṣaya āsaṅga durduṣṭam pāpāya eva pravartate śārīram api akaraṇāt su nivartyam matam mama cañcala tvāt hi cittānām mānasam bahu pātakam bhūmau tṛṇam asaṃkhyātam yathā ca divi tārakāḥ aharniśam manuṣyāṇām sātatyena pravartate tat na asti naraka uttāraḥ varṣa koṭī śataiḥ api tat asya praśamāya alam prāyaścittam narādhipa śṛṇuṣva yena citta uttham sadyas pāpam vyapohati om namaḥ vāsudevāya puruṣāya mahātmane viṣṇave jiṣṇave nityam śāntāya anagha rūpiṇe nārāyaṇāya viśvāya viśveśāya īśvarāya ca keśavāya ati sūkṣmāya brahma mūrtimate namaḥ namaḥ parama kalyāṇa kalyāṇāya ātmayonaye janārdanāya devāya śrīdharāya sumedhase mahātmane vareṇyāya namaḥ paṅkajanābhaye smṛta mātra agha ghātāya kṛṣṇāya akliṣṭa karmaṇe namaḥ natāya namra īśaiḥ aśeṣaiḥ vāsava ādibhiḥ hiraṇyagarbha garbhāya jagataḥ kāraṇa ātmane govindāya ādi bhūtāya śra ādīnām mahātmane namaḥ bhūta ātma bhūtāya ātmane paramātmane dāmodarāya śucaye yajñeśāya namaḥ namaḥ hṛṣīkeśāya ca īśāya sarva bhūta ātma rūpiṇe saṃsāra sāgara uttāra jñāna pota pradāyine karāla saumya rūpāya vaikuṇṭhāya namaḥ namaḥ yathā na viṣṇu bhakteṣu pāpam āpnoti saṃsthitim smṛta mātraḥ yathā viṣṇuḥ sarvam pāpam vyapohati upayātu tathā nāśam mama agham citta saṃbhavam pāpam praṇāśam mama saṃprayātu yat mānasam yat ca karomi vācā śārīram api ācaritam ca yat me smṛte jagaddhātari vāsudeve prayāntu doṣāḥ mama nāśam āśu rāga ādayaḥ kāraṇa kāraṇa īśe nipapāta tad ambhasi tatra āśvāsya kṛta āhlādaḥ papau vāri narādhipa ujjīvayan muni varaḥ jihvā tālu śanais śanais saḥ api kṣatriya dāyādaḥ muni trāṇa parāyaṇaḥ vihāya sa śaram cāpam ujjahāra bisāni atha yayau ca tṛptim vipraḥ api bisa nāla ambu bhakṣaṇāt tam āśvastam kṛta āhāram upaviṣṭam suśītale nyagrodha śākhā saṃchanne niṣpaṅke sarasaḥ taṭe saṃvāhayām āsa ca tam kṣatrabandhuḥ śanais śanais kṛpālukaḥ upakāriṇam ugreṇa karmaṇā tam vidūṣitam api śaknoṣi saṃyantum akārya prasṛtam manaḥ prāṇi pīḍā nivṛttim ca kartum krodha ādi saṃyamam api maitrīm jane kartum śaknoṣi tvam mudhā eva yā aihika āmuṣmikī vīra kriyamāṇā mahā phalā na śaknomi kṣamām kartum na maitrīm mama cetasi prāṇinām avadhāt brahman na asti dāra ādi poṣaṇam anāyattam ca me cittam viṣayān eva dhāvati tad aprāptau ca sarveṣām krodha ādīnām samudbhavaḥ saḥ aham na maitrīm na kṣāntim na hiṃsā ādi vivarjanam tathā api ati kṛpālu tvāt kṣatrabandhum abhāṣata aśakyam uktam bhavatā cañcala tvāt hi cetasaḥ vāc śarīra viniṣpādyam yat śakyam tat udīraya uttiṣṭhatā prasvapatā prasthitena gamiṣyatā govinda iti sadā vācyam kṣuta praskhalita ādiṣu kāryam vartmani mūḍhānām kṣema mārge avatāraṇam hitam ca vācyam pṛṣṭena śatrūṇām api yat yat ca adhvani vimūḍhānām kṛtam vartma avatāraṇam hitam uktam ca pṛṣṭena tasya jāti smṛtiḥ phalam saḥ aham jātismaraḥ bhūyas kariṣyāmi ati saṃkaṭe yasya uccāraṇa mātreṇa jātā jāti smṛtiḥ mama tam eva ārādhayiṣyāmi jagatām īśvaram harim viṣ mūtra pūya kalile garbha vāse atipīḍanāt duḥkham ca jāyamānānām gātra bhaṅga ādi pīḍanāt vātena preryamāṇānām mūrchā kāri ati bhīti dam bāla tve ātmānam ātmanā evam sa proktvā jātismaraḥ dvijaḥ tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ praṇataḥ puruṣottamam praṇipatya akṣaram viśvam viśva hetum nirañjanam kartāram a kṛtam viṣṇum sarva kāraṇa kāraṇam aṇoḥ
