visṛṣṭeḥ amara ādi bhinnaiḥ vikāśam āyāsi vibhūti bhedaiḥ kiṃtu īśa māyā bhavataḥ nijā iyam āviṣkṛta āviṣkṛta loka sṛṣṭe yayā aham eṣaḥ anyatamaḥ mama iti madīyam asya abhivadanti mūḍhāḥ bhūmi ambara agni salileṣu deva jāgrat suṣupta ādiṣu duḥkhitena na santi tāvanti jalāni a pīḍya sarveṣu nātha abdhiṣu sarvakālam stanyāni yāvanti mayā ati ghore pītāni saṃsāra mahā samudre saṃpad śilānām himavat mahendra kailāsa meru ādiṣu nā eva tādṛś na santi te deva bhuvi pradeśāḥ na yeṣu jātaḥ asmi tathā vinaṣṭaḥ attā mayā yeṣu na jantavaḥ ca saṃbhakṣitaḥ yaiḥ ca na jantu saṃghaiḥ siṃhena bhūtvā bahavaḥ mayā āttāḥ vyāghreṇa bhūtvā bahavaḥ mayā āttāḥ tathā anya rūpaiḥ bahavaḥ mayā āttāḥ saṃbhakṣitaḥ aham bahubhiḥ tatas ca utkrānti duḥkhāni ati duḥsahāni sahasraśas yāni anusaṃsmarāmi taiḥ saṃsmṛtaiḥ tat kṣaṇam eva deva taḍit yathā me hṛdayam prayāti tatas ca duḥkhāni anivāraṇāni yantra agni śastra ogha samudbhavāni bhavanti yāni acyuta nārakānām tāni eva teṣām upamāna mātram bhavanti yāni cyavataḥ ca garbhāt teṣām svarūpam gaditum na śakyam duḥkhāni bāleṣu mahanti nātha kaumārake yauvaninaḥ ca puṃsaḥ jvara atisāra akṣi ruj ādikāni samasta duḥkha ālayaḥ eva vṛddhaḥ karoti karma acyuta tad kṣaṇena pāpam naraḥ kāya manaḥ vacobhiḥ yasya abda lakṣaiḥ api na antam eti śastra ādi yantra agni nipīḍaneṣu duḥkhāni yāni iṣṭa viyoga jāni bhavanti saṃsāra vihāra bhājām pratyekaśaḥ teṣu narāḥ vināśam icchanti asūnām mamatā abhibhūtāḥ śoka abhibhūtasya mama aśru deva yāvat pramāṇam na jalam payodā tāvat pramāṇam na jalam payodāḥ muñcanti anekaiḥ api varṣa lakṣaiḥ manye dharitrī paramāṇu saṃkhyām upaiti pitroḥ gaṇa nāma śeṣam mitrāṇi amitrāṇi anujīvi bandhūn saṃkhyātam īśaḥ asmi na devadeva saḥ aham bhṛśa ārtaḥ karuṇām kuru tvam saṃsāra gātre patitasya viṣṇo mām uddhara asmāt uru duḥkha paṅkāt saṃsāra gartāt sva parigraheṇa dharma ātmanām avikalām tvayi nātha bhaktim śraddhāvatām satatam udvahatām vareṇya jñātvā yayā akhilam asāram asāram eva bhūta indriya ādikam apāram amukti mūlam brahma indra rudra marut aśvi divākara ādyāḥ jñātum na yam parama guhyatamam samarthāḥ na tvām alam stuti patheṣu aham īśitāram stoṣyāmi moha kaluṣa alpa matiḥ manuṣyaḥ ittham kṛpām kuru mayi praṇate kila īśa tvām stotum ambuja bhavaḥ api hi deva na īśaḥ bhūmi ambu vāyu gaganam jagatām samuhām stoṣyāmi tam stuti padaiḥ katamaiḥ bhavantam yasya agni rudra kamala udbhava vāsava ādyaiḥ sva aṃśa avatāra karaṇeṣu sadā aṅghri yugmam cittam ca na tvayi samāhitam īśa doṣaiḥ ākṣipyate kathaya kim nu karomi pāpaḥ tat tvam prasīda bhagavan kuru mayi anāthe viṣṇo kṛpām parama kāruṇikaḥ kila tvam saṃsāra bandha bhītena kṛṣṇaḥ pratyakṣa tām yayau sa tam pratyakṣam īśānam anantam aparājitam śirasā dharaṇīm gatvā yata vāc kāya mānasaḥ parāpara īśvaram viṣṇum jiṣṇum ādyam anopamam vara arthinām dvijaśreṣṭha na aphalam mama darśanam janma saṃpad citā deva pāpa saṃpad mama akhilā prayātu nāśam īśa īśa tvad prasādāt adhokṣaja yaḥ stutaḥ asmi kṣayam pāpam tena eva akhilam āgatam yat akṣaram yat acalam vyāpi sūkṣmam ca yat param viśeṣa aiḥ aviśeṣam ca gaccheyam tat padam tava bhūpāla tam dvijaśreṣṭham gataḥ antardhānam īśvaraḥ evam akṣīṇa pāpaḥ api jagatām īśvara īśvaram vyapāśritaḥ harim yāti pāpa muktaḥ param padam etat tvayā na avratine na ca aśuśrūṣave param ākhyeyam rāja śārdūla yaḥ ca nā arcayate harim viṣṇu bhaktāya dāntāya vratine puṇya śīline kathanīyam idam bhūpa rahasyam paramam hareḥ bahuśas bhavatā proktam sāṃpratam ca yat īritam yad svarūpam yad ādhāram yad pramāṇam yad ātmakam sādhu etat bhavatā pṛṣṭam pṛṣṭam ātma jñāna samāśritam tat kathyamānam ekāgraḥ śṛṇu viṣṇoḥ param padam tad svarūpam ca rāja indra śṛṇuṣva iha samāhitaḥ pradhāna ādi viśeṣa antam yat etat paṭhyate jagat janma svapna ādi rūpa ādi duḥkha ādi rahitam ca yat kṣīṇa kleśāḥ tu saṃsāra vimukti patham āśritāḥ paśyatām api anirdeśyam yatas vāc viṣaye na tat brahma prakāśate teṣām tat vareṇa eva sarvagam pradhāna ādi viśeṣa antam yatra etat akhilam jagat tasya anantasya kaḥ śaktaḥ pramāṇam gaditum naraḥ sūkṣmāṇām tat param sūkṣmam sthūlānām tat mahattaram parāṅmukhānām govinde viṣaya ākrānta cetasām teṣām tat paramam brahma dūrāt dūratare sthitam viṣaya tyāginaḥ teṣām vijñeyam ca tat antike sarvatas pāṇi pāda antam sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati bhūta bhartṛ ca tat jñeyam grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca jñānam jñeyam jñāna gamyam hṛdi sarvasi adhiṣṭhitam tat ca ādyaḥ jagatām īśaḥ para īśaḥ parameśvaraḥ parāpara sva rūpeṇa viṣṇuḥ sarva hṛdi sthitaḥ kecid viṣṇum harim kecid kecid keśava saṃjñitam kecid govinda nāmānam puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam kecid viriñcim brāhmaṇam abjayonim tathā apare śarvam īśam ajam rudram śūlinam ca apare nṛpa hiraṇyagarbham kapilam kṣetrajñam kālam īśvaram svabhāvam antarātmānam ātmānam buddhi rūpiṇam vadanti nāmabhiḥ ca anyaiḥ anāmānam arūpiṇam śrūyatām tu nara vyāghra veda vedānta niścayaḥ yajñeśaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa saṃjñitaḥ tat viṣṇoḥ paramam brahma yatas na āvartate punar kṣetrajña ākhyaḥ tathā eva anyāḥ saṃjñābhiḥ procyate budhaiḥ saṃjñā tu tasya na evā asti na rūpam na api kalpanā sa sarva bhūta anugataḥ parama ātmā sanātanaḥ pariṇāmaḥ na tasya asti nirguṇam sarvagam yatas sanātanāt sarva gatāt pariṇāma vivarjitāt katham saṃjāyate kṛtsnam tasmāt apaguṇāt api nimitta kāraṇam pūrvam dvitīyam pariṇāmi ca yathā kumbhasya karaṇe kulālaḥ prathamam nṛpa kāraṇam pariṇāma ākhyam mṛd dravyam aparam smṛtam kāraṇam pariṇāma ākhyam nimitta ākhyam tu tat param kāraṇam kāla gagane yathā saṃnidhi mātrataḥ avikāri tayā brahma tathā sṛṣṭeḥ nareśvara ajñāna paṭalāt śanais eka deśa ātma vṛttibhiḥ yatas saṃbandhavān ebhiḥ aśeṣaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ prabhuḥ tayoḥ svarūpam nṛpate śrūyatām ubhayoḥ api anādi saṃbandhavatyā kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetra vidyayā saṃkṣīna aśeṣa karmā tu param brahma prapaśyati abhedena ātmanaḥ śuddham śuddha tvāt akṣayaḥ akṣayam karmiṇām karma bhedena bhedāt eva ādayaḥ yatas karma kṣayāt aśeṣāṇām bhedānām saṃkṣayaḥ tatas avidyā tu kriyā sarvā vidyā jñānam pracakṣate abhedena tava ākhyātam yat etat brahma śāśvatam jñāna jñeya aikya sadbhāvam tat eva advaita saṃjñitam manasaḥ hi amatībhāve dvaita abhāvāt tat āpnuyāt agrāhi tat ca vidhṛtam yoginām viṣayam prati kṣīṇa kleśāḥ tu saṃsāra vimukti patham āśritāḥ ye api karmāṇi kurvanti bhagavantam apāśritāḥ kriyā yoga parāḥ rājan kāma ākāṅkṣā vivarjitāḥ brahma niṣṭhāḥ dhyāna parāḥ brahmaṇi eva vyavasthitāḥ te api tad bhāvam āyānti vimukti patham āśritāḥ karmaṇaḥ bhāvanā yā iyam sā brahma paripanthinī tādṛś bhavataḥ vijñaptiḥ yādṛśī karma bhāvanā kṣaye tasyāḥ param brahma svayam eva prakāśate yathāvat karma niṣṭhānām tad prāptiḥ kathitam tathā vāsudeva mayasya anyat kim bhūyas kathayāmi te viṣṇuḥ eva jagat dhātā yoginām vartate yatas upāyaḥ tasya yaḥ prāptaḥ viṣṇoḥ īśasya bhārgava yena janma jarā mṛtyu mahā grāha bhava arṇavam tvad vākya nāvam āruhya mukti tīram avāpnuyām tasya apagamane yatnaḥ kāryaḥ saṃsāra bhīruṇā śārīraiḥ ca tathā kleśaiḥ śāstra uktaiḥ tad śamaḥ bhavet devatā stuti sat śāstra śravaṇaiḥ puṇya darśanaiḥ guru śuśrūṣaṇāt ca eva pāpa bandhaḥ praṇaśyati prapā kūpa taḍāgāni devatāyatanāni ca yoginām atha śuśrūṣām tathā eva āvasathāt nṛpa kurvan pūrta āśritam ca anyat pāpa bandhāt pramucyate viṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vāsudevaḥ govindaḥ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ viśvaḥ viśva īśvaraḥ viśva vidhātā dhāma śāśvatam padmanābhaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ keśavaḥ madhusūdanaḥ viṣṇau pratiṣṭhitam viśvam viṣṇuḥ viśve pratiṣṭhitaḥ viṣṇuḥ viśveśvaraḥ viśvam iti bhāvāt pramucyate evam saṃśānta pāpasya puṇya vṛddhimataḥ nṛpa mukti dāyīni karmāṇi niṣkāmena kṛtāni tu nitya naimittikāni iha karmāṇi uktāni yāni vai teṣām niṣkāma kāraṇāt puṇya bandhaḥ praśāmyati aneka janma saṃsāra citasya api dṛḍha ātmanaḥ karma bandhasya śaithilya kāraṇam ca aparam śṛṇu titikṣā sama darśi tvam maitrī ādau daṇḍa saṃyamaḥ ṛju tvam indriya jayaḥ śaucam ācārya pūjanam avivādaḥ tathā mūḍhaiḥ amūḍhaiḥ praśna sat kathā sadbhiḥ saha asya satatam yoga abhyāsaḥ mita ukti tā para yoṣit vilāsānām kāvya ālāpa vivarjanam gīta vādita nṛtteṣu mṛdaṅgeṣu apareṣu ca asṛj māṃsa ādi bhūta tvāt nija deha jugupsanam sarvāṇi etāni bhūtāni viṣṇuḥ iti acalā matiḥ tatra eva aśeṣa bhūta īśe bhaktiḥ avyabhicāriṇī ete guṇāḥ mayā ākhyātāḥ manaḥ nirvṛti kārakāḥ ebhiḥ śāntim gate citte dhyāna ākṛṣṭaḥ sthitaḥ hariḥ śamam nayati karmāṇi sita miśra asitāni vai bhūyas ca śṛṇu śāstra artham saṃkṣepāt vadataḥ mama nitya naimittikānām tu niṣkāmasya hi yā kriyā nisiddhānām sa kāmānām tathā eva akaraṇam nṛpa prayacchati nṛṇām muktim mā te bhūt atra saṃśayaḥ ākhyātam etat akhilam yat pṛṣṭaḥ asi mayā dvija jāyate śama kāmānām praśamaḥ karmaṇām yathā kiṃtu atra bhavatā proktā praśāntiḥ sarva karmaṇām na atyanta nāśaḥ śāntānām udbhavaḥ bhavitā punar nija kāraṇam āsādya stokasya agneḥ yathā tṛṇam na karmaṇām kṣayaḥ bhūpa janmanām ayutaiḥ api karma kṣayam ṛte yogāt yoga agniḥ kṣapayet param tam yogam mama vipra ṛṣe praṇatasya abhiyācataḥ tvam ācakṣva kṣayaḥ yena jāyate akhila karmaṇām pṛṣṭaḥ provāca yam yogam tam samāsena me śṛṇu anādi kāla prasṛtā yathā vidyā mahīpate tam paraṃparayā śrutvā munayaḥ atra dayālavaḥ prakāśayanti bhūtānām upakāra cikīrṣavaḥ devāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ rājan tathā rājarṣayaḥ akhilāḥ śreyaḥ arthinaḥ purā jagmuḥ śaraṇam kapilam kila te tam ūcuḥ bhavān nityam dayāluḥ sarva jantuṣu saḥ asmān uddhara saṃmagnān itas saṃsāra kardamāt yat śreyaḥ sarva varṇānām strīṇām api upakārakam ādau ante ca madhye ca nR̥ṇām yat upakārakam api kīṭa pataṃgānām tat naḥ śreyaḥ param vada na asti yogāt param śreyaḥ kiṃcid iti uktavān purā yathā janma ayutaiḥ kleśāḥ sthairyam cetasi upāgatāḥ saḥ eva abhyasatām nR̥ṇām tīvra saṃvegi cetasām āsanna tām prayāti āśu viṣṇuḥ saṃnyasta karmaṇām brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām strī śūdrasya ca pāvanam śāntaye karmaṇām na anyat yogāt asti hi muktaye yoga svarūpam tat teṣām strī śūdra tve vyavasthitam yoga abhyāsaḥ nṛṇām yeṣām na asti janma antara āhṛtaḥ yogasya prāptaye teṣām śūdra vaiśya ādikaḥ kramaḥ anūcānaḥ tathā yajvī karma nyāsī tatas param yeṣām tu jāti mātreṇa yoga abhyāsaḥ tirohitaḥ yathā vāta īritaḥ kakṣam dahati ūrdhva śikhaḥ analaḥ yathā dagdha tuṣam bījam abīja tvāt na jāyate yoga dagdhaiḥ tathā kleśaiḥ na ātmā saṃjāyate punar adṛṣṭā dṛṣṭa tattvānām yoginām yoga vicyutiḥ yeṣām bhavati yogi tvam prāpnuvanti iha te punar sat jāti prāpakam karma kṛtam tena tad ātmanā jātim prayānti vipra ādyāḥ yoga karma anurañjitāḥ tatra api aneka janma uttha yoga abhyāsa anurañjitāḥ jaigīṣavyaḥ yathā vipraḥ yathā ca eva asita ādayaḥ hiraṇyanābhaḥ rājanyaḥ tathā vai janaka ādayaḥ pūrva abhyastena yogena tulādhāra ādayaḥ viśaḥ saṃprāptāḥ paramām siddhim śūdrāḥ pailavaka ādayaḥ maitreyī sulabhā gārgī śāṇḍilī ca tapasvinī strī tve prāptāḥ parām siddhim anya janma samādhitaḥ varṇa avara tve saṃprāptāḥ saṃsiddhim śravaṇī tathā pūrva abhyastam ca tat teṣām yoga jñānam mahātmanām tat śṛṇuṣva vadāmi eṣa vācyam śuśrūṣatām satām yaḥ dadyāt bhagavat jñānam kuryāt vā dharma deśanām kṛtsnām vā pṛthivīm dadyāt na tad tulyam kathaṃcana kṣayiṣṇūni aparāṇi iha dānāni manuja adhipa ekam eva akṣayam śastam jñāna dānam anuttamam dānāni eka phalāni iha trailokye dadatā satām jñānam prayacchatā samyak kim na dattam bhavet nṛpa jñānāni anyāni asārāṇi śilpinī iva nareśvara ekam eva param jñānam yat yoga prāpti kārakam aham vaktā bhavān śrotā vācyaḥ yogaḥ vimukti daḥ prāṇinām upakārāya saṃpad eṣā guṇa adhikā pareṇa brahmaṇā sārdham ekatvam yat nṛpa ātmanaḥ tayoḥ svarūpam vakṣyāmi tat iha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu sattā mātram param brahma viṣṇu ākhyam a viśeṣaṇam vātālī cañcalam cittam anālambanam asthiti sūkṣma tvāt brahmaṇaḥ rājan agrāhi a grāhya dharmiṇaḥ yadi antarāya doṣeṇa na apakarṣaḥ narādhipa yoginaḥ yoga rūḍhasya tāla agrāt patanam yathā jñānam prayacchatām samyak kim vadatu bhavet nṛpa viṣṇu ākhyam brahma duṣprāpam viṣaya ākṛṣṭa cetasā manuṣyeṇa iti tad prāptau upāyam aparam śṛṇu surūpām pratimām viṣṇoḥ prasanna vadana īkṣaṇām kṛtvā ātmanaḥ prīti karīm suvarṇa rajata ādibhiḥ tasyāḥ ca lakṣaṇam bhūpa śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ mama suvarṇa rūpya tāmraiḥ tu ārakūṭa mayīm tathā śailadāru mṛdā vā api lekhya jām vā api kārayet kāryaḥ tu viṣṇuḥ bhagavān saumya rūpaḥ catur bhujaḥ salila ādhmāta megha ābhaḥ śrīmān śrīvatsa bhūṣitaḥ ābaddha makuṭaḥ sragvī hāra bhāra arpita udaraḥ svakṣeṇa cāru cipukaḥ su lalāṭena subhruṇā kaṇṭhena śubha lekhena vara ābharaṇa dhāriṇā nānā ratna ānata ārtābhyām śravaṇābhyām alaṃkṛtaḥ puṣṭa śliṣṭa āyata bhujaḥ tanu tāmra nakha aṅguliḥ madhyena trivalībhaṅga bhūṣitena ca cāruṇā su pādaḥ su ūru yugalaḥ su kaṭī gulpha jānukaḥ vāma pārśve gadā devī cakram devasya dakṣiṇe ūrdhva dṛṣṭim adhas dṛṣṭim tiryak dṛṣṭim na kārayet nimīlita akṣaḥ bhagavān na praśastaḥ janārdanaḥ saumyā tu dṛṣṭiḥ kartavyā kiṃcid prahasitā iva ca kāryaḥ caraṇa vinyāsaḥ sarvatas su pratiṣṭhitaḥ caraṇa antara saṃsthā ca bibhratī rūpam uttamam kāryā vasuṃdharā devī tad pāda tala dhāriṇī yādṛgvidhā vā manasaḥ sthairya lambhā upapādikā nṛsiṃha vāmana ādīnām tādṛśīm kārayet budhaḥ tām ārcayet tām praṇamet tām smaret tām vicintayet tām arcayan tām praṇaman tām smaran tām ca cintayan viśati apāsta doṣaḥ tu tām eva brahma rūpiṇīm saṃkalpana kriyā ārūḍhaḥ sva rūpeṇa nṛpa ātmanaḥ kurvīta bhāvanām tatra tad bhāva utpatti kāraṇāt yamaiḥ ca niyamaiḥ ca eva pūta ātmā pṛthivīśvara mūrtim bhagavataḥ saṃyak pūjayet tad mayaḥ sadā yamān ca niyamān ca eva śrotum icchāmi bhārgava yamāḥ tava ete kathitāḥ niyamān api me śṛṇu saṃtoṣa śauca svādhyāyāḥ tapaḥ ca īśvara bhāvanā niyamāḥ kaurava śreṣṭha yoga saṃsiddhi hetavaḥ śraddadhānasya ca anyāni yoga aṅgāni nibodha me madhyamaprāṇam acalam sukha dāyi śubham śuci yoga saṃsiddhaye bhūpa yoginām āsanam smṛtam prāṇāyāmaḥ tridhā vāyoḥ prāṇasya hṛdi dhāraṇam ete nibodha mātrāḥ tu na ālambana guṇa anvitāḥ sa ālambanaḥ caturthaḥ anyaḥ bāhya antar viṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ indriyāṇām sva viṣayāt buddhiḥ pratyekaśaḥ tu yat karoti āharaṇam jñeyaḥ pratyāhāraḥ sa paṇḍitaiḥ dhyāna ākhyā labhate rājan samādhim api me śṛṇu kathitāni tava etāni yoga aṅgāni kṛtaiḥ tu yaiḥ yogāṅgāni aṅga bhūtāni dhyānasya etāni aśeṣatas dhyānam eka vratānām tu kuśala akuśaleṣu tat śubha a vyāvartitam dhyānam avivekasya jāyate saṃsāra duḥkha dam rājan aśubha ālambi tat yatas tat eva ākṛṣya duṣṭebhyaḥ viṣayebhyaḥ śubha aśubham sarva saṃsāra kāntāra pāram abhyeti mānavaḥ duḥkha dāgha praśamane yā cintā aharniśam nṛṇām tad dhyānam aviśuddha artham sukha dānām apālane manaḥ vṛttiḥ manuṣyāṇām dhyānam etat śubham dvidhā sukha abhilāṣaḥ yat muktau bandhu duḥkha ādi pīḍanāt a vāñchita phalam lobham a lobha aṃśa vivarjitam śubha aśubha phalam dhyānam a raktam dviṣṭam iṣyate dṛṣṭa anumāna āgamikam dhyānasya ālambanam tridhā na hi nirviṣayam dhyānam mūḍha vṛttiḥ iva iṣyate prāk sthūleṣu padārtheṣu tatas sūkṣmeṣu paṇḍitaḥ dhyānam kurvīta tad paścāt paramāṇau mahīpate kurvīta ālambanam kāle kasmiṃścid api pārthiva prāṇinaḥ karma janita saṃskāra vaśavartinaḥ yatas tatas na te dhyāne dhyāninām upakārakāḥ avidyā antargatāḥ sarve te hi saṃsāra gocarāḥ paścāt udbhūta bodhāḥ ca dhyātāḥ na eva upakārakāḥ dhyeyam dhyāna vidām samyak yat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam tat ca viṣṇoḥ param rūpam anirdeśyam ajam sthiram anidram ajam a svapnam a rūpa a nāma śāśvatam yoginaḥ tam prapaśyanti jñāna dṛśyam sanātanam nirdhūta puṇya pāpāḥ ye te viśanti evam īśvaram tat ca sarva gatam brahma viṣṇuḥ sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ paramātmā paraḥ proktaḥ sarva kāraṇa kāraṇam ananta śaktim īśa īśam sva pratiṣṭham anopamam yatra sarvam yatas sarvam yaḥ sarvam sarvatas ca yaḥ sarga ādi kāraṇam yasya svabhāvāt eva śaktayaḥ nirdhūta puṇya pāpāḥ yam viśanti avyayam īśvaram yat uktam lakṣaṇam tat me gadataḥ śrotum arhasi na anya ālambana sāpekṣam yoginaḥ siddhi kārakam evam ekāgra cittasya puṇya apuṇyam aśeṣatas prayāti saṃkṣayam ṛte deha ārambha kare nṛpa deha ārambha karasya api karmaṇaḥ saṃkṣaya āvahaḥ yaḥ yogaḥ pṛthivīpāla śṛṇu tasya api lakṣaṇam puruṣaḥ kāranā abhāvāt bhedam na eva anupaśyati tad ākhyaḥ tad mayaḥ bhūtvā gṛhyate na viśeṣataḥ na bhedaḥ kalaśa ākāśa nabhasoḥ iva jāyate prakṣīṇa aśeṣa karmā tu yadā brahma mayaḥ pumān ghaṭa dhvaṃse ghaṭa ākāśam na bhinnam nabhasaḥ yathā brahmaṇā heya vidhvaṃse viṣṇu ākhyena pumān tathā bhinne dṛtau yathā vāyuḥ na eva anyaḥ saha vāyunā kṣīṇa puṇya agha bandhaḥ tu tathā ātmā brahmaṇā saha āhlādam anyam atulam kam api āpnoti śāśvatam ādarśasya mala abhāvāt vaimalyam kāśate yathā yathā na kriyate jyotsnā mala prakṣālana ādinā doṣa prahāṇam na jñānam ātmanaḥ kriyate tathā yathā heya gaṇa dhvaṃsāt avabodha ādayaḥ guṇāḥ jñāna vairāgyam aiśvaryam dharmaḥ ca manuja īśvara punar ca śrūyatām eṣa saṃkṣepāt gadataḥ mama nānā dvā ekatva vijñāna svarūpam avanīpate ātmā kṣetrajña saṃjñaḥ ayam saṃyuktaḥ prākṛtaiḥ guṇaiḥ dhyeyam brahma pumān dhyātā upāyaḥ dhyāna saṃjñitaḥ yaḥ tu etat karaṇeṣu āste tad varge kā vibhāga tā saṃkṣepāt api bhūpāla saṃkṣepan aparam śṛṇu putrāya yat pitā brūyāt sva śiṣyāya athavā guruḥ saṃsāra pāram param īpsamānaiḥ ārādhanīyaḥ hariḥ ekaḥ eva ārādhitaḥ arthān dhana kāṅkṣakānām dharma arthinām dharmam aśeṣa dharmī dadāti kāmān ca manaḥ niviṣṭān mokṣa arthinām mukti daḥ eva viṣṇuḥ śūdraḥ vaiśya tvam abhyeti katham vaiśyaḥ ca bhārgava kṣatriya tvam dvijaśreṣṭha brāhmaṇa tvam katham tatas mayā ucyamānam akhilam varṇānām upakārakam śūdra dharmān aśeṣeṇa kurvan śūdraḥ yathāvidhi sarveṣām eva varṇānām svadharmam anuvartatām sadā ucchritiḥ nyūna kṛtaḥ hāniḥ ca utkṛṣṭa karmaṇaḥ teṣām ca brāhmaṇa ādīnām varṇa dharmān anukramāt anasūyā dayā kṣāntiḥ śaucam maṅgalam aspṛhā akārpaṇyam anāyāsaḥ tathā anyaḥ sārvavarṇikaḥ aṣṭau ete guṇāḥ puṃsām paratra iha ca bhūtaye bhavanti kuru śārdūla pṛthak dharmān ca me śṛṇu yajña adhyayana dānāni brahma kṣatra viśām nṛpa sādhāraṇāni teṣām tu jīvikā karma kathyate bhṛtya ādi bharaṇam kuryāt yajñān ca vibhave sati bhṛtya ādi bharaṇe na alam sva vṛttyā hi yadā dvijaḥ tadā jīvet samālambya vṛttim kṣatriya vaiśyayoḥ saṃtyajeta samastān tān na kuryāt vṛtti saṃkaram prajānām pālanam samyak vidhiḥ prathama kalpitaḥ rājanyasya mahīpāla śastra ājīvena vā bhṛtiḥ tasya api āpadi vaiśyasya yā vṛttiḥ sā vidhīyate vāṇijyam vaiśya jātasya paśūnām pālanam kṛṣiḥ dvijāti jana śuśrūṣām kraya vikraya jaiḥ dhanaiḥ śūdraḥ yajet pākayajñaiḥ dadyāt iṣṭāni ca arthinām tasmai śuśrūṣave deyam jīrṇa vastram upānahau caturṇām api varṇānām dharmaḥ te kathitaḥ mayā śṛṇuṣva ca mahīpāla dharmam āśramiṇām atas kṛta upanayanaḥ pūrvam brahmacārī guroḥ gṛhe guru śuśrūṣaṇam kuryāt bhaikṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ guroḥ bhuktavataḥ paścāt na ati svādu mudāvatā vahni śuśrūṣaṇam veda āharaṇam eva ca guroḥ arthe sadā toyam samidh āharaṇam tathā puṣpa ādīnām ca kurvīta supte tasmin śayīta ca āhūtaḥ ca paṭhet tena tad manāḥ na anyatas mukhaḥ vratāni caratā saṃyak grāhyaḥ vedaḥ yata ātmanā daṇḍa vat plavanam snāne śastam na asya aṅga śodhanam adhītya vedān vedau vā vedam vā api yathākramam yathā iṣṭām dakṣiṇām dattvā gurave kuru nandana tatas anujñām samāsādya gṛhastha āśramam āvaset tena eva antam vrajet prājñaḥ tad śuśrūṣaṇa tatparaḥ vānaprastha āśramam tasmāt caturtham vā api saṃśrayet gṛhastha āśrama vṛtti artham avyaṅgām vidhinā nṛpa ākhyāta varṇa dharmeṇa dhanam labdhvā mahīpate kurvīta śraddhayā yuktaḥ nitya naimittikīḥ kriyāḥ abhyāgata atithīn bandhūn bhṛtya ādīn āturān tathā ṛtau upagamaḥ ca eva gṛhasthasya api śabditaḥ dharmaḥ dharma bhṛtām śreṣṭha yajña ucchiṣṭam ca bhojanam havyena prīṇayet devān pitṛn kavyena śaktitas manuṣyān anna pānena svādhyāyena ṛṣi tarpaṇam kuryāt ca prīṇanam nityam bhūtānām bali karmaṇā śubhena karmaṇā ātmānam upadeśena ca ātmajān anujīvi janam vṛtyā gṛhasthaḥ toṣayet sadā tathā eva apara mānebhyaḥ pradeyam gṛhamedhinā annam bhikṣā arthinaḥ ye ca parivrāj brahmacāriṇaḥ evam gṛhāśrame devāḥ pitaraḥ munayaḥ tathā sarva kāmān prayacchanti manuṣyāḥ ca su pūjitāḥ gṛhasthaḥ tu yadā paśyet valī palitam ātmanaḥ apatyasya tathā apatyam tadā araṇyam samāśrayet pitṛ deva atithīnām tu smṛtam tatra api pūjanam tathā eva araṇya bhogaḥ ca tapobhiḥ ca ātma karṣaṇam brahmacaryam mahī śayyā homaḥ triṣavaṇa āplutiḥ mauna ādi karaṇam śastam jaṭā valkala dhāraṇam grīṣme pañcatapobhiḥ ca varṣāsu abhrāvakāśikaiḥ iṅguda eraṇḍa tailena gātra abhyaṅgāni ca iṣyate śyāmāka nīvāra mayam phala mūlaiḥ ca bhojanam apraveśaḥ tathā grāme vānaprastha vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ āśramaṇam tu aparam bhikṣoḥ śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ mama sarva saṅga parityāgaḥ kṣāntiḥ indriya saṃyamaḥ vikāla bhaikṣa caraṇam anārambhaḥ tathā nṛpa ātma jñāna avabodha icchā ātma avalokanam ca eva bhikṣoḥ śastāni pārthiva kramāt vimukti kāmānām puruṣāṇām ayam vidhiḥ evam tu varṇa dharmeṇa tathā ca āśrama karmanā nijena saṃpūjya harim siddhim āpnoti mānavaḥ brahmacārī gṛhasthaḥ ca bhikṣuḥ vaikhānasaḥ tathā yatas hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ brahma ādyāḥ kuru nandana aṃśa bhūtāḥ jagaddhātuḥ viṣṇoḥ avyakta janmanaḥ viśve devāḥ yatas viṣṇuḥ viṣṇuḥ pitṛ gaṇaḥ yatas devāḥ yajñabhujaḥ ca īśaḥ yatas pāpa haraḥ hariḥ viśve bhūtāni bhūtāni yatas viṣṇuḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ tatas sarva āśramāṇām hi pūjyaḥ ekaḥ janārdanaḥ varam vareṇyam vara dam variṣṭham viṣṇum kriyāvān yajate manuṣyaḥ ārādhya yam bhuvana bhāvanam acyuta ākhyam aiśvaryam īpsitam avāpa patiḥ surāṇām kamala ja hara sūrya candra śakraiḥ satatam abhiṣṭutam ādyam īśitāram viṣṇoḥ bhṛgu kula śreṣṭha yat ca dvaite mahātmanaḥ vinivṛtti rūpāḥ yena teṣām yena vadeḥ ha tam sarva īśvara īśvara īśasya yat ca rūpam hareḥ param jagataḥ pālana arthāya durvṛtta nidhanāya ca sva icchayā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ saṃbhavati eva bhū tale turīya aṃśena dharmasya bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ yadā avatāram kṛtavān tadā tad caritam śṛṇu naraḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca eva hariḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tathā eva ca viṣṇoḥ aṃśa aṃśakāḥ hi ete catvāraḥ dharma sūnavaḥ teṣām nārāyaṇa narau gandhamādana parvate ātmani ātmānam ādhāya tepate paramam tapaḥ dhyāyamānau anaupamyam sva kāraṇam akāraṇam tayoḥ tapaḥ prabhāveṇa na tatāpa divākaraḥ vavau ca āśaṅkitaḥ vāyuḥ sukha sparśaḥ hi asarkaraḥ siṃha vyāghra ādayaḥ saumyāḥ ceruḥ saha mṛgaiḥ girau tayoḥ gaurava bhāra ārtā pṛthivī pṛthivīpate cacāla bhūdharāḥ celuḥ cukṣubhuḥ ca mahā abdhayaḥ devāḥ ca sveṣu dhiṣṇyeṣu niṣprabheṣu hata prabhāḥ babhūvuḥ avanīpāla paramam kṣobham āgatāḥ yuyoja apsarasaḥ śubhrāḥ tayoḥ vighna cikīrṣayā alambuṣe miśrakeśi puṇḍarīke varūthini nara nārāyaṇau tatra tapaḥ dīkṣā anvitau dvijau tau asmākam varārohāḥ kurvāṇau paramam tapaḥ karma atiśaya duḥkha ārti pradāvayati nāśakau tat gacchata na bhīḥ kāryā bhavatībhiḥ idam vacaḥ smaraḥ sahāyaḥ bhavitā vasantaḥ ca vara aṅganāḥ rūpam ca vaḥ samālokya madana uddīpanam param bhṛṅga mālā ruta ravaiḥ ramaṇīyam abhūt vanam kiṃnara uraga yakṣāṇām babhūva ghrāṇa tarpaṇaḥ vara aṅganāḥ ca tāḥ sarvāḥ nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī jaguḥ manoharam kāścid nanṛtuḥ ca atra ca aparāḥ avādayan tathā eva anyāḥ manoharataram nṛpa hāvaiḥ bhāvaiḥ smitaiḥ trāsaiḥ tathā anyāḥ valgu bhāṣitaiḥ tayoḥ kṣobhāya tanvaṅgyaḥ cakruḥ udyamam aṅganāḥ tathā api na tayoḥ kaścid manasaḥ pṛthivīpate vikāraḥ abhavat adhyātma pāra saṃprāpta cetasoḥ nivāta sthau yathā dīpau a kampau nṛpa tiṣṭhataḥ pūryamāṇaḥ api ca ambhobhiḥ bhuvam anyām mahā udadhiḥ smaraḥ api na śaśāka atha praveṣṭum hṛdayam tayoḥ puṣpa ujjvalān taru varān vasantam dakṣiṇa anilam tāḥ ca eva apsarasaḥ sarvāḥ kandarpam ca mahā munī yat ca ārabdham tapaḥ tābhyām ātmānam gandhamādanam dadṛśāte akhilam rūpam brahmaṇaḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha dāhāya na analaḥ vahneḥ na apaḥ kledāya ca ambhasaḥ tatas vijñāna vijñāta para brahma svarūpayoḥ cakrāte tāḥ ca tanvaṅgyaḥ tad kṣobhāya punar punar atha nārāyaṇaḥ dhairya gāmbhīrya udārya mānasaḥ ūroḥ utpādayām āsa tām vara ūru balām tadā guṇa lāghavam abhyeti yasyāḥ saṃdarśanāt anu tām vilokya mahīpāla cakampe mādhava anilam vasantaḥ vismayam yātaḥ saṃyātaḥ saṃsmaram smaraḥ rambhā tilottamā ādyāḥ ca vilakṣāḥ deva yoṣitaḥ na rejuḥ avanīpāla tad lakṣa hṛdaya īkṣaṇāḥ tatas kāmaḥ vasantaḥ ca pārthiva apsarasaḥ ca tāḥ mohitāḥ sma vijānīmaḥ na antaram vandya nindyayoḥ dhāma bhūtasya lokānām anādeḥ atra tiṣṭhati nara nārāyaṇau devau śārṅga cakra āyudhau ubhau āstām prasāda su mukhau asmākam aparādhinām nidhānam sarva vidyānām sarva pāpa indhana analaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ naḥ bhagavān sarva pāpam vyapohatu śārṅga cakra āyudhaḥ śrīmān ātma jñāna mayaḥ anaghaḥ naraḥ samasta pāpāni hatvā ātmā sarva dehinām jaṭā kalāpa bandhaḥ ayam anayoḥ akṣaya ātmanoḥ saumyā ca dṛṣṭiḥ pāpāni hantu sarvāṇi naḥ śubhā prasīdatu naraḥ asmākam tathā nārāyaṇaḥ avyayaḥ kva naḥ śarīrakāṇi īdṛś miśra karma citāni vai tathā api avidyā duṣṭena manasā yaḥ kṛtaḥ hi vām asmābhiḥ aparādhaḥ ayam kṣamyatām su mahā dyutī śaraṇam ca prapannānām tava asmi iti ca vādinām prasādam pitṛ hantR̥ṇām api kurvanti sādhavaḥ eṣaḥ eva varaḥ asmākam a viveka āhṛtaḥ mahān prasīda deva vijñāna ghana mūḍha dṛśām api dṛṣṭvā etat naḥ samutpannam yathā strī ratnam īdṛśam tvayi nārāyaṇa utpannā śreṣṭhā pāravatī matiḥ nārāyaṇa prasīda iti sarva loka parāyaṇa namasyāmaḥ naram devam tathā nārāyaṇam harim namaḥ narāya namyāya namaḥ nārāyaṇāya ca prasannānām anāthānām aparādhavatām prabhuḥ śam karotu naraḥ asmākam śam nārāyaṇa dehi naḥ prāha īśaḥ sarva bhūtānām sādhyaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ nṛpa yat kāryam āgatānām vaḥ iha asmābhiḥ tat ucyatām yūyam saṃsiddhaye nūnam asmākam valaśatruṇā saṃpreṣitāḥ tatas asmākam nṛtta geya ādi darśitam na vayam nṛtta gītena na aṅga ceṣṭā ādi bhāṣitaiḥ lubhyāmaḥ viṣataḥ manye viṣayāḥ dāruṇa ātmakāḥ śabda ādi saṅga duṣṭāni yadā na akṣāṇi naḥ śubhāḥ tadā nṛtta ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ katham lobha pradāyinaḥ te siddhāḥ sma na vai sādhyāḥ bhavatīnām smarasya ca mādhavasya ca śakraḥ api svāsthyam yātu a viśaṅkitaḥ yaḥ asau parasmāt paramaḥ puruṣāt parameśvaraḥ paramātmā hṛṣīkeśaḥ sthāvarasya carasya ca sa sarva vāsi deva tvāt vāsudeva iti udāhṛtaḥ vayam aṃśa aṃśakāḥ tasya catur vyūhasya māyinaḥ tam sarva bhūtam sarva īśam sarvatra sama darśinaḥ paśyantaḥ kutra rāga ādīn kariṣyāmaḥ vibhedakān yadā saḥ eva viśvātmā tadā dveṣa ādayaḥ katham pṛthivī āpaḥ tathā tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam eva ca tathā indriyāṇi ahaṃkāraḥ buddhiḥ ca na pṛthak yatas sama dṛṣṭiḥ yatas kutra rāga dveṣau pravartataḥ ātmā ca ayam abhedena yatas sarveṣu jantuṣu sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ viṣṇuḥ kutra rāga ādayaḥ tatas brahmāṇam indram īśānam ādityān marutaḥ akhilān viśvedevān ṛṣīn sādhyān vasūn pitṛ gaṇān tathā yakṣa rākṣasa bhūta ādīn nāga sarpa sarīsṛpān makṣikā maśaka ādaṃśān śalabhān alasān kṛmīn gulma vṛkṣa latā valli tvaksāra tṛṇa jāti jān yat ca kiṃcid adṛśyam vā dṛśyam vā tridaśa aṅganāḥ jānamānaḥ katham viṣṇum ātmānam paramam ca yat rāga dveṣau tathā lobham kaḥ kuryāt amara aṅganāḥ nipātyatām pṛthak bhūte kutra rāga ādikaḥ gaṇaḥ evam asmāsu yuṣmāsu sarva bhūteṣu ca abalāḥ tad maya tva eka bhūteṣu rāga ādi avasaraḥ kutas bhūta indriya antaḥkaraṇa pradhāna puruṣa ātmakam yathā agneḥ arciṣaḥ pītāḥ piṅgala aruṇa dhūsarāḥ bhavatībhiḥ ca yat kṣobham asmākam sa puraṃdaraḥ bhavatyaḥ sa ca devendraḥ lokāḥ ca sa sura asurāḥ yathā iyam cāru sarva aṅgī bhavatīnām mayoḥ utas darśitā darśayiṣyāmi tathā atra eva akhilam jagat yūyam ca mā smayam yāta santi rūpa anvitāḥ striyaḥ kim surūpam kurūpam vā yadā bhedaḥ na dṛśyate tāratamyam surūpa tve satatam bhinnadarśinām bhavatīnām smayam matvā rūpa audārya guṇa udbhavam yasmāt mad ūroḥ udbhūtā iyam indīvara īkṣaṇā urvaśī nāma kalyāṇī bhaviṣyati tatas apsarāḥ tat iyam devarājāya nīyatām varavarṇinī bhavatyaḥ tena ca asmākam preṣitāḥ prītim icchatā vaktavyaḥ ca sahasrākṣaḥ na asmākam bhoga kāraṇāt tapaḥ caryāḥ na ca a prāpya phalam prāptum abhīpsitam yadi kaścid tava ābādhām karoti tridaśeśvara tam aham vārayiṣyāmi nirvṛtaḥ bhava vāsava kartāsi ced tvam ābādhām aduṣṭasya iha kasyacid tava api śāstā etat aham pravartiṣyāmi asaṃśayam etat jñātvā na saṃtāpaḥ tvayā kāryaḥ hi mām prati upakārāya jagatām avatīrṇaḥ asmi vāsava yā ca iyam urvaśī mattaḥ samudbhūtā puraṃdara iti ukte apsarasaḥ sarvāḥ praṇipatya ati vismitāḥ ūcuḥ nārāyaṇam devam tad darśana kutūhalāḥ proktaḥ sa sarvaḥ vijñātaḥ māhātmyam viditam ca te darśitā iyam viśāla akṣī darśayiṣyāmi vaḥ jagat darśaya ātmānam akhilam darśitā iyam yathā urvaśī yadi deva aparāddheṣu na asmāsu kupitam tava manaḥ tat jagatam īśa darśaya ātmānam ātmanā paśyata iha akhilān lokān mama dehe sura aṅganāḥ madhum madanam ātmānam yat ca anyat draṣṭum icchatha iti uktvā bhagavān devaḥ tadā nārāyaṇaḥ nṛpa brahmā prajāpatiḥ śakraḥ saha rudraiḥ pinākadhṛk ādityāḥ vasavaḥ sādhyāḥ viśvedevāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ nāsatya dasrau anilāḥ sarve sarve tathā agnayaḥ yakṣa gandharva siddhāḥ ca piśācāḥ kiṃnara uragāḥ samasta apsarasaḥ vidyāḥ sa aṅgāḥ vedāḥ tad uktayaḥ manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ kīṭāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ pādapāḥ tathā sarīsṛpāḥ ca ye sūkṣmāḥ yat ca anyat jīva saṃjñitam samudrāḥ sakalāḥ śailāḥ saritaḥ kānanāni ca dvīpāni aśeṣāṇi tathā nadāḥ sarva sarāṃsi ca nagara grāma pūrṇā ca medinī medinīpate deva aṅganābhiḥ devasya dehe dṛṣṭam mahātmanaḥ dadṛśuḥ tāḥ su cāru aṅgyaḥ tasya antar viśva rūpiṇaḥ na ūrdhvam na tiryak na adhas ca yadā antaḥ tasya dṛśyate madanena samam sarvāḥ madhunā ca sura aṅganāḥ sa sādhvasāḥ bhaktimatyaḥ param vismayam āgatāḥ paśyāma na ādim tava deva na antam na madhyam avyākṛta rūpa pāram parāyaṇam tvā jagatām anantam natāḥ sma nārāyaṇam ātma bhūtam mahī divam vāyu jala agnayaḥ tvam śabda ādi rūpaḥ ca parāpara ātman draṣṭā asi rūpasya rasasya vettā śrotā ca śabdasya hare tvam ekaḥ spraṣṭā bhavān spraśavataḥ akhilasya ghrātā asi gandhasya pṛthak śarīrī rudra antaka ādīni ca raudravatsu rūpeṣu rūpāṇi tava uttamāni kṣamā dhaneṣu kṣiti rūpam agryam rūpam tava agryam balavatsu vāyuḥ manuṣya rūpam tava rājaseṣu mūḍheṣu sarveśvara pādapaḥ asi dṛśya sva rūpaḥ ca hutāśane tvam sparśa sva rūpaḥ bhagavān samīre paśyāma te nābhi saroja madhye brahmāṇam etam ca haram bhrukūṭyam tatra aśvinau karṇa gatau samastān avasthitān bāhuṣu lokapālān pādau dharitrīm jaṭharam samastān lokān hṛṣīkeśa vilokayāmaḥ jaṅghe viyat pāda kara aṅgulīṣu piśāca rakṣa uraga siddha saṅghān puṃstve prajānām patiḥ oṣṭha yugme pratiṣṭhitāḥ te kratavaḥ samastāḥ sarvā iṣṭayaḥ te daśaneṣu deva daṃṣṭṛāsu vidyā bhavataḥ catasraḥ romasu aśeṣāḥ tava deva saṅghāḥ vidyādharāḥ nātha kara aṅghri rekhāḥ sa aṅghāḥ samastāḥ tava deva vedāḥ samāsthitāḥ bahuṣu saṃdhi bhūtāḥ varāha rūpam dharaṇī dhṛtaḥ te nṛsiṃha rūpam ca saṭā karālam amī samudrāḥ tava deva dehe meru ādayaḥ śaila varāḥ tava amī imāḥ ca gaṅgā pramukhāḥ sravatyaḥ dvīpāni aśeṣāṇi vanāni ca eva tvām īśitāram jagatām anantam yajñeśam arcanti ca yajvinaḥ amī tvattaḥ na śītam na ca keśava uṣṇam sarva sva rūpa atiśayī tvam ekaḥ kim vā aparāddham tava deva mūḍhaiḥ yat māyayā naḥ hṛdayam tathā api pāpa avaśam kim praṇata ārti hārin manaḥ hi naḥ viṅkala tām upaiti tat kṣamyatām sṛṣṭikaraḥ tava eva deva aparādham sṛjataḥ vivekān tvad nāma smaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣam naḥ praṇaśyatu tvad nāma smaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣam naḥ praṇaśyatu namaḥ namaḥ te vaikuṇṭha śrīvatsa aṅka abja locana vareṇya yajñapuruṣa prajāpālaka vāmana tvad nāma smaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣam naḥ praṇaśyatu saṃsāra arṇava potāya namaḥ tubhyam adhokṣaja tvad nāma smaraṇāt pāpam aśeṣam naḥ praṇaśyatu namaḥ parasmai śrīśāya vāsudevāya vedhase upasaṃhāra viśvātman rūpam etat samantataḥ vardhamānam na naḥ draṣṭum samartham cakṣuḥ īśvara pramāṇena diśaḥ bhūmiḥ gaganam ca samāvṛtam sarvam jagat iha ekastham piṇḍitam lakṣayāmahe kim varṇayāmaḥ rūpam te kim pramāṇam idam hare māhātmyam kiṃtu te deva jihvāyāḥ yat na gocaram vaktrāṇām ayutena api buddhīnām ayuta ayutaiḥ guṇānām varṇanam nātha tava vaktum na śakyate tat etat darśitam rūpam prasādaḥ paramaḥ kṛtaḥ divya jñāna upapannānām tāsām pratyakṣam īśvaraḥ viveśa sarva bhūtāni svaiḥ aṃśaiḥ bhūtabhāvanaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sarva bhūteṣu līyamānam adhokṣajam vismayam paramam jagmuḥ samastāḥ deva yoṣitaḥ sa ca sarva īśvaraḥ śailān pādapān sāgarān bhuvam jalam agnim tathā vāyum ākāśam ca viveśa ha kāle dikṣu atha sarvātmā manuṣya ātmani atha api ca ātma rūpaḥ sthitaḥ svena mahimnā bhāvayan jagat deva dānava rakṣāṃsi yakṣa vidyādhara uragān manuṣya paśu kīṭa ādīn mṛga pakṣi antarikṣa gān ye antarikṣe tathā bhūmau divi ye ye jala āśrayāḥ tān praviśya sa viśvātmā punar tat rūpam āsthitaḥ nareṇa sārcham yat tābhiḥ dṛṣṭa pūrvam ariṃdama tāḥ param vismayam gatvā sarvāḥ tridaśa yoṣitaḥ praṇemuḥ sādhyasāḥ pāṇḍu vadanāḥ nṛpa sattama nārāyaṇaḥ api bhagavān āha tāḥ tridaśa aṅganāḥ nīyatām urvaśī bhadrā yatra āste tridaśeśvaraḥ bhavatīnām hita arthāya sarva bhūteṣu asau iti jñānam utpāditam bhūyaḥ layam bhūteṣu kurvatā tam ajam sarva bhūta īśam jānīta paramam padam aham bhavatyaḥ devāḥ ca manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ ca ye devadevasya vistṛtiḥ etat jñātvā samam sargam sa deva asura mānuṣam sa paśu ādi gaṇam ca eva draṣṭavyam tridaśa aṅganāḥ praṇamya tau sa madanāḥ sa vasantāḥ ca pārthiva ādāya ca urvaśīm bhūyas devarājam upāgatāḥ ācakhyuḥ ca yathāvṛttam devarājāya tat tathā jānan evam aśeṣeṣu bhūteṣu parameśvaram vāsudevam katham doṣān lobha ādīn na prahāsyasi sarva bhūtāni govindāt yadā na anyāni bhūpate tadā vaira ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ kriyatām kutra pārthiva iha paśyan jagat sarvam vāsudeva ātmakam nṛpa etat eva hi kṛṣṇena rūpam āviṣkṛtam tadā janma ādi bhāva rahitam tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam saṃkṣepeṇa ca bhūpāla śrūyatām yat vadāmi te yat matau puruṣaḥ kṛtvā param nirvāṇam ṛcchati sarvam viṣṇuḥ samastau hi bhāva abhāvau ca tad mayau sat asat sarvam īśa īśaḥ vāsudevaḥ param padam bhava jaladhi gatānām dvandva vāta āhatānām suta duhitṛ kalatra trāṇa bhāra arditānām viṣama viṣaya toye majjatām aplavānām bhavati śaraṇam ekaḥ viṣṇu potaḥ narāṇām svarūpam ca jagaddhātuḥ ārādhana viniścayaḥ ārādhitāt phalam yat ca keśavāt prāpyate naraiḥ kathitaḥ ca mahābhāga dānānām vistarāt vidhiḥ saḥ eṣa sarva pravaraḥ sarva bhūtaḥ ca mādhavaḥ tri yugam puṇḍarīkākṣam apavarga mahā hradam tri yugena tadā viṣṇoḥ kriyate kim viśeṣaṇam kṛtam tretā dvāparam ca kaliḥ ca iti caturyugam yadā jagati vikhyātam tadā tri yuga tā kutas sādhu pṛṣṭaḥ asmi bhūpāla bhavatā tri yuga āśritam kāṣṭhā pārthiva vijñeyā nimeṣāḥ daśa pañca ca kāṣṭhātriṃśat kalāḥ jñeyāḥ muhūrtam tāvatīḥ kalāḥ triṃśat muhūrtāḥ bhūpāla tathā ahorātram ucyate ayanam dakṣiṇam māsāḥ ṣaṭ māsāḥ ca tathā uttaram ayana dvitaya ākhyaḥ ca kālaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇam tu ayanam rātriḥ devānām uttaram dinam śata trayeṇa varṣāṇām ṣaṣṭyā ca pṛthivīpate manuṣya saṃkhyayā varṣam devānām api gaṇyate catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām kṛtam ucyate tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ tretā trīṇi sahasrāṇi divya abdānām nara ṛṣabha tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ dvāparam dve sahasre tu varṣāṇām abhidhīyate tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ kaliḥ sahasram ekam tu divya abdānām nara ṛṣabha tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ kṛtam nāma yugam pūrvam yatra dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ na tatra dharmāḥ sīdanti na ca kṣīyanti vai prajāḥ tatas kṛta yugam nāma guṇataḥ procyate yugam deva dānava gandharvāḥ yakṣa rākṣasa pannagāḥ na sāma yajuḥ ṛk varṇāḥ kriyā na āsīt ca mānavī na asūyā na api ruditam na darpaḥ na api paiśunam na bhayam na api saṃtāpaḥ na ca īrṣyā na api matsaraḥ tatas paramakam brahma yā gatiḥ yoginām parā ātmā ca sarva bhūtānām śuklaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ tadā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca kṛta lakṣaṇāḥ kṛte yuge bhavanti iha sva karma niratāḥ prajāḥ svam āśramam svam ācāram samyak jñāna samanvitam catur āśrama yuktena karmaṇā kāla yoginā a kāma phala saṃyogāt prāpnuvanti parām gatim ātma yoga samāyuktaḥ dharmaḥ ayam kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ kṛte yuge catuṣpādaḥ caturvarṇyasya śāśvataḥ tretām api nibodha tvam yādṛś rūpam pravartate pādena hrasate dharmaḥ rakta tām yāti ca acyutaḥ satya pravṛttāḥ ca narāḥ kriyā dharma parāyaṇāḥ tatas yajñāḥ pravartante dharmāḥ ca vividhāḥ kriyāḥ tretāyām bhāva saṃkalpāḥ kriyā dāna phala udayāḥ pracaranti tatas varṇāḥ tapaḥ dāna parāyaṇāḥ sva karma sthāḥ kriyāvantaḥ sama tvāt rajasā anvitāḥ dvi vedāḥ ca eka vedāḥ ca anṛcaḥ ca tathā apare evam śāstreṣu bhinneṣu bahudhā nīyate kriyā tapaḥ dāna pravṛttā ca rājasī bhavati prajā alpa āyuṣaḥ narāḥ vedaḥ su mahān ca iti dustaraḥ karoti bahudhā vedān vyāsa rūpī tadā hariḥ kāmāḥ ca upadravāḥ ca eva tadā daivata kāritāḥ yaiḥ ardyamānāḥ su bhṛśam tapaḥ tapyanti mānavāḥ dhana kāmāḥ svarga kāmāḥ yajñān tanvanti ca apare evam dvāparam āsādya prajāḥ kṣīyanti adharmataḥ tāmasam yugam āsādya kṛṣṇaḥ bhavati keśavaḥ vrata ācārāḥ praśāmyanti dharma yajña kriyāḥ tathā ītayaḥ vyādhayaḥ tandrī doṣāḥ krodha ādayaḥ tathā upadravāḥ ca vardhante manaḥ tāpāḥ ca saṃgatāḥ yugeṣu āvartamāneṣu lokaḥ vyāvartate punar loke kṣīṇe kṣayam yānti bhāvāḥ loka kriyā yajñān manaḥ yajñān tatas narāḥ tatas sthūlataraḥ panthāḥ dāna ātmā kriyate naraiḥ yathā satyam tathā kṣāntiḥ ahiṃsā ca kalau yuge para upatāpāt viratiḥ narāṇām upakārikā tasmin ghore yuge prāpte kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇa tvam āgate yādṛś rūpam jagat idam bhavati iha śṛṇuṣva tat rājānaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca manuja īśvara vyāja dharma parāḥ ca eva dharmavaitaṃsikāḥ janāḥ satyam saṃkṣipyate loke naraiḥ paṇḍita mānibhiḥ satya hānyā tatas teṣām su alpam āyuḥ bhaviṣyati āyuṣaḥ prakṣayāt vidyām na śakṣyanti upaśikṣitum vidyā hīnān abuddhīn tān lobhaḥ api abhibhaviṣyati lobha krodha parāḥ mūḍhāḥ kāma vaśyāḥ ca mānavāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ saṃkīryantaḥ parasparam śūdra tulyāḥ bhaviṣyanti tapaḥ satya vinākṛtāḥ antyāḥ madhyāḥ bhaviṣyanti madhyāḥ ca antāvasāyinaḥ īdṛśaḥ bhavitā lokaḥ kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇa tvam āgate vastrāṇām pravarā śāṇī dhānyānām koradūṣakaḥ bhāryā mitrāḥ ca puruṣāḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge matsya āmiṣeṇa jīvantaḥ duhantaḥ ca api ajāvikāḥ goṣu naṣṭāsu puruṣāḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā nṛpa sarit tīreṣu kuddālaiḥ vāpayiṣyanti ca oṣadhīḥ tāḥ ca api alpa phalāḥ teṣām bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye a niṣkrāntāḥ tu saṃbandhāḥ sva gotrāt puruṣa ṛṣabha a niṣkrāntāni śrāddhāni bhaviṣyanti ca gehataḥ na vratāni cariṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ veda nindakāḥ prāyaśas kṛpaṇānām ca tathā bandhimatām api vidhavānām ca vittāni hariṣyanti bala anvitāḥ anyāya upātta vitteṣu kariṣyanti narāḥ spṛhām veśyā bhujaḥ devāḥ ye veda paṭhitāḥ dvijāḥ brahma ādyāḥ tān parityajya narāḥ kāla balātkṛtāḥ hetuvāda parāḥ devān kariṣyanti aparān tadā ye yava annāḥ janapadāḥ godhūma annāḥ tathā eva ca tān deśān prāpte kṛṣṇe kārṣṇya upalakṣite vinindām prathame pāde kariṣyanti hareḥ narāḥ yuga ante tu hareḥ nāma na eva kaścid gṛhīṣyati dhanyāḥ te puruṣa vyāghra pāpa ambhodhau a pāpinaḥ ye nāma api kalau viṣṇoḥ gṛhīṣyanti akṣaya ātmanaḥ bahu pāṣaṇḍa saṃkīrṇe jagati asmin kalau yuge kṛṣṇāya iti namaḥ astu atra sukṛtī yadi vakṣyati pāṣaṇḍinaḥ kariṣyanti cāturāśramya dūṣakāḥ pāṣaṇḍa bhūtam atyartham jagat etat asatkṛtam bhaviṣyati tadā bhūpa vṛthā pravrajita utkaṭam na tu dvijāti śuśrūṣām na svadharma anupālanam kariṣyanti tadā śūdrāḥ pravrajyā liṅginaḥ vṛthā utkocāḥ saugatāḥ ca eva mahāyāna bhojanāḥ bhaviṣyanti durātmānaḥ śūdrāḥ pravrajitāḥ tadā ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabha brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ bhaviṣyanti tathā pare rāja śulka harāḥ kṣudrāḥ gṛhastha parimoṣakāḥ muni veṣa ākṛti channāḥ vāṇijyam upajīvikāḥ na dvijān na kalau devān pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ mleccha bhāṣā nibandhaiḥ tu hetuvādaiḥ vikūlitāḥ evam teṣu ati duṣṭeṣu vimārga pathivartinaḥ bhaviṣyanti apare duṣṭāḥ teṣām mārga anuyāyinaḥ a saṃskṛta ukti vaktāraḥ veda śāstra vinindakāḥ jagat unmārga kartāraḥ bhaviṣyanti tadā narāḥ jagatī atra tadā nR̥ṇām su alpam āyuḥ bhaviṣyati parama āyuḥ ca bhavitā tadā varṣāṇi ṣoḍaśa tatas prāṇān prahāsyanti kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇa tvam āgate pañcame vā atha ṣaṣṭhe vā varṣe kanyā prasūyate sapta varṣa aṣṭa varṣāḥ vā narāḥ tadā alpa dravyāḥ vṛthāliṅgāḥ hiṃsā rati parāyaṇāḥ hartāraḥ na tu dātāraḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau narāḥ śukla ādāna parāḥ kṣudrāḥ para pāka āśinaḥ dvijāḥ vaiśyāḥ tathā tu rājānaḥ na tu kṣatriya vaṃśa jāḥ śūdrāḥ bhikṣavatā viprāḥ śuśrūṣā vipaṇa āśritāḥ bhaviṣyanti nṛpa śreṣṭha kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇa tvam āgate na śiṣyaḥ na guruḥ kaścid na putraḥ na pitā tathā etat kāla svarūpam te śatānīka mayā uditam viṣṇu bhaktān nara śreṣṭha na narān bādhate kaliḥ ye tad manaskāḥ tiṣṭhanti prayāntaḥ saṃsthitāḥ tathā yasya bhāvaḥ na tam bhūpa kadācid bādhate kaliḥ kali prabhāvaḥ duṣṭa uktiḥ pāṣaṇḍānām tathā uktayaḥ an iṣṭvā api mahāyajñaiḥ a kṛtvā api pitṛ svadhām kṛṣṇam abhyarcya yat bhaktyā na enam śvomaraṇam tapet yasya agratas tathā pṛṣṭhe gacchataḥ tiṣṭhataḥ api vā govinde niyatam cetaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ sadā eva saḥ śaraṇyam śaraṇam gacchan govindam na avasīdati kali kalmaṣa kakṣa agnim nirvāṇam padam avyayam sarva kāraṇam avyaktam viṣṇum dhyāyan na sīdati yatra arcite arcanīyaḥ ca jāyate tam namāmi aham jagatsraṣṭāram iśa īśam anādim paratas param aśeṣa agha haram viṣṇum hari varṇam harim namaḥ yad kīrtanāt aghaḥ śuddhaḥ smṛte yatra aśuciḥ suciḥ tam ātmani sthitam bhūpa puṇḍarīkekṣaṇam namaḥ yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣam sa bāhya abhyantaraḥ śuciḥ tathā api saṃsmaran viṣṇum sa bāhya abhyantaraḥ śuciḥ kalau atra ati doṣa āḍhye viṣaya āsakta mānasaḥ kṛtvā api pāpam govindam dhyāyan pāpaiḥ vimucyate tat dhyānam yatra govindaḥ sā kathā yatra keśavaḥ na etat pitā tanūjāya na śiṣyāya guruḥ nṛpa suhṛdaḥ ca tathivā anye na upadeśaḥ nṛpa īdṛśaḥ upadeṣṭā paraḥ bandhuḥ īdṛśaḥ yaḥ vimuktaye yaḥ nā ekāgra manāḥ viṣṇau iti jñātvā api pārthiva upadeśa pradānena saṃbhūti traye āsuraḥ na eva viṣṇu paraḥ bhūpa bhavati akṣīṇa kalmaṣaḥ hetuvāda āśritaḥ mūḍhaḥ dadāti uttaram akṣayam āsurasya api tanmātrā jāyate nṛpate matiḥ tvayā acyutāt matiḥ bhūpa na apaneyā kathaṃcana a prāpya vāñchati ratim sarvadā eva nṛṇām manaḥ sukha prīti karam nR̥ṇām patatām nirvṛti pradam yeṣām gṛheṣu likhitam etat sthāsyati nityadā na tad gṛhāṇi daiva utthāḥ bādhiṣyante hi upadravāḥ kim tīrthaiḥ kim pradānaiḥ vā kim yajñaiḥ kim upoṣitaiḥ śṛṇoti ślokam ekam ca dharmasya asya samam hi tat adhyāya pāraṇam ca asya go pradānāt viśiṣyate śṛṇvan ca asya daśa adhyāyān sadyas pāpaiḥ pramucyate śrotum vāñchā samastam tat pārthivasya vyapohati kapilānām śate datte yat bhavet jyeṣṭhapuṣkare narendra viṣṇu dharmāṇām tat avāpnoti pāraṇe na asti anyat viṣṇu dhamāṇām sadṛśam śāstram uttamam paṭhan anudinam dharmān etān śṛṇvan tathā api vā bhaktyā matimatām śreṣṭha sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate na garbha hāriṇī bhītiḥ na ca bālagrahāḥ gṛhe śṛṇvan vipraḥ veda vid syāt kṣatriyaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ṛddhim prayāti vaiśyaḥ ca śūdraḥ ca ārogyam ṛcchati viṣṇau manaḥ samāveśya sarvatra samadarśanaḥ tasya pāpam tathā rogān duḥsvapna ādya abhicārukān hemante yaḥ imān dharmān śṛṇoti vasudhādhipa śiśire ca nara vyāghra yaḥ śṛṇoti yathāvidhi puṇḍarīkasya yajñasya sa prāpnoti phalam naraḥ madhu mādhava saṃjñe tu yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ tu imān śṛṇvan etān nidāghe ca dharmān dharma bhṛtām vara varṣāsu ca imān yaḥ dharmān saṃśṛṇvan vasudhādhipa rājasūya kratoḥ puṇyam akhilam samavāpnuyāt śarad kāle ca saṃśṛṇvan dharmān etān nara ṛṣabha ṛtuṣu eteṣu etat eva paṭhatām api pārthiva phalam bhavati duṣṭeṣu graheṣu ete śubha pradāḥ kapilānām śatasya uktam yat phalam jyeṣṭhapuṣkare bhūyaḥ bhūyaḥ tat āpnoti pāraṇe pāraṇe gate saḥ arcayati avanīpāla jñāna yajñena keśavam sarva ābādhāḥ tathā pāpam akhilam manuja īśvara viṣṇu dharmāḥ vyapohanti saṃsmṛtāḥ paṭhitāḥ śrutāḥ etat te sarvam ākhyātam rahasyam paramam hareḥ na atas parataram kiṃcid śrāvyam śruti sukha āvaham
